# q-bio.BM [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Bayesian Learning of Distance Metrics Beyond RMSD for Biomolecule Alignment, Clustering, and Domain Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07352)
*Saumyak Mukherjee,Gerhard Hummer*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: 本文提出贝叶斯最优RMSD（Bayes-optimal RMSD, BRMSD），通过最大化贝叶斯后验（Bayesian posterior）优化每个原子的权重，解决经典RMSD因柔性区域主导全局指标而忽略刚性功能核心的问题，并提供了结构对齐、轨迹平滑、软K均值聚类（soft K-means clustering）和刚性域识别等分析模块，已在两个分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）系统中完成基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典均方根偏差（root-mean-square deviation, RMSD）对所有原子赋予等权重（equal weight），导致柔性环区（flexible loops）和无序区（disordered regions）在全局RMSD中占主导，而结构刚性且功能重要的核心区域贡献极小，因此需要一种能够自适应区分不同原子运动性的结构比较指标。

Method: BRMSD通过最大化贝叶斯后验（Bayesian posterior）联合优化每个原子的权重（per-atom weights）与结构平均（structural averages），引入位置涨落参数σ（position-fluctuation parameter σ）控制从经典RMSD（σ→∞）到聚焦刚性核心（σ→0）的过渡，实现低RMSD与权重均匀性（weight uniformity）之间的权衡。

Result: 该框架已在开源Python包BRMSD中实现，涵盖结构对齐、指定域聚焦对齐、轨迹平滑、软K均值聚类（soft K-means conformational clustering）和刚性域识别（rigid-domain identification）模块，并在内质网转位相关蛋白SND3和磷酸转移酶腺苷酸激酶（adenylate kinase）两个MD系统上完成了基准测试。

Conclusion: BRMSD通过贝叶斯框架自动识别刚性功能核心，克服了经典RMSD的权重均等问题，为分子动力学模拟的结构比较提供了一种更合理的度量方法。

Abstract: Root-mean-square deviation (RMSD) is the standard metric of structural comparison in molecular dynamics (MD) simulations. In its conventional form, RMSD assigns equal weight to all atoms regardless of mobility. Hence, flexible loops and disordered regions can dominate a global RMSD, while the rigid functional core contributes negligibly to the overall metric. To address this issue, we introduce the Bayes-optimal RMSD (BRMSD), which optimizes per-atom weights jointly with structural averages by maximizing a Bayesian posterior. In a trade-off between low RMSD and weight uniformity, a position-fluctuation parameter $σ$ controls the transition from classical RMSD ($σ\to \infty$) to a progressive focus on a rigid core ($σ\to 0$). The BRMSD framework supports analysis modules for structural alignment, focused alignment onto a user-specified domain, trajectory smoothing, soft $K$-means conformational clustering, and rigid-domain identification. These modules are implemented in the open-source Python package BRMSD (https://github.com/bio-phys/BRMSD) and benchmarked on two MD systems, the endoplasmic reticulum translocon-associated protein SND3 and the phosphotransferase adenylate kinase.

</details>


<div id='math.PR'></div>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Loop Equations Characterize Random Matrix Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07617)
*Paul Bourgade,Jiaoyang Huang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中的通用局部点过程可由其回路方程层级（loop equation hierarchies）唯一刻画：对于每个有理数 β>0，Sine_β 点过程是体回路方程层级的唯一解，Airy_β 点过程是边回路方程层级的唯一解。这一唯一性结果为普适性（universality）提供了直接路径——只需验证系综满足相应的近似回路方程即可。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机矩阵理论中的普适性（universality）现象——即不同随机矩阵系综（random matrix ensembles）在局部尺度上收敛到相同的点过程（如 Sine_β 或 Airy_β 过程）——长期以来是核心问题。本文旨在从回路方程层级（loop equation hierarchies）的视角为这一普适性提供一种简洁的证明路径。

Method: 作者证明在有理数 β>0 情形下，体回路方程层级（bulk loop equation hierarchy）和边回路方程层级（edge loop equation hierarchy）分别唯一地确定了 Sine_β 点过程和 Airy_β 点过程。基于这一唯一性结果，只要验证一个随机矩阵系综在相应局部尺度上近似满足对应的回路方程，即可直接得出该系综在局部尺度下的普适性。

Result: 对于每个有理数 β>0，Sine_β 点过程是体回路方程层级的唯一解，Airy_β 点过程是边回路方程层级的唯一解。这一唯一性将普适性证明简化为验证系综的近似回路方程。

Conclusion: 该唯一性结果为随机矩阵理论中的局部普适性提供了一条直接且统一的验证途径。在许多模型中，近似回路方程可通过局部律（local laws）和分部积分（integration by parts）加以建立。

Abstract: We prove that the universal local point processes of random matrix theory are characterized by their loop equation hierarchies. More precisely, for every rational $β>0$, the $\mathrm{Sine}_β$ point process is the unique solution of the bulk loop equation hierarchy, and the $\mathrm{Airy}_β$ point process is the unique solution of the edge loop equation hierarchy.
  These uniqueness results provide a direct route to universality: it suffices to verify the corresponding approximate loop equations for the ensemble. In many models, these equations follow from local laws and integration by parts.

</details>


<div id='physics.atom-ph'></div>

# physics.atom-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Hadronic vacuum polarization in hydrogen-like atoms and ions amid the interplay of recoil and finite-size effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07658)
*Franziska Hagelstein,Vadim Lensky,Bogdan Malaescu,Vladimir Pascalutsa*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用色散数据驱动方法和最先进的R比值参数化，评估了强子真空极化（hVP）对普通氢、μ子氢及类氢氦-3离子中兰姆移位和超精细分裂（HFS）的贡献，揭示了反冲与有限大小效应之间的相互作用，并首次计算了次领头阶hVP-有限大小修正，得到的HFS结果与此前所有评估存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子真空极化（hadronic vacuum polarization, hVP）以微小但决定性的量级进入简单原子系统，对当前高精度光谱学实验至关重要，因此需要对其进行精确的理论评估。

Method: 采用色散数据驱动方法（dispersive data-driven approach）与最新经验参数化的R比值（R ratio），分析反冲（recoil）效应与有限大小效应（finite-size effects）的相互作用，并引入核弹性形状因子（elastic form factors, FFs）以说明反冲修正的抑制机制。

Result: 朗姆移位（Lamb shift）的领头阶hVP贡献与文献在不确定度内一致；首次计算了次领头阶O(Z⁵α⁶) hVP-有限大小修正，该修正对μ³He⁺不可忽略；基态HFS结果为：μH中2.153(11) μeV，μ³He⁺中−15.19(57) μeV，普通H中0.0860(4) kHz，普通³He⁺中−0.476(17) kHz，其中μH的结果与此前评估相差约十倍于即将开展的CREMA和FAMU实验所预期的实验精度。

Conclusion: 反冲修正主导μ子素（muonium, Mu）的HFS，但被核弹性形状因子抑制；本文提供的hVP对HFS的贡献与此前所有评估显著偏离，表明现有理论理解需要修正，相关偏差足以影响CREMA和FAMU等高精度实验的预期测量。

Abstract: Hadronic vacuum polarization (hVP) enters simple atomic systems at a level that is small yet decisive for the precision spectroscopy now underway. We evaluate the hVP contributions to the Lamb shift and the hyperfine splitting (HFS) in ordinary and muonic hydrogen (H and $μ$H) and hydrogen-like helium-3 ions ($^3$He$^+$ and $μ^3$He$^+$), using the dispersive data-driven approach and state-of-the-art empirical parametrizations of the $R$ ratio. At the centre of the analysis is the interplay of recoil and finite-size effects: the recoil corrections that dominate the HFS in muonium (Mu), where both constituents are pointlike, are shown to be suppressed by the nuclear elastic form factors (FFs). Our results for the leading hVP contribution to the Lamb shift agree with the literature within uncertainties. Furthermore, we present a first evaluation of the subleading $O(Z^5α^6)$ hVP-finite-size correction, which is by no means negligible in $μ^3$He$^+$. Our results for the hVP contribution to the HFS deviate significantly from all previous evaluations. For the ground-state HFS, we obtain $2.153(11)~μ$eV in $μ$H and $-15.19(57)~μ$eV in $μ^3$He$^+$, as well as $0.0860(4)~$kHz and $-0.476(17)~$kHz in ordinary H and $^3$He$^+$, respectively. Notably, our result for $μ$H differs from previous evaluations by roughly ten times the experimental precision anticipated by the upcoming CREMA and FAMU measurements.

</details>

# nlin.SI [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [On difference-differential Lax pairs and integrals of Painlevé equations in finite characteristic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06980)
*Nalini Joshi,Tomas Lasic Latimer,Pieter Roffelsen*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该论文收集了经典潘勒韦方程（Painlevé equations）的二阶差分-微分Lax对（rank two difference-differential Lax pairs），将其整理为2×2矩阵形式（其中谱方程的系数矩阵为二次矩阵多项式），并描述了一种通用方法，从这些Lax对中导出特征p（characteristic p）下的运动积分（integrals of motion），从而为每个相关潘勒韦方程得到一份可数无穷的运动积分列表，每个素数p对应一个条目。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典潘勒韦方程在可积系统理论中具有核心地位，但其在特征p（有限特征域）下的运动积分结构尚缺乏系统的处理方法。该工作旨在填补这一空白，建立从Lax对到特征p运动积分的通用推导框架。

Method: 首先从文献中收集经典潘勒韦方程的二阶差分-微分Lax对，将其统一为2×2矩阵形式，其中谱方程（spectral equation）的系数矩阵为二次矩阵多项式（degree two matrix polynomial）。然后描述并应用一种通用方法，从这些Lax对推导特征p下的运动积分。

Result: 对于每个相关的潘勒韦方程，该方法生成一个可数无穷的运动积分列表，每个素数p对应一个积分条目。所有结果均以统一的矩阵形式呈现。

Conclusion: 该研究为经典潘勒韦方程在特征p下的可积结构提供了系统性的描述方案，所提出的通用方法可推广至其他可积系统在有限特征域下的分析。

Abstract: We collect rank two difference-differential Lax pairs for classical Painlevé equations in the literature and put each in $2\times 2$ matrix form with the coefficient matrix of the spectral equation a degree two matrix polynomial. We describe and apply a general method to obtain integrals of motion in characteristic $p$ from these Lax pairs. For every relevant Painlevé equation, this leads to a countable list of integrals of motion, with one entry for each prime $p$.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.EP'></div>

# astro-ph.EP [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Extra Invariant in Magnetohydrodynamics of Planets and Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07654)
*Alexander M. Balk*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 该论文在旋转分层流体的磁流体动力学（MHD）中建立了一个新的额外不变量（extra invariant），该不变量在绝热条件下（即长时间尺度上近似）守恒，并且与著名的发电机现象（dynamo phenomenon）存在关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁流体动力学（MHD）中守恒不变量极为罕见，发现新的不变量本身就具有重要的理论价值；此外，该不变量与发电机现象（dynamo phenomenon）的潜在联系进一步提升了其研究意义。

Method: 论文从旋转分层流体层的磁流体动力学（MHD）方程出发，通过理论分析建立了一个额外不变量（extra invariant），并证明了该不变量在绝热近似下（即长时间尺度上）近似守恒。

Result: 成功建立了一个在旋转分层流体层的磁流体动力学（MHD）中守恒的额外不变量（extra invariant），该不变量在绝热条件下近似守恒。

Conclusion: 该额外不变量（extra invariant）不仅本身具有理论重要性（因这类不变量极为罕见），而且与发电机现象（dynamo phenomenon）存在联系，为进一步理解磁流体动力学（MHD）中的相关物理过程提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The paper establishes extra invariant in magnetohydrodynamics (MHD) of rotating and stratified fluid layer. This invariant is conserved adiabatically, i.e. approximately over long time. The existence of the invariant is interesting by itself, as such invariants are extremely rare. However, in addition, this invariant appears to be connected to the famous dynamo phenomenon.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.IM'></div>

# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Machine learning pipeline for identifying tracks of muons and hadrons at GRAPES-3 muon telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07263)
*Mansi Talwar,Sambit Sarkar,Pravata K. Mohanty*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本研究针对GRAPES-3缪子望远镜（G3MT）中的穿透强子背景噪声问题，开发了一套机器学习流程，用于区分次级缪子（muon）与强子（hadron）的径迹。研究采用CORSIKA模拟的质子簇射作为Geant4探测器仿真的输入，先后实现了基于XGBoost的单粒子分类（准确率88.7%）、基于图神经网络（GNN）的多粒子分类，以及基于Dynamic Reduction Network的粒子数量回归估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRAPES-3实验通过地面广延大气簇射（extensive air shower）阵列和缪子望远镜（muon telescope）探测次级缪子，但穿透强子（punch-through hadron）会引入背景噪声。准确估计簇射中相关缪子的数量对于理解原初宇宙线（primary cosmic ray）的性质至关重要，因此需要开发有效方法区分缪子与强子的信号。

Method: 使用CORSIKA模拟能量范围为100–158 TeV的质子簇射，并将其作为Geant4探测器仿真的输入。单粒子分类阶段采用决策树（decision tree）、随机森林（random forest）、神经网络（neural network）和XGBoost四种方法进行对比；多粒子分类阶段将每个事件建模为以探测器击中点为节点的图（graph），构建带有边卷积层（edge convolution layer）的图神经网络（Graph Neural Network, GNN）对每个节点进行分类；此外开发了基于Dynamic Reduction Network的深度学习回归模型，用于同时估计撞击G3MT的粒子数和缪子数。

Result: 在单粒子分类中，XGBoost取得了最高的分类准确率88.7%。多粒子分类任务的具体分析结果将在论文中展示。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了机器学习方法，尤其是XGBoost和图神经网络（GNN），可有效用于G3MT中次级缪子与强子的径迹区分，为降低穿透强子背景噪声、提高缪子计数准确性提供了可行的技术路线。

Abstract: The GRAPES-3 experiment is a ground-based extensive air shower array which consists of approximately $400$ closely packed plastic scintillator detectors and a large area muon telescope. Estimating the number of associated muons created in an air shower is crucial to understand the properties of primary cosmic rays. The GRAPES-3 muon telescope (G3MT) records these secondary muons, however, the punch-through hadrons can introduce background noise. This study aims to develop a machine learning pipeline to distinguish the tracks of secondary muons and hadrons at G3MT. We have used CORSIKA-simulated proton showers having energy in the range 100-158 TeV as an input for a Geant4-based detector simulation to analyze the signatures of both type of particles. Initially, single-particle classification was performed using decision trees, random forests, neural networks, and XGBoost, with XGBoost achieving the highest accuracy of 88.7\%. For multiparticle classification, we modelled Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) where each event was represented as a graph with detector hits as nodes. A GNN with edge convolution layers was developed to classify each node as a muon or hadron hit. Following this, a deep learning regression model using Dynamic Reduction Network was developed to estimate the number of particles and muons striking G3MT simultaneously. Details of the analysis and results of the multiparticle classification task will be presented.

</details>


### [7] [The Deep Learning Cosmic Ray Energy Reconstruction Pipeline for the GRAPES-3 Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07265)
*Sambit Sarkar,Mansi Talwar,Pravata K. Mohanty*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图神经网络（GNN）的模块化、动态能量重构算法，用于GRAPES-3实验中的宇宙线初级能量测量。该算法通过自动化特征映射并在潜空间（latent space）中缩放度量，显著提升了响应分辨率，并在不同质量组和簇射年龄下对重构能量、偏差及分辨率进行了系统比较与微调优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙线的质量无关能量重构（mass independent energy reconstruction）对于理解其起源、加速和传播至关重要，同时精确的初级能量测量有助于改善质量分类并实现各元素随能量变化的各向异性图谱。GRAPES-3实验原有的基于电子大小标定曲线的方法精度有限，因此需要开发更精确的重构算法。

Method: 采用模块化且动态的图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）重构算法，实现特征映射的自动化。通过研究模型的潜空间（latent space）来观察学习过程，并在潜空间中缩放度量以提升响应分辨率。对不同的微调模型进行了重构能量和偏差的全面比较，同时研究了不同质量组和簇射年龄下的分辨率变化。

Result: 基于GNN的重构算法相比传统的电子大小标定曲线方法，能够建立显著更优的精度。在潜空间中缩放度量可进一步改善响应分辨率。不同微调模型在重构能量和偏差上存在差异，且分辨率随不同质量组和簇射年龄而有所变化。

Conclusion: 研究表明，模块化、动态的GNN重构算法在GRAPES-3实验中可有效提升宇宙线初级能量的测量精度，潜空间分析为模型学习提供了可解释性，微调策略有助于针对不同质量组和簇射年龄优化性能。

Abstract: The mass independent energy reconstruction of cosmic rays is crucial for understanding their origin, acceleration, and propagation. Precise measurement of the primary energy can also lead to better mass classification and could enable energy dependent anisotropy maps for individual elements. The GRAPES-3 experiment located in Ooty consisting of 400 scintillator detector array placed 8 m apart covering an area of 25000 m$^2$ with a dedicated muon detector made of 3712 proportional counters, is designed to do these kinds of measurements. Previously electron size calibration curves have been used to find primary energy in the GRAPES-3 data analysis framework however significantly better precision can be established using graph neural network. Thus, in this work we have implemented a modular and dynamic GNN based reconstruction algorithm that automates feature mapping. We demonstrate how the model is learning by studying its latent space and show that scaling the metric in the latent space can lead to further improvements in response resolution. Fine-tuned strategies are presented and a thorough comparison of the reconstructed energy and bias is done for different fine-tuned models along with studying the resolution variation for different mass groups and shower age.

</details>


<div id='hep-th'></div>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Towards gauge independence in asymptotically safe quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06657)
*Kevin Falls,Renata Ferrero,Giovanni Oglialoro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究渐进安全量子引力中固有时间重整化群流的规范依赖性。通过在本质方案（essential scheme）中使用场重定义，将冗余的离壳贡献与物理耦合的壳上运行分离。研究发现，尽管流动方程依赖于规范参数，但通过吸收冗余项可以实现阶阶抵消；在四导数近似和球对称背景上，规范依赖性可在特定条件下完全消除，关键依赖于调节函数（regulator）的选择。最终得到的本质流（essential flow）展现出规范无关的非高斯不动点，支持量子引力中的普适信息编码于壳上本质扇区（on-shell essential sector）的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中的重整化群方法常受到规范依赖性问题的困扰，即物理可观测量不应依赖于规范固定参数，但在流动方程中这种依赖往往不能自动消除。该工作旨在系统研究固有时间重整化群（proper-time renormalisation group）框架下规范依赖性的抵消机制，并验证在本质方案中壳上物理耦合是否能够获得规范无关的结果。

Method: 采用本质方案，通过场重定义（field redefinitions）将冗余的离壳贡献从物理耦合的壳上运行中分离出来。在两种近似下展开分析：一是在一般背景上投影至最多四导数项（忽略边界项）；二是在最大对称背景上保留Ricci标量的所有阶数。利用壳上条件验证单圈阶的抵消机制。

Result: 在四导数近似中，牛顿常数（Newton's constant）的β函数中保留的规范参数依赖性在耦合的三阶上消失。在球对称（sphere）背景下，流动对一般规范的两个参数在所有曲率阶数和耦合阶数上均不依赖。单圈验证表明，规范依赖的涨落贡献与鬼扇区（ghost sector）在壳上精确抵消。最终本质流呈现规范无关的非高斯不动点（non-Gaussian fixed point）。

Conclusion: 该抵消机制依赖于调节函数的选择，并非自动成立。结果表明，量子引力中普适性（universal）信息确实编码于壳上本质扇区，本质方案为提取规范无关的可重整化流提供了可行框架。

Abstract: We study gauge dependence in proper-time renormalisation group flows for asymptotically safe quantum gravity. Working in an essential scheme, we use field redefinitions to separate redundant off-shell contributions from the on-shell running of physical couplings. We consider two approximations: in the first, we work on general backgrounds and project onto all terms with up to four derivatives, neglecting boundary terms; in the second, we work on a maximally symmetric background and retain all orders in the Ricci scalar. Although the flow equation depends on the gauge parameters, this dependence can be cancelled order by order once the redundant terms are absorbed by field redefinitions. In the four-derivative approximation, the dependence on the retained gauge parameter drops out of the beta function for Newton's constant to third order in the coupling. On the sphere, the flow becomes independent of both parameters of the general gauge to all curvature orders, and all orders in the coupling. Crucially, this cancellation depends on the choice of regulator. We verify the mechanism explicitly at one loop, where the gauge-dependent fluctuation contributions are cancelled by the ghost sector on shell. The resulting essential flow displays a gauge-independent non-Gaussian fixed point, supporting the interpretation that universal information in quantum gravity is encoded in the on-shell essential sector.

</details>


### [9] [Perturbiner methods in scattering amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06661)
*Renann Lipinski Jusinskas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对基于微扰子方法（perturbiner method）推导的Berends--Giele流（Berends--Giele currents）进行了综述性介绍，涵盖其在不同场论模型中的基本构建以及最新的研究进展，其中包含部分此前未发表的隐性知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Berends--Giele流近年来在散射振幅社区（amplitude community）中重新引起广泛关注，在引力振幅（gravitational amplitudes）、宇宙学关联函数（cosmological correlators）和弦理论（string theory）等多个新背景中都有重要应用。然而，相关方法的知识分散，部分关键结果尚未正式发表，因此需要一篇系统性的教学综述来整合该领域的基本原理与最新进展。

Method: 本文采用微扰子方法作为统一框架，该方法是三十年前提出的、以经典多粒子解（classical multi-particle solutions）形式组织树级散射数据（tree-level scattering data）的理论工具。综述从该方法的公式化出发，涵盖多种场论模型（但未做穷举），并逐步延伸到最新的文献成果。

Result: 综述整合了Berends--Giele流在不同物理系统中的构建与应用，并包含了若干此前未在正式出版物中出现的社区隐性知识（tacit knowledge）。

Conclusion: 本文为该领域提供了一份兼具教学性与前沿性的导引，有助于推动微扰子方法在散射振幅及相关研究中的进一步应用。

Abstract: Berends--Giele currents have recently attracted renewed attention across the amplitude community, appearing in new contexts ranging from gravitational amplitudes to cosmological correlators and string theory. They can be derived from first principles using the perturbiner method, a thirty-year-old framework that organizes tree-level scattering data in the form of classical multi-particle solutions to field theory equations of motion. After its rediscovery about a decade ago, it has been systematically studied and applied in many different contexts. This review aims to provide a pedagogical introduction to the method, covering its basic formulation across a broad (but certainly not exhaustive) range of models and progressing to some of the most recent findings in the literature. This includes several unpublished results, many of which represent tacit knowledge of the community that has not previously appeared in print.

</details>


### [10] [Generalised global symmetries in 5d $\mathcal{N}=1$ theories from the blow-up equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06663)
*William Harding,Noppadol Mekareeya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从吹胀方程（blow-up equations）中提取五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超共形场论（superconformal field theories, SCFTs）广义全局对称性数据的方法，包括高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetries）、2-群对称性（2-group symmetries）及其't Hooft反常（'t Hooft anomalies），并在多种规范理论与非拉格朗日理论（non-Lagrangian theories）中进行了验证与新结果推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超共形场论具有丰富的广义全局对称性，但此前缺乏系统提取这些对称性数据（如1-形式对称性的立方自反常、混合反常以及2-群对称性）的直接方法。

Method: 核心工具是吹胀方程（blow-up equations），其经典预因子 $\exp(-V_n)$ 为每个磁通量（magnetic flux）赋予权重。在该预因子中，指数的小数部分编码了1-形式对称性的立方自反常及其与瞬子（instanton）、味（flavour）、引力（gravitational）和 $\mathrm{SU}(2)_R$ 对称性的混合反常。同时结合超共形指标（superconformal index）确定的紫外不动点（ultraviolet fixed point）忠实连续全局对称性，来判断是否存在2-群对称性或混合't Hooft反常。

Result: 在 $\mathrm{SU}(4)$、$\mathrm{USp}(4)$（带反对称超多重态）以及 $\mathrm{Spin}(7)$、$\mathrm{Spin}(8)$（带矢量超多重态）等规范理论中验证了该方法。在非拉格朗日理论中获得新结果：推导出 $B_N$ 和 $B_N^{(1,2,3)}$ 族的有效预势（effective prepotentials）、秩二理论 $\mathbb{P}^2\cup\mathbb{F}_3$ 和 $\mathbb{P}^2\cup\mathbb{F}_6$ 的立方1-形式反常，以及多个涉及1-形式对称性与味对称性的混合反常。

Conclusion: 吹胀方程是提取五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ SCFT 广义全局对称性数据的有效工具，能够同时确定高阶形式对称性的反常结构、2-群对称性及其't Hooft反常，并适用于非拉格朗日理论。

Abstract: Five-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ superconformal field theories admit a rich variety of generalised global symmetries, including higher-form symmetries, 2-group symmetries, and their 't$~$Hooft anomalies. We show that this data can be extracted directly from the blow-up equations that govern the instanton partition functions of such theories on the $Ω$-background. The central object is the classical prefactor $\exp(-V_n)$ that weights each magnetic flux on the blown-up geometry: evaluated on a background for the electric 1-form symmetry, the fractional parts of its exponents encode the cubic self-anomaly of the 1-form symmetry, as well as its mixed anomalies with the instanton, flavour, gravitational, and $\mathrm{SU}(2)_R$ symmetries. Combined with the faithful continuous global symmetry of the ultraviolet fixed point, which we determine from the superconformal index, the same data decides whether the theory possesses a 2-group symmetry or a mixed 't$~$Hooft anomaly. We illustrate the method in gauge theories, including $\mathrm{SU}(4)$ and $\mathrm{USp}(4)$ with antisymmetric hypermultiplets, and $\mathrm{Spin}(7)$ and $\mathrm{Spin}(8)$ with vector hypermultiplets, as well as in several families of non-Lagrangian theories, for which we obtain new results: notably, the effective prepotentials of the $B_N$ and $B_N^{(1,2,3)}$ families, the cubic 1-form anomalies of the rank-two theories $\mathbb{P}^2\cup\mathbb{F}_3$ and $\mathbb{P}^2\cup\mathbb{F}_6$, and several mixed anomalies involving the 1-form and flavour symmetries.

</details>


### [11] [Effective Field Theories for Material Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06666)
*Angelo Esposito,Alberto Nicolis,Riccardo Penco*

TL;DR: 本文从高能理论视角综述了凝聚态系统中集体激发和局域激发的有效场论（effective field theory）描述，特别强调时空对称性及其自发破缺所驱动的戈德斯通动力学（Goldstone dynamics），并试图弥合子领域间的语言差异，揭示概念上的相似性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弥合高能理论与凝聚态物理之间的语言隔阂，揭示两者在描述集体和局域激发时所共享的对称性破缺框架和概念相似性。

Method: 采用综述性方法，从高能理论视角系统梳理和回顾了有效场论（effective field theory）在固态和流体系统中描述集体激发与局域激发的应用，重点分析时空对称性及其自发破缺机制。

Result: 指出戈德斯通动力学（Goldstone dynamics）可作为多种物理现象的底层统一机制，并识别出不同子领域之间在概念上的大量相似之处。

Conclusion: 有效场论框架能够有效统一描述凝聚态系统中的集体和局域激发，时空对称性的自发破缺是关键组织原理；跨领域的概念桥接有助于深化对凝聚态系统的理解。

Abstract: We review recent progress in understanding certain aspects of condensed matter systems from a high energy theory perspective. We discuss effective field theories that describe collective bulk and localized excitations in a variety of solid and fluid systems. Particular emphasis is placed on the role played by spacetime symmetries and their spontaneous breaking. The resulting Goldstone dynamics can be seen as underlying a wide variety of phenomena. We attempt to bridge the language gap between subfields while underscoring the numerous conceptual similarities.

### [12] [Monodromy defects in Chern-Simons theory and Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06669)
*Federico Ambrosino,Jaume Gomis,Suriyah Rajalingam Kannagi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在具有电荷共轭对称性的陈-西蒙斯理论中构造了一类新可观测对象——余维二单值性缺陷，并证明其由扭仿射李代数标记，与由未扭仿射李代数标记的威尔逊环一起构成完整的线缺陷谱，从而实现了Kac仿射李代数分类中所有代数的物理解释。文章进一步给出了SU(N)_k理论中该类缺陷的't Hooft展开及其在拓扑弦论中的全息对偶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 陈-西蒙斯理论中的威尔逊环算子已揭示量子场论、分数量子霍尔效应、拓扑学、共形场论和弦论之间的深刻联系。为了进一步探索该理论中的可观测对象及其物理意义，本文在具有电荷共轭对称性的情况下构造了一类全新的可观测对象——余维二单值性缺陷（codimension-two monodromy defects），并系统研究其数学结构、关联函数及全息对偶。

Method: 本文首先在具有电荷共轭（charge conjugation）对称性的陈-西蒙斯理论中构造余维二单值性缺陷，其特点是围绕缺陷的场回到自身但经过电荷共轭变换。通过关联函数分析，建立了缺陷由扭仿射李代数（twisted affine Lie algebra）的可积表示标记的机制，并利用模数据（modular data）和融合数据（fusion data）确定威尔逊线和单值性缺陷的精确关联函数。此外，在SU(N)_k理论中计算了单值性缺陷的't Hooft展开。

Result: 威尔逊环由未扭仿射李代数（untwisted affine Lie algebra）的可积表示标记，而单值性缺陷由对应的扭仿射李代数的可积表示标记；两者共同构成一个Z₂-交叉辫子张量范畴（Z₂-crossed braided tensor category）。线缺陷谱实现了Kac仿射李代数分类中的全部代数。最轻单值性缺陷的插入将Gopakumar-Vafa对偶中的解链锥体背景替换为该解链锥体的特定定向折叠（orientifold），将定向弦理论转变为非定向弦理论。激发态单值性缺陷则对应于定向折叠背景中的膜集合。

Conclusion: 陈-西蒙斯理论中的线缺陷谱给出了Kac仿射李代数分类中所有代数的物理实现，其中威尔逊环对应未扭情形，单值性缺陷对应扭情形。该发现扩展了陈-西蒙斯理论的可观测对象体系，并为仿射李代数分类提供了直接的场论解释。此外，单值性缺陷在拓扑弦论中的全息对偶效应——将定向弦转变为非定向弦——展示了几何背景的深刻转变。

Abstract: Wilson loop operators in Chern-Simons theory have revealed profound links between quantum field theory, the fractional quantum Hall effect, topology, conformal field theory, and string theory. In Chern-Simons theories with charge conjugation symmetry, we construct a new class of observables: codimension-two monodromy defects around which fields return to themselves up to charge conjugation. Whereas Wilson loops are labeled by integrable representations of an untwisted affine Lie algebra, monodromy defects are labeled by those of the corresponding twisted affine algebra. The modular and fusion data of these two algebras determine the exact correlation functions of Wilson lines and monodromy defects, which together furnish a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-crossed braided tensor category. The spectrum of line defects in Chern-Simons theory thus gives a physical realization of every algebra in Kac's classification of affine Lie algebras: untwisted for Wilson loops, twisted for monodromy defects. We also determine the exact 't Hooft expansion of monodromy defects in $SU(N)_k$ Chern-Simons theory and identify their holographic duals in topological string theory. The insertion of the lightest monodromy defect has a striking effect: it replaces the resolved conifold background of the Gopakumar-Vafa duality by a specific orientifold of the resolved conifold, transmuting the dual theory of oriented strings into one of unoriented strings. Each excited monodromy defect is then realized as a collection of branes in the orientifold background, with the brane content determined by the representation of the twisted affine algebra that labels the defect.

</details>


### [13] [Classical conformal invariance and superhorizon dynamics in de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06679)
*Maria Cristina Fiore,Andrea F. Sanfilippo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究软 de Sitter 有效场论（soft de Sitter effective theory）在经典共形不变理论中的应用，以共形耦合的 φ⁴ 理论为例，指出标准有效理论构造不适用于此类模型，并提出识别超视界自由度的新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软 de Sitter 有效理论是描述 de Sitter 空间中等时关联函数在晚期行为的有效候选框架，但它在具有经典共形不变性（classical conformal invariance）的理论中是否适用尚不清楚，需要检验。

Method: 以共形耦合的 φ⁴ 理论为玩具模型，分析四点关联函数（trispectrum）的树图匹配（tree-level matching）是否符合有效理论的幂次计数方案（power-counting scheme），并与共形耦合的 φ³ 理论中的三点关联函数（bispectrum）匹配结果进行对比。

Result: 发现 φ⁴ 理论中四点关联函数的树图匹配不符合预期的幂次计数方案，而 φ³ 理论中三点关联函数的匹配则一致有效。这表明标准有效理论构造无法直接描述这类模型的量子晚期动力学。

Conclusion: 提出一种识别共形不变理论中主导超视界自由度（superhorizon degrees of freedom）的规则，作为构建其晚期有效描述的起点，并简要讨论了 log(-kη) 形式对数项在该语境下的解释。

Abstract: Soft de Sitter Effective Theory is a well-motivated candidate for the correct effective late-time description of equal-time correlation functions in de Sitter space. In this work, we study its application to theories that enjoy classical conformal invariance, using the conformally-coupled $φ^4$-theory as a toy model. While quantum effects generate non-trivial late-time dynamics in such models, we argue that it is not described by the standard construction of the effective theory as discussed thus far in the literature. We show that the tree-level matching of the trispectrum onto the effective theory does not fit into the expected power-counting scheme, and we contrast it with the matching of the tree-level bispectrum in the conformally-coupled $φ^3$-theory, where it works consistently. We then propose a prescription to identify the leading superhorizon degrees of freedom in such theories, which should serve as the starting point for the construction of their late-time effective description. The interpretation of logarithms of the form $\log(-kη)$ in this context is briefly discussed.

### [14] [Integrable systems inspired by DAHA and DIM algebra: type $C^\vee C$ versus type $A$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06738)
*L. Bishler,A. Mironov,A. Popolitov*

TL;DR: 本文探讨了丁-伊哈拉-三木代数（DIM algebra）与两类量子可积系统——Ruijsenaars 系统和 Cherednik DAHA 系统——之间的关联，重点分析了 A 型和 C^∨C 型系统中对称与非对称 Koornwinder 多项式作为本征函数的性质及其异同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究 Koornwinder 多项式（对称与非对称形式）作为可积系统本征函数的数学结构，澄清 A 型和 C^∨C 型系统之间的相似性与关键区别。

Method: 通过 DIM 代数与球面 DAHA（spherical DAHA）之间的对应关系，将 Ruijsenaars 系统与 DAHA 哈密顿量相联系；进而利用球面 DAHA 构造可积的 Koornwinder 哈密顿量，并分别求解其对称与非对称 Koornwinder 多项式本征函数。

Result: 给出了 A 型和 C^∨C 型两类可积系统中 Koornwinder 多项式的生成机制，指出二者在结构上具有高度相似性，但也存在重要差异。

Conclusion: Koornwinder 多项式可通过 DAHA 框架统一理解，C^∨C 型系统为 Koornwinder 哈密顿量的自然来源，而 A 型系统则提供了类比参照；两类系统的对比有助于深化对量子可积系统本征函数结构的认识。

Abstract: The Ding-Iohara-Miki (DIM) algebra (quantum toroidal algebra of $\widehat{gl_1}$) is related to a wide class of quantum many-particle integrable systems, a typical one being the Ruijsenaars trigonometric system with eigenfunctions that are a triad formed by the Noumi-Shiraishi power series, the Macdonald polynomials, and the Baker-Akhiezer multivariable function. Other integrable systems of this type are obtained from the Ruijsenaars system by twisting. At the same time, the Ruijsenaars Hamiltonians are directly related to the Hamiltonians of another quantum integrable system, the Cherednik DAHA Hamiltonians of type $A$ (and their twisted versions in the twisted case), due to the correspondence between the DIM algebra and the spherical DAHA. The eigenfunctions of the DAHA Hamiltonians are non-symmetric Macdonald polynomials. Similarly, there is a class of integrable DAHA Hamiltonians of type $C^\vee C$, the spherical version of which, in turn, allows one to generate integrable Koornwinder Hamiltonians. The eigenfunctions of these two integrable systems are, respectively, non-symmetric and symmetric Koornwinder polynomials, which are our main interest in this paper. Here we consider the cases of both type $A$ and type $C^\vee C$ systems, since they are sufficiently similar, and point out important distinctions between them.

### [15] [Evidence for renormalized instantons in real-time simulations of vacuum decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06680)
*Emilie Hertig,Alexander C. Jenkins,Hiranya V. Peiris,Andrew Pontzen,Matthew C. Johnson*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上真空衰变用欧几里得瞬子方法（Euclidean instanton method）描述，而格点模拟可实现宇宙学及冷原子类比实验相关动力学可观测量（dynamical observables）的真实时间建模，但两种形式学之间缺乏明确的定量联系。

Method: 通过对相对论性标量场（relativistic scalar field）进行零温度格点模拟，提取系综平均的气泡轮廓（ensemble-averaged bubble profiles），并将其与Coleman瞬子解及经典热学预测进行对比；进一步在恰当重整化的势中求解瞬子解，考察其与模拟结果的匹配程度。

Result: 模拟观测到的气泡轮廓与裸Coleman瞬子（bare Coleman bounce）及经典热学预测存在显著差异；但在重整化势（renormalized potential）中的瞬子解能够复现测量的轮廓及其对紫外截断（UV cutoff）的依赖，且预测的衰变率在考察参数范围内与模拟一致。

Conclusion: 单一重整化欧几里得对象（single renormalized Euclidean object）能够捕捉这些独立可观测量，强有力地表明重整化（renormalization）解释了两种形式学之间的差异，并为瞬子预测、格点模拟及未来真空衰变实验检验之间建立了定量联系。

Abstract: While vacuum decay is traditionally described by Euclidean instanton methods, lattice simulations enable real-time modeling of dynamical observables relevant to cosmology and upcoming cold-atom analog experiments. We investigate the relationship between these approaches by extracting ensemble-averaged bubble profiles from zero-temperature simulations of a relativistic scalar field. Our observed profiles differ markedly from the bare Coleman bounce and classical thermal predictions. However, we find that instanton solutions in an appropriately renormalized potential reproduce both the measured profiles and their dependence on the UV cutoff, and predict decay rates consistent with simulations across the parameter range considered. The fact that a single renormalized Euclidean object captures these independent observables provides strong evidence that renormalization accounts for the discrepancy between the two formalisms, and establishes a quantitative link between instanton predictions, lattice simulations, and forthcoming empirical tests of vacuum decay.

</details>


### [16] [Geometry-induced Casimir response in a helicoidal spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06695)
*Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了无挠螺旋时空（torsionless helicoidal spacetime）中大质量标量场的卡西米尔响应（Casimir response），发现模式层面存在线性螺旋分裂（linear helicoidal splitting），但非手性真空求和（nonchiral vacuum sum）中线性项抵消，主导修正为扭曲的二次项，定义了螺旋真空磁化率（helicoidal vacuum susceptibility），并在圆柱形狄利克雷腔（cylindrical Dirichlet cavity）中计算了该磁化率及其对径向卡西米尔力（radial Casimir force）的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在具有几何扭曲的弯曲时空中，真空涨落的卡西米尔效应如何受到时空非对角度规分量的影响，特别是模式级别的手征性（chirality）如何产生有限的二次响应。

Method: 研究采用 Levi-Civita 联络（Levi-Civita connection）的无挠螺旋时空背景，该背景为超静态弯曲时空（ultrastatic and curved），标量曲率 \(R=-2Ω^2\)。通过分析大质量标量场的本征模式，考察非对角度规分量诱导的角量子数与轴向量子数之间的几何耦合，并在局部紫外减法（local ultraviolet subtractions）后定义螺旋真空磁化率。

Result: 单个模式呈现线性螺旋分裂，但非手性真空求和导致线性项抵消；主导的卡西米尔修正为扭曲的二次项。在圆柱形狄利克雷腔中，计算了方案依赖的螺旋真空磁化率及其对径向卡西米尔力的修正。

Conclusion: 无挠螺旋几何提供了一种可控的设定，在该设定中模式级别的手征性能使真空涨落产生有限的二次响应。

Abstract: We investigate the Casimir response of a massive scalar field in a torsionless helicoidal spacetime with Levi-Civita connection. The background is ultrastatic and curved, with scalar curvature \(R=-2Ω^2\), and its off-diagonal metric component induces a geometric coupling between angular and axial quantum numbers. We show that individual modes exhibit a linear helicoidal splitting, whereas the linear contribution cancels in the nonchiral vacuum sum. The leading Casimir correction is therefore quadratic in the twist and defines a helicoidal vacuum susceptibility after local ultraviolet subtractions. For a cylindrical Dirichlet cavity, we compute this scheme-defined susceptibility and the associated correction to the radial Casimir force. The results identify torsionless helicoidal geometry as a controlled setting in which mode-level chirality produces a finite quadratic response of vacuum fluctuations.

### [17] [BMS$_3$ invariant field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06826)
*Diego Hidalgo,Stefan Vandoren,Huaxuan Zeng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文综述并构建了具有BMS₃对称性的二维场论，涵盖带有和不带中心扩展的多种模型，包括电性、磁性和正则标量理论及其耦合。通过分析边界贡献和反项，建立了BMS₃不变性所需的变分原理，并推导了通量-平衡定律。在平空间全息框架下，一个简单的自由电性BMS₃模型可通过适当的中心荷再现三维爱因斯坦引力的单值性分类。此外，AdS₃和dS₃的平空间极限分别由Liouville理论和欧几里得Liouville理论的Carroll极限描述，两种理论谱同构但超平移荷和中心荷符号相反，表明AdS₃和dS₃的平空间极限为平空间全息提供了互补的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用构造性场论方法，系统构建了多种具有BMS₃对称性的标量场论模型（包括电性、磁性和正则版本），并通过引入边界反项和外部源，严格分析角点边界贡献以维持BMS₃不变性；同时利用平空间极限（flat-space limit）从AdS₃和dS₃的边界动力学（Liouville理论和欧几里得Liouville理论）推导出Carroll极限（Carrollian limit）下的BMS₃理论。

Result: 得到的主要结果包括：(1) 成功构造了具有BMS₃对称性的电性、磁性和正则标量理论及其耦合模型；(2) 确定了BMS₃不变性所需的边界条件和反项，并导出了相应的通量-平衡定律（flux-balance laws）；(3) 发现自由电性BMS₃模型可复现三维爱因斯坦引力的单值性分类（monodromy classification）；(4) 揭示了AdS₃和dS₃平空间极限下的BMS₃理论谱同构，但超平移荷（supertranslation charges）和中心荷（central charge）符号相反。

Conclusion: 本文表明平空间全息可以通过AdS₃和dS₃的平空间极限以互补方式实现，两类极限下的BMS₃理论在谱结构上等价但在荷符号上存在差异，这为深入理解平空间引力全息对应提供了新的理论工具和视角。

Abstract: We review existing and construct new two-dimensional field theories that exhibit BMS$_3$ symmetry, with and without central extensions. These include interacting electric, magnetic and canonical BMS$_3$ scalar theories, as well as couplings between the electric and magnetic sectors. We provide a careful analysis of boundary contributions at the corner points $u\rightarrow\pm\infty$, determine the counterterms and boundary conditions required by BMS$_3$ invariance, and study the corresponding variational principles. Furthermore, we introduce external sources and derive the associated flux-balance laws. Within the framework of flat-space holography, we show that a simple free electric BMS$_3$ model with the appropriate central charge reproduces the monodromy classification of three-dimensional Einstein gravity. Finally, we investigate the flat-space limits of both AdS$_3$ and dS$_3$, whose boundary dynamics are described by Carrollian limits of Liouville and Euclidean Liouville theory, respectively. Although the resulting BMS$_3$ theories possess isomorphic spectra, they differ in the signs of the supertranslation charges and the central charge. This suggests that the flat-space limits of AdS$_3$ and dS$_3$ provide complementary realizations of flat-space holography.

Conclusion: 该几何方法为研究5d SCFT的Higgs分支及相关的重整化群流（RG flows）提供了新的视角，磁quiver的一致性检验支持了所提出对应关系的有效性。

Abstract: Higgs Branches of 5d SCFTs are hyperkähler cones, symplectic varieties with interesting nested singularities governing the structure of possible Higgs branch RG flows. The main purpose of this note is to investigate 5d Higgs Branches via a geometric route: we study 5d SCFTs geometrically engineered from M-theory on non-compact Calabi-Yau threefolds, with non-isolated singularities. We match the (dynamical) complex structure deformations of the threefold with the symplectic leaves in the Higgs branch of the 5d SCFT, constructing its stratification purely relying on geometry. Consistency checks for our proposal are presented exploiting magnetic quivers.

### [19] [On Integrable Structures on Non-compact Boundaries in Three-Dimensional Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06867)
*Hamed Adami,Kristiansen Lara,Anouchah Latifi,René Meyer*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非紧致空间边界上的三维爱因斯坦引力，并探索有限截止全息术与可积系统之间的深层联系，特别是全息 $T\bar T$ 形变的精确实现机制。

Method: 采用陈-西蒙斯形式下的精确流体/引力对偶，推导准局部应力张量的径向流方程；并发展边界动力学的逆散射描述，分析谱数据的引力解释及孤子解的有限截止形变。

Result: 证明了径向流方程实现了有限截止处的全息 $T\bar T$ 形变；发现尽管边界演化由可积双哈密顿层次（integrable bi-Hamiltonian hierarchy）控制，但径向流本身相对于规范泊松结构是非哈密顿的。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个统一框架，将可积性、准局部引力可观测量、逆散射理论以及非紧致边界上的有限截止全息术有机整合。

Abstract: We study three-dimensional Einstein gravity with negative cosmological constant on non-compact spatial boundaries within the Chern-Simons formulation. Using an exact fluid/gravity correspondence, we derive a closed radial flow equation for the quasi-local stress tensor and show that it realizes the holographic $T\bar T$ deformation at finite cutoff. We further develop the inverse-scattering description of the boundary dynamics, identifying the gravitational interpretation of the associated spectral data and analyzing the finite-cutoff deformation of soliton solutions. Although the boundary evolution is governed by an integrable bi-Hamiltonian hierarchy, we show that the radial flow itself is not Hamiltonian with respect to the canonical Poisson structure. Our results establish a unified framework connecting integrability, quasi-local gravitational observables, inverse scattering, and finite-cutoff holography on non-compact boundaries.

### [20] [Phase transitions and uberholography of holographic pure-state geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06870)
*Ning Bao,Keiichiro Furuya,Jacob March*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了纯态全息几何的纠错性质，推导了AdS₃/CFT₂中纠缠楔连通/断开转变的交叉比阈值关系，并分析了递归打孔过程的代码特性，包括分形维数与价格、距离的上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用表面/态对应（surface/state correspondence）将混合边界子区域替换为Ryu-Takayanagi测地线，在AdS₃/CFT₂中推导交叉比阈值关系；通过递归打孔数值模拟分析分形维数和纠错码参数上界。

Result: 推导出交叉比阈值关系 η'/η = e^{ΔH/2}，其中ΔH完全由终止于RT边界的测地线贡献，并分类了其符号由孔端点模式决定的条件。递归打孔不能在RT边界内部启动，但未受扰动的渐近边界仍可分形化，分形维数约为α≈0.786。价格和距离上界具有过程依赖性，保留RT边界时获得的界比先迹掉RT边界再分形化更严格。

Conclusion: 纯态全息几何中的递归打孔行为受到RT边界的约束，分形维数呈现普适性，但纠错码参数上界依赖于具体操作过程。

Abstract: We study the error-correcting properties of pure-state holographic geometries, in which mixed boundary subregions are replaced, via the surface/state correspondence, by the Ryu--Takayanagi (RT) geodesic bounding their entanglement wedges. In AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ we derive a cross-ratio threshold relation $η'/η= e^{ΔH/2}$ for the connected/disconnected transition of the entanglement wedge when two holes are punched in such a geometry. The quantity $ΔH$ is sourced entirely by geodesics ending on RT boundaries. It shifts the standard two-interval threshold $η= 1/2$, and we classify when its sign is fixed by the pattern of hole endpoints. Turning to code properties, we show that the recursive hole-punching underlying uberholography cannot start within an RT-boundary, while an untouched asymptotic boundary can still fractalize, and we find numerically that in the configurations we study it does so with the universal fractal dimension $α\approx 0.786$. The resulting upper bounds on price and distance are nevertheless procedure dependent. In the configurations we study, punching holes on the asymptotic boundary while retaining the RT-boundary yields strictly tighter bounds than first tracing out the RT-boundary and then fractalizing.

### [22] [Thermodynamics of Deformed AdS-Schwarzschild Black Holes Beyond the Bekenstein Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07234)

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在非相互作用时空模型中引入高阶修正，采用非广延熵形式——Tsallis熵（Tsallis entropy）和Barrow熵（Barrow entropy）——对变形AdS-Schwarzschild黑洞进行热力学分析，并计算焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀（Joule-Thomson expansion）等关键热力学量。

Result: 强熵变形下黑洞热力学行为显著偏离常规结果；随着非广延性程度降低，系统渐近恢复经典特征，显示出跨统计区间的涌现普适性（emergent universality）。同时获得了质量、温度、热容、吉布斯自由能、焓、内能和焦耳-汤姆逊系数等关键热力学量的计算结果。

Abstract: This work investigates the thermodynamic behavior of deformed AdS-Schwarzschild black holes by incorporating higher-order corrections within non-interacting spacetime models and extended entropy frameworks. To address the inadequacies of classical statistical mechanics in describing gravitational systems with non-local and long-range interactions, we employ non-extensive entropy formalisms, specifically Tsallis and Barrow entropies, which capture quantum-scale deviations and extended correlations. The resulting thermodynamic analysis reveals significant departures from conventional black hole behavior under strong entropy deformations. Notably, as the degree of non-extensivity decreases, the system asymptotically recovers classical features, indicating an emergent universality across statistical regimes. Furthermore, the Joule-Thomson (JT) expansion is examined to analyze the temperature-pressure response during adiabatic processes. Key thermodynamic quantities, including mass, temperature, heat capacity, Gibbs free energy, enthalpy, internal energy, and the JT coefficient, are computed under the influence of non-extensive entropy corrections. These results provide deeper insight into black hole thermodynamics in quantum-corrected spacetimes and offer new avenues for exploring gravitational systems beyond the traditional Bekenstein-Hawking (BH) framework.

Method: 采用相对等变局域化方法处理量子M理论的路径积分；通过固定M2膜电荷将局域化的路径积分转化为Airy积分形式；利用十一维陈-西蒙斯耦合和X8修正分别贡献巨势的三次项和电荷移动。

Result: 成功推导出ABJM结果及其环面卡拉比-丘推广，并得到黑洞及其他时空的引力块，但前因子和非微扰修正尚未包含在推导中。

Conclusion: 量子M理论的相对等变局域化为M2膜理论的Airy函数配分函数提供了统一的推导框架，揭示了其三阶巨势和电荷移动的深层起源，并可推广到更广泛的时空几何。

Abstract: We show that Airy function partition functions for M2-brane theories may be derived from relative equivariant localization of quantum M-theory. The eleven-dimensional Chern--Simons coupling gives the cubic term in the grand potential, while the $X_8$ correction gives the charge shift. Fixing the M2-brane charge turns the localized M-theory path integral into an Airy integral. In this way we derive the ABJM result, its toric Calabi--Yau generalizations, and gravitational blocks for black holes and other spacetimes, up to the prefactor and non-perturbative corrections.

</details>


### [24] [Massive Graviton Dark Matter from a Gapped Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07295)
*Eugenio Megias,Miguel Prieto,Mariano Quiros*

Main category: hep-th

Method: 通过自能辐射修正（self-energy radiative corrections）研究孤立共振态有质量引力子的存在性及其作为冻入机制产生的弱相互作用长寿命暗物质候选者；将有质量间隙连续谱引力子识别为全息流体（holographic fluid），并采用紫外冻入机制描述其产生过程。

Result: 亚MeV质量区间的有质量引力子满足所有理论与实验约束；膜上定域化的暴胀子（inflaton）质量约为10^11 GeV，再加热温度低于TeV尺度，可重现近期宇宙学观测量；全息暗物质的丰度主要取决于再加热温度，根据质量间隙与再加热温度的取值，暗物质可来自其中一种组分或两种组分共存。

Conclusion: 在翘曲额外维与线性膨胀子背景的膜世界框架下，存在两种可能的暗物质组分，分别对应离散共振态与连续谱，为暗物质的多组分图像提供了新的理论实现路径。

Abstract: We consider the possibility of dark matter in a warped extra-dimensional theory in presence of a linear dilaton background, with a gapped continuum spectrum, in a brane-world cosmological scenario. Firstly, triggered by self-energy radiative corrections, we study the existence of an isolated resonance of massive gravitons, and its realization as a long-lived feebly interacting dark matter candidate, produced by the freeze-in mechanism. This massive graviton is proved to satisfy all theoretical and experimental constraints, in the sub-MeV mass range. We further consider the close relationship between the existence of this component of dark matter and the presence of an inflaton localized on the brane, with a mass around $10^{11}$ GeV and a sub-TeV reheating temperature, in a brane inflationary scenario that allows to reproduce the most recent cosmological observables. Secondly, the gapped continuum of gravitons, a particular five dimensional realization of the physics of unparticles, is identified as a holographic fluid which can play the role of holographic dark matter. The production of the holographic fluid goes by an ultra-violet freeze-in mechanism, with an abundance mainly depending on the reheating temperature. Depending on the values of the mass gap and the reheating temperature, one or both components of dark matter can be present.

### [25] [Horizon-Restricted Leading Soft QED as Open Quantum System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07342)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将黑洞视界引发的电荷分支编码退相干（decoherence）表述为限定于外部代数上的领头软QED（leading-soft QED）开量子系统，通过Feynman-Vernon恒等式、Schur信道及Bargmann和乐（holonomy）等工具，建立了可证伪的量子擦除边界、非马尔可夫性检验和软硬标度判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于将黑洞视界（black hole horizon）诱导的退相干纳入严格的量子电动力学（QED）框架，揭示软光子（soft photon）在视界辐射代数中的角色，并构造可实验检验的量子信息判据。

Method: 采用开量子系统（open quantum system）形式，将领头软QED限制在外部代数上；利用固定历史的Feynman-Vernon恒等式 ${\cal F}[J,J]=1$ 和不等历史影响因子刻画退相干；在相干程近似（coherent eikonal regime）下导出完全正定的Schur信道 $({\cal E}_H^{(0)}ρ)_{ab}=\langleΦ_b^{H,(0)}|Φ_a^{H,(0)}\rangle \, ρ_{ab}$，并将领头软输入投影到视界辐射代数上。

Result: 导出了Gram正定性约束、外部量子擦除边界（quantum-eraser bound）、有限时间非马尔可夫性（non-Markovianity）检验、软/硬标度判据，以及一个带电qutrit干涉仪，其测量对象为领头软Bargmann和乐相位——即视界软相空间中三角形的重定相不变辛面积（rephasing-invariant symplectic area）。

Conclusion: 该和乐相位的方向、共模、三角剖分及完全正定行列式恒等式提供了超越两路径可见度（pairwise two-path visibility）的可证伪检验，表明视界退相干效应原则上可通过量子干涉实验加以区分和验证。

Abstract: I formulate black-hole-horizon-induced decoherence of charged branch codes as the leading-soft QED restricted to an exterior algebra, formulated as an open quantum system. The fixed-history Feynman--Vernon identity ${\cal F}[J,J]=1$ remains exact. Decoherence enters through the unequal-history influence factor that survives exterior monitoring and belongs to the complementary horizon output. In the coherent eikonal regime, I derive the completely positive Schur channel $({\cal E}_H^{(0)}ρ)_{ab}=\langleΦ_b^{H,(0)}|Φ_a^{H,(0)}\rangle \, ρ_{ab}$. The leading soft input is the eikonal factor, projected onto the horizon radiative algebra. The channel yields Gram-positivity constraints, an exterior quantum-eraser bound, finite-time non-Markovianity tests, soft/hard scaling criteria, and a charged-qutrit interferometer measuring a leading-soft Bargmann holonomy. The holonomy phase is the rephasing-invariant symplectic area of a triangle in horizon soft phase space. I show that its orientation, common-mode, triangulation, and completely positive determinant identities render falsifiable tests beyond pairwise two-path visibility.

Method: 采用带 O5-平面的五维 brane 图（5-brane web）构造；利用含 O5-平面的拓扑顶点形式（topological vertex formalism）推导配分函数；通过配分函数的热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）导出 Cameral 曲线（Cameral curve）和 Seiberg-Witten 曲线。

Result: 得到了两类理论（两个旋量 vs. 一个旋量加一个共轭旋量）配分函数的新表达式；证明了旋量与共轭旋量的差异最终表现为 Seiberg-Witten 曲线在 orientifold 平面（orientifold plane）处边界条件的差异。

Conclusion: 本文方法有效区分了五维超对称规范理论中旋量与共轭旋量超多重态的贡献，为理解 orientifold 平面下边界条件与表示结构的关系提供了新的理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate five-dimensional $\mathcal{N} = 1$ supersymmetric $SO(2N)$ gauge theories coupled to hypermultiplets in spinor/conjugate spinor representation based on 5-brane web constructions with O5-planes. Based on the topological vertex formalism with O5-plane, we find new expressions for the partition functions for these theories, emphasizing the difference between the case with two spinors and that with one spinor and one conjugate spinor. Through the thermodynamic limit of these partition functions, we derive the Cameral and Seiberg-Witten curves. We show that the difference between the spinor and the conjugate spinor appears as a difference in the boundary conditions of the Seiberg-Witten curves at the orientifold planes.

### [27] [Topological changes and response singularities in black hole thermodynamic branch structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07364)
*Di Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过带电AdS黑洞示例，证明热力学拓扑相变与支路响应奇异性是同一零点支路几何（zero point branch geometry）的两种不同诊断，二者具有不同的局部起源：前者源于边界成员身份和指标流事件，后者源于有限半径处支路湮灭的转向点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑热力学支路结构的不同诊断（diagnostics）并不总是指向相同的局域事件，现有研究对这两种诊断之间的关系尚不明确，因此需要在一个已知存在热力学拓扑相变（thermodynamic topological phase transition）的带电AdS黑洞示例中厘清二者的区别。

Method: 基于JHEP 06 (2024) 213中报道的同一零点支路几何（zero point branch geometry），分别重新分析总拓扑数改变时的逆温度τ_a和固定电荷参数支路响应出现奇异性时的逆温度τ_b，追踪两种诊断对应的局部结构变化。

Result: τ_a处的变化是正半径物理支集（positive radius physical branch set）的边界成员身份和指标流（index flow）事件——一个具有非零绕数（nonzero winding）的零点进入或离开计数域；τ_b处的奇异性则由有限半径处的转向点（turning point）引起，在该点一对支路相互湮灭，且因两支路携带相反绕数，该事件改变支路计数但不改变总拓扑数。

Conclusion: 在所分析的示例中，热力学拓扑相变与支路响应奇异性是同一零点支路几何的两种不同诊断，具有不同的局部起源。

Abstract: Different diagnostics of black hole thermodynamic branch structure do not always identify the same local event. We examine this issue in charged AdS black hole examples where a thermodynamic topological phase transition is known to occur. In these examples, previously reported in [JHEP 06 (2024) 213}], the inverse temperature $τ_a$ at which the total topological number changes is separated from the inverse temperature $τ_b$ at which the fixed charge parameter branch response considered here becomes singular. Reanalyzing the same zero point branch geometry, we find that the two diagnostics track different local structures. The change at $τ_a$ is a boundary membership and index flow event of the positive radius physical branch set: a zero point with nonzero winding enters or leaves the counted domain. The singularity at $τ_b$ is instead caused by a turning point at finite radius, where a pair of branches annihilates. Since the two branches carry opposite windings, this event changes the branch count but preserves the total topological number. Thus, in the analyzed examples, the thermodynamic topological phase transition and the branch response singularity are distinct diagnostics of the same zero point branch geometry, with different local origins.

</details>


### [28] [Phenomena in the kink-antikink Collisions of $φ^8$ Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07495)
*Yun Feng,Yunguo Jiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在(1+1)维φ⁸标量场论中研究了扭结-反扭结（kink-antikink）碰撞，发现完整湮灭（complete annihilation）机制和丰富的分形共振窗口（fractal resonance windows），并提出了基于有效势（effective potential）分类的碰撞结果预测框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高次标量场论（φ⁸模型）中扭结-反扭结碰撞的新动力学特征，这些特征在低阶场论（如φ⁴理论）中尚不存在。

Method: 针对由比率n=p₂/p₁表征的不同真空结构（重点研究n=2和n=3的四重简并真空情形），给出显式孤子解（soliton solutions），并在所有拓扑扇区（topological sectors）中进行系统数值模拟。

Result: 在(1/2, 1)扇区发现一个完整湮灭区域，扭结-反扭结对在所有初始速度下均发生湮灭；在扇区(-1, -1/2)、(-1, -1/3)和(-1/3, 1/3)中揭示出多跳共振窗口（multi-bounce resonance windows）的完整分形图景（fractal cartography）；识别出当孤子对（soliton pairs）相互穿越时，势类型的突变可以解释扇区变化（sector-change）和湮灭现象。

Conclusion: 有效势分类方案（effective potential classification scheme）为碰撞结果（包括逃逸（escape）、双子（bion）形成、扇区变化和湮灭）提供了预测性框架，建立了拓扑结构（topological structure）、振动模式（vibrational modes）与有效势之间的联系。

Abstract: We investigated kink-antikink collisions in a $(1+1)$-dimensional $φ^8$ scalar field theory with multiple degenerate vacua. We presented explicit soliton solutions for different vacuum structures characterized by the ratio $n = p_2/p_1$. We focused on the cases $n=2$ and $n=3$ with four distinct vacua, and performed systematic numerical simulations across all topological sectors. We revealed that there is a complete annihilation regime in the $(1/2,\,1)$ sector, where kink-antikink pairs annihilate for all initial velocities. Up to our knowledge, such phenomenon is first reported in the kink antikink collisions. We revealed a comprehensive fractal cartography of multi-bounce resonance windows across sectors $(-1,\,-1/2)$, $(-1,\,-1/3)$, and $(-1/3,\,1/3)$. Given the kink antikink ($K\bar{K}$, or $\bar{K}K$) ordering, the effective potential and the spectrum of the Schrödinger like equation were presented. By collecting all the effective potential and collision phenomena, we proposed that the effective potential classification scheme provides a predictive framework for collision outcomes including escape, bion formation, sector change, and annihilation. Especially, it is identified that, when soliton pairs pass through each other, the abrupt changes of the potential type could explain both the sector-change and annihilation phenomena. Our work highlight novel dynamical features of the $φ^8$ model absent in lower-order field theories, and establish connections between topological structure, vibrational modes, and effective potentials.

</details>


### [29] [Odd-Dimensional Localization in Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07621)
*Pietro Benetti Genolini,Florian Gaar,Jerome P. Gauntlett,Jaeha Park,James Sparks*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个适用于包含陈-西蒙斯（Chern-Simons）相互作用的奇数维超引力（supergravity）理论的局域化（localization）原理。通过将规范不变部分的作用量的等变延拓（equivariant extension）与陈-西蒙斯反常形式（Chern-Simons anomaly form）的等变完备化（equivariant completion）结合，构造出一个相对等变上同调类（relative equivariant cohomology class），从而导出一个普适的不动点公式（fixed point formula），用于表达超对称解的在壳作用量（on-shell action），该公式由反常形式和等变欧拉类（equivariant Euler class）给出。在 D=11 和 D=5 超引力中演示了该形式体系，应用包括 M5-膜的超对称卡西米尔能量（supersymmetric Casimir energy）和超共形指标（superconformal index），以及黑环（black ring）和黑透镜（black lens）解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立适用于含陈-西蒙斯相互作用的奇数维超引力理论的局域化原理，以统一计算超对称解的在壳作用量。

Method: 将规范不变部分作用量的等变延拓与陈-西蒙斯反常形式的等变完备化结合，构造相对等变上同调类，从而导出由反常形式和等变欧拉类表达的不动点公式。

Result: 得到了一个普适的不动点公式，并在 D=11 和 D=5 超引力中验证了该形式体系的有效性；应用包括 M5-膜的超对称卡西米尔能量与超共形指标，以及黑环和黑透镜解。

Conclusion: 该局域化原理为含陈-西蒙斯项的奇数维超引力提供了计算超对称解在壳作用量的统一框架，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: We establish a localization principle for odd-dimensional supergravity theories containing Chern--Simons interactions. Our construction relies on combining an equivariant extension of the gauge-invariant part of the action with an equivariant completion of the Chern--Simons anomaly form $Φ^{(\text{anom})}$ to form a relative equivariant cohomology class. This leads to a universal fixed point formula for the on-shell action of supersymmetric solutions that is expressed in terms of $Φ^{(\text{anom})}$ and an equivariant Euler class. We illustrate the formalism in $D=11$ and $D=5$ supergravity, with applications including the supersymmetric Casimir energy and superconformal index of M5-branes, as well as black ring and black lens solutions.

### [30] [Unification of polynomial and exponential cosmological attractors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07684)

Method: 构造一族α吸引子模型，其势能形式包含一个插值参数μ，使得模型可在指数型吸引子（exponential attractor）与多项式型吸引子（polynomial attractor）之间连续过渡。

Result: 通过变化插值参数μ，该模型能够覆盖广泛的谱指数n_s取值范围，从而兼容CMB和DESI实验的各种数据组合。

Conclusion: 该族模型为连接不同宇宙学吸引子类型与多源观测数据提供了统一且灵活的理论工具。

Abstract: We introduce a family of simple $α$-attractor models that can interpolate between exponential and polynomial cosmological attractors. By varying the interpolation parameter $μ$ in these models, one can scan a wide range of values of the spectral index $n_{s}$ matching any combination of CMB and DESI data.

### [31] [Recent highlights from the STAR Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07254)
*Rutik Manikandhan*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于STAR实验的多观测量分析，研究了RHIC重离子碰撞中QCD相结构及临界点。观测涵盖双粒子横动量关联、净质子累积量（最高四阶）、全同介子费米尺度和重子-奇异数关联等，跨sqrt(sNN)=3-200 GeV能区，为QCD状态方程和临界点位置提供新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解QCD相结构（QCD phase structure）以及临界点（critical point）是否存在是RHIC重离子计划的核心目标之一。本文旨在通过多种观测量从不同角度探测碰撞产生的高温致密物质性质。

Method: 研究基于STAR实验在Au+Au碰撞中获取的数据，采用多类观测量：双粒子横动量关联（two-particle transverse momentum correlations）、净质子累积量（net-proton cumulants）至四阶、全同介子费米尺码（identical-pion femtoscopy），以及重子-奇异数关联（baryon-strangeness correlations）。此外还包括重子-重子对的费米尺码测量，以研究超子-核子与超子-超子相互作用。

Result: 多种观测量在碰撞能sqrt(sNN)=3-200 GeV范围内提供了互补的系统演化探针。重子-重子对的费米尺码测量揭示了超子-核子（hyperon-nucleon）和超子-超子（hyperon-hyperon）相互作用的信息，并暗示了奇异双重子态（strange dibaryon states）的可能形成。

Conclusion: 这些综合结果为QCD状态方程（equation of state）和QCD临界点的位置提供了新的约束。多种观测量在宽能区内的互补性有助于更深入地理解QCD相结构。

Abstract: Understanding the QCD phase structure and the possible existence of a critical point remains one of the central goals of the heavy-ion program at RHIC. In this proceeding, we present recent STAR results across multiple observables that probe different aspects of the hot and dense matter created in Au+Au collisions. These include two-particle transverse momentum correlations of mean transverse momentum, net-proton cumulants up to fourth order, identical-pion femtoscopy, and baryon-strangeness correlations. We also discuss femtoscopic measurements of baryon-baryon pairs, which provide insight into hyperon-nucleon and hyperon-hyperon interactions and the possible formation of strange dibaryon states. Together, these results provide complementary probes of the system's evolution across a wide collision-energy range (sqrt(sNN) = 3-200 GeV), offering new constraints on the QCD equation of state and the location of the QCD critical point.

</details>

# physics.chem-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [32] [Hydrogen-Bond Donor-Acceptor Imbalance in Low-Frequency Terahertz Water Spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06780)
*Lilian Najm Alsayed,Florian Pabst,Giuseppe Cassone,Ali Hassanali,Fabio Novelli*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 液态水在0.14–1.21 THz范围内的低频介电响应可用集体德拜弛豫（collective Debye relaxation）加上一个受限于零直流电导率极限的Drude-Smith项来表征。该过剩响应随温度升高和同位素替代（D₂O vs H₂O）而变化，分子动力学模拟与第一性原理计算表明其源于氢键网络中瞬态供体-受体不平衡所导致的局域化核-电混合介电响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液态水的低频介电响应通常由一个主导的德拜弛豫（Debye relaxation）和若干更快贡献叠加描述，但这些更快贡献的微观起源一直存在争议。摘要旨在澄清这一争议，揭示0.1–1.2 THz范围内过剩介电响应的物理本质。

Method: 实验上测量了纯H₂O从20 °C到50 °C以及D₂O在20 °C条件下的介电函数（0.14–1.21 THz），用集体德拜弛豫加上零直流电导率极限约束的Drude-Smith项进行拟合。结合考虑核量子效应（nuclear quantum effects）的分子动力学模拟和基于第一性原理（ab initio）的频谱计算。

Result: Drude-Smith谱权重随H₂O温度升高（20 °C→50 °C）而增加，随同位素替代（H₂O→D₂O）而减小。模拟显示氢键供体与受体数目不相等的水分子群体发生相关变化。第一性原理计算表明~0.1–1 THz响应同时包含核运动贡献和显式电子极化/电荷重分布贡献。

Conclusion: 过剩的低频太赫兹（THz）响应被解释为一种局域化的、核-电混合的介电响应，该响应与氢键网络中瞬时的供体-受体不平衡相关联。

Abstract: The low-frequency dielectric response of liquid water is commonly described by a dominant Debye relaxation together with additional faster contributions whose microscopic origin remains debated. Here we show that the dielectric function of water between 0.14 and 1.21 THz can be represented by a collective Debye relaxation plus a Drude-Smith term constrained to the zero-dc-conductivity limit. The Drude-Smith spectral weight increases upon heating pure H2O from 20 C to 50 C and decreases upon isotopic substitution (D2O at 20 C vs. H2O at 20 C). Molecular dynamics simulations including nuclear quantum effects show correlated changes in the population of water molecules with unequal numbers of donated and accepted hydrogen-bonds. Ab-initio-based spectra calculations further indicate that the ~0.1-1 THz response contains both nuclear-motion and explicit electronic-polarisation/charge-redistribution contributions. We therefore interpret the excess low-frequency THz response as a localised, mixed nuclear-electronic dielectric response correlated with transient donor-acceptor imbalance in the hydrogen-bond network.

</details>

### [33] [ACT-DR6 consistent inflation in generalised entropic cosmology and $f(Q)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06582)
*Shin'ichi Nojiri,Sergei D. Odintsov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义熵宇宙学（generalised entropic cosmology）及其等价的 $f(Q)$ 引力框架下，构建了与 Atacama 宇宙学望远镜（ACT）最新观测及 Planck-BAO 联合数据一致的暴胀（inflation）场景，并通过标量势的选择获得了多种符合 ACT-DR6 数据的暴胀模型，指出广义熵可能统一描述早期宇宙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建与最新高精度宇宙学观测（ACT-DR6 结合 Planck-BAO 数据）相一致的暴胀模型，并在广义熵宇宙学与 $f(Q)$ 引力的统一框架下探索早期宇宙的正确熵形式。

Method: 利用 $f(Q)$ 引力及其重构方案（reconstruction scheme）推导符合观测的任意宇宙演化；通过广义熵（generalised entropy，包含 Tsallis、Rényi、Barrow 等作为特例）与 $f(Q)$ 引力的对应关系，将标量场耦合至 $f(Q)$ 引力及熵引力（entropic gravity），并借助标量势（scalar potential）的选择实现与 ACT-DR6 数据一致的暴胀。

Result: 获得了多类通过 ACT-DR6 联合 Planck-BAO 数据验证的显式暴胀宇宙学（explicit inflationary cosmologies）；展示了对于任意本文考虑的广义熵，通过选择标量势均可得到与 ACT-DR6 一致的广义熵暴胀（generalised entropic inflation）。

Conclusion: 广义熵框架下的暴胀模型与最新观测高度一致，研究结果可能指向能够统一描述早期宇宙的正确熵形式。

Abstract: Within the framework of generalised entropic cosmology and its equivalent $f(Q)$ gravity, we construct inflationary scenarios consistent with recent Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) observations combined with Planck-BAO data. We work with $f(Q)$ gravity and use the reconstruction scheme from which one can obtain an arbitrary cosmological evolution consistent with desirable theoretical or observational considerations. Explicit inflationary cosmologies of the above theory, which pass ACT-Data Release 6 (DR6) data combined with Planck and BAO, are obtained. For $f(Q)$ gravity coupled with scalar, we obtain ACT inflation for large classes of $f(Q)$ via the choice of the scalar potentials. The entropic cosmology based on generalised entropy, which includes most of the known entropies like Tsallis, Rényi, Barrow, etc as a particular case, is investigated. The corresponding FRW equations, depending on the parameters of generalised entropy, are presented. Using the correspondence between the generalised entropy and $f(Q)$ gravity, we obtain generalised entropic inflation, which is consistent with the ACT-DR6. At the next step, the entropic gravity coupled with scalar is considered. It is demonstrated how one can obtain ACT-DR6-consistent inflation for such a theory based on any generalised entropy considered in this paper via the choice of scalar potentials. These findings may point towards the correct unifying entropy of the early universe.

</details>


### [34] [On the image of the scattering map for horizon-regular solutions of the linear scalar wave equation on the Schwarzschild black hole exterior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06668)
*Hamed Masaood*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构造希尔伯特空间同构（Hilbert-space isomorphisms），建立了施瓦西时空中事件视界（event horizon）与零无穷远（null infinity）上辐射场之间的对应关系，并分析了线性标量波方程（linear scalar wave equation）球谐模式解的辐射与衰减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解施瓦西黑洞外部时空（Schwarzschild exterior）中线性波的辐射结构，特别是事件视界与零无穷远上辐射场之间的联系与差异，以及不同边界条件下解的衰减性质。

Method: 利用向前散射映射（forward scattering map）诱导的希尔伯特空间同构，将事件视界与零无穷远上的辐射场空间等同起来；基于柯西数据集（Cauchy data sets）在t=0时刻的初始条件，并限制在固定球谐模式（spherical harmonic mode）下进行分析。

Result: 固定球谐模式解中，若事件视界上无辐射，则解必须随时间指数衰减（exponential decay），衰减速率由表面引力（surface gravity）决定。另一方面，构造了零无穷远上无辐射的固定球谐模式解实例，该解沿事件视界呈多项式衰减（polynomial decay）。此外，还构造了在事件视界上正则、球谐模式支撑无界、且不诱导事件视界辐射的多项式衰减解。

Conclusion: 事件视界与零无穷远上的辐射条件对施瓦西时空中线性标量波的衰减行为有决定性影响：视界上无辐射导致指数衰减，而无穷远上无辐射可允许多项式衰减；同时存在球谐模式无界且视界正则的多项式衰减解。

Abstract: We construct Hilbert-space isomorphisms identifying the spaces of radiation fields on the event horizon and null infinity that are induced by the forward scattering map on the Schwarzschild exterior for fixed spherical harmonic mode solutions to the linear scalar wave equation arising from Cauchy data sets at $t=0$ which are regular at the event horizon, in the sense that the local energy at the event horizon is finite. We show that fixed spherical harmonic mode solutions with no radiation on the event horizon must decay exponentially in time, at a rate that is determined by the surface gravity. On the other hand, we construct examples of fixed spherical harmonic mode solutions with no radiation on null infinity and which have polynomial decay along the event horizon. Finally, we construct examples of polynomially decaying solutions to the linear scalar wave equation which are regular at the event horizon, have unbounded support in spherical harmonic modes, and induce no radiation on the event horizon.

</details>


### [35] [Foundations of Direct Waves in Schwarzschild Ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06677)
*Sizheng Ma,Hai-Yang Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从第一性原理出发，利用格林函数（Green's function）的因果结构，在史瓦西时空中推导了黑洞并合铃宕（ringdown）过程中的直接波（direct wave），证明其非零且由近视界源动力学主导，从而为直接波作为探知近视界动力学的新工具建立了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究发现黑洞并合铃宕信号中存在一种称为“直接波”的新成分，被认为携带视界信息，但缺乏坚实的理论依据。本文旨在填补这一空白，从第一性原理出发为直接波提供严格的理论基础。

Method: 在史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中，利用格林函数的因果结构（causal structure of the Green's function）从第一性原理推导直接波的起源与性质。

Result: 直接波并不为零，且由其近视界源动力学（near-horizon source dynamics）所控制。

Conclusion: 本文建立了直接波作为近视界动力学探针的理论基础，使其能够与准正则模（quasinormal modes）互为补充，共同用于研究黑洞视界附近的物理过程。

Abstract: Recent studies have identified a new component in black-hole ringdown from merging binaries, termed the \emph{direct wave}. This component was argued to be tied to the dynamical source evolution near the black-hole horizon, and thus to encode horizon information. Yet a firm theoretical foundation for the direct wave has been lacking. Here we fill this gap by deriving direct waves from first principles in Schwarzschild spacetime, using the causal structure of the Green's function. We show that the direct wave does not vanish and is governed by the near-horizon source dynamics. Our results establish a theoretical basis for direct waves as a probe of near-horizon dynamics, complementary to quasinormal modes.

</details>


### [36] [Joule-Thomson Effect and Geodesic Structure of Charged AdS Black Holes in f(R,T) Coupled with Nonlinear Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06704)
*Shyamalee Bora,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi,Pralay Kumar Karmakar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了修正引力中带电反德西特黑洞的焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀过程和测地线性质，发现黑洞电荷对焦耳-汤姆逊行为影响最大，非线性电磁和修正引力参数进一步修正了反转温度和冷却特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究修正引力与非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamic, NLED）源耦合下带电反德西特（anti-de Sitter, AdS）黑洞的焦耳-汤姆逊（Joule-Thomson, JT）膨胀过程与测地线性质，以揭示其热力学和几何特性。

Method: 采用热力学分析研究焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀过程，并利用测地线方法分析黑洞的几何性质。

Result: 黑洞电荷对焦耳-汤姆逊行为影响最为显著；非线性电磁扇区与修正引力参数进一步修正了反转温度（inversion temperature）和冷却特征（cooling characteristics）；在天体物理相关距离上，几何结果与预期结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 修正引力中带电AdS黑洞的焦耳-汤姆逊行为主要受黑洞电荷调控，非线性电动力学和修正引力参数提供了额外修正；该几何在远距离上复现了预期结果。

Abstract: We herein study both the Joule-Thomson (JT) expansion process and the geodesic properties of a charged anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole arising in modified gravity with nonlinear electrodynamic (NLED) sources. Our thermodynamic study reveals that the black hole charge has the most pronounced impact on the JT behaviour. The nonlinear electromagnetic sector together with the modified gravity parameters introduces further corrections to the inversion temperature and the associated cooling characteristics. At astrophysically relevant distances, the geometry closely reproduces expected outcomes.

</details>


### [37] [The Era of Precision in Computational Models of Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06728)
*Ulrich Sperhake*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文回顾了通过数值计算方法求解爱因斯坦广义相对论方程的发展历程，重点介绍了2000年代中期双体问题的最终解决，以及该成果在2015年LIGO发现引力波（gravitational waves）并获得诺贝尔奖中所发挥的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（general relativity）的爱因斯坦方程是物理学中最复杂的方程组之一，除理想化物理场景外，只能依靠高性能计算系统通过数值方法求解，这一挑战驱动了对数值相对论（numerical relativity）的持续探索。

Method: 采用数值计算方法，在高性能计算系统上求解爱因斯坦方程；该方法涉及数学理论、物理解释和计算挑战等多个领域的交叉。

Result: 2000年代中期成功解决了广义相对论的两体问题（two-body problem），为引力波探测奠定了理论基础和数值计算支持。

Conclusion: 广义相对论双体问题的数值求解成果直接支撑了LIGO在2015年发现引力波，后者获得了诺贝尔奖（Nobel Prize），表明数值相对论在现代物理学前沿探索中具有不可替代的作用。

Abstract: Einstein's equations of general relativity are one of the most complicated set of equations in all of physics and, for all but idealized physical settings, can only be solved by numerical methods on high-performance computing systems. Generating such solutions is a veritable Odyssey in its own right with adventures across the fields of mathematical theory, physical interpretation and computing challenges. These endeavors came to fruition in the mid 2000s when the two-body problem of general relativity was finally solved. And not too soon, as these results and their follow-up investigations came to play a key role in the Nobel-Prize winning discovery of gravitational waves by LIGO in 2015.

</details>


### [38] [A new framework for lightning-fast gravitational wave analysis of pulsar timing data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06834)
*Aiden Gundersen,Rutger van Haasteren,Neil J. Cornish,Michele Vallisneri,Patrick M. Meyers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出通过在傅里叶系数（Fourier coefficients）空间中进行采样而非解析边际化（analytical marginalization）的方法，结合坐标变换（coordinate transformation）和哈密顿蒙特卡洛（Hamiltonian Monte Carlo, HMC）采样，将脉冲星计时阵列数据分析的计算时间从数月缩短至约15分钟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）数据分析的计算成本极高，限制了可研究模型的复杂程度；随着数据集规模和模型复杂度不断增长，亟需更快、可扩展的推断方法。

Method: 在傅里叶系数空间中采样，而非传统的解析边际化处理；通过适当的坐标变换使傅里叶系数近似服从标准正态分布（standard normal distribution），进而采用哈密顿蒙特卡洛（Hamiltonian Monte Carlo, HMC）方案实现高效采样。

Result: 在处理与NANOGrav 15年数据释放规模和复杂度相当的数据集时，新方法可在NVIDIA GeForce RTX 3090 GPU上约15分钟内获得多种模型（含脉冲星间相关信号、随机信号及确定性信号）的收敛后验分布。

Conclusion: 与需要CPU集群数月计算时间的传统PTA分析软件ENTERPRISE相比，新方法实现了三个数量级以上的加速，为更大规模和更复杂模型的分析提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Pulsar timing array data analysis is computationally expensive, limiting the complexity of models which can be studied. As pulsar timing datasets and their respective models grow in size and sophistication, faster and scalable inference methods are essential. In this paper, we accelerate pulsar timing analyses by sampling in the space of Fourier coefficients instead of analytically marginalizing over them. Previous studies have shown the Fourier space induces a complex, high-dimensional posterior geometry, from which it is generally difficult to sample. We show that under an appropriate coordinate transformation the Fourier coefficients approximately follow a standard normal distribution, and may be efficiently sampled using a Hamiltonian Monte Carlo scheme. Under this coordinate transformation, for datasets of size and complexity comparable to the NANOGrav 15-year release, the new method produces converged posterior distributions for a range of models which include inter-pulsar correlations, stochastic, and deterministic signals in approximately 15 minutes on an NVIDIA GeForce RTX 3090 GPU. By comparison, the legacy pulsar timing analysis software \texttt{ENTERPRISE} would require months of computation on a CPU cluster to analyze comparable datasets under the same joint stochastic and deterministic models.

</details>


### [39] [Slowly rotating condensate dark stars beyond the mean-field approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06898)
*Grigoris Panotopoulos,Ángel Rincón,Ilidio Lopes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论框架下，系统研究了缓慢旋转的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚暗星（Bose-Einstein condensate dark stars）的转动性质与普适关系，重点分析了超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）的Lee-Huang-Yang（LHY）修正对转动惯量、潮汐Love数和无量纲潮汐形变性的影响，并发现LHY项在固定紧致度下可显著降低无量纲转动惯量，同时I-Λ普适关系保持成立。研究提供了I-Λ和I-C关系的多项式拟合，表明LHY效应可作为区分量子效应的诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多针对平均场（mean-field）层次的致密星体，而超越平均场的量子修正（如LHY项）对暗星可观测性质的影响尚未被充分探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过计算旋转BEC暗星的转动惯量、潮汐Love数等关键物理量，检验LHY修正是否在可观测范围内留下可辨识的信号。

Method: 采用适用于稀薄自相互作用玻色气体的多方指数n=1的状态方程（equation of state），由玻色子质量m和s波散射长度a_s参数化。在广义相对论框架下，同时积分Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程和Hartle的偶极方程（dipole equation）以求解参考系拖曳角速度（frame-dragging angular velocity），进而计算转动惯量、引力电潮汐Love数（gravito-electric tidal Love number）及无量纲潮汐形变性（dimensionless tidal deformability）。

Result: 平衡序列给出的引力质量范围为1–2 M⊙，半径范围为10–20 km，与NICER及LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA网络当前探测窗口一致。LHY项导致无量纲转动惯量在固定紧致度（compactness）下出现可测量的减小，而I-Λ普适关系（universal relation）的变化幅度在百分之几以内。

Conclusion: LHY修正在暗星可观测性质上留下了足够大的信号，可作为探测超越平均场量子物理的干净诊断工具。该诊断可补充现有基于脉冲星质量和状态方程解释来自超轻致密残余HESS J1731-347的暗物质约束。

Abstract: We investigate rotational properties and universal relations of slowly rotating Bose-Einstein condensate dark stars in the context of General Relativity, both at the mean-field level and when the leading beyond-mean-field Lee-Huang-Yang correction is retained self-consistently. Adopting the polytropic $n=1$ equation of state appropriate to a dilute, self-interacting Bose gas, parameterised by the boson mass $m$ and the $s$-wave scattering length $a_s$, we integrate the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations together with Hartle's dipole equation for the frame-dragging angular velocity, and we compute the moment of inertia, the gravito-electric tidal Love number and the dimensionless tidal deformability. The resulting equilibrium sequences yield gravitational masses in the $1$--$2\,M_{\odot}$ range with radii of $10$--$20\,\mathrm{km}$, squarely within the window presently probed by NICER and the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network. We observe that the LHY term produces a measurable reduction of the dimensionless moment of inertia at fixed compactness, whilst the I-$Λ$ universal relation is preserved to within a few per cent. We supply polynomial fits for the I-$Λ$ and I-$C$ relations, and show that the LHY footprint is large enough to serve as a clean diagnostic of beyond-mean-field quantum physics in a putative dark star population, complementing existing dark matter constraints from pulsar masses and from the equation-of-state interpretation of the unusually light compact remnant HESS~J1731-347.

</details>


### [40] [Primordial black hole in Lorentz-violating theories: Insights from Bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07011)
*Mohsen Khodadi,Javad T. Firouzjaee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Bumblebee引力模型中的原初黑洞形成，发现该模型虽能通过三种机制增强原初黑洞丰度使其成为暗物质候选者，但模型本身存在鬼态不稳定性（ghost instability）和快标度不稳定性（tachyonic instability），导致宇宙学可行性与自发对称性破缺条件相互排斥，理论根基存在根本性不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用Bumblebee引力（Bumblebee gravity, BG）模型——一种通过与非最小耦合于曲率的矢量场实现自发洛伦兹对称性破缺的理论——探索宇宙学中洛伦兹破缺效应，并检验该模型能否为原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）作为暗物质候选者提供可行的产生机制。

Method: 在Bumblebee引力框架下推导完整的修正扰动方程组，分析由类时矢量场（timelike vector field）驱动的BG模型对原初黑洞形成的影响；同时对二次作用量（quadratic action）进行系统分析以检查理论的自洽性。

Result: BG模型通过三种机制——修正的膨胀历史（modified expansion history）、抑制的坍缩阈值（suppressed collapse threshold）和放大的功率谱（amplified power spectrum）——显著增强原初黑洞丰度，在适度的洛伦兹破缺耦合下使原初黑洞在小行星质量窗口（asteroid-mass window）内成为可行的暗物质候选者。然而，矢量扇区存在固有的鬼态不稳定性，且稳定对称性破缺极小值的要求会在远低于宇宙学尺度的时间尺度上诱发快标度不稳定性。

Conclusion: 最小Bumblebee框架中宇宙学可行性与自发对称性破缺的条件相互排斥，模型存在根本性不一致。研究既展示了洛伦兹破缺对早期宇宙可观测量（early Universe observables）的强大影响能力，也强调了此类预测必须建立在一致的理论基础之上。

Abstract: The Bumblebee gravity (BG) model, featuring spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking via a vector field non-minimally coupled to curvature, has been widely used to explore Lorentz-violating effects in cosmology. We investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation within this framework, deriving the complete set of modified perturbation equations. We demonstrate that BG, sourced by a timelike vector field, introduces three distinct enhancements to PBH abundance--modified expansion history, suppressed collapse threshold, and amplified power spectrum--which together render PBHs viable dark matter candidates across the asteroid-mass window for modest Lorentz-violating couplings. However, a systematic analysis of the quadratic action reveals that these phenomenological consequences emerge from a theoretically pathological foundation. The vector sector exhibits an intrinsic ghost instability, while the requirement of a stable symmetry-breaking minimum simultaneously induces a tachyonic instability on timescales far below cosmological scales. The model thus suffers from a fundamental inconsistency: the conditions for cosmological viability and spontaneous symmetry breaking are mutually exclusive within the minimal Bumblebee framework. Our results illustrate both the notable power of Lorentz violation to influence early Universe observables and the necessity of a consistent theoretical foundation for such predictions.

</details>


### [41] [The twin paradox in the vicinity of rotating black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07058)
*Shuiquan Bai,Geraint F. Lewis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于广义相对论的弯曲时空，围绕Kerr旋转黑洞附近的孪生子悖论（twin paradox）展开数值研究。通过残差图（residual maps）与优化方法识别可能轨迹，揭示了旅行者固有时（proper time）与方位角距离及加速度大小之间的强负相关性，并利用数值Jacobi场分析（Jacobi field analysis）发现Kerr几何中仅最小方位角距离的测地线（geodesic）不含共轭点（conjugate points）。该工作为初学广义相对论的学生提供了修正平直时空直觉的可视化工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孪生子悖论是狭义相对论中的基础思想实验，但该悖论在广义相对论的弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中尚未被充分探索。本文旨在研究旋转黑洞附近弯曲时空背景下孪生子悖论的复杂性，特别是多重路径的存在所带来的新问题。

Method: 研究采用基于残差图（residual maps）和优化（optimisation）的数值框架来识别可能的运动轨迹。同时应用数值Jacobi场分析（numerical Jacobi field analysis）以检验Kerr几何（Kerr geometry）中测地线（geodesics）上的共轭点（conjugate points）。

Result: 发现旅行者所经历的固有时（proper time）与方位角距离（azimuthal distance）以及加速度大小（magnitude of acceleration）之间存在强负相关性（strong negative correlation）。在Kerr几何中，仅具有最小方位角距离的测地线不包含共轭点。

Conclusion: 该研究为广义相对论的初学者提供了理解弯曲时空概念的可视化工具，有助于纠正基于平直时空（flat-spacetime）的直觉。

Abstract: The twin paradox is a foundational thought experiment in the special theory of relativity where a returning twin ages less than the one who remains stationary. However, the intricacies of the twin paradox remain relatively underexplored in the curved spacetimes of general relativity. Here we explore the twin paradox in the vicinity of a rotating black hole, where the existence of multiple paths between two events creates significant complexity. We develop a numerical framework based on residual maps and optimisation to identify possible trajectories. We find a strong negative correlation between a traveller's experienced proper time and both the azimuthal distance travelled and the magnitude of acceleration. We apply numerical Jacobi field analysis to examine conjugate points along geodesics within the Kerr geometry, finding that only the geodesic with the minimal azimuthal distance contains no conjugate points. This provides beginner students of general relativity with a visual tool to understand general relativistic concepts, helping to correct flat-spacetime intuitions.
