### [42] [Testing General Relativity with GWTC-4.0 through mixture models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07070)
*Koustav Chandra,Juan Calderón Bustillo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合模型（mixture-model）框架，用于引力波致密双星并合事件的广义相对论（GR）检验。该模型允许一部分事件与GR一致、另一部分偏离GR，不限制偏离参数分布。应用于LVK合作O1-O4a数据后，发现数据与所有事件满足GR一致，但贝叶斯因子远小于现有LVK分析结果，表明数据需要更灵活的模型来刻画可能的偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波检验引力（gravity）的方法假设偏离广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）的效应在所有事件中均匀分布，这种假设限制了分析的灵活性，并可能使推断的证据产生偏差。因此需要一种更灵活的统计框架来评估GR的遵从性。

Method: 引入一个简单的混合模型（mixture-model）框架：设参数ζ为事件中与GR一致的比例，1-ζ为偏离GR的比例，且不对偏离参数的总体分布施加额外约束。将该方法应用于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）合作发布的O1-O4a致密双星并合数据，这些数据来自FTI、pSEOBNR和KerrPostMerger三种检验途径。

Result: 数据整体与所有事件满足GR一致。然而，针对三种检验（FTI、pSEOBNR、KerrPostMerger）分别得到的贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）B^{ζ=1}_{ζ≠1}约为20、10和15，远小于现有LVK标准分析给出的结果，表明数据需要更灵活地建模可能的偏离。

Conclusion: 建议在致密并合目录中检验GR时使用灵活的混合模型（mixture model），除非存在明确的物理动机（如引力子质量估计）来施加更具限制性的模型。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave observations of compact binary mergers have enabled precision tests of gravity in the strong-field dynamical regime. Current approaches combine single-event results that assume deviations from General Relativity (GR) are uniformly distributed across events, limiting their flexibility and potentially biasing the inferred evidence. We introduce a simple mixture-model framework in which a fraction $ζ$ of events is consistent with GR, while a fraction $1 - ζ$ deviates from it, without imposing constraints on the population distribution of the deviation parameters. We apply this method to publicly available results from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration on O1-O4a compact binary mergers obtained through FTI, pSEOBNR, and KerrPostMerger tests. We find that the data are consistent with all events satisfying GR. However, we obtain respective Bayes factors $B^{ζ=1}_{ζ\neq 1} \simeq 20 $, $10$ and $15$, which are much smaller than those inferred from existing LVK analyses, indicating that the data require greater flexibility in modelling possible deviations than standard approaches permit. In light of our results, we recommend using flexible mixture models to test GR across compact-merger catalogues, unless there are obvious physical motivations to impose more restrictive models, as in the case of graviton-mass estimates.

</details>


### [43] [Naked Singularities beyond Spherical Symmetry: Singular Inner Cauchy Horizons for the Einstein-Scalar Field System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07134)
*Xinliang An,Shengrong Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对无对称性假设的3+1维爱因斯坦-标量场系统，通过构造非球对称初始数据，推广了Christodoulou的球对称自相似裸奇点解，证明了整体存在性，并揭示了内柯西视界（inner Cauchy horizon）处的奇异结构与不可延拓性，建立了弱宇宙监督检验（weak cosmic censorship）失效与强宇宙监督检验（strong cosmic censorship）机制之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索爱因斯坦-标量场系统中裸奇点（naked singularity）的形成机制，特别是在放弃球对称假设的一般情形下，考察弱宇宙监督检验失效时是否伴随强宇宙监督检验意义上的定量不可延拓性。

Method: 采用四型差分（four-type differences）概念，设计了一套标度不变的加权范数（scale-invariant weighted norms）系统来控制几何结构；在入射和出射两类初始零超曲面（null hypersurfaces）上给定非球对称初始数据，推广Christodoulou的球对称自相似解。

Result: 构造的时空保留了全局裸奇点结构，表现为不完备的未来零无穷远（future null infinity）和奇异的内柯西视界；推导了内柯西视界附近的详细渐近行为，并证明了该解具有$C^{1, \fracκ{1-κ}+}$不可延拓性（其中$κ\in (0,1/3)$为自相似参数）。

Conclusion: 对于本文构造的一类非球对称解，弱宇宙监督检验在其严格表述下的失效伴随着内柯西视界处的一种定量不可延拓机制，这揭示了弱宇宙监督检验与强宇宙监督检验之间的内在联系。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the formation of naked singularities for the $3+1$-dimensional Einstein-scalar field system without symmetry assumptions. We generalize the spherically symmetric and self-similar naked-singularity solution constructed by Christodoulou in [4] by prescribing non-spherically symmetric initial data along both incoming and outgoing initial null hypersurfaces. We then establish global existence for the resulting solutions and analyze the singular structure of the inner Cauchy horizon. Our construction is based on employing a notion of four-type differences and designing a system of scale-invariant weighted norms to control the corresponding geometry. We show that the constructed spacetimes retain a global naked-singularity structure, characterized by an incomplete future null infinity and a singular inner Cauchy horizon. Moreover, we derive detailed asymptotics near the inner Cauchy horizon and prove the desired $C^{1, \fracκ{1-κ}+}$ inextendibility of these solutions, where $κ\in (0,1/3)$ is the self-similar parameter. This indicates a connection between weak and strong cosmic censorship: for the class of non-spherically symmetric solutions constructed here, the failure of weak cosmic censorship in its strict formulation is accompanied by a quantitative inextendibility mechanism at the inner Cauchy horizon.

### [44] [Hierarchy of Angular Instabilities in Scalarized Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07208)
*Jose Luis Blázquez-Salcedo,Luis Manuel González-Romero,Fech Scen Khoo,Jutta Kunz,Pablo Navarro Moreno*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解标量化黑洞在经典引力理论中的稳定性，特别是角向扰动下的不稳定性行为及其组织结构。

Method: 沿着标量化黑洞的基本分支（fundamental branches）进行线性稳定性分析，考察不同多极子（multipole）模式的角向扰动行为，分析不稳定性阈值及其标度律。

Result: 初始稳定的解首先在eikonal区域（高角动量模式）失去球对称稳定性，而低阶多极子保持稳定；随着分支延续，不稳定性系统地扩展到低阶多极子，形成从eikonal到四极子（quadrupole）的有序层级，但偶极（dipole）扇区始终保持稳定。不稳定性阈值服从共同标度律，并趋向有限eikonal极限，定义了角向稳定区域的边界。先前识别的四极子不稳定性与角-Laplacian不稳定性通过连续层级相联系。

Conclusion: 标量化黑洞存在与径向稳定性不同的、独立的有序角向不稳定性层级，这一角向组织结构此前未被探索，揭示了该理论中新的不稳定性分类机制。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of scalarized black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet-Ricci theory along their fundamental branches. We show that initially stable solutions first lose nonspherical stability in the eikonal regime, while lower multipoles remain stable. As the branch is continued, instability extends systematically toward lower multipoles, forming an ordered hierarchy of deformation instabilities extending down to the quadrupole mode, while the dipole sector remains stable. The instability thresholds obey a common scaling law and approach finite eikonal limits, defining the boundary of the angularly stable region. We demonstrate that the previously identified quadrupole and angular-Laplacian instabilities are connected by a continuous hierarchy of instability thresholds spanning the angular sectors of the theory. This hierarchy is distinct from radial stability, which changes only at branch turning points, and reveals a previously unexplored angular organization of instabilities in scalarized black holes.

Conclusion: 该框架通过为每个候选事件提供一个统一的、校准良好的置信度度量（confidence measure），实现了对引力波目录和实时警报中候选事件的简化、系统化评估，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: The detection of transient gravitational wave signals relies on independent search algorithms that analyse detector data and assign significance measures to candidate events. However, varying performance complicates their interpretation. We use supervised machine learning combined with conformal prediction, a framework to quantify uncertainties, to merge multi-pipeline information into well-calibrated confidence scores. We demonstrate that this approach is robust across different classifier architectures and remains stable when trained on different simulated datasets. When applied to events across the GWTC catalogue up to and including the second part of the fourth observing run, the framework identifies several subthreshold candidates with elevated confidence, including the binary neutron star candidate GW200311_103121. We examine the reliability of these up-rankings, finding evidence that high-confidence predictions correspond to signal-like events. This framework enables simplified systematic candidate assessment for gravitational wave catalogues and real-time alerts by providing a single, well-calibrated confidence measure per candidate.

Result: 在100 mHz以上频率观察到明显的角度增强效应，且最优入射角取决于$Z_A H_0$，从而提供了一种直接的红移无关测量哈勃参数的方法。LISA有望以此将$H_0$的测量精度控制在百分之几以内。

Abstract: It was previously shown that $H_0$ influences gravitational wave propagation beyond simple redshift, by modifying the effective wavenumber. Modeling the LISA arm geometry, we derive the timing residual and identify a clear angular enhancement at frequencies above 100 mHz. Using the stationary phase approximation and numerical methods, we show that the optimal incidence angle depends on $Z_A H_0$, providing a direct, redshift-independent measurement of the Hubble parameter. We estimate that LISA could determine $H_0$ to within a few percent using this method, independent of standard siren approaches.

### [47] [Neural-Spectral Discovery of Rotating Black Holes Beyond General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07418)
*Felipe Agurto-Sepúlveda,Marcelo Oyarzo,Anxo Biasi,Devansh Agarwal,Ethan Tregidga,James F. Steiner,Jose D. Edelstein,Gaston Giribet,Cecilia Garraffo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Akribeia的混合框架，结合物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks）与伪谱精化步骤（pseudo-spectral refinement step），用于在高曲率引力理论中系统性地构造认证的旋转黑洞解（certified neural-field rotating black hole solutions）。该方法首次在二次和三次曲率理论中构造了具有多个非零角动量的旋转黑洞族，并通过高精度残差验证确保了解的可靠性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Akribeia采用混合框架，核心包括两个步骤：首先使用物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks）生成初始近似解，随后通过伪谱精化步骤（pseudo-spectral refinement step）进行高精度校正。最终获得连续、全局定义且以耦合常数为参数的认证神经场旋转黑洞解（certified neural-field rotating black hole solutions），并通过残差验证确保解对场方程满足极高精度。

Result: 该方法成功应用于曲率二次和三次理论，首次构造出具有多个非零角动量、以新耦合常数为参数的旋转黑洞族。在与已知的五维时空（five-dimensional spacetimes）进行验证后，该方法进一步生成了高度非线性/非微扰（non-linear/non-perturbative）常微分方程组场景下的新解。

Conclusion: Akribeia框架能够系统地适应其他涉及偏微分方程（partial differential equations）的构型，为高曲率引力理论中的黑洞解研究提供了一种通用且可验证的新工具。

Abstract: Finding rotating black hole solutions in higher-curvature theories of gravity is a problem of fundamental importance. Virtually every approach to reconcile gravity with quantum mechanics predicts corrections to the Einstein-Hilbert action, yet no systematic solution-generating method exists for the stationary sector. We close this gap with {\sc Akribeia}, a novel hybrid framework that pairs physics-informed neural networks with a pseudo-spectral refinement step, yielding certified neural-field rotating black hole solutions -- continuous, globally defined functions, parametric in the coupling constants -- whose residuals against the field equations are verified to extreme precision. We apply the method to theories quadratic and cubic in the curvature and construct, for the first time, families of rotating black holes featuring multiple non-vanishing angular momenta, parametric in the new coupling constants. After validating against previously known five-dimensional spacetimes, we present new solutions in scenarios leading to a highly non-linear/non-perturbative coupled system of ordinary differential equations. Our method can be systematically adapted to other setups involving partial differential equations as well.

TL;DR: 本文通过物质介质方法（material medium approach）研究了无质量粒子在旋转轴对称Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) 黑洞周围的偏折，分析了均匀磁场对光线轨迹的影响，并从热力学角度考察了熵与霍金温度随磁场强度和旋转参数的变化。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转轴对称Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞在存在均匀磁场时，其时空几何对光线轨迹的偏折效应，并进一步研究磁场对黑洞热力学性质的影响。

Method: 采用物质介质方法（material medium approach），通过推导偏转角解析表达式，分析框架拖拽效应（frame dragging effect）和折射率（refractive index）来研究光线偏折。

Result: 磁场会增强黑洞的引力效应，使光线弯曲更强，并永久改变黑洞远处空间使其不再是正常平坦真空。熵随磁场强度和旋转参数单调递减；霍金温度随均匀磁场增强而升高，但随自旋参数（spin parameter）增大而降低。

Conclusion: 磁场对KBR黑洞周围的时空几何和热力学性质均有显著影响，不仅增强了光线偏折，还改变了热力学行为。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the deflection of massless particles due to a rotating, axially symmetric Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole via; material medium approach. We explored the effect of spacetime geometry on the trajectory of light rays in the presence of a uniform magnetic field. To derive an analytical expression for the deflection of light rays due to the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole, the frame dragging effect and refractive index were also studied in greater detail. From the analysis it is evident that the magnetic field actively adds to the black hole's gravity, making the bending of light stronger and permanently changing the space far away from the black hole, preventing it to act as a normal flat vacuum. From thermodynamical investigation, it is clear that entropy monotonically decreases with magnetic field strength and rotation parameter; whereas the Hawking temperature increases with a uniform magnetic field but decreases with spin parameter.

</details>


### [49] [Scalar and Electromagnetic Perturbations around a Black Hole with a Topological Defect: Quasinormal Modes and Quasi-bound States in a Plasma Medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07487)
*Dilmurod Umarov,Farruh Atamurotov,Ahmadjon Abdujabbarov,Chengxun Yuan,G. Mustafa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了等离子体环境对带有拓扑缺陷（参数k）的黑洞的光学和扰动性质的影响，发现等离子体导致准正则模频率和阻尼率发生偏移，且拓扑缺陷参数k增大时会抑制准正则模实部；同时，电磁扰动在冷无磁化等离子体中轴向和极向部分解耦，均匀等离子体中仅当等离子体频率低于由k和多极指数l决定的临界阈值时才存在准束缚态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究等离子体环境对带有拓扑缺陷的黑洞的光学性质和扰动性质（包括准正则模和电磁扰动）的影响，以理解等离子体与黑洞拓扑缺陷之间的耦合效应。

Method: 首先建立了eikonal极限下准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）频率实部与黑洞阴影半径的直接对应关系；利用第三阶和第六阶WKB近似，在均匀等离子体、径向非均匀等离子体（包括奇异等温球SIS和非奇异等温球NSIS密度分布）背景下计算了有质量标量场扰动的QNM频谱；推导了冷无磁化等离子体中的电磁扰动动力学方程，并分析了轴向和极向扇区的解耦条件。

Result: 与光子球相关的Lyapunov指数对等离子体频率仅有弱依赖，但随拓扑缺陷参数k增大而单调递减；等离子体使振荡频率和阻尼率均发生偏移，k值较大会系统性地抑制QNM频率的实部；NSIS模型通常产生比SIS和均匀模型略高的振荡频率；均匀等离子体中，仅当等离子体频率低于由k和l决定的临界阈值时，轴向扇区才允许准束缚态存在。

Conclusion: 等离子体环境和拓扑缺陷参数共同调控黑洞的扰动行为，电磁扰动在等离子体中轴向与极向部分解耦，且均匀等离子体中的准束缚态存在阈值条件由拓扑缺陷参数和多极指数共同决定。

Abstract: We investigated the influence of a plasma environment on the optical and perturbative properties of a black hole with a topological defect, characterized by the parameter \(k\). We first established a straightforward correspondence between the real part of the quasinormal-mode (QNM) frequencies in the eikonal limit and the black-hole shadow radius. We then demonstrated that the Lyapunov exponent associated with the photon sphere exhibits only a weak dependence on the plasma frequency, while it monotonically decreases as the topological-defect parameter \(k\) increases. Subsequently, we analyzed massive scalar-field perturbations by deriving the associated effective potential and computing the QNM spectrum using the third- and sixth-order WKB approximations for both homogeneous and radially inhomogeneous plasma configurations, including the singular isothermal sphere (SIS) and non-singular isothermal sphere (NSIS) density profiles. Our results show that the presence of plasma induces shifts in both the oscillation frequencies and the damping rates of the modes, and that larger values of \(k\) systematically suppress the real part of the QNM frequencies. Among the plasma models considered, the NSIS profile generally yields slightly higher oscillation frequencies than both the SIS and homogeneous cases. Finally, we derived the dynamical equations governing electromagnetic perturbations in a cold, unmagnetized plasma and demonstrated that the axial and polar sectors decouple. In the axial sector, the plasma frequency enters as an effective mass term, thereby permitting the existence of quasi-bound states only in the case of a homogeneous plasma and only when the plasma frequency lies below a critical threshold that depends on the topological-defect parameter \(k\) and the multipole index \(l\).

</details>


### [50] [Vacuum polarization and renormalized stress-energy tensor of spherical thin shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07583)
*Julio Arrechea,Cormac Breen,Adrian Ottewill,Lorenzo Pisani,Peter Taylor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了薄壳时空（thin shell spacetime）中Boulware真空（Boulware vacuum）的性质，通过计算无质量标量场的重整化真空极化（renormalized vacuum polarization）和应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor），揭示了薄壳趋近黑洞极限时的标度行为，并发现壳外真空在高度致密无视界天体附近可能具有普适性（universality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究高度致密但无事件视界的物质构型（如薄壳）在黑洞极限下真空量子场的性质，特别是Boulware真空的极化与应力-能量张量的行为，为理解量子场在非黑洞致密天体背景下的预期值计算奠定基础。

Method: 采用扩展坐标方案（extended-coordinate prescription）计算重整化真空极化与应力-能量张量；在薄壳表面附近运用两种独立方法——高频近似（high-frequency approximation）和弱场近似（weak-field approximation）——获得领头阶奇异性行为；在壳中心通过半经典爱因斯坦方程（semiclassical Einstein equations）计算Casimir型非局域贡献的反作用（backreaction）；在解析方法不适用区域进行数值计算。

Result: 薄壳表面附近获得了两种量的领头阶奇异性行为；壳中心存在有限大小的非局域Casimir类贡献，且在黑洞极限下保持有限；数值计算覆盖了广泛的壳致密度（compactness）与场耦合参数；在黑洞极限下，壳外真空极化与重整化应力-能量张量迅速趋近Schwarzschild黑洞的结果。

Conclusion: 壳外真空在高度致密无质量视界天体的黑洞极限下表现出可能普适的行为，指向量子真空在类黑洞背景下的普适性特征；本研究为未来在物质构型中计算重整化期望值提供了概念性与技术性基础。

Abstract: We provide a thorough study of the properties of the Boulware vacuum in the spacetime of a spherical, static thin shell with a Minkowski interior. To this end, we calculate the renormalized vacuum polarization and stress-energy tensor of massless scalar fields via the extended-coordinate prescription, paying particular attention to their scaling as the shell approaches the black hole limit. Near the surface of the thin shell, we obtain the expected leading-order singular behavior of both quantities via two independent methods: a high-frequency approximation for the modes, and a weak-field approximation. At the center of the shell we find non-local, Casimir-like contributions that remain finite in the black hole limit, and whose backreaction effects we compute via the semiclassical Einstein equations. Away from these regions amenable to analytic treatment, we obtain numerical results for a wide range of shell compactnesses and field couplings. In the black hole limit, we show that the vacuum polarization and renormalized stress-energy tensor outside the shell quickly approach the ones generated by a Schwarzschild black hole, suggesting a possible universality in the vacuum outside highly compact horizonless objects. This work addresses the conceptual and technical aspects necessary for computing renormalized expectation values in matter configurations, laying the foundations for future explorations on the subject.

### [51] [On relativistic observables in black bounce spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07679)
*Víctor Ovejero-Bermúdez,Álvaro de la Cruz-Dombriz,Riccardo Della Monica*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过解析与数值相结合的方法，系统研究了黑洞反弹时空（black bounce spacetimes）中类时和类光测地线的相对论可观测量，揭示了反弹参数α导致的近星点进动、光线偏折、红移相位偏移和临界碰撞参数等可观测效应，并指出穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）分支会显著改变光子轨迹的临界碰撞参数，从而为区分黑洞与虫洞结构提供了观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞反弹几何在弱场和强场下的可观测特征，旨在揭示由反弹参数α引入的规则化修正（regularization correction）如何改变标准黑洞预言，并评估这些时空能否被未来的强引力观测所约束。

Method: 采用哈密顿-雅可比（Hamilton--Jacobi）与拉格朗日（Lagrangian）形式推导弱场解析表达式，计算大质量粒子的近星点进动（periastron advance）和光线的偏折角（deflection angle）；同时利用PyGRO代码进行数值积分以验证解析结果，并数值计算类光测地线的临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）。

Result: 反弹参数α增大会使近星点进动和光线偏折均强于史瓦西（Schwarzschild）情形；在规则黑洞分支中临界碰撞参数与史瓦西值相同，但在穿越虫洞分支中该参数显著增大；此外还识别出与修正几何相关的累积时间相位偏移（cumulative temporal phase shifts）。

Conclusion: 黑洞反弹时空可产生偏离标准黑洞预言的可观测差异，为利用当前和未来的强引力观测约束这些几何结构提供了可能性。

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenology of black bounce spacetimes through a combined analytical and numerical study of relativistic observables associated with both time-like and null geodesics. Black bounce geometries provide a continuous interpolation between Schwarzschild black holes and traversable wormholes by introducing a regularization bounce parameter $α$, which removes the central singularity by replacing it with a finite-radius throat. Using the Hamilton--Jacobi and Lagrangian formalisms, we derive weak-field analytical expressions for the periastron advance of massive particles and the deflection angle of light, highlighting the leading corrections induced by the bounce parameter. These results are systematically compared with numerical integrations performed with the PyGRO code. We show that increasing $α$ enhances both the periastron precession and the light deflection with respect to the Schwarzschild case. Additionally, we analyze the relativistic redshift of bound orbits and identify cumulative temporal phase shifts associated with the modified geometry. For null geodesics, we also determine numerically the critical impact parameter separating scattered and captured (or transmitted through the throat) photon trajectories. Although this quantity remains identical to the Schwarzschild value in the regular black hole branch, it increases significantly in the traversable wormhole regime, providing a clear observational signature of the throat structure. Our results demonstrate that black bounce spacetimes can produce measurable deviations from standard black hole predictions, opening the possibility of constraining these geometries with current and future observations of strong gravitational fields.

</details>


### [52] [When one sign is not enough: 2+1 circular motion Unruh effect at low energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07686)
*Leo J. A. Parry,Christopher J. Fewster,Jorma Louko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在2+1维时空中研究圆周运动的Unruh效应，通过点状Unruh-DeWitt探测器耦合无质量标量场。在渐近标度开关族（ASSF）框架下，证明探测器-场耦合的符号变化对于在长时间-小能隙双极限下获得非零的有效温度是必要的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆周运动Unruh效应（circular motion Unruh effect）的有效温度远小于线性加速情形，但Parry等人发现通过合适的耦合设计可在双极限下恢复线性加速Unruh温度量级。本文旨在证明这种耦合必须包含符号变化，回答符号变化是充分条件还是必要条件的问题，为相关实验验证奠定理论基础。

Method: 在渐近标度开关族（asymptotically scaled switching families, ASSFs）框架下，施加技术性有界性和局域化条件，对探测器-场耦合（detector-field coupling）进行数学分析，证明符号变化是获得非零极限有效温度的必要条件。

Result: 在ASSF框架及给定的有界性与局域化条件下，探测器-场耦合的符号变化（sign change）对于在长时间-小能隙双极限下获得非零的有效温度是必要的。

Conclusion: 符号变化并非仅仅是此前构造中的充分设计，而是一个必要条件；这一结论受到当前模拟时空实验中验证圆周运动Unruh效应工作的推动，对实验设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: We address the circular motion Unruh effect in 2+1 spacetime dimensions, as probed by a pointlike Unruh-DeWitt detector coupled to a massless scalar field. The effective temperature due to circular acceleration, operationally defined in terms of the detector's excitation and de-excitation probabilities, is known to be much smaller than the linear acceleration Unruh temperature when the detector's energy gap is small and the interaction lasts for a long time. It was shown by Parry et al. [Class. Quant. Grav. 42, 245012 (2025), arXiv:2508.19987] that a temperature of the order of the linear acceleration Unruh temperature can nevertheless be recovered in a simultaneous long-time-small-gap double limit, using suitable classes of detector-field couplings described by asymptotically scaled switching families (ASSFs). The successful constructions presented there required the coupling to change sign. Here we prove, within the ASSF framework and under certain technical boundedness and localisation conditions, that sign changes in the detector-field coupling are in fact *necessary* for obtaining a nonvanishing limiting effective temperature. Our analysis is motivated by current work towards an experimental verification of the circular motion Unruh effect in analogue spacetime experiments.

### [53] [Involution-equivariant topological recursion and mirror symmetry for the affine binary dihedral Calabi--Yau threefold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07355)
*Bohan Fang,Zhuoming Lan,Jingxiang Ma*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文证明了对仿射二元二面体Calabi-Yau轨道三维流形（affine binary dihedral Calabi-Yau orbifold threefold）$\mathcal X=[\mathbb C^2/Γ\times\mathbb C]$ 的一个闭弦重塑（closed-string remodeling）陈述，其中Γ是SU(2)的二元二面体子群。通过将Bouchard-Klemm-Mariño-Pasquetti（BKMP）重塑猜想从环面（toric）情形推广到非环面情形，作者建立了由类型-D_l 对数Toda曲线（type-$D_l$ logarithmic Toda curve）和$\mathbb Z_2$-等变拓扑递归（equivariant topological recursion）构成的B模型，与A模型等变Gromov-Witten不变量之间的等价关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BKMP重塑猜想此前仅适用于环面Calabi-Yau三维流形，本文旨在将其推广到非环面的二元二面体轨道奇点情形，填补了非环面Calabi-Yau轨道流形上闭弦/开弦对应（closed/open string correspondence）的理论空白。

Method: 将环面镜面对称的镜像曲线替换为类型-D_l 对数Toda曲线，并将Chekhov-Eynard-Orantin拓扑递归替换为Giacchetto-Kramer-Lewański的$\mathbb Z_2$-等变拓扑递归，在Toda曲线对合的符号扇区（sign sector）中以Prym核（Prym kernel）作为两点输入。通过识别轨道量子上同调（orbifold quantum cohomology）Frobenius流形与Toda曲线的不变Jacobian Frobenius结构，并利用正则化驻相法（regularized stationary phase）定义B模型R矩阵，证明其等于A侧光滑振荡腔（smooth oscillatory chamber）上的规范Givental-Teleman R矩阵；该等式通过Toda曲线的半稳定退化（semistable degeneration）锚定在轨道点处。

Result: 经过宇称扭曲的叶代换（parity-twisted leaf substitution）后，符号扇区拓扑递归与稳定范围（$2g-2+n>0$ 且 $n>0$）内$\mathcal X$的后裔Gromov-Witten生成函数（descendant Gromov-Witten generating functions）相一致，且递归自由能（recursion free energies）与$\mathcal X$在$g\geq2$时的等变Gromov-Witten自由能相等。

Conclusion: 成功将BKMP重塑猜想从环面情形推广到二元二面体轨道奇点这一非环面情形，建立了B模型等变拓扑递归与A模型Gromov-Witten不变量之间的精确等价关系，为非环面Calabi-Yau流形上的镜面对称（mirror symmetry）和拓扑递归提供了新范例。

Abstract: We prove a closed-string remodeling statement for the affine binary dihedral Calabi--Yau orbifold threefold $\mathcal X=[\mathbb C^2/Γ\times\mathbb C]$, where $Γ$ is a binary dihedral subgroup of $SU(2)$. This target lies outside the toric setting of the Bouchard--Klemm--Mariño--Pasquetti remodeling conjecture: the toric mirror curve is replaced by the type-$D_l$ logarithmic Toda curve of Brini--Ma--Strachan, and the Chekhov--Eynard--Orantin topological recursion is replaced by the $\mathbb Z_2$-equivariant topological recursion of Giacchetto--Kramer--Lewański, run in the sign sector of the Toda-curve involution with the Prym kernel as its two-point input. We identify the equivariant orbifold quantum cohomology Frobenius manifold of $\mathcal X$ with the invariant Jacobian Frobenius structure of the Toda curve, and we prove that the B-model $R$-matrix, defined by regularized stationary phase, equals the A-side normalized canonical Givental--Teleman $R$-matrix on the smooth oscillatory chamber; this equality is anchored at the orbifold point through a semistable degeneration of the Toda curve. Comparing the resulting Givental--Teleman and Dunin-Barkowski--Orantin--Shadrin--Spitz graph sums then identifies, after a parity-twisted leaf substitution, the sign-sector recursion with the descendant Gromov--Witten generating functions of $\mathcal X$ in the stable range ($2g-2+n>0$ with $n>0$), and identifies the recursion free energies with the equivariant Gromov--Witten free energies of $\mathcal X$ for $g\geq2$.

### [54] [Newton polygons for the non-bipartite dimer model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07503)
*Vladimir Bošković*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了环面（torus）上两类非二分图（non-bipartite graphs）的二聚体模型（dimer model），建立了这些图与底层二分图（bipartite graphs）的牛顿多边形（Newton polygons）之间的关系，证明了三角晶格和六角晶格Fisher图的边际多项式的实根性，并引入了一类保持二聚体配分函数（dimer partition function）的局域变换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二聚体模型在非二分图上的研究相对不足，尤其是其在紧致曲面上的几何与组合结构尚不清晰。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统分析两类非二分图族与对应二分图之间的牛顿多边形关系，并探索边际多项式的代数性质。

Method: 通过构造两类非二分图族（三角替换图与角图（corner graphs）），利用牛顿多边形（Newton polygons）和原始边向量（primitive edge vectors）分析其同调类（homology classes）。进一步，通过边际多项式（marginal polynomials）的实根性（real-rootedness）证明与因式分解，并引入新的局域变换（local moves）来保持配分函数。

Result: 确定了上述两类非二分图与底层二分图在牛顿多边形上的关系；将牛顿多边形的原始边向量与锯齿路径（zig-zag paths）的同调类对应；证明了三角晶格与六角晶格Fisher图的边际多项式是实根的，并给出了根的一个显式分解；引入了一类包括非平面图上的局域变换在内的新变换，这些变换保持二聚体配分函数（仅差一个尺度因子）。

Conclusion: 本文为环面上非二分图的二聚体模型提供了系统的几何与组合刻画，展示了牛顿多边形作为核心分析工具的效力；边际多项式的实根性揭示了特定晶格模型的结构化代数性质；新的局域变换拓宽了配分函数不变性的适用范围，为后续研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: We study the dimer model on two families of non-bipartite graphs on a torus. The first family is obtained by replacing degree $3$ vertices in a bipartite torus graph with triangles, while the second consists of corner graphs associated with bipartite torus graphs. We determine the relationship between the Newton polygons of these graphs and those of the underlying bipartite graphs. We also identify the primitive edge vectors of the Newton polygons with the homology classes of the zig-zag paths.
  We further consider the marginal polynomials obtained by restricting to monomials corresponding to a boundary side of the Newton polygon. For the triangular lattice and the Fisher graph of the hexagonal lattice, we prove that these polynomials are real-rooted and obtain an explicit factorization of their roots. Finally, we introduce new local moves, including a move on non-planar graphs, that preserve the dimer partition functions up to a scale.

</details>

### [55] [Polyconvexity does not imply true-stress-true-strain monotonicity in the incompressible three-dimensional case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06568)
*Dominik K. Klein,Maximilian P. Wollner,Patrizio Neff*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过反例证明，对于三维不可压缩材料的超弹性势，多凸性（polyconvexity）并不蕴含真应力-真应变单调性（true-stress-true-strain monotonicity），因此仅凭多凸性不足以保证理想弹性中物理上合理的响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在三维不可压缩材料的超弹性（hyperelastic）本构条件中，多凸性是否足以确保真应力-真应变关系的单调性，从而评估多凸性作为物理合理性判据的充分性。

Method: 通过构造反例（counterexample）进行理论分析，检验多凸性与真应力-真应变单调性之间的蕴含关系。

Result: 发现多凸性并不蕴含真应力-真应变单调性，即存在满足多凸性但真应力-真应变关系非单调的超弹性势。

Conclusion: 多凸性单独作为条件不足以保证理想弹性（idealized elasticity）中物理上合理的力学响应，需要更强的本构约束条件。

Abstract: We study constitutive conditions of hyperelastic potentials for incompressible material behavior in three dimensions. By means of a counterexample, we show that polyconvexity does not imply true-stress-true-strain monotonicity. Thus, polyconvexity alone is not strong enough to guarantee a physically reasonable response for idealized elasticity.

</details>

### [56] [Turing mechanisms in a multimode open quantum system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07449)
*Giorgia Comparato,Francesco Gargano,Rosario Lo Franco*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究玻色子模式有限链中的图灵型不稳定性（Turing-type instabilities）、模式竞争与图案选择（pattern selection），通过GKSL主方程连接经典反应-扩散动力学与量子耗散系统，并利用相空间方法和约化Wigner函数对比半经典分岔图景与量子动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多模开放量子系统中空间自组织（spatial self-organization）的形成机制，特别是将图灵不稳定性（Turing instabilities）从经典非线性动力学扩展到量子耗散系统，并揭示模式竞争（mode competition）与图案选择（pattern selection）的量子对应。

Method: 基于Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL)主方程建立有限链玻色子模型，结合局域参量驱动（parametric driving）、非线性阻尼（nonlinear damping）和非局域耗散耦合（nonlocal dissipative couplings）；在经典极限下推导反应-扩散类动力学；采用相空间方法（phase-space methods）和约化Wigner函数（reduced Wigner functions）对比确定性分岔与量子动力学。

Result: 系统可呈现不同稳态非均匀构型、振荡波态或多模式交互后的主导图案；量子动力学与半经典反应-扩散分岔图景之间存在可比较的模式竞争与选择行为。

Conclusion: 图灵不稳定性、模式竞争和图案选择可推广至多模开放量子系统，从而在非线性动力系统、耗散量子力学与空间自组织之间建立桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate pattern formation in a finite chain of bosonic modes whose dynamics is governed by a Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) master equation. The model combines local parametric driving and nonlinear damping with nonlocal dissipative couplings between modes that work on different discrete spatial scales. In the classical limit, these mechanisms generate a reaction-diffusion-like dynamics, allowing the emergence of Turing-type instabilities. The key aspect of the analysis is the coexistence and competition of different unstable spatial modes. Depending on the range of parameters, the system may select different stationary nonuniform configurations, oscillatory wave-like states, or regimes in which multiple modes interact before a dominant pattern is established, thus providing a mechanism for pattern selection. We compare the deterministic bifurcation scenario, generated by a reaction-diffusion-like system derived from semiclassical drift dynamics, with the quantum dynamics, derived via the GKSL master equation, using phase-space methods and reduced Wigner functions. The results show how Turing instabilities, mode competition, and pattern selection can be extended to multimode open quantum systems, providing a bridge between nonlinear dynamical systems, dissipative quantum mechanics, and spatial self-organization.

</details>


### [57] [Multi-channel collective dissipation via the symmetric irreducible representation of SU(4)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07701)
*M. Lutsukh,M. Bazarsana,T. Begzjav,G. O. Ariunbold*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文将Agarwal的多能级集体自发辐射形式主义（multi-level collective spontaneous-emission formalism）特化到四能级情形，通过在完全对称的SU(4)表示中表述N个全同原子系统，导出了紧凑的Pauli型布居数速率方程和总发射强度的闭式表达式，并针对七种偶极允许的四能级拓扑结构进行了数值求解，发现所有情况下发射强度均出现延迟合作爆发，其峰值服从拓扑依赖的幂律超线性标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多能级原子系综的集体自发辐射（collective spontaneous emission）是量子光学中的核心问题，但此前针对四能级系统的统一代数形式化框架尚不完善，尤其是如何从群表示论角度统一描述多种拓扑构型的集体耗散动力学。

Method: 采用完全对称的SU(4)不可约表示(N,0,0)，以占据数基（occupation-number basis）构建四面体重权格点（tetrahedral weight lattice），利用六个嵌入的su(2)跃迁子代数作为阶梯算符（ladder operators），推导出Pauli型布居数速率方程和总发射强度的解析表达式，并针对七种偶极允许拓扑结构（tripod、inverted tripod、Y、inverted Y、double-Λ、closed cascade和diamond）进行数值求解至N=50。

Result: 在每种拓扑结构中，发射强度均呈现延迟合作爆发（delayed cooperative burst），其峰值I_peak服从幂律I_peak = a N^p，拟合指数p位于1.81至1.92区间，表明超线性（superlinear）标度行为；不同拓扑对应的参数(a,p)存在差异。

Conclusion: SU(4)四面体流（tetrahedral flow）与七种构型依赖的瞬态过程共同提供了四能级原子系综多通道集体耗散（multi-channel collective dissipation）的统一几何图像，为理解和调控多能级集体辐射行为奠定了代数框架基础。

Abstract: We specialize Agarwal's multi-level collective spontaneous-emission formalism to the four-level case by formulating it in the fully symmetric \SU(4) representation of $N$ identical atoms. In the irreducible representation $(N,0,0)$, the occupation-number basis forms a tetrahedral weight lattice on which the six embedded $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ transition subalgebras act as ladder operators. From these algebraic factors we obtain a compact Pauli-type population-rate equation and a closed-form expression for the total emitted intensity that apply to any combination of open dipole channels. The formalism is then specialized to the seven dipole-allowed four-level topologies -- tripod, inverted tripod, Y, inverted Y, double-$Λ$, closed cascade, and diamond -- and the resulting rate equations are solved numerically for atom numbers up to $N=50$. In every case the emitted intensity develops a delayed cooperative burst whose peak height obeys a power law $I_{\mathrm{peak}}=aN^{p}$ with topology-dependent parameters $(a,p)$; the fitted exponents lie in the range $1.81\lesssim p\lesssim 1.92$, indicating a superlinear. The \SU(4) tetrahedral flow and the seven configuration-dependent transients together provide a unified geometric picture of multi-channel collective dissipation in four-level atomic ensembles.

</details>


### [58] [Tomography of a Macroscopic Quantum State influenced by Classical Self-Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06967)
*Wenjie Zhong,Yubao Liu,Yanbei Chen,Haixing Miao,Yiqiu Ma*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于薛定谔-牛顿（Schrödinger-Newton, SN）理论，研究经典自引力如何影响宏观机械振子的连续量子态层析（quantum state tomography），并发现当使用量子引力（quantum gravity, QG）优化的重构映射时，SN协方差会偏离标准高斯协方差区域，从而为区分引力是量子相互作用还是经典场提供了可量化的判别依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观光力学系统（macroscopic optomechanical systems）为检验引力是量子相互作用还是经典场提供了实验平台。SN理论作为半经典引力（semi-classical gravity）的非相对论极限，其预测与标准量子力学/量子引力（QG）存在差异，因此需要量化这种差异以判断引力的量子性质。

Method: 基于SN理论，研究宏观机械振子在变角度零差探测（variable-angle homodyne detection）下的连续量子态层析过程。分析SN理论中测量记录（measurement record）来源于与QG不同的条件测试质量动力学（conditional test mass dynamics），并由此推导QG优化重构映射产生的额外态依赖贡献（state-dependent contribution），最后用Hellinger距离（Hellinger distance）量化QG与SN的可区分性。

Result: QG优化重构映射引入的额外态依赖贡献使得重构协方差（reconstructed covariance）依赖于所选的层析角度，并可将经QG滤波后的SN协方差推至海森堡不确定原理（Heisenberg uncertainty principle）所规定的标准高斯协方差区域之外。该可区分性依赖于测量强度和温度。

Conclusion: SN理论与QG在条件动力学上的差异导致层析映射（tomographic map）出现非线性模型依赖修正，这推广到了非线性量子力学（nonlinear quantum mechanics）的框架中，为利用光力学系统检验引力的量子性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Macroscopic optomechanical systems offer a promising testbed for distinguishing whether gravity acts as a quantum interaction or as a classical field. Schrodinger-Newton (SN) theory is the nonrelativistic limit of semi-classical gravity where quantum matter couples to classical gravity. Based on SN theory, this work investigates how classical self-gravity affects continuous quantum state tomography of a macroscopic mechanical oscillator monitored by variable-angle homodyne detection. In the Schrodinger-Newton (SN) theory, the measurement record arises from a different conditional test mass dynamics from that in quantum-gravity (QG)/standard quantum mechanics, consequently, applying the QG-optimised reconstruction map introduces an additional state-dependent contribution. We show that this contribution makes the reconstructed covariance depend on the chosen set of tomography angles and can drive the SN covariance--after QG filtering--outside the standard Gaussian-covariance domain set by the Heisenberg uncertainty principle. We quantify the resulting QG-SN distinguishability via the Hellinger distance and analyse its dependence on measurement strength and temperature. We then formulate the same issue in the broader setting of nonlinear quantum mechanics: when the system's conditional dynamics during the readout process depends on the state being inferred, the tomographic map acquires nonlinear, model-dependent corrections to the usual Radon or Gaussian reconstruction map.

</details>


### [59] [Analytical Landscape of Maximal Magic for Two-Qutrit States and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07197)
*Marco Knipfer,Alexander Roman,Katia Matcheva,Konstantin T. Matchev*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了两量子三元（qutrit）和两量子五元（ququint）系统中固定纠缠下的极端魔术（magic）帕累托前沿（Pareto frontiers），给出了最小魔术的紧凑函数形式、最大稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）的严格上界及对应最大魔术态的解析构造，并基于此提出了针对素数维度二分系统最大魔术的猜想公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现真正的量子优势依赖于两种非经典资源——纠缠（entanglement）和魔术（magic或nonstabilizerness），它们分别限制了经典模拟的可行性。然而，这两种资源在高维系统中的相互关联尚未被充分理解，尤其对于维度d≥3的情形。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统刻画固定纠缠下极端魔术行为的帕累托边界。

Method: 对于两qutrit系统，利用Schmidt谱（Schmidt spectrum）中的两个独立纠缠参数构建二维帕累托曲面；通过解析推导最小魔术关于并发度（concurrence）和负性（negativity）的紧凑函数形式；对于上界，采用稳定子Rényi熵M₂作为魔术量化指标，结合数值搜索与对称性分析确定最大魔术值及对应态的结构；对于d=5情形，进行数值分析并归纳出素数维度下的通用公式。

Result: 两qutrit情形：最小魔术的上界为ln2；最大稳定子Rényi熵M₂ = ln(81/17) ≈ 1.561，收紧此前理论界ln5≈1.609；最大魔术对应18个不同极值点，分为三族每族六个置换等价谱。两ququint情形：发现6个置换不等价的最大值，峰值M₂ = ln(625/49) ≈ 2.546。基于这些结果，提出素数维度d下最大魔术的猜想公式M₂ = ln[d⁴/(2d²−1)]。

Conclusion: 本文在高维量子系统中建立了纠缠与魔术之间精确的定量关系，揭示了Schmidt谱多维参数空间对帕累托边界的直接影响，并给出了可验证的解析结果。提出的素数维度最大魔术猜想为未来研究更高维量子优势的边界提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Achieving a genuine quantum advantage relies on two distinct non-classical resources that restrict efficient classical simulation: entanglement and magic (nonstabilizerness). We investigate the interplay between these resources by characterizing the Pareto frontiers of extreme magic at fixed entanglement for systems of two qutrits ($d=3$) and two ququints ($d=5$). Unlike the case of two qubits, the Schmidt spectrum for two qutrits features two independent entanglement parameters, resulting in two-dimensional Pareto surfaces. For the lower frontier, we recast the minimal magic as a compact function of concurrence and negativity, with a maximal value of $\ln 2$. For the upper frontier, we determine the maximal stabilizer Rényi entropy to be $M_2 = \ln(81/17) \approx 1.561$, which tightens the previous theoretical bound of $\ln 5\approx 1.609$ and improves on earlier numerical estimates. The maximum magic is achieved at eighteen distinct maxima categorized into three families of six permutation-equivalent spectra. We provide analytical expressions for the maximal magic in the neighborhood of each maximum and for the corresponding maximally magical states which turn out to be Weyl-Heisenberg-covariant fiducial states for mutually unbiased bases. Finally, numerical analysis of two ququints ($d=5$) reveals six permutation-inequivalent maxima with a peak magic value of $M_2 = \ln(625/49) \approx 2.546$. Based on these findings, we conjecture that the maximal magic for a bipartite system of two qudits with prime dimension $d$ is given by $\ln [ d^4 / (2d^2 - 1) ]$, which reproduces the previously known value for qubits, as well as the values derived here for qutrits and ququints.

</details>


### [60] [Localized Thermometry via Dayem Bridges Integrated on Superconducting Qubit Chips](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06670)
*Ella O. Lachman,Dave P. Pappas,Jayss Marshall,Josh Y. Mutus*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了一种基于超导Dayem桥的片上测温方法，将其集成在transmon量子比特同一芯片上，通过测量临界电流获得局部温度，无需微波校准或专用量子比特控制序列，并展示了其在诊断温度相关退相干机制中的实用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 片上温度精确测量对理解和优化超导量子比特性能至关重要，但毫开尔文温度下的直接测温仍具挑战；现有基于量子比特的测温方法需专用测量协议和设计，限制了其常规诊断的实用性和硬件测试效率。

Method: 将超导Dayem桥与transmon量子比特集成在同一芯片上，通过I-V测量提取Dayem桥的临界电流（critical current），获得局域定量温度值；校准临界电流随温度的变化关系，并与量子比特激发态布居数进行同步比对验证。

Result: Dayem桥温度计与量子比特激发态布居数在相关温度范围内吻合，验证了该方法与已有量子比特测温法的一致性；将独立测量的芯片温度与量子比特能量弛豫时间和退相位时间关联，展示了诊断温度相关退相干机制的能力。

Conclusion: 集成Dayem桥提供了一种简单、非侵入、可扩展的低温硬件开发工具和超导量子电路片上测温方案。

Abstract: Accurate knowledge of the on-chip temperature is essential for understanding and optimizing the performance of superconducting qubits, yet direct thermometry at millikelvin temperatures remains challenging. While qubits themselves are sensitive to the temperature of their environment, other factors may affect the qubits` effective temperature, and using them as thermometers with any accuracy requires specialized measurement protocols and qubit designs, limiting their practicality for routine diagnostics and adding complex infrastructure to any hardware testing apparatus. Here we demonstrate a complementary on-chip thermometry method based on superconducting Dayem bridges that are integrated on the same chip as transmon qubits. By extracting the critical current of the Dayem bridge from I-V measurements, we obtain a local, quantitative measure of the chip temperature without the need for microwave calibration or qubit-specific control sequences. To demonstrate the utility of the Dayem bridges as thermometers, we fabricate them in-situ with qubits on the same chip, calibrate the Dayem bridge critical current as a function of temperature, and characterize its resolution and stability at cryogenic temperatures. We additionally perform simultaneous measurements of the Dayem bridge thermometer and qubit excited-state population, and show agreement over the relevant temperature range, validating the method against established qubit thermometry. Furthermore, we correlate the independently measured chip temperature with qubit energy relaxation and dephasing times, demonstrating the utility of this approach for diagnosing temperature-dependent decoherence mechanisms. These results establish integrated Dayem bridges as a simple, non-invasive, and scalable tool for cryogenic hardware development, and on chip thermometry in superconducting quantum circuits.

</details>


### [61] [Spin singlets are useful](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06672)
*Silas Hoffman,Edward H. Chen,Matthew Brooks,Stephen Carr,Daniel Volya,Alan Tran,Tyler Keating,Thaddeus D. Ladd,Charles Tahan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文评估了交换耦合自旋阵列中自旋零流形（spin-zero manifold）在量子计算与量子模拟中的效用，证明其相比传统交换只控制（exchange-only control）能提供更大计算空间，并通过推广交叉熵基准测试等方法验证了资源利用优势，可加速半导体自旋量子比特实现计算量子优势（computational quantum advantage）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交换只控制（exchange-only control）将自旋阵列组织为由n个自旋构成的模块化单元，仅编码N/n个量子比特，导致希尔伯特空间维度指数级缩小至2^{N/n}。本文旨在探索利用完整的自旋零流形（spin-zero manifold）来释放阵列的更大计算潜力。

Method: 首先证明自旋零流形可通过交换作用单独控制，且其希尔伯特空间维度渐近接近完整自旋空间的2^N维度。随后将交叉熵基准测试（cross-entropy benchmarking）、镜像基准测试（mirror benchmarking）以及时序外关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators）推广至该流形体系，用以评估资源利用率。

Result: 自旋零流形的近似维度为2^N/(N/2)^{3/2}，渐近接近于完整自旋空间的2^N。与将阵列组织为n自旋模块化单元的交换只控制方案相比，自旋零流形能够提供指数级更大的计算希尔伯特空间。

Conclusion: 在半导体自旋量子比特中，利用自旋零流形进行运算可加速实现计算量子优势（computational quantum advantage），为资源利用提供了更优的基准度量。

Abstract: We evaluate the utility of the spin-zero manifold of an exchange-coupled array of $N$ spins for tasks in quantum computation and quantum simulation. Since pairs of electrons can be readily initialized into a product state of singlets in semiconducting quantum dot arrays, the full spin-zero manifold is available with exchange-only control, providing a Hilbert space of approximate dimension $2^N/(N/2)^{3/2}$, asymptotically close to the $2^N$ dimension of the full spin Hilbert space. Leveraging the spin-zero manifold enables larger computational space in a given array compared to traditional exchange-only control, in which spin arrays are organized into modular units of $n$ spins comprising $N/n$ encoded qubits, limiting to the exponentially smaller Hilbert dimension $2^{N/n}$. Here we focus on benchmarking metrics for this resource utilization by generalizing cross-entropy benchmarking, mirror benchmarking, and out-of-time-ordered correlators to this system. We show that operating in the spin-zero manifold can accelerate the realization of computational quantum advantage applications in semiconductor-based spin qubits.

</details>


### [62] [Universal purification dynamics of monitored Clifford circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06683)
*Beatrice Magni,Federico Gerbino,Xhek Turkeshi,Andrea De Luca*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在克利福德（Clifford）监测量子电路中，纯化动力学可以简化为密度矩阵秩的马尔可夫衰变过程，并给出了所有Rényi熵的通用标度函数，避免了传统复制技巧（replica trick）所需的解析延拓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱监测量子电路会在指数长的纯化时间尺度$T_P$上表现出普遍的纯化动力学，但以往对此的定量描述必须借助复制技巧（replica trick）及其微妙的解析延拓，缺乏更简洁的解析框架。

Method: 研究聚焦于素数维度$q$的$L$个量子比特（qudit）上的监测克利福德电路（Clifford circuit），在固定标度变量$x = t/T_P(L)$的极限下，将纯化过程映射为密度矩阵秩的马尔可夫衰变（Markovian decay），并利用精确的稳定子模拟（stabilizer simulation）在$q=2,3,5$下验证理论预测。

Result: 所有Rényi熵坍缩到一条通用曲线$\langle S(x) \rangle$上；全局模型无需拟合参数，局域砖墙电路仅需拟合$T_P$一个参数。复制技巧问题等价于同一马尔可夫过程的倾斜版本。克利福德电路有两个独特特征：短标度时间$x\to0$时熵涨落趋于$O(1)$方差而非零，以及可观测量的时间调制呈现$\log_q x$周期性。

Conclusion: 监测克利福德电路中的纯化动力学可被精确求解为秩的死亡过程，复制技巧（replica trick）对应其倾斜版本；秩的量子化导致克利福德动力学区别于一般监测电路的两种标志性行为。

Abstract: Quantum circuits under sufficiently weak monitoring purify on a timescale $T_P$ exponentially long in the system size. This slowness underlies a universal purification dynamics, whose quantitative description has so far required the replica trick, with a delicate analytic continuation. We show that monitored Clifford circuits on $L$ qudits of prime dimension $q$ bypass this construction entirely: in the scaling limit at fixed $x = t/T_P(L)$, purification reduces to the Markovian decay of the density-matrix rank, an exactly solvable death process descending from infinity. We compute the full scaling functions in compact form: all Rényi entropies collapse onto a universal curve $\langle S(x) \rangle$. Exact stabilizer simulations at $q=2,3,5$ confirm the predictions, with no fitting parameter for the global model and $T_P$ as the only fitted scale for local brick-wall circuits. Also, the replica problem amounts to a tilted version of the same Markov process, in agreement with exact computations from the Clifford commutant. Finally, the quantization of the rank leaves two hallmarks that distinguish Clifford dynamics from generic monitored circuits: the entropy fluctuations saturate at short scaled times $x\to0$ to an $O(1)$ variance, instead of vanishing, and observables develop a temporal modulation periodic in $\log_q x$, which cannot be captured by the replica approach.

</details>


### [63] [Universal spin-squeezing dynamics in spinor condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06842)
*Nikolaos Giovanoudis,Navid Kazemiseresht,Fabio Mezzacapo,Emilia Witkowska,Tommaso Roscilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了通过自旋（spin）玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）中的本征自旋改变碰撞（spin-changing collisions）与任意二次塞曼位移（quadratic Zeeman shift）相结合，可产生可扩展的自旋压缩（spin squeezing），遵循单轴扭曲模型（one-axis-twisting model）的普适范式。压缩动力学可分别由二次塞曼位移或自旋改变碰撞驱动，并可通过关闭塞曼位移冻结集体自旋动力学，从而实现对被测外场的唯一调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模纠缠态（large-scale entangled states）的制备是下一代量子技术的主要目标之一，尤其是在纠缠辅助量子传感（entanglement-assisted quantum sensing）领域具有直接应用潜力。超冷自旋气体（ultracold spinor gases）因其原子具有大内禀自旋并对磁场敏感，成为实现该目标的一个非常有前景的平台。

Method: 利用自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的本征自旋改变碰撞与任意二次塞曼位移的结合，遵循单轴扭曲模型的普适范式，在系综的集体自旋（collective spin）中生成可扩展的自旋压缩。当二次塞曼位移较小时，压缩动力学由此位移驱动；当位移较大时，压缩由自旋改变碰撞以闪光压缩（stroboscopic squeezing）的形式驱动。

Result: 研究结果表明，自旋改变碰撞与二次塞曼位移的组合能够实现可扩展的自旋压缩，且通过关闭塞曼位移可以冻结集体自旋动力学，使后续的集体自旋动力学唯一地受控于待感测的外场。

Conclusion: 该理论结果为在大自旋的自旋玻色气体中开展纠缠的基础研究以及先进计量学（metrology）应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: The production of large-scale entangled states is one of the main goals of next-generation quantum technologies, with an immediate potential for applications in the context of entanglement-assisted quantum sensing. A very promising platform to achieve this goal is offered by ultracold spinor gases, made of atoms with a large internal spin sensitive to magnetic fields. Here we show that the native spin-changing collisions in a spinor Bose-Einstein condensate, combined with an arbitrary quadratic Zeeman shift, can generate scalable spin squeezing in the collective spin of the ensemble, following the universal paradigm of the celebrated one-axis-twisting model. Squeezing dynamics is driven by the quadratic Zeeman shift when this shift is small; and by the spin-changing collisions for large shifts, in the form of stroboscopic squeezing. Turning off the Zeeman shift freezes out the collective-spin dynamics, so that the ensuing collective spin dynamics can be uniquely governed by an external field to be sensed. Our theoretical results pave the way for the use of spinor Bose gases with a large spin in fundamental studies of entanglement, as well as in advanced metrological applications.

</details>


### [64] [A "squeezed polaron" variational wavefunction for the spin boson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06850)
*Diego Barberena,Nigel Cooper*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对亚欧姆自旋-玻色子模型（sub-Ohmic spin-boson model）的局域化转变（localization transition），提出了一种“压缩极化子”（squeezed polaron）波函数，通过引入高斯型玻色子-玻色子关联，在低能区修正了标准相干态-极化子变分法的解析缺陷，从而正确捕捉了临界幂律标度、基态能量和临界耦合，并揭示了非平均场临界指数以及局域化转变处消失的涌现能量尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚欧姆自旋-玻色子模型在低频率下的局域化转变会产生玻色子浴关联，但标准相干态-极化子（coherent-state-polaron）变分法在解析上无法处理这些关联，因此需要引入更精确的波函数变分方案。

Method: 作者提出了一种“压缩极化子”波函数，该波函数包含由自旋杂质（spin impurity）诱导的通用高斯型玻色子-玻色子关联（Gaussian boson-boson correlations），作为变分基态进行系统分析。

Result: 新波函数给出了局域化转变附近浴观测量正确的临界幂律标度（critical power-law scaling），系统改进了基态能量（ground state energy），并更准确地确定了临界耦合（critical coupling）。在深亚欧姆区域捕获了转变的平均场（mean-field）本质，在浅亚欧姆区域显示出非平均场临界指数（non-mean-field critical exponents）。

Conclusion: 以压缩极化子为起点，推导了玻色子的散射相移（scattering phase shifts），并展示了这些相移如何编码在局域化转变处消失的涌现能量尺度（emergent energy scale）。

Abstract: The localization transition of the sub-Ohmic spin-boson model generates boson bath correlations that are, at low frequencies, analytically inaccessible to standard coherent-state-polaron variational ansatzes. In this paper, we introduce a ``squeezed polaron'' wavefunction incorporating generic Gaussian boson-boson correlations induced by the spin impurity. This gives the correct critical power-law scaling of bath observables near the localization transition together with a systematically improved ground state energy and a more accurate determination of the critical coupling. Our wavefunction captures the correct mean-field nature of the transition in the deep sub-Ohmic region. It also displays non-mean-field critical exponents in the shallow sub-Ohmic regime. Using the squeezed polaron as a starting point, we derive scattering phase shifts for bosons, and show how they encode the emergent energy scale that vanishes at the localization transition.

### [65] [Explaining the magnitude of Chirality-Induced Spin Selectivity via electron-electron exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06858)
*Bence Csakany,Alex J. W. Thom*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过哈特里-福克（Hartree–Fock）自洽平均场近似下的电子-电子库仑交换作用模拟，证明了吸附在Cu(111)上的3-甲基环己酮（3-methylcyclohexanone）可产生约2%的显著自旋极化（spin polarization），该效应放大了初始约0.0014%的微小偏置，为理解手性诱导自旋选择性（Chirality-Induced Spin Selectivity, CISS）的微观起源提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性分子结构可与电子自旋耦合产生自旋极化效应，即手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）。该效应最早在吸附于金表面的DNA分子中被报道，但其微观起源尚不明确。本文旨在通过从头算（ab-initio）模拟揭示CISS的微观机制。

Method: 采用自洽平均场近似下的哈特里-福克（Hartree–Fock）方法，通过电子-电子库仑相互作用产生的交换项（exchange term）进行模拟计算，研究3-甲基环己酮（3-methylcyclohexanone）吸附在Cu(111)表面体系中的自旋极化行为。

Result: 模拟显示，电子间的交换相互作用可将初始约0.0014%的微小偏置放大为约2%的显著自旋极化（spin polarisation），该结果与实验一致。对称性考量保证了结果的物理意义，从头算性质确保了所有参数具有物理现实性。

Conclusion: 该放大机制与哈特里-福克中自旋对称性破缺（spin-symmetry breaking）的已有研究相联系，为将CISS理解为相互作用电子（interacting electrons）涌现现象（emergent phenomenon）提供了理解其量级的新途径。

Abstract: Chiral molecular structure can couple to electron spin, leading to unexpected spin polarization effects. This Chirality-Induced Spin Selectivity (CISS) was first reported for DNA molecules adsorbed on gold but its microscopic origin remains unclear. We demonstrated though simulation that the exchange arising from electron-electron Coulomb interactions within the self-consistent mean field (Hartree--Fock) approximation can yield significant ($\sim 2\%$) spin polarisation for $3$-methylcyclohexanone adsorbed on Cu(111) amplifying a much smaller ($\sim 0.0014\%$) initial bias, consistent with experiment. Symmetry considerations ensure the result is physically meaningful, while its ab-initio nature ensures all parameters are physically realistic. This amplification is connected to existing studies on spin-symmetry breaking in Hartree--Fock, providing a new pathway for understanding the magnitude of CISS as an emergent phenomenon of interacting electrons.

### [66] [Anyon-induced non-Hermitian topological phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06934)
*Yi-An Wang,Kun Ding,Linhu Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现任意子交换统计（anyon exchange statistics）可以激活非厄米点能隙拓扑（non-Hermitian point-gap topology），这种拓扑在无统计效应时是不存在的。该拓扑随统计相位振荡频率随任意子数增加而加快，并表现出对粒子数的奇偶依赖性。分析表明，分数统计与依赖于子晶格的耗散（dissipation）结合，产生粒子数依赖的非互易性（non-reciprocity）和复谱缠绕（complex spectral winding），从而将交换统计确立为在受控耗散下实现非厄米拓扑的一种资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索任意子交换统计能否在原本拓扑平庸的体系中激活非厄米点能隙拓扑，并揭示其物理机制，从而将交换统计确立为一种实现非厄米拓扑的新资源。

Method: 采用微扰分析（perturbative analysis）方法，研究分数统计（fractional statistics）如何导致动量项失配（mismatch between momentum terms），并结合依赖于子晶格的耗散（sublattice-dependent dissipation）产生粒子数依赖的非互易性和复谱缠绕。

Result: 任意子交换统计能激活非厄米点能隙拓扑；该拓扑随统计相位振荡，且振荡频率随任意子数增加而加快；拓扑行为表现出对粒子数的奇偶依赖性。

Conclusion: 任意子交换统计可以作为一种资源，在受控耗散条件下实现非厄米拓扑，其机制依赖于相互作用束缚的任意子（interaction-bound anyons）的形成与交换。

Abstract: We show that anyonic exchange statistics can activate non-Hermitian point-gap topology in models that are topologically trivial in its absence. The emergent topology oscillates more rapidly with the statistical phase as the anyon number increases, and exhibits a parity dependence on the particle number. A perturbative analysis reveals the mechanism: fractional statistics induces a mismatch between momentum terms that, combined with sublattice-dependent dissipation, produces particle-number-dependent non-reciprocity and complex spectral winding. As these effects rely on the formation and exchange of interaction-bound anyons, our results establish exchange statistics as a resource for enabling non-Hermitian topology under programmed dissipation.

</details>


### [67] [Spin Textures and Eigenstate Evolution of Isospectrally Patterned Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07502)
*Peter Schmelcher*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现等谱图案化晶格（isospectrally patterned lattices）具有复合能带结构，其局域化与离域化本征态的比例可通过相位梯度调控；通过将晶格哈密顿量映射为在旋转磁场中自旋翻转跳跃的单自旋系统，揭示了振荡包络、准节点处的自旋峰以及从局域化到离域化转变在傅里叶谱中的指纹特征，并量化了自旋纹理的重新排列转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将晶格哈密顿量解释为单个自旋在旋转磁场中允许自旋翻转跳跃的模型；通过傅里叶谱分析本征态从局域化到离域化的交叉行为；利用自旋涨落全变差（total variation of local spin fluctuations）量化自旋纹理的（不）规则图案。

Result: 低能和高能区的局域态呈现振荡包络和准节点（quasi-nodes），准节点处出现自旋峰；自旋纹理随激发程度增加而复杂化；局域化-离域化转变在傅里叶谱中表现为双峰分布展宽并最终收窄为极窄频率峰；自旋纹理经历涉及不同（不）规则图案的重新排列转变。

Conclusion: 等谱图案化晶格展现出丰富的谱特性，尤其是在更高晶格或胞体维度下具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: Isospectrally patterned lattices exhibit a composite band structure with a tunable ratio of localized versus delocalized eigenstates that is controlled by the underlying phase gradient. We show that the lattice Hamiltonian can be interpreted as that of a single spin exposed to a rotating magnetic field which is allowed to hop with a spin-flip across the lattice. In the low- and high-energy part of the band the localized states show an envelope of oscillatory character separated by quasi-nodes. Spin peaks occur at the locations of these quasi-nodes and provide a unique spin texture to the eigenstates which becomes increasingly complex with increasing degree of excitation. The crossover from localization to delocalization and vice versa leaves its fingerprints in the Fourier spectrum of the eigenstates: the original bimodal frequency distribution widens with increasing degree of excitation, moves across the spectral window and finally culminates in an extremely narrow frequency peak. In the course of this evolution the spin texture undergoes a rearrangement transition involving different characteristic (ir)regular patterns which we quantify by considering the total variation of the local spin fluctuations. Our results demonstrate the variety of the spectral properties of isospectrally patterned lattices which holds great prospect in particular when considering higher lattice or cell dimensions.

### [68] [Variational Learning with Sparse Long-range Entangling Gates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07547)
*Helene M. Lösl,Aydin Deger,Andrew J. Daley*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了稀疏长程连接（尤其是幂二连接图PWR2）对变分量子算法性能的影响，发现扩展的算子空间本身不足以确保可训练性，并提出了将层次化长程哈密顿量映射为几何局域哈密顿量的变分方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分量子算法（variational quantum algorithms）的性能通常依赖于参数化量子电路（parametrized quantum circuit）的结构，但最常见的ansätze基于局域耦合。受中性原子和囚禁离子实验中可实现的扩展连接性启发，本文旨在考察结构化长程连接何时能成为有用的资源。

Method: 采用动力学李代数分析（dynamical Lie-algebra analysis）、近似酉设计诊断（approximate unitary-design diagnostics）以及有限深度的表达性（expressibility）和纠缠（entanglement）度量，来评估稀疏幂二连接图（power-of-two, PWR2）如何扩大可访问的算子空间。此外，还提出了一种变分方案，将层次化长程哈密顿量（hierarchical long-range Hamiltonians）映射为几何局域哈密顿量。

Result: 扩展的算子空间本身并不足以确保参数化电路对于给定目标问题的可训练性（trainability）。在有/无长程耦合的示例问题上评估性能后，识别出稀疏连接图在哪些场景下可能提供优势、哪些场景下则不然。

Conclusion: 电路几何结构（circuit geometry）和量子比特可重构性（qubit reconfigurability）应被视为变分算法中与任务相关的资源。这些发现对具有长程连接性的量子硬件的发展具有参考意义。

Abstract: The performance of variational quantum algorithms depends in general on the structure of the parametrized quantum circuit, but the most common ansätze are typically based on local couplings. Motivated by the extended connectivity available with neutral atoms and trapped ions, we examine when structured long-range connectivity provides a useful resource, focusing on sparse power-of-two (PWR2) coupling graphs. Using dynamical Lie-algebra analysis, approximate unitary-design diagnostics, and finite-depth measures of expressibility and entanglement, we examine how these geometries enlarge the accessible operator space. This enlarged space alone is not sufficient to ensure trainability of the parameterized circuit for given target problems, and we explore performance across example problems with and without long-range coupling, identifying where sparse coupling graphs are or are not likely to provide an advantage. We also introduce a variational scheme that maps hierarchical long-range Hamiltonians to geometrically local ones that can be optimized with short-range circuits. Together, these results identify circuit geometry and qubit reconfigurability as task-dependent resources for variational algorithms, relevant to ongoing developments in quantum hardware with long-range connectivity.

</details>

### [69] [Synthesis of Bulk Superconducting LiNbO$_2$ Crystals through CaH$_2$ Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06819)
*Ryan Paxson,Stephanie J. Hong,Bicky Moirangthem,Parham Kabirifar,Saya Takeuchi,Tianyu Li,Chih-Yu Lee,Haotong Liang,Keenan Avers,Kamal Joshi,Amlan Datta,Makariy Tanatar,Shanta Saha,Peter Zavalij,Ruslan Prozorov,Alexander J. Grutter,Efrain E. Rodriguez,Ichiro Takeuchi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以LiNbO₃单晶为前驱体，通过CaH₂还原实现块体相变，将Nb价态从5+还原至3+，得到产物LiNbO₂。采用二次离子质谱（SIMS）和X射线光电子能谱（XPS）表征脱锂空穴掺杂；通过隧道二极管谐振器的磁化率和交流磁化率测量确认超导体的块体特性。

Conclusion: 极端氢化物还原是诱导非拓扑路径相变的有效方法，可用于合成具有奇异物性的块体材料。

Abstract: We have synthesized layered superconducting LiNbO$_2$ crystals through a bulk phase transformation from LiNbO$_3$ single crystals via CaH$_2$ reduction. As the Nb valence is reduced from 5+ to 3+, the material undergoes a structural transformation to the resulting product, LiNbO$_2$, which is accompanied by metallic behavior and a superconducting transition, Tc onset, as high as 14.4 K. Secondary ion mass spectroscopy (SIMS) and X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS) show that the resulting phase is hole-doped through de-lithiation during the reduction. Magnetization and AC susceptibility measurements from a tunnel diode resonator confirm the bulk nature of superconductivity with a superconducting volume fraction of approximately 77% and an upper critical field approaching 26 T. Our study demonstrates extreme hydride reduction as an effective method to induce phase transformations with non-topotactic pathways and can be used to synthesize bulk materials with exotic properties.

### [70] [Emergent superconductivity upon disordering a topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07163)
*Carlos Eduardo S. P. Corsino,Hermann Freire,Anurag Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过无符号问题的量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，研究量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（quantum spin Hall insulator）中由杂质诱导的超导增强现象，发现杂质周围的子能级环态（subgap ring states）首先成核 Cooper 配对，进而演变为全局超导相，并指出该机制源于量子几何（quantum geometry）的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在强量子几何体系中，杂质能否通过束缚态促进超导电性的产生，特别是在近平坦能带（nearly flat-band）系统如莫尔材料（moiré materials）中的潜在机制。

Method: 采用无符号问题的量子蒙特卡洛模拟，对具有吸引相互作用的 Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang (BHZ) Hubbard 模型进行研究，在不同杂质密度下扫描相互作用强度，观测量子相变（quantum phase transition）。

Result: 在清洁极限下，系统需超过有限临界 Hubbard 相互作用强度 $\vert U \vert$ 才出现体超导；而强杂质显著降低了触发超导所需的 $\vert U \vert$。Cooper 配对先在杂质周围的子能级环态中成核，随后发展为全局相干超导相。

Conclusion: 杂质生成的束缚态可在强量子几何体系中促进超导电性，该机制对量子几何起主导作用的近平坦带系统（如莫尔材料）具有潜在关联性。

Abstract: We study the emergence of superconductivity in a quantum spin Hall insulator and identify a disorder-driven enhancement of pairing arising from quantum geometry. Using sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo simulations of the attractive Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang (BHZ) Hubbard model, we obtain a quantum phase transition as a function of interaction strength for different impurity densities. In the clean limit, the system develops bulk superconductivity for Hubbard interaction $\vert U \vert$ above a finite critical strength. Interestingly, strong impurities significantly reduce such $\vert U \vert$ required for the onset of superconductivity. Our calculations indicate that Cooper pairing first nucleates in subgap ring states surrounding the impurities and then evolves into a globally coherent superconducting phase. Our results demonstrate that impurity-generated bound states can promote superconductivity in systems with strong quantum geometry. This mechanism is expected to be relevant in nearly flat-band systems like moiré materials where quantum geometry plays a dominant role.

### [71] [Nucleation and Enhancement of Superconductivity under Tip-Induced Strain Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07210)
*Ghulam Mohmad,Vishal Tripathi,Goutam Sheet*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示了点接触下非均匀单轴应力场是针尖诱导/增强超导电性（TISC/TESC）的物理根源，通过赫兹接触力学与金兹堡-朗道变分分析结合，推导出TISC/TESC的成核判据，并为21种材料确定了实验可测的单轴耦合标度$C^{\mathrm{exp}}$。该框架无自由参数地解释了拓扑半金属中的临界温度，并预言了Sb和Y元素中的TISC现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属点接触在非超导或弱超导材料上常会诱导或增强局域超导电性，但该现象缺乏统一的理论描述。本文旨在建立基于应力场不均匀特性的理论框架，解释并预测针尖诱导/增强超导电性（TISC/TESC）。

Method: 将赫兹接触力学（Hertzian contact mechanics）与金兹堡-朗道变分分析（Ginzburg-Landau variational analysis）相结合，推导TISC/TESC的成核判据；通过实验可测的单轴耦合标度$C^{\mathrm{exp}}$来估计应力场与电子结构之间的耦合强度。

Result: 确定了21种材料的$C^{\mathrm{exp}}$值；对于具有无能隙能带交叉（ungapped band crossings）的拓扑半金属（topological semimetals），该框架无自由参数地解释了观测到的临界温度；对于其他材料，$C^{\mathrm{exp}}$提供了单轴应变敏感性的直接实验测定。模型预测在元素Sb和Y中分别存在TISC，临界温度$T_c$分别约为2.8 K和12 K。

Conclusion: 点接触下空间非均匀且以单轴为主的应力场是TISC/TESC的关键物理机制；所建立的框架为理解针尖诱导超导提供了统一的理论基础，并能定量预测新体系中的超导电性。

Abstract: A metallic point contact formed on a non-superconducting or weakly superconducting material often nucleates or enhances superconductivity confined under the contact. However, no unified theoretical description of the phenomenon exists. We show that the spatially inhomogeneous, predominantly uniaxial nature of the stress field under a point contact is fundamental for such tip-induced and tip-enhanced superconductivity (TISC/TESC). We also show that the coupling of such a stress field to the electronic structure can be estimated through an experimentally measurable uniaxial coupling scale $C^{\mathrm{exp}}$. Combining Hertzian contact mechanics with a Ginzburg-Landau variational analysis, we derive a criterion for the nucleation of TISC/TESC and determine $C^{\mathrm{exp}}$ for twenty-one materials. For topological semimetals with ungapped band crossings, the framework explains observed critical temperatures with no free parameters and for all others, $C^{\mathrm{exp}}$ provides a direct experimental determination of the uniaxial strain sensitivity and a target scale for microscopic theories.The work predicts TISC in elemental Sb and Y with $T_c \approx 2.8$\,K and $T_c \approx 12$\,K respectively.

</details>


### [72] [Pressure-induced Structural Phase Transition, Metallization, and Superconductivity in layered metalloid dichalcogenide 1T-SiTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07569)
*Ying-Jie Zhang,Heng Xu,Zhe-Ning Xiang,Zong-Hui Wu,Qing Li,Hai-Hu Wen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告了层状类金属二硫属化物1T-SiTe₂在压力诱导下的结构相变、金属化和超导电性。常压下为半导体，在约6.7 GPa压力下超导电性出现，超导转变温度（Tc）随压力升高持续上升，在30 GPa以上时饱和于约5.5 K。压缩过程中观察到三次结构相变，其相变压力与电阻异常响应高度一致，表明输运行为变化由结构驱动。该工作将过渡金属二硫属化物（TMD）超导体拓展至类金属体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状过渡金属二硫属化物（TMD）作为探索涌现物理和潜在器件应用的平台备受关注，而类金属（metalloid）基二硫属化物却鲜有探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究层状类金属二硫属化物1T-SiTe₂在高压下的结构与输运性质变化。

Method: 采用高压实验手段，对层状类金属二硫属化物1T-SiTe₂施加压力，通过电阻测量和结构表征监测其输运行为与晶体结构随压力的演化。

Result: 常压下1T-SiTe₂为三角晶系半导体；约6.7 GPa时超导电性出现，Tc随压力升高持续上升，30 GPa以上饱和于约5.5 K；压缩过程中经历三次结构相变，相变压力与输运异常高度吻合。

Conclusion: 1T-SiTe₂在压力下呈现结构驱动的超导电性，将TMD超导体拓展至类金属体系，为探索不含过渡金属元素的准二维材料中的新奇物理提供了新平台。

Abstract: Layered transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) have attracted considerable attention as promising platforms for exploring emergent physics and potential device applications. In contrast, metalloid-based dichalcogenide counterparts remain largely underexplored. Here, we report the pressure-induced structural phase transition, metallization, and superconductivity in the layered metalloid dichalcogenide 1T-SiTe$_2$. At ambient pressure, 1T-SiTe$_2$ crystallizes in a trigonal crystal structure (space group: $P\bar{3}m1$) and exhibits intrinsic semiconducting transport characteristics. Upon pressurization, in concomitant with the suppression of semiconducting behavior in resistance, superconductivity emerges at around 6.7 GPa. The superconducting transition temperature (T$_c$) rises continuously with increasing pressure and finally saturates at approximately 5.5 K for pressures above 30 GPa. During the compression, 1T-SiTe$_2$ experiences three structural phase transitions, and the phase transition pressures are highly consistent with the anomalous transport responses observed experimentally, indicating that the changes of transport behavior of 1T-SiTe$_2$ under pressure are structurally-driven. Our work extends TMD superconductors into the realm of metalloid systems and provides a new platform for exploring novel physics in quasi two-dimensional materials without transition-metal elements.

</details>

### [73] [Data Preservation in High Energy Physics: Global Report 2026](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06775)
*Matthew Bellis,Jamie Boyd,Daniel Britzger,Andy Buckley,Chris Burr,Micheal Buchar,Gang Chen,Andrew Chisholm,Jiri Chudoba,Michael Davis,Cristinel Diaconu,David Dobrigkeit Chinellato,Marcus Ebert,Apranik Fatehi,Dillon S. Fitzgerald,Jose Benito Gonzalez Lopez,Richard William Gran,Giovanni Guerrieri,Martin Habedank,Hao Hu,David Horvat,Luka Lambrecht,Clemens Lange,Kati Lassila-Perini,Jerome Lauret,Jean-Yves Le Meur,Dietrich Liko,Panna Liptak,Zach Marshall,Thomas McCauley,Cameron Duncan McClymont,Wesley Middelbos,Micha Moskovic,Piet Nogga,Ryunosuke O'Neil,Stefano Piano,Alan Price,Tomasz Procter,Fazhi Qi,Diana Rand,Hossein Rashidi,Emily Rensch,Pablo Saiz,Ulrich Schwickerath,Tibor Šimko,Andrii Verbytskyi,Dirk Zerwas,Zhengde Zhang,Graham Wilson*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文总结了2026年第五届DPHEP研讨会关于高能物理（HEP）数据保存（data preservation, DP）领域的最新进展，涵盖遗留数据复活、可持续性挑战、跨领域技术创新、人工智能（AI）与机器学习（ML）自动化的兴起，以及开放科学原则（FAIR principles）的广泛采纳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HEP数据保存面临长期资金、基础设施维护和技术更新等可持续性挑战，同时遗留实验数据（legacy data）的再利用价值需要被证实和推广。本文旨在总结DPHEP社区自2024年以来的进展，明确未来里程碑和趋势。

Method: 基于2026年3月5-6日在欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）举行的第五届DPHEP研讨会（5th DPHEP workshop）的贡献进行综述，涵盖遗留数据再分析案例展示、可持续性讨论、跨领域技术方案进展以及开放科学政策分析。

Result: 观察到HEP数据保存的显著进展：遗留数据成功利用当代方法进行再分析，验证了长期科学价值；可持续发展问题被识别，需长期资金与机构支持；横向创新项目持续推进通用可移植DP技术；自动化趋势明显，AI/ML日益用于数据整理、元数据提取和工作流优化；开放科学势头增强，FAIR原则和开放数据政策被更广泛采纳，各实验承诺公开数据发布。

Conclusion: HEP数据保存领域正在稳步推进，主要体现在遗留数据价值验证、可持续性投入、技术自动化转型和开放科学普及四个方面，未来需继续加强长期资金保障和机构协作。

Abstract: This document summarizes the contributions to the 5th DPHEP workshop March 5-6, 2026, CERN, and reflects the advancements since 2024, as well as future milestones and tendencies. Impressive progress in HEP data preservation is observed. Legacy data revival was showcased through successful reanalysis of archived data using contemporary methods, demonstrating the long-term scientific value of preservation. Sustainability challenges were noted, emphasizing the need for long-term funding and institutional support to maintain data preservation infrastructure, particularly for legacy experiments transitioning to archival modes. Innovative transverse projects display constant progress towards common technologies for a robust and transferrable DP. In particular, there is a clear shift toward automation, with increasing use of AI and machine learning for data curation, metadata extraction, and workflow optimization. Open science momentum is growing, with wider adoption of FAIR principles and open data policies, and experiments committing to public releases.

</details>


### [74] [The Dark Photon in the PHELEX Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07074)
*A. V. Kopylov,I. V. Orekhov,V. V. Petukhov,A. E. Solomatin*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: PHELEX实验在2023–2026年间使用多阴极计数器对单电子计数率进行了日间测量，观测结果暗示存在质量在10–40 eV范围内的暗光子（dark photon）。Fe阴极与Al阴极计数率的相关性表明该效应与阴极材料的磁性无关，从而排除了依赖磁矩的暗物质模型。若经独立实验证实，该结果可将候选暗物质范围缩小至主要通过电场（或纵向场）相互作用、对自旋不敏感的类型，而具有动力学混合（kinetic mixing）的暗光子恰好符合这一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质（dark matter）候选粒子，特别是寻找质量在10–40 eV范围内的暗光子（dark photon）的实验证据。

Method: 在PHELEX实验中，使用多阴极计数器（multi-cathode counters）在2023至2026年期间对单电子计数率（single-electron count rate）进行日间（diurnal）测量，并对比Fe阴极与Al阴极的计数率相关性。

Result: 观测到的单电子计数率变化暗示可能存在质量范围为10–40 eV的暗光子效应；Fe与Al阴极计数率的相关性表明该效应与阴极材料的磁性无关。

Conclusion: 该结果对许多依赖磁矩的暗物质模型构成否定论据；若经独立实验验证，可将候选暗物质缩小至主要通过电场（或纵向场）相互作用且对自旋不敏感的类型，而具有动力学混合（kinetic mixing）的暗光子是理想的候选者。

Abstract: This paper presents diurnal measurements of the single-electron count rate in the PHELEX experiment using multi-cathode counters over the period from 2023 to 2026. The results obtained are interpreted as an indication of a possible effect from dark photons with masses ranging from 10 to 40 eV. The correlation of the measured rates in counters with Fe and Al cathodes suggests that the effect does not depend on the magnetic properties of the cathode material. This can be interpreted as an argument against many dark matter models related to magnetic moments. The result, if confirmed in an independent experiment, could narrow the range of possible candidates to those that interact primarily through an electric (or longitudinal) field, insensitive to spin. A dark photon with kinetic mixing fits this description ideally.

</details>

H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器收集的20.3 fb⁻¹数据样本，在6.0σ统计显著性下首次观测到e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻ηJ/ψ过程，并搜寻了Z_c(3900)的同位旋标量伙伴X(3900)，未发现显著信号，给出了截面与分支积的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻ηJ/ψ过程的存在性，并搜寻已知奇特强子态Z_c(3900)的同位旋标量（isoscalar）伙伴X(3900)，以检验强子谱学与奇特态理论。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在质心能量（center-of-mass energy）4.18至4.95 GeV范围内采集的积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为20.3 fb⁻¹的数据，对e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻ηJ/ψ过程进行信号重建与统计显著性分析，并在ηJ/ψ末态中搜索X(3900)信号。

Result: 以包含系统不确定性的6.0σ统计显著性（statistical significance）观测到e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻ηJ/ψ过程；在ηJ/ψ末态中未观察到X(3900)的显著信号。

Conclusion: 实验首次证实了e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻ηJ/ψ过程的存在；未发现Z_c(3900)的同位旋标量伙伴X(3900)，并针对不同质量与宽度假设给出了Born截面（Born cross section）σ^{Born}[e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻X(3900)]与分支比（branching fraction）B[X(3900)→ηJ/ψ]乘积的上限。

Abstract: Using a data sample corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 20.3 fb$^{-1}$ collected at center-of-mass energies from 4.18 to 4.95 GeV with the BESIII detector, we observe the process $e^+e^-\toπ^+π^-ηJ/ψ$ with a statistical significance of $6.0 σ$, including systematic uncertainties. The isoscalar partner of the $Z_c(3900)$, denoted $X(3900)$, is searched for in the $ηJ/ψ$ final state, and no significant signal is observed. The upper limits on the product of the Born cross section $σ^{\rm Born}[e^{+}e^{-}\toπ^{+}π^{-} X(3900)$] and the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}[X(3900)\toηJ/ψ]$ are given with various assumptions for the mass and width of the $X(3900)$.

</details>


### [76] [First Demonstration of a Hybrid Cherenkov and Scintillation Detector in a Proof-of-Principle Axion Search at a Beam Dump](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07476)
*Darcy A. Newmark*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本论文首次在束流倾倒设施（beam dump facility）上展示了混合切伦科夫与闪烁体光学探测器（hybrid Cherenkov and scintillation optical detector），用于对MeV尺度轴子类似粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）进行原理验证型搜索。研究基于Coherent CAPTAIN-Mills (CCM)实验的10吨液态氩探测器，通过波长移植物涂层和2 ns时间分辨能力增强切伦科夫灵敏度，首次实现了亚MeV电子的逐事件切伦科夫-闪烁体分离，并利用机器学习实现位置（~5 cm）与能量（~10% at 1 MeV）重建。结合四种观测量构建似然比检验统计量（likelihood ratio test statistic）抑制稳态本底，未观察到显著超出，但在更小曝光量下以90%置信水平排除了ALP质量-耦合参数空间的新区域，同时探索了液态氩在DUNE超新星中微子物理及下一代大型混合光学探测器中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探测器难以有效区分MeV尺度ALP信号与稳态本底，亟需一种能够在高光产额闪烁体探测器中识别切伦科夫辐射的新型探测方案，以实现对低能弱相互作用粒子的灵敏搜索。

Method: 利用CCM实验10吨液态氩探测器，将80%光电倍增管（PMT）涂覆波长移植物（wavelength-shifting material），保留20%未涂覆，通过波长甄别和2 ns时间分辨能力增强切伦科夫灵敏度。对¹²²Na校准数据进行详细建模，首次全面表征闪烁光与切伦科夫光的产生与传播及其系统不确定性。开发基于机器学习的位置重建（~5 cm分辨率）与能量重建（1 MeV处~10%分辨率）。将切伦科夫时间、波长敏感性、方向性、脉冲形状及事件拓扑结构四种观测量结合为似然比检验统计量，用于抑制≤10 MeV ALP诱发事件的稳态本底。

Result: 未观察到显著信号超出，但在更小曝光量下以90%置信水平（confidence level）排除了相较于先前CCM分析新的ALP质量-耦合参数空间区域。首次实现高光产额闪烁体探测器中亚MeV电子的逐事件切伦科夫辐射分离。

Conclusion: 混合切伦科夫-闪烁体光学探测器（hybrid Cherenkov-scintillation detector）在未来的弱相互作用物理实验中具有重要潜力，液态氩探测器在DUNE超新星中微子物理及下一代大规模混合光学探测器中的应用值得进一步探索。

Abstract: This thesis presents the first demonstration of a hybrid Cherenkov and scintillation optical detector at a beam dump facility for a proof-of-principle search for MeV-scale axion-like particles (ALPs). The work utilizes the Coherent CAPTAIN-Mills (CCM) experiment, a 10-ton liquid argon detector at Los Alamos National Laboratory instrumented with 200 PMTs. Coating 80% of the PMTs with wavelength-shifting material while leaving 20% uncoated enables enhanced Cherenkov sensitivity through wavelength discrimination and 2 ns timing resolution. This work includes detailed modeling of $^{22}$Na calibration data, providing the first comprehensive characterization of scintillation and Cherenkov light production and propagation in such a detector, including systematic uncertainties. Using the same source, it demonstrates the first event-by-event separation of Cherenkov radiation from sub-MeV electrons in a high light-yield scintillation detector. Additionally, this work develops machine learning-based position reconstruction with ~5 cm resolution and energy reconstruction with ~10% resolution at 1 MeV. Four observables exploiting Cherenkov timing, wavelength sensitivity, directionality, pulse shape, and event topology are combined into a likelihood ratio test statistic to suppress steady-state backgrounds for $\leq10$ MeV ALP-induced events. No significant excess is observed. Nevertheless, this improved background rejection excludes new regions of ALP mass-coupling parameter space at the 90% confidence level compared to a previous CCM analysis, despite a smaller exposure. Finally, this thesis explores liquid argon applications to supernova neutrino physics in DUNE and discusses next-generation large-scale hybrid optical detectors. These results demonstrate the potential of hybrid Cherenkov-scintillation detectors for future weakly interacting physics experiments.
