### [77] [Connecting Microseismicity to Lithology via a Model of Slip Avalanches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06886)
*Ethan A. Mullen,Yanbo Wang,Jordan J. Sickle,Frank W. DelRio,Pania Newell,Anastasia G. Ilgen,Karin A. Dahmen*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过一个简单的微力学滑移雪崩模型（micromechanical slip avalanche model），统一描述了从纳米尺度压痕实验到米尺度微地震观测的滑移统计规律，并指出该统计行为仅依赖于少数基本性质，而层状沉积地层中的统计偏差可由有限尺寸与应力积分效应解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对流体注入地壳引发的小型频繁地震，准确预测其大小与时间分布对于非常规油气开采、增强型地热系统（enhanced geothermal systems）及地质碳封存（geologic carbon storage）的安全运行至关重要。

Method: 采用一个描述缓慢变形固体中滑移雪崩的简单微力学模型，将其预测结果与不同尺度（米级微地震观测与纳米至微米级纳米压痕实验）的实验数据进行对比验证。

Result: 来自多种岩性地质盆地的高压流体注入微地震目录以及不同温度与矿物组成页岩的纳米压痕实验，均展现出与模型预测一致的统计规律。层状沉积地层中此前存在争议的统计偏差，可归因于力学弱层面（weak bedding planes）导致的有限尺寸效应与应力积分效应（finite-size and stress-integrative effects）。

Conclusion: 滑移统计规律仅取决于少数基本性质，因而具有跨材料、温度与尺度的普适性（universality）；这些统计规律可提供关于层面结构与尺度的关键信息，反之盆地结构也可用于预测触发微地震事件的尺寸概率分布。

Abstract: Fluid injection into the earth's crust can induce small and frequent earthquakes in the subsurface. Predicting their sizes and temporal occurrences via statistical analysis is crucial for safe operations in unconventional oil and gas recovery, enhanced geothermal systems, and geologic carbon storage. Here we show that a simple micromechanical model of slip avalanches in slowly deforming solids predicts the slip statistics observed over drastically different spatial scales, namely meter-scale microseismic observations and nanometer- to micrometer-scale nanoindentation experiments can be described with this model. Microseismic catalogs extracted from high-pressure fluid injection operations into geological basins with various lithologies and nanoindentation experiments on shale across a wide range of temperatures and mineral compositions yield statistics consistent with model predictions. This universality across materials, temperatures, and scales is consistent with the prediction that the slip statistics result from only a few basic properties. Previously debated deviations of the statistics in layered sedimentary formations are explained by finite-size and stress-integrative effects resulting from mechanically weak bedding planes. The slip statistics therefore provide important information about the structure and scales of the bedding planes. Conversely, the basin structure can also be used to predict the probability distribution for the sizes of triggered microseismic events.

</details>


### [78] [Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya Gradients Unlock Topological Dimensional Reduction in Magnetic Hopfions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07048)
*Kui Yuan,Hailong Shen,Jiawei Dong,Xin Zhang,Longqing Chen,Yihan Wang,Bo Liu,Qing Zhang,Zhengshang Wang,Wenbin Qiu,Xiaoyi Wang,Bing Han,Yang Qiu,Kun Zhang,Xudong Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本研究通过化学非均匀掺杂（chemical inhomogeneity）可控地破坏三维磁孤子（magnetic soliton）的拓扑保护，将类霍普夫子（hopfion-like）环形织构转化为准二维斯格明子弦（skyrmion string）。结合透射电镜与微磁模拟，揭示了均匀与非均匀Y掺杂调控拓扑相变的双重机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维磁孤子的拓扑保护依赖于自旋场的连续性，而化学非均匀性如何打破这种保护并驱动拓扑相变尚不清楚。本文旨在通过可控掺杂揭示这一机制。

Method: 采用倾转依赖洛伦兹透射电镜（tilt-dependent Lorentz transmission electron microscopy）、电子能量损失谱（electron energy-loss spectroscopy）和微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations），分析嵌入FeCrNiMn基体中的原始、均匀Y掺杂与非均匀Y掺杂无序TiO2纳米颗粒。

Result: 均匀Y掺杂富集Ti³⁺/氧空位（oxygen-vacancy）局域中心，稳定具有霍普夫不变量（Hopf invariant）Q_H ≈ 1的闭合环；非均匀Y掺杂形成Ti⁴⁺富集、空位贫化的边界，产生尖锐的q=D/(2A)梯度和弱磁矩泄漏通道（weak-moment leakage channel），耦合的失配力矩（mismatch torque）与连续性泄漏将环分裂，留下斯格明子弦残骸和场敏感螺旋织构。

Conclusion: 化学非均匀性可作为一种可控手段，通过调节掺杂分布来破坏三维拓扑保护、实现拓扑织构的维度降级（hopfion→skyrmion string），为拓扑自旋电子学（topological spintronics）中的人造拓扑相变提供新路径。

Abstract: Three-dimensional magnetic solitons retain topological protection only while their spin field remains continuous. Here we show that chemical inhomogeneity can break this protection in a controlled way, converting a hopfion-like toroidal texture into an effectively two-dimensional skyrmion string. Tilt-dependent Lorentz transmission electron microscopy, electron energy-loss spectroscopy, and micromagnetic simulations of pristine, uniformly Y-doped, and nonuniformly Y-doped disordered TiO2 nanoparticles embedded in a FeCrNiMn host reveal two regimes. Uniform Y doping enriches Ti3+/oxygen-vacancy localization centers and stabilizes closed rings with Hopf invariant QH approximately 1. Nonuniform Y doping forms a Ti4+-rich, vacancy-depleted boundary that creates a sharp q=D/(2A) gradient and a weak-moment leakage channel. This coupled mismatch torque and continuity leakage split the ring, leaving a skyrmion-string remnant and a field-sensitive helicity texture.

</details>


### [79] [Thermal-response Functions and the Peierls-Boltzmann Equation for Second Sound and Phonon Hydrodynamics in Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07644)
*Antonio Martinez-Margolles,Patrick K. Schelling*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过求解弛豫时间近似（relaxation-time approximation, RTA）下的佩尔斯-玻尔兹曼方程（Peierls-Boltzmann equation, PBE），建立了声子相空间分布函数与热波演化的微观物理联系，并基于密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）计算发展出热响应函数，揭示了第二声（second sound）传播的条件，进而讨论了超越RTA的多体理论扩展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将声子相空间分布函数的表达式与热波演化的微观物理联系起来，并系统探讨瞬态热光栅（transient thermal grating, TTG）实验中周期性热源引起的干涉效应对声子分布的影响。

Method: 在弛豫时间近似（RTA）下求解佩尔斯-玻尔兹曼方程（PBE），并基于密度泛函理论（DFT）计算数据发展热响应函数。

Result: 展示了PBE的解如何与第二声（second sound）作为元激发的传播相联系，阐明了第二声传播和观测的必要条件；揭示了在较短长度尺度下干涉和声子退相干效应的重要性。

Conclusion: 所发展的方法表明，声子流体动力学和第二声的PBE理论可以被修正以恰当描述干涉与退相干效应；同时，多体理论可通过包含耦合散射通道而扩展，从而提供超越RTA的定量理论。

Abstract: We connect expressions for phonon phase-space distribution functions to microscopic physics of the evolution of heat waves. The role of interference effects that arise as a result of a periodic heating source typically encountered in transient thermal grating (TTG) experiments is then explored. The distribution functions are evaluated as solutions to the Peierls-Boltzmann equation (PBE) in the relaxation-time approximation (RTA). Starting from the PBE, we next develop thermal response functions. The response functions are computed using data from density-functional theory (DFT) calculations. Using this approach, it is shown how solutions to the PBE can be related to the propagation of second phonons as elementary excitations, and within this perspective the necessary conditions for the propagation and observation of second sound is elucidated. The approach developed therefore shows how PBE theory for phonon hydrodynamics and second sound can be modified to properly describe interference and phonon decoherence effects that are likely important at shorter length scales. Finally, we then discuss how many-body theory can be extended to include coupled scattering channels and hence provide a quantitative theory beyond the RTA.

### [80] [Relativistic Common-envelope Dynamics of a Stellar-mass Black Hole II: Kerr Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07462)
*Alejandro Cruz-Osorio,Fabio D. Lora-Clavijo*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过简化二维模拟，研究了恒星质量黑洞与红超巨星包层在共有包层（common envelope）阶段中的相互作用，重点考察质量吸积率、动量吸积率随马赫数（Mach number）和密度梯度的变化，并与经典 Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton 吸积理论进行对比，最终给出了包含黑洞自旋、密度梯度和马赫数在内的吸积率及轫致辐射光度的解析拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共有包层阶段对双星系统演化至关重要，但其中黑洞与恒星包层相互作用的吸积特性尚缺乏系统数值研究，尤其是考虑密度梯度和自旋效应的广义相对论流体动力学建模仍属空白。

Method: 采用简化二维流体动力学模拟，在不同马赫数和密度梯度条件下，模拟恒星质量黑洞穿越红超巨星包层的过程，测量质量吸积率和动量吸积率，并与 Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton 吸积分析结果进行对比。

Result: 模拟结果与经典 Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton 吸积分析一致，观察到下游激波锥（shock cone）形成、特定构型下的弓形激波（bow shocks）以及激波流中的亚声速区；当共有包层中存在显著压力梯度时激波锥被拖曳，高自旋情况下黑洞附近出现额外拖曳。

Conclusion: 提供了关于质量吸积率、动量吸积率以及轫致辐射（bremsstrahlung）光度的解析拟合公式，建立了黑洞自旋、密度梯度和马赫数之间的函数关系，为共有包层阶段长期演化的广义相对论流体动力学建模提供了初步认识。

Abstract: The common envelope phase plays a critical role in binary system evolution. In this study, we investigate the mass and momentum accretion rates during the interaction between a stellar mass black hole and the envelope of a red supergiant using simplified two dimensional simulations. We explore various Mach numbers and density gradients, finding that our simulations align with previous Bondi Hoyle Lyttleton accretion analyses. We observe the formation of a shock cone in the downstream flow, bow shocks in specific configurations, and subsonic regions within shocked flows. The shock cone is dragged when significant pressure gradients are present in the common envelope, with additional dragging near the black hole for highly rotating cases. We provide analytical fits for mass and momentum accretion rates, as well as bremsstrahlung luminosity, as functions of black hole spin, density gradients, and Mach number, offering first insights into general relativistic hydrodynamics modelling of the secular evolution of the common envelope phase.

</details>


### [81] [Population statistics of nanohertz gravitational wave sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07477)
*Jiming Yu,Zhen Pan,Xiao Xue,Liang Dai*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文针对脉冲星计时阵（pulsar timing arrays, PTA）探测到的纳赫兹引力波背景（gravitational wave background）的起源争议，提出了一个层次化贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）框架，能够利用非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）信息区分引力波背景来自超大数据质量黑洞双星（supermassive black hole binaries, SMBHBs）还是原初过程，并同时推断SMBHB的种群性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PTA近期探测到纳赫兹引力波背景，但其起源——来自天体物理的SMBHB还是早期宇宙的原初引力波——尚不明确。先前研究表明，在探测到任何单个源之前，引力波背景的非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）是区分这两种起源的关键判据。

Method: 本文提出一个层次化贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）框架，通过最优利用单个明亮源中的非高斯信息以及引力波背景功率谱波动（power spectrum fluctuations）中的非高斯信息，对引力波源的种群性质进行推断。

Result: 该框架不仅能利用PTA数据衡量不同引力波起源的证据，还能推断天体物理SMBHB的种群性质。

Conclusion: 所提出的层次化贝叶斯推断方法为利用非高斯性区分引力波背景起源提供了一种系统性手段，并能够同时约束SMBHB的种群参数。

Abstract: The recent detection of a nanohertz gravitational wave (GW) background by pulsar timing arrays (PTA) has sparked extensive discussions regarding its origin-whether it arises from astrophysical supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs) or from primordial GWs generated by various early universe processes. Previous studies suggest that a key discriminant between these two origins is the non-Gaussianity of the GW background prior to the detection of any individual source. In this Letter, we introduce a hierarchical Bayesian inference framework for inferring population properties of GW sources. This approach enables not only the measurement of evidence for different GW origins using PTA data but also the inference of population properties of astrophysical SMBHBs, by optimally leveraging non-Gaussian information in individual bright sources and in power spectrum fluctuations of the GW background.

</details>


### [82] [Subsolar-mass binary mergers of strange stars and neutron stars: gravitational waves and ejecta](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07668)
*Yong Gao,Ming-Zhe Han,Kenta Kiuchi,Masaru Shibata,Enping Zhou,Kenta Hotokezaka*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文首次对亚太阳质量双奇异星（strange star, SS）并合进行了数值相对论模拟，并与双中子星（neutron star, NS）并合进行了对比。研究发现SS的自束缚性质使其在旋近阶段形变更小、表面更锐利，导致更强的激波加热和径向反弹，从而在接触前达到更高的引力波截断频率（cutoff frequency, $f_\mathrm{cut}$），但并合后峰值频率（$f_2$）更低。两类并合的频率比 $f_2/f_\mathrm{cut}$ 可清晰区分SS与NS事件，且均可抛射约 $10^{-2}\,M_\odot$ 的物质，可能产生可观测的电磁对应体，从而检验亚太阳质量事件的SS或NS起源假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对亚太阳质量致密双星并合的研究主要集中在双中子星，而对奇异星（一种完全由奇异夸克物质组成的致密天体）并合的数值相对论模拟尚属空白。本文旨在填补这一空缺，通过首次模拟双奇异星并合，比较其与双中子星并合的引力波特征和物质抛射行为，为区分两类天体提供理论依据。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical-relativity）模拟方法，对亚太阳质量双奇异星并合进行首次模拟。研究涵盖了不同物态方程（equations of state）、质量及质量比下的双奇异星并合，并与对应的双中子星并合进行系统对比。

Result: 奇异星的自束缚性使其在旋近过程中形变更小，表面保持锐利直至接触，从而驱动远强于中子星的激波加热和径向反弹。因此，奇异星在接触前达到更高的引力波截断频率 $f_\mathrm{cut}$，但并合后峰值频率 $f_2$ 较低。两类天体的 $f_\mathrm{cut}$ 和 $f_2$ 均与潮汐形变参数（tidal deformability）存在准普适关系（quasi-universal relations），且频率比 $f_2/f_\mathrm{cut}$ 能清晰区分两类事件。两类并合均可抛射约 $10^{-2}\,M_\odot$ 的物质：中子星抛射富中子物质，奇异星抛射解压缩夸克物质（decompressed quark matter）。

Conclusion: 双奇异星并合与双中子星并合在引力波特征和抛射物性质上存在显著差异，其频率比 $f_2/f_\mathrm{cut}$ 可作为区分两类天体的有效观测诊断。两类并合抛射的物质均可产生电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart），未来对亚太阳质量致密双星并合事件的观测有望检验其究竟是奇异星还是中子星。

Abstract: We present the first numerical-relativity simulations of subsolar-mass binary strange star (SS) mergers and compare with binary neutron star (NS) mergers across equations of state, masses, and mass ratios. The self-bound nature of SSs makes them less deformed during the inspiral and keeps a sharp surface up to contact, driving strong shock heating and a large radial bounce that are far weaker in the NS. The more compact SS thus reaches a higher gravitational-wave cutoff frequency $f_\mathrm{cut}$ before contact but a lower post-merger peak frequency $f_2$. Within each class these frequencies follow quasi-universal relations with the tidal deformability, and their ratio $f_2/f_\mathrm{cut}$ cleanly separates the two classes. Both classes can eject $\sim10^{-2}\,M_\odot$ of material, neutron-rich for the NS and decompressed quark matter for the SS, a potential source of an electromagnetic counterpart whose observation could test the SS and NS hypotheses for subsolar-mass events.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文对正交辛李超代数（orthosymplectic Lie superalgebras）上的Segal-Sugawara向量进行了计算，包括其在Harish-Chandra同态下的像、相关联的Sugawara算子和Casimir元素，并进一步构造了高阶Gaudin哈密顿量和量子平移参数子代数（quantum shift-of-argument subalgebras）中的元素。附录回顾了广义线性李超代数（general linear Lie superalgebras）的类似结果。

Method: 通过Harish-Chandra同态（Harish-Chandra homomorphism）计算Segal-Sugawara向量的像，并将该计算推广至相关的Sugawara算子和Casimir元素；利用构造结果进一步产生高阶Gaudin哈密顿量（higher Gaudin Hamiltonians）和量子平移参数子代数中的元素。

Conclusion: 本研究将Segal-Sugawara向量的相关分析从广义线性李超代数扩展至正交辛情形，为李超代数表示论和量子可积系统提供了新的代数构造工具。

Abstract: We consider the recently constructed Segal--Sugawara vectors for the orthosymplectic Lie superalgebras. We calculate their images with respect to the Harish-Chandra homomorphism and extend this calculation to the associated Sugawara operators and Casimir elements. We also produce higher Gaudin Hamiltonians and elements of the quantum shift-of-argument subalgebras in the orthosymplectic enveloping algebra. In the Appendix, we review analogous results for the general linear Lie superalgebras.

### [84] [Athinization of irreducible $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$-modules with dominant highest weights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07653)
*Mikhail Bershtein,Evgeny Mukhin,Leonid Rybnikov,Aleksandr Trufanov*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文通过将仿射李代数 $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ 的 generic Verma 模视为仿射杨代数 $Y(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_n)$ 上的 thin 模，利用周期 Gelfand-Tsetlin 模式实现其基，并引入“thinization”构造将不可约模实现为更大代数上的 thin 模，进而得到 admissible 表示的新组合基与特征标公式，并推广到量子仿射代数量子环面代数情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为仿射李代数 $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ 的 admissible 表示（Kac-Wakimoto 意义下）提供显式的 Gelfand-Tsetlin 型基，建立这类表示的新组合实现，并将特征标公式与 $A_n$ 型 $W$-代数 minimal 模型的主流特化结果进行对比。

Method: 将 $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ 的 generic Verma 模视为仿射杨代数 $Y(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_n)$ 上的 thin 模，利用周期 Gelfand-Tsetlin 模式给出 Yangian 作用的显式公式，并将其与 Kodera 引入的 evaluation 模等同。通过“thinization”过程，将一般 dominant 最高权情形下的不可约模实现为 $Y(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_n)$ 上的 thin 模，这对应于在周期 Gelfand-Tsetlin 基中限制到允许模式子集。

Result: 建立了从 generic 最高权到 dominant 最高权（不必是整型）的特化，得到 thinization 构造；证明了允许模式的线性张成空间具有良定义的仿射杨代数作用，从而给出 $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ 的 admissible 表示的显式 Gelfand-Tsetlin 型基与特征标公式；并将该特征标与 $A_n$ 型 $W$-代数 minimal 模型的主流特化特征标进行对比；进一步将类似结果推广到量子环面代数上的 $U_q\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ 表示。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 thinization 构造为仿射李代数及其量子化表示提供了一种统一的组合框架，通过将非 thin 模嵌入更大代数上的 thin 模，揭示了 admissible 表示与仿射杨代数（affine Yangian）及量子环面代数（quantum toroidal algebra）之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We study the Gelfand-Tsetlin realization of generic Verma modules for the affine Lie algebra $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ by viewing them as thin modules over the affine Yangian $Y(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_n)$. By results of arXiv:0812.4656, these modules admit a basis indexed by periodic Gelfand-Tsetlin patterns with explicit formulas for the Yangian action, and we identify them with the evaluation modules introduced by Kodera arXiv:1806.09884.
  Our main result describes the specialization from generic highest weights to dominant highest weights (not necessarily integral). We call the resulting construction athinization: an irreducible $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$-module, which is not thin as a module over the affine Kac-Moody algebra, is realized as a thin module over the larger (and ''more affine'') algebra $Y(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_n)$. Combinatorially, this realization is obtained by restricting the generic periodic Gelfand-Tsetlin basis to a distinguished subset of permitted patterns. We prove that the span of these patterns carries a well-defined affine Yangian action.
  In particular, this construction yields explicit Gelfand-Tsetlin-type bases for admissible representations of $\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ in the sense of Kac-Wakimoto, providing a new combinatorial realization of these modules. We compare the formulas for characters coming from this combinatorics with those for minimal models of $W$-algebras of the type $A_n$ via the principal specialization.
  Further, we obtain analogous results for representations of $U_q\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}_n$ via their realization as thin modules over the quantum toroidal algebra of $\mathfrak{gl}_n$.

### [85] [Fingerprint, Not Blueprint: How Positional Schemes Set the Default Spectral Algebra of Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06621)
*Li Hengyu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从非厄米矩阵（non-Hermitian matrix）与随机矩阵（random matrix）视角系统分析了注意力头中QK双线性形式的谱结构，在静态、动态和因果三个层面揭示了位置编码方案（positional scheme）如何塑造注意力头的默认谱代数（spectral algebra），并证明该谱特征是在功能形成后固化的指纹（fingerprint），而非功能的必要先决条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 注意力头中pre-softmax得分是双线性形式 $x_i^T M x_j$，其中算子 $M = W_q^T W_k$ 通常是非对称（non-symmetric）且非正规（non-normal）的，其复本征谱和非正交本征向量落在非厄米与随机矩阵理论的适用范围。现有研究缺乏对这一谱结构的系统性理解，本文旨在揭示该谱在不同层次（静态、动态、因果）上编码的信息，及其与位置编码方案的关系。

Method: 在静态层面，对七种预训练模型（覆盖三种位置编码方案）进行分析，利用谱旋转（spectral rotation）特性区分previous-token heads；在动态层面，跟踪Pythia公开检查点（checkpoints），将每个注意力头的谱演化与随机矩阵空（Ginibre null）进行对比；在因果层面，通过约束两层的玩具模型训练，系统性禁止各谱通道（spectral channel）并观察功能保留情况。

Result: 静态结果表明：RoPE下的previous-token heads呈现谱旋转特征，而学习型绝对位置（learned-absolute）和ALiBi则呈现非旋转的内容型（content-like）特征，模型层级的区分在每一top-k下都完全可分（精确排列检验 $p=0.029$），且置零RoPE的每频率相位 $Im(M_t)$ 可消除已识别的induction head功能。动态结果表明：每个注意力头起源于随机矩阵（Ginibre）空；旋转特征随行为同步涌现而非提前出现，种群中位数的压制（suppression）在电路形成后发生，因此谱特征是固化的指纹（fingerprint）而非前兆。因果结果表明：无任何谱通道是必要的；禁止任意通道后能力保持完整，但存在显著的延迟（四个预先登记的对比，$q_{BH} \le 0.016$）。额外揭示：强制对称性使learned-absolute模型变慢2.9倍，而RoPE头即使静态M完全对称，仍可通过相位通道实现方向性路由。

Conclusion: 在所考察的设置中，位置编码方案设定了注意力头解的默认谱代数（spectral algebra）；该谱特征是在功能形成后被塑造的指纹，而非对功能施加的硬约束（hard constraint）。

Abstract: The pre-softmax score of an attention head is a bilinear form $score(i,j) = x_i^T M x_j$ in a learned operator $M = W_q^T W_k$. Because M is generally non-symmetric, hence non-normal, it has a complex eigenspectrum and non-orthogonal eigenvectors, the regime where non-Hermitian and random-matrix tools apply. We ask what this spectrum encodes, at three levels for previous-token and induction circuits. Statically, across seven pretrained models spanning three positional schemes, the strongest previous-token heads are spectrally rotational under RoPE and non-rotational, or content-like, where position enters outside QK (learned-absolute and ALiBi); the model-level separation is perfect at every top-k examined (exact permutation $p=0.029$), and zeroing the per-frequency RoPE phase $Im(M_t)$ eliminates induction on a pre-identified previous-token head in all three RoPE models. Dynamically, over public Pythia checkpoints every head originates at the random-matrix (Ginibre) null; the rotational signature emerges with the behavior, not before it, and the population-median suppression that yields the final profile follows circuit formation, so the profile is a consolidated fingerprint, not a precursor. Causally, and at toy scale, no spectral channel is necessary: constrained two-layer training reroutes around every ban with capability intact, albeit at a significant formation delay (four pre-registered contrasts, $q_BH <= 0.016$). The cost structure exposes each scheme's default: imposing symmetry slows learned-absolute models by a factor of 2.9, whereas a RoPE head with a fully symmetric static M still routes directionally via the phase channel, impossible under absolute positions. Within the settings examined, the positional scheme sets the default spectral algebra of an attention head's solution: a fingerprint sculpted after function, not a hard constraint upon it.

### [86] [Reconnection diagnostics for vortex tangles in Bose-condensed and superfluid dark matter halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07121)
*Kazım Yavuz Ekşi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文结合格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基（Gross-Pitaevskii）重连定律和薛定谔-泊松（Schrödinger-Poisson）模拟标定的涡旋线密度，分析了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）暗物质或超流暗物质（SFDM）晕中涡旋重连将动能转化为暗声子、密度波、开尔文波和涡旋环的微观通道，并评估了其对晕核演化的动力学重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超流暗物质（SFDM）晕中的相干波状核心可能包含量子化涡旋，涡旋重连可能为晕核演化提供微观能量耗散通道，但该通道的动力学重要性尚未被定量评估。

Method: 将局域的格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基（Gross-Pitaevskii）涡旋重连定律与基于薛定谔-泊松（Schrödinger-Poisson）模拟校准的晕尺度涡旋线密度相结合，构建最小模型来估计重连释放的能量。

Conclusion: 涡旋重连为SFDM晕核演化提供了微观能量传输通道，但仅凭暗物质内部过程不足以产生标准模型可观测信号，需引入超出最小模型的暗物质-标准模型耦合。

Abstract: Bose-Einstein-condensed (BEC) and superfluid dark-matter (SFDM) halos can contain coherent, wave-supported cores whose angular momentum is carried by quantized vortices. When vortices form a tangle, reconnections convert part of the vortex kinetic energy into dark phonons, density waves, Kelvin waves, and vortex loops, providing a microscopic channel by which SFDM vortex structure can affect halo-core evolution. We estimate the dynamical importance of this channel by combining the local Gross-Pitaevskii reconnection law with a halo-scale vortex-line density calibrated against Schrödinger-Poisson simulations. In the minimal model the released energy stays in the dark sector, and standard-model luminosity requires additional portal physics.

### [87] [Scalar-Wave Dispersion in Vectorial Photonic Crystals via Site-Adapted p Orbitals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07224)
*Yan-Long Chen,Kin Hung Fung,C. T. Chan,Qinghua Guo*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文证明，通过位点自适应p轨道可以在三维光子晶体中实现标量波色散，其能带表示在单维特征扭转（one-dimensional character twist）下与标量基本能带表示同构，从而保留了对称性强制简并（symmetry-enforced degeneracies）和相容关系（compatibility relations）。实验上，该机制在三维光子超晶体（photonic meta-crystals）中得到验证，为从矢量光子自由度到标量能带工程（scalar band engineering）提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电磁波本质上是矢量波，需要通过偏振（polarization）描述；而三维空间中横向性约束（transversality constraint）导致在Γ点无法建立全局光滑的横向偏振框架，这看似排除了三维光子晶体（photonic crystals）具有简单标量能带结构的可能性。作者旨在寻找一种在三维体系中实现标量波色散的可行方案。

Method: 作者提出使用位点自适应的p轨道（site-adapted p-orbitals）来构建能带表示，该表示在单维特征扭转下与标量基本能带表示（scalar elementary band representation）同构。实验上，在三维光子超晶体中通过根据对称性逐位点调整局部p轨道轴来实现这一构造。

Result: 该构造不同于固定偏振约化（如二维情形），在保持位点偏振纹理（site-polarization textures）的同时，支持每格点一个振幅的标量网络（scalar network）。实验在三维光子超晶体中成功验证了该机制。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一条从矢量光子自由度通向标量能带工程的路径，使得偏振可作为主动设计参数（active design knob）加以利用。

Abstract: Electromagnetic waves are intrinsically vectorial and require description via polarization, unlike scalar fields such as acoustic pressure or electronic wavefunctions. In three dimensions, the transversality constraint further prevents any globally smooth transverse-polarization frame at the $Γ$ point, which would apparently rule out a simple scalar band structure for three-dimensional (3D) photonic crystals. We show here that site-adapted $p$-orbitals can realize scalar-wave dispersion: the induced band representation is isomorphic to the scalar elementary band representation up to a one-dimensional character twist, so the symmetry-enforced degeneracies and compatibility relations are the same. We demonstrate this mechanism experimentally in 3D photonic meta-crystals, where the local $p$-orbital axes adapt from site to site according to symmetry. In contrast to a fixed-polarization reduction (e.g., in 2D), our construction preserves site-polarization textures while simultaneously supporting a scalar network with one amplitude per site. Thus, it offers a pathway from vectorial photonic degrees of freedom to scalar band engineering, keeping polarization as an active design knob.

</details>


### [88] [Rayleigh Bound States in the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07228)
*Ilya Karavaev,Mingzhao Song,Andrey Bogdanov*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文预测了一类在非亚波长周期性超表面中出现的连续谱束缚态（Rayleigh BICs），它们精确产生于瑞利异常（Rayleigh anomalies）处，即衍射通道开启的临界点。Rayleigh BICs 在多个衍射通道开启时仍保持非辐射特性，其形成源于集体晶格共振（collective lattice resonances）、瑞利异常与超原子（metaatoms）环形偶极态（anapole states）的相互作用，并展现出独特的品质因子立方标度律（$Q \propto 1/k^3$），为超越亚波长区设计超表面非辐射态提供了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统对称保护型（symmetry-protected）和偶然型（accidental）连续谱束缚态通常只能在亚波长区（subwavelength regime）内、仅有少数几个辐射通道（radiation channels）的条件下实现。本文的动机在于突破这一限制，在非亚波长区、多衍射通道开启的情形下构造并理解连续谱束缚态（bound states in the continuum, BICs）。

Method: 作者通过理论分析，揭示了Rayleigh BICs 精确出现在瑞利异常（Rayleigh anomalies）处——即衍射通道（diffraction channels）开启的临界波矢位置。其形成机制来自集体晶格共振（collective lattice resonances）、瑞利异常与超原子（metaatoms）的环形偶极态（anapole states）三者之间的协同相互作用。

Result: Rayleigh BICs 在倒空间（reciprocal space）中展现出独特的品质因子立方标度律（$Q \propto 1/k^3$），这与对称保护型或偶然型BICs的标度行为截然不同。此外，即使在多个衍射通道开启的情况下，Rayleigh BICs 仍能保持非辐射状态（nonradiating state），远超出亚波长区的传统限制。

Conclusion: 这些发现建立了一条在超表面（metasurface）中超越亚波长区、构造非辐射态（nonradiating states）的工程化路径，为设计具有高Q值、多通道非辐射特性的光学器件提供了新的理论基础。

Abstract: We predict a class of bound states in the continuum (BICs) in non-subwavelength periodic metasurfaces -- Rayleigh BICs -- that emerge precisely at Rayleigh anomalies, where diffraction channels open. In contrast to conventional symmetry-protected and accidental BICs, which are typically engineered in the subwavelength regime with only a few radiation channels, Rayleigh BICs remain nonradiating far beyond this limit, even when multiple diffraction channels are open. Their formation originates from the interplay between collective lattice resonances, Rayleigh anomalies, and anapole states of the constituent metaatoms. We show that Rayleigh BICs are characterized by an unusual cubic scaling of the quality factor in reciprocal space, ($Q \propto 1/k^3$), an asymptotic behavior that is not characteristic of either symmetry-protected or accidental BICs. Our results establish a constructive route for engineering nonradiating states in metasurfaces beyond the subwavelength regime.

</details>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [Local Markov Order and Global Inference in Many-Body Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06689)
*Thomas Iadecola*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究经典随机过程（对称排斥过程）中守恒荷如何影响观测者的记忆效应，发现测量记录的马可夫化（Markovianization）时间尺度取决于观测者对全局电荷（总粒子数）的认知程度，并存在由体测量驱动的电荷可学习性相变（charge-learnability transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解守恒荷（conserved charge）在经典随机过程中对观测者记忆效应的影响，特别是全局电荷已知与否如何改变测量记录的时间关联特性。

Method: 以对称排斥过程（symmetric exclusion process, SEP）为模型，考虑观测者持续测量单个格点，分析测量记录的马可夫性（Markovianity）；通过引入体测量（bulk measurements）来研究全局电荷的可学习性及其对记忆时间尺度的影响。

Result: 观测者测量记录的马可夫化时间尺度依赖于其对全局电荷（总粒子数）的认知程度；当全局电荷先验未知时，马可夫化时间尺度受到从测量记录中学习该电荷所需时间的约束。体测量的加入会引发电荷可学习性相变，区分电荷模糊相（charge-fuzzy phase）与电荷清晰相（charge-sharp phase）。记忆时间尺度追踪可学习性时间尺度：在模糊相中发散，在清晰相中保持有限。

Conclusion: 全局电荷的可学习性决定了观测者测量记录的记忆时间尺度，电荷可学习性相变标志着记忆效应的根本性改变。

Abstract: We consider how the presence of conserved charges affects memory in a classical stochastic process, the symmetric exclusion process, with an observer constantly measuring a single site. We find that the observer's measurement record becomes Markovian (i.e., loses memory) on a timescale that depends on their knowledge of the global charge, namely the total particle number. In particular, when the global charge is unknown a priori, the observer's time series Markovianizes on a timescale constrained by their ability to learn it from their measurement record. Augmenting the observer's record with bulk measurements drives a charge-learnability transition between charge-fuzzy and -sharp phases. We show that the memory timescale tracks the learnability timescale, diverging in the fuzzy phase and remaining finite in the sharp phase.

</details>


### [90] [Microscopic Dynamical Entropy I: Quantifying Hamiltonian Irreversibility in Large and Small Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06787)
*Mingnan Ding,Michael E. Cates*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian systems）提出了一种微观动力学熵（Microscopic Dynamical Entropy, MDE），它是基于系统X与环境Y之间自由度划分的条件相空间体积（conditional phase-space volume）构建的熵泛函。MDE仅依赖于边缘分布ρ_X(t)，能够在不引入近似动力学的情况下恢复热力学熵的微观起源，包括dS = dQ/T关系、不可逆弛豫以及瞬态熵减行为，并在时间尺度分离下严格单调增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热力学熵的微观起源尚不清晰，尤其是在精确哈密顿动力学（Hamiltonian dynamics）框架下，如何从微观可逆运动中涌现出宏观不可逆熵增行为。本文旨在构造一个仅依赖于系统边缘分布的熵泛函，在保留精确动力学的同时解释热力学熵的微观基础。

Method: 将哈密顿系统的自由度划分为系统X和环境Y，基于未监测自由度Y的条件相空间体积（即条件玻尔兹曼熵）构造微观动力学熵（MDE）。该熵定义为从联合XY系统的吉布斯熵（Gibbs entropy）中丢弃与Y相关的条件微观信息后得到的熵泛函，仅依赖于系统X的边缘分布ρ_X(t)。

Result: MDE能够恢复热力学基本关系dS = dQ/t，将熵增与系统和环境之间的热流联系起来。在X与Y之间存在时间尺度分离时，MDE严格单调增长，恢复不可逆热力学的标准结构。即使在仅含N=10个粒子的孤立小系统中，若X为质心等适当选定的自由度子集，MDE在弛豫过程中仍表现出朝向平衡态的单调增长行为，且随着N增大单调性增强。

Conclusion: 微观动力学熵（MDE）为精确哈密顿动力学框架下的非平衡热力学熵及其时间依赖性提供了一种微观解释，揭示了热力学第二定律的微观起源。

Abstract: We introduce a Microscopic Dynamical Entropy (MDE) for Hamiltonian systems, defined with respect to a chosen partition of degrees of freedom into a system X and its environment Y. The construction is based on the conditional phase-space volume (CPV), or conditional Boltzmann entropy, associated with the unmonitored degrees of freedom Y. The MDE is a microscopically defined entropy functional of the marginal distribution $ρ_X(t)$, obtained by discarding conditional microscopic information associated with Y from the Gibbs entropy of the joint XY system, while retaining exact Hamiltonian dynamics. This construction clarifies the microscopic origin of thermal entropy. The dependence of MDE solely on $ρ_X(t)$ is consistent with the thermodynamic assumption that the entropy increment of a heat bath Y depends on its heat content and temperature, not on details of its probability distribution. Indeed, the MDE recovers dS = dQ/T connecting entropy increments to heat flow between system and environment. More generally, it provides a consistent description of irreversible relaxation under exact Hamiltonian dynamics, while permitting transient entropy decreases in small systems and in spin-echo type protocols. Under time-scale separation between X and Y, the MDE becomes strictly monotonic in time, recovering the familiar structure of irreversible thermodynamics. The MDE can foreshadow thermodynamics even in a small isolated Hamiltonian system, if X is a well chosen subset of its degrees of freedom. An example is the centre of mass of interacting particles confined to a box. Even for as few as N=10 particles, the MDE increases during relaxation towards a maximum at equilibrium, with increasing monotonicity at larger N. Taken together, our results show that the MDE offers a microscopic interpretation of nonequilibrium thermal entropy and its time dependence within exact Hamiltonian dynamics.

</details>


### [91] [Taming nonlinear energy diffusion: The case of time-crystal energy condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07325)
*P. I. Hurtado,G. Cortés-Guillén*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种Kipnis-Marchioro-Presutti随机能量扩散模型的体驱动非线性变体，通过局部碰撞偏置诱导净能流。从微观主方程出发，在局部平衡近似下推导了流体力学描述，获得了能量流、扩散率及迁移率等输运系数的显式表达式。动力学蒙特卡洛模拟验证了理论结果，并展示了该驱动机制可通过诱导时间晶相控制非线性能量输运，尤其是设计了适当的堆积场（packing fields）可自发形成行波能量凝聚体，呈现类连续时间晶体（time crystals）的鲁棒长程时间序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机能量扩散模型（如Kipnis-Marchioro-Presutti模型）通常缺乏对体驱动效应的系统描述，尤其是非线性输运机制及其可控性尚不明确。该研究旨在建立从微观动力学到宏观输运的理论框架，并探索利用体驱动诱导时空有序相（如时间晶体）的可能性。

Method: 从微观主方程（master equation）出发，采用局部平衡近似（local equilibrium approximation）推导流体力学（hydrodynamic）描述；通过解析计算获得能量流、扩散率（diffusivity）及迁移率（mobility）等非线性输运系数的显式表达式；利用动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo, kMC）模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 解析推导给出了体驱动非线性模型中输运系数的显式表达式；模拟结果与理论预测一致；通过设计适当的堆积场（packing fields），成功诱导出行波能量凝聚体（traveling energy condensates），呈现长程时间序，其行为与连续时间晶体（continuous time crystals）类似。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个简单而强大的框架，用于研究随机多体系统中的体驱动非线性能量扩散，连接了微观动力学、宏观输运与可控时空有序。研究成果展示了通过体驱动机制调控非线性能量输运并诱导时间晶相的可行性。

Abstract: We study a bulk-driven nonlinear variant of the Kipnis-Marchioro-Presutti model of stochastic energy diffusion in which local collisions are biased to induce a net energy flow, resembling the effect of an external field. Starting from the microscopic master equation, we derive the hydrodynamic description of the driven system via a local equilibrium approximation, obtaining explicit expressions for the energy current and the associated diffusivity and mobility transport coefficients, which are nonlinear functions of the local energy density. We test our findings in kinetic Monte Carlo simulations of the model and, as a proof of concept, we demonstrate the versatility of this driving mechanism to control nonlinear energy transport by inducing time-crystalline phases. In particular, we show that appropriately designed packing fields induce the spontaneous formation of traveling energy condensates, exhibiting robust long-range temporal order reminiscent of continuous time crystals. Our results provide a simple yet powerful framework to study bulk-driven nonlinear energy diffusion in stochastic many-body systems, offering a bridge between microscopic dynamics, macroscopic transport, and controlled spatiotemporal order.

</details>


### [92] [Microscopic Dynamical Entropy II: Statistical and Stochastic Thermodynamics of Hamiltonian Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06814)
*Mingnan Ding,Michael E. Cates*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文扩展了微观动力学熵（MDE）框架，使其适用于任意总能量分布和含时哈密顿量，从而在有限封闭哈密顿系统中直接定义功和热，并在驱动系统和极小热浴条件下验证了MDE的单调增长与涨落关系，为经典和随机热力学提供了有限系统哈密顿基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将原有的微观动力学熵（MDE）框架从固定总能量的封闭哈密顿系统推广到任意总能量分布和含时哈密顿量情形，以便直接处理随机热力学、经典热力学及驱动系统中的做功交互问题。

Method: 通过将完整的微观描述约化为选定变量x与瞬时总能量(x,E)的描述，未监测自由度Y通过其条件相空间体积（conditional phase-space volume, CPV）Ω_Y(x,E,t)进入框架，从而在有限哈密顿复合系统中直接定义功和热。

Result: 在混合与时间尺度分离条件下，即使对于具有任意能量分布的驱动系统，MDE也呈现单调增长，对应宏观第二定律。在轨迹层面，推导了MDE的细致与积分涨落关系（fluctuation relations），推广了标准大热浴结果。在仅含十到二十个自由度的驱动少粒子哈密顿系统中，数值验证了集体坐标（如质心位置）的随机热力学行为。

Conclusion: 这些结果为经典和随机热力学的涌现提供了有限系统的哈密顿基础，并将其适用范围扩展至极小热浴情形。

Abstract: The Microscopic Dynamical Entropy (MDE) introduced in Ref. [1] describes irreversible relaxation of selected variables x within a finite closed Hamiltonian system of fixed total energy E. Here we extend the framework to arbitrary total-energy distributions and time-dependent Hamiltonians. This allows work interactions with external agents or protocols, crucial in stochastic and classical thermodynamics, and driven systems more generally, to be addressed directly. The central step is to reduce the full microscopic description in terms of selected variables x and unmonitored variables y to one in terms of the selected variables and the instantaneous total energy (x,E). The unmonitored degrees of freedom y in Y enter through their conditional phase-space volume (CPV) $Ω_Y(x,E,t)$. This construction allows work and heat to be defined directly for finite Hamiltonian composites, including cases where Y is so small that its temperature is not well defined. We demonstrate monotonic MDE growth, corresponding to the macroscopic second law, under mixing and time-scale separation even for driven systems with arbitrary energy distributions. At trajectory level, we derive detailed and integral fluctuation relations for the MDE, generalising standard large-bath results. We verify these numerically in a driven few-particle Hamiltonian system, showing the emergence of stochastic thermodynamics for collective coordinates, such as the centre-of-mass position, even in closed systems with only ten or twenty degrees of freedom. Physically, these fluctuation relations connect irreversibility to the change in the number of unmonitored microstates compatible with initial and final data for the observed coordinates. Together, our results provide a finite-system Hamiltonian foundation for the emergence of classical and stochastic thermodynamics and extend their applicability to surprisingly small heat baths.

</details>


### [93] [A neural-network Maxwell's demon learns cold damping for work extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06822)
*Stephen Whitelam,Sergio Ciliberto,Ludovic Bellon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文训练一个神经网络麦克斯韦妖（neural-network Maxwell's demon），从受热噪声（thermal noise）影响的欠阻尼微机械悬臂梁（underdamped micromechanical cantilever）模型中提取功。当输入包含振荡器速度时，该网络发现了接近理论功率极限的“冷阻尼（cold damping）”策略，揭示了一种近最优功提取的简单物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索神经网络是否能够在热力学系统中自发学习并优化功提取（work extraction）策略，超越人工设计协议的性能。

Method: 训练一个神经网络麦克斯韦妖，它周期性地调整谐振陷阱（harmonic trap）的位置，以最大化稳态运行下的提取功率。网络分别以悬臂梁位置与陷阱位置、或振荡器速度作为输入。

Result: 当输入为位置信息时，网络学习到一种改进版的人工设计协议，性能显著提升。当输入包含速度时，网络发现了一种定性不同的策略，提取的功接近理论功率上限（theoretical power bound）。该策略实现了冷阻尼：陷阱位置与速度近似线性位移，有效增加了阻尼系数（damping coefficient）并降低了有效温度（effective temperature）。

Conclusion: 神经网络麦克斯韦妖重新发现了光力学（optomechanics）中著名的冷却策略，表明近最优功提取背后存在一个简单的物理机制——冷阻尼。

Abstract: We train a neural-network Maxwell's demon to extract work from a model of an underdamped micromechanical cantilever subject to thermal noise. The demon, which periodically adjusts the position of a harmonic trap, is trained to maximize the power extracted under steady-state operation. When the demon is given the cantilever position and trap position as inputs it learns a refined version of an existing hand-designed protocol, yielding a substantial improvement in performance. When the demon receives the oscillator velocity as input it discovers a qualitatively different strategy that extracts substantially more work, close to the theoretical power bound. Analysis of the protocol shows that it implements {\em cold damping}: the trap position is displaced approximately linearly with velocity, producing an effective increase of the oscillator's damping coefficient and a reduction of its effective temperature. Thus a neural-network Maxwell's demon rediscovers a well-known cooling strategy from optomechanics, revealing a simple physical mechanism underlying near-optimal work extraction from thermal fluctuations in an underdamped system.

</details>


### [94] [Thermodynamic description of worldwide distribution of energy and carbon emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07315)
*Klaus M. Frahm,Dima L. Shepelyansky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于公开数据，利用洛伦兹曲线（Lorenz curve）和帕累托曲线（Pareto curve）分析了过去40-50年间世界各国能源与碳排放的分布，发现这些分布在重新缩放后保持高度稳定，且基尼系数（Gini coefficient）很高，表明能源分布存在严重不平等。作者提出能量热化假设（ENergy Thermalization Hypothesis, ENTH），认为这些分布源于各国主体的瑞利-金斯（Rayleigh-Jeans, RJ）热化与凝聚，该假设能很好地描述数据，并将不平等与低能态的RJ凝聚联系起来，同时探讨了与全球财富不平等的相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究揭示了全球能源与碳排放分布存在显著不平等，但其背后的物理机制尚不清晰。作者试图从统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角出发，为这种长期稳定的分布模式提供一个统一的理论解释。

Method: 基于公开数据，采用洛伦兹曲线和帕累托曲线对过去40-50年各国能源与碳排放分布进行可视化与重新缩放分析；提出能量热化假设（ENTH），将各国主体类比为统计力学中的粒子，以瑞利-金斯热化与凝聚过程描述其分布演化。

Result: 重新缩放后的洛伦兹曲线和帕累托曲线在40-50年间保持高度稳定；基尼系数持续处于高位，反映能源分配的强不平等性；ENTH假设能够极好地拟合上述时间段内的数据分布；不平等自然源于低能态下的瑞利-金斯凝聚（RJ condensation）。

Conclusion: ENTH假设为全球能源分布的不平等现象提供了基于统计力学的理论依据，并揭示了其与全球财富不平等之间的内在平行关系。

Abstract: Based on public data, we analyze the distributions of energy and carbon emission over world countries on a scale of the last 40-50 years using their presentation via Lorenz and Pareto curves. These curves in rescaled format remain remarkably stable on this time period being characterized by high values of the Gini coefficient indicating a strong inequality of energy distribution. To explain these distributions, we introduce the ENergy Thermalization Hypothesis (ENTH) according to which these distributions result from the Rayleigh-Jeans (RJ) thermalization and condensation of agents representing different countries. We show that this hypothesis provides an excellent description of Lorenz and Pareto curves obtained from data on the above time period. It also gives natural grounds for inequality relating it to the RJ condensation at low energy states. We additionally trace parallels with the wealth inequality in the world.

</details>


### [95] [Entanglement Asymmetry in Random Quantum Automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07556)
*Olalla A. Castro-Alvaredo,Dávid Szász-Schagrin,Michele Mazzoni*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机量子自动机系综（random quantum automaton ensembles）中的子系统纠缠不对称性（subsystem entanglement asymmetry），发现其局部对称化（symmetrization）行为与Haar随机电路相似，但对称化尺度依赖于初始态，这一现象与参与熵守恒（conservation of participation entropy）及电荷扇区均匀探索相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究随机量子自动机系综这一新型量子动力学模型中的子系统纠缠不对称性行为，并与已知的Haar随机电路结果进行对比，以揭示其独特的对称化机制。

Method: 通过对希尔伯特空间中的基态进行置换（permuting basis states）并施加全局相位移动（global phase shifts）来生成随机量子自动机系综；计算不同连接几何（connectivity geometries）下U(1)子系统不对称性的系综平均；分析不同子系统尺寸下的对称化行为。

Result: 2-局部电路几何（2-local circuit geometry）对应的系综在晚期极限下的平均值与全连接系综（all-to-all ensemble）平均值一致；系统表现出类似Haar随机电路的局部对称化，但对称化尺度依赖于初始态；子系统不对称性的增长与子系统相干性（subsystem coherence）的增长由相同的对称化尺度表征。

Conclusion: 随机量子自动机系综的对称化动力学与Haar随机电路有本质区别，其尺度对初始态的依赖源于参与熵守恒与电荷扇区均匀探索之间的相互作用。

Abstract: We investigate the subsystem entanglement asymmetry in random quantum automaton ensembles, which are generated by permuting the basis states in the Hilbert space and applying global phase shifts. We compute the ensemble average of the $U(1)$ subsystem asymmetry in different connectivity geometries, showing that the late-time limit of the ensemble associated to a 2-local circuit geometry coincides with the all-to-all ensemble average. By focusing on different subsystem sizes, we demonstrate that, similarly to Haar-random circuits, the system locally symmetrizes. However, in sharp contrast to the Haar-random setting, the scale at which symmetrization happens depends on the initial state, a phenomenon we associate with the interplay of conservation of the participation entropy and the uniform exploration of charge sectors. Additionally, we connect the growth of the subsystem asymmetry to the subsystem coherence and show that their growth is characterized by the same symmetrization scale.

</details>


### [96] [Feller diffusion in an interval: Inhomogeneous fluctuation-induced asymmetric escape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07649)
*Prashanta Bauri,Debasish Mondal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限区间内Feller扩散在非均匀涨落驱动下的不对称逃逸现象，发现乘性噪声在灭绝边界处被抑制，导致逃逸偏向爆发状态，平均逃逸时间呈现非单调行为，且涨落主导均值，揭示了随机决策中的速度-精度权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非均匀涨落（inhomogeneous fluctuations）如何影响有限区间内Feller扩散的不对称逃逸行为，特别是乘性噪声（multiplicative fluctuations）被边界抑制时对逃逸偏向和平均逃逸时间（mean exit time）的影响。

Method: 采用Feller扩散模型，对应于过阻尼布朗运动（overdamped Brownian motion）在平移谐振势（shifted harmonic potential）中并带有状态依赖扩散系数（state-dependent diffusivity）。设置两个等势能、等距的逃逸点，分别代表灭绝位点（extinction site）和爆发点（outbreak point）。

Result: 平均逃逸时间对初始条件和漂移-噪声强度比呈非单调依赖（non-monotonic dependence），在粒子初始位于灭绝（低噪声）边界时达到最大值。即使初始偏向低噪声边界，爆发可能性仍更大。最低变异系数（coefficient of variation, CV）的空间位置与最大逃逸时间高度吻合。逃逸时间的涨落在非平凡函数形式下主导其均值。

Conclusion: 观察到的逃逸不对称性塑造了随机决策事件（stochastic decision-making events）中的速度-精度权衡（speed-accuracy trade-off）。

Abstract: We present an inhomogeneous fluctuation-induced asymmetric escape event of a Feller diffusion confined to a finite interval with two competing absorbing boundaries. The dynamics correspond to an overdamped Brownian motion in a shifted harmonic potential with state-dependent diffusivity. We set two exit points (equal potential energies), equidistant from the potential minima: an extinction site near the origin and an outbreak point. The multiplicative fluctuations are suppressed near the extinction boundary, biasing trajectories toward the outbreak state. The mean exit time exhibits a non-monotonic dependence on the initial condition and the drift-to-noise strength ratio, attaining a maximum when the particle is initialized toward the extinction (low-noise) site. The outbreak possibility is more likely even if the process started with a small initial bias towards the low-noise boundary. The spatial location of the lowest coefficient of variation (CV) is nicely corroborated by the maximum exit time, which is the hallmark of a stochastic escape from an interval. The fluctuation in escape time is found to dominate its mean as a non-trivial function of the drift-to-noise strength and the initial spatial bias. The observed asymmetries in escape also shape the speed-accuracy trade-off in stochastic decision-making events.

</details>

### [97] [Impact of Courant number on the results of numerical simulating of signal propagation in non-dispersive homogeneous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06707)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论推导与命题证明的方式，针对二维无色散均匀介质中的 FDTD 建模，系统分析了数值色散随 Courant 数的变化规律，并据此确定最优 Courant 数的条件。

Result: 以四个命题、若干推论和评注的形式，明确了数值色散的性质、Courant 数的最优值选取方法以及方法的适用范围。

Conclusion: Courant 数的最优选择能够消除数值色散，并且该方法可推广至折射率小于真空折射率的介质以及具有负折射性质的介质。

Abstract: The paper is devoted to the study of the connection between the numerical dispersion arising in FDTD modeling of electromagnetic signal propagation in nondispersive homogeneous media optically different from vacuum and the Courant number in the 2D case. The main results are formulated in the form of four statements, as well as a number of corollaries and remarks that determine the nature of the numerical dispersion, the optimal value of the Courant number and the limitations of the method. It is proved that the optimal choice of the Courant number eliminates the numerical dispersion and extends the capabilities of the developed numerical algorithm to media, which refractive index lesser than refractive index of vacuum, as well as media with negative refraction.

### [98] [Radiation Damage Cascades in Fullerite Using Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06962)
*Ethan P. Turner,Paolo Raiteri,Nigel A. Marks*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟研究了固态C60（fullerite）在环境条件下的辐射级联过程，发现其因C60分子间弱热传导而表现出异常长的热化阶段（数百皮秒），并揭示了级联造成的分子损伤与交联之间的线性关系，计算得到的位移阈值为18 eV，与实验一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究固态C60（fullerite）在辐射条件下的级联行为（cascade behavior），尤其是其因分子间弱耦合而可能表现出的独特辐射响应（radiation response）。

Method: 采用分子动力学（Molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，使用环境依赖碳相互作用势（Environment Dependent Interaction Potential, EDIP）结合Ziegler-Biersack-Littmark（ZBL）短程势描述能量与力；对初位错原子（Primary Knock-On Atom, PKA）能量在0.1–1 keV范围内沿多个方向采样以收集统计；通过追踪动能、杂化态（hybridization）和键连通性（bond connectivity）随时间的变化表征级联行为。

Result: C60分子间的弱热传导导致热化阶段（thermalization phase）长达数百皮秒；级联会破坏C60分子并将其交联（cross-linked），且交联分子数量与新产生的sp³杂化原子数量之间存在线性关系；计算的位移阈值能量（threshold displacement energy）为18 eV，与实验吻合。

Conclusion: 固态C60因分子间热传输效率低，展现出与大多数材料不同的辐射响应特性；级联导致的分子交联行为可通过新sp³原子数量定量预测；模拟得到的位移阈值能量验证了方法的可靠性。

Abstract: Molecular dynamics is used to study radiation cascades in solid C60 under ambient conditions. Simulations are performed for Primary Knock-On Atom (PKA) energies from 0.1 to 1 keV, and cascades are sampled over many PKA directions to collect statistics. Energies and forces are described using the Environment Dependent Interaction Potential for carbon paired with the Ziegler-Biersack-Littmark potential for short-range interactions, and cascade behaviour is characterized by tracking kinetic energy, hybridization and bond connectivity as a function of time. Compared to most materials, fullerite exhibits an unusual radiation response due to weak thermal transfer between C60 molecules leading to a thermalization phase lasting hundreds of picoseconds. The cascades damage the C60 molecules and link them together, and a linear relation is found between the number of cross-linked molecules and the number of new sp3 atoms. The threshold displacement energy computed is 18 eV, in agreement with experiments

### [99] [Semilocal exchange functionals from the exact-exchange condition for the hydrogen atom: Hydrogenic exactness and recovery of Rydberg-like bound states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07648)
*Fumihiro Imoto*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过重新审视 Gill 和 Pople 的 GP93 交换泛函，将其作为尾部生成成分（tail-generating ingredient）整合到开关式半局域泛函中，使该泛函能够产生束缚的类里德伯（Rydberg-like）虚拟 Kohn-Sham 态，并改善最高占据轨道本征值对实验电离能的逼近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半局域密度泛函（semilocal density functionals）中交换势在原子和分子外部区域衰减过快，缺乏正确的 $-1/r$ 尾部行为，导致从 PBE 到现代 meta-GGA（如 SCAN）等泛函无法支持原子的束缚类里德伯态。本文旨在解决这一缺陷，恢复正确的渐近尾部行为。

Method: 将 GP93 交换增强因子（enhancement factor）作为尾部生成成分，通过反问题（inverse problem）方法求解。该因子在氢原子 $1s$ 密度上精确，并通过均匀坐标缩放（uniform coordinate scaling）推广至类氢 $1s$ 离子。将 GP93 因子与动能密度指示器（kinetic-energy-density indicator）结合，使其发散分支仅作用于类单电子区域；通过少量开关参数校准，平衡尾部恢复与自洽场稳定性。

Result: 所构建的泛函在全电子 H、He 以及使用大芯赝势（large-core pseudopotentials）的 Li、Na、K 等最外壳为类单电子 $s$ 壳层的体系中产生了束缚类里德伯虚拟 Kohn-Sham 态序列，并将最高占据本征值推向实验电离能。对于 $p$ 壳层原子（Ne、Ar），开关关闭，适用领域由设计限定。固定密度测试表明，约化拉普拉斯开关（reduced-Laplacian switch）能区分原子尾部和共价键中心，纯密度动能泛函可使整个开关不依赖轨道。

Conclusion: GP93 增强因子提供了氢精确的尾部渐近形式 $O[s(\ln s)^{2/3}]$，区别于 Armiento 和 Kümmel 的 $s\ln s$ 形式。通过开关机制，该泛函在保持非经验性的同时，成功恢复了类单电子体系中的束缚里德伯态，且无需广义 Kohn-Sham（generalized Kohn-Sham）求解器。

Abstract: In semilocal density functionals the exchange potential decays too rapidly outside atoms and molecules and lacks the correct $-1/r$ tail; as a consequence, functionals from PBE to modern meta-GGAs such as SCAN support no bound Rydberg-like state of an atom. We revisit the gradient-corrected exchange functional that Gill and Pople (GP93) constructed to reproduce the exact exchange potential of the hydrogen atom, solve their equation as an inverse problem, and use the resulting enhancement factor -- the GP93 factor -- as a tail-generating ingredient of a switched semilocal functional. The GP93 factor is exact on the hydrogen $1s$ density and, by uniform coordinate scaling, on hydrogenic $1s$ ions, where it yields the eigenvalue $-Z^2/2$ exactly (hydrogenic exactness). Its large-gradient growth has the hydrogen-exact form $O[s(\ln s)^{2/3}]$, distinct from the $s\ln s$ form of Armiento and Kümmel. The factor is combined with a kinetic-energy-density indicator so that its divergent branch acts only in one-electron-like regions; the GP93 ingredient is nonempirical, while a few switching parameters are calibrated to balance tail recovery against self-consistent-field stability. The resulting functional produces Rydberg-like series of bound virtual Kohn--Sham states in systems whose outermost shell is a one-electron-like $s$ shell -- all-electron H and He, and Li, Na, and K with large-core pseudopotentials -- and moves the highest-occupied eigenvalue toward the experimental ionization energy. For $p$-shell atoms (Ne, Ar) the switch closes, so the domain of applicability is fixed by design. Fixed-density tests indicate that a reduced-Laplacian switch distinguishes atomic tails from covalent bond centers, and that a density-only kinetic-energy functional renders the entire switch orbital-independent, so that no generalized Kohn--Sham solver is required.

</details>

### [100] [On the Gross-Pitaevskii model with a moving impurity: Cauchy problem and superfluidity criterion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07115)
*Paolo Antonelli,Martino Caliaro*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究带有移动δ势阱（traveling delta potential）和非零无穷远处边界条件的一维Gross-Pitaevskii方程，证明了该Cauchy问题在能量空间中的全局适定性，并分析了共动参考系中静止态的存在性与轨道稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型描述了量子流体中运动杂质（moving impurity）的效应，旨在严格建立其数学理论，包括适定性和静止态的稳定性分析。

Method: 通过定义保守能量并引入重整化动量（renormalized momentum）概念，证明Cauchy问题在能量空间中的全局适定性；在共动参考系中研究静止态的存在性，并利用能量方法证明具有较高最小密度的静止态的轨道稳定性（orbital stability）。

Result: 证明了Cauchy问题在能量空间中的全局适定性；存在一个依赖于杂质的临界速度（critical velocity），高于该速度时不存在静止态，低于该速度时出现两个不同的静止态，其中具有较高最小密度的那个是轨道稳定的。

Conclusion: 该研究为运动杂质在量子流体中的动力学行为提供了严格的数学基础，明确了静止态的存在条件和稳定性特性。

Abstract: We study the one-dimensional Gross-Pitaevskii equation with a traveling delta potential and non-zero conditions at infinity. This model describes the effect of a moving impurity in a quantum fluid. Firstly, we show that the associated Cauchy problem is globally well-posed in the energy space. This requires the definition of a conserved energy, which involves the notion of renormalized momentum. Secondly, we study the existence and stability of stationary states in a co-moving reference frame. It is known that there exists an impurity-dependent critical velocity above which no stationary state exists. For velocities below the critical one, two different stationary states appear. We show the orbital stability of the one with higher minimal density.

### [101] [Semiclassical Schrödinger operators with purely imaginary potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07301)
*Victor Arnaiz,Jean-Francois Bony,Laurent Michel*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了有界域上具有纯虚势的薛定谔算符（Schrödinger operator）$P = -h^{2}\Delta + iV(x)$，证明在$h \to 0$极限下，其最左侧特征值由势函数$V$最退化临界点对应的局部模型渐近决定，并将该结果应用于流体力学中的剪切流（shear flows）演化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有纯虚势的薛定谔算符（Schrödinger operator with purely imaginary potential）在$h \to 0$极限下的谱渐近行为，特别是左端特征值的渐近分布规律。

Method: 假设势函数$V$在临界点附近可被齐次多项式（homogeneous polynomial）近似，利用局部模型（local model）方法分析最退化临界点对特征值渐近行为的贡献。

Result: 在$h \to 0$极限下，算符$P$的最左侧特征值渐近地由与$V$的最退化临界点（most degenerated critical points）相关联的局部模型决定。

Conclusion: 该谱渐近结果可应用于相关的演化问题，包括流体力学中的剪切流（shear flows）问题，表明该理论在非自伴算符（non-selfadjoint operator）谱分析及流体稳定性研究中有潜在价值。

Abstract: We consider Schrödinger operators with purely imaginary potential $P = - h^{2} Δ+ i V ( x )$ on a bounded domain. Assuming that near its critical points the potential $V$ can be approximated by an homogeneous polynomial, we show that in the limit $h \to 0$ the leftmost eigenvalues of $P$ are asymptotically given by the local model associated to the most degenerated critical points of $V$. We give applications of this result to the associated evolution problem including shear flows in fluid mechanics.

### [102] [Time-periodic vortices near translating symmetric dipole patches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07613)
*Luca Franzoi,Taoufik Hmidi,Riccardo Montalto*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了二维不可压缩欧拉方程（incompressible Euler equations）中存在从平移涡旋对（translating vortex pair）分岔出的时间周期解，通过组合Lyapunov-Schmidt约化、Nash-Moser方案和谱分析（spectral analysis）等方法，构造了一类大Cantor参数集上的非刚性时间周期涡旋片（vortex patch）解，揭示了平移偶极子（translating dipoles）的丰富动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为涡旋片运动遵循刚性（rigid）范式，即涡旋边界在运动中保持形状不变。本研究旨在探索涡旋对在分离距离较大时是否存在更丰富的动力学行为，特别是非刚性、时间周期性的涡旋片解。

Method: 采用移动坐标系（co-moving frame）和轮廓动力学（contour dynamics）表述，将问题约化为涡旋边界的非线性输运方程（nonlinear transport equation）。针对线性化算子的退化问题，组合运用Lyapunov-Schmidt约化、Nash-Moser方案以及具有特征值渐近展开（asymptotic expansions）的谱分析来克服退化性。

Result: 在大的Cantor参数集上，成功构造了非刚性、时间周期的涡旋片解家族。分析表明平移偶极子附近的动力学远比经典的刚性范式丰富。

Conclusion: 所建立的方法灵活且稳健，有望推广至流体力学（Fluid Mechanics）中具有退化行为的一类更广泛的非局部偏微分方程（nonlocal PDEs）。

Abstract: We prove the existence of time-periodic solutions of the two-dimensional incompressible Euler equations bifurcating from a translating vortex pair. The reference configuration consists of two symmetric vortex patches of equal strength and opposite sign traveling at constant speed. In a regime of large separation between the vortices, the dynamics may be viewed as a small perturbation of an integrable system. Working in a co-moving frame and using the contour dynamics formulation, we reduce the problem to a nonlinear transport equation for the vortex boundaries. The linearized operator exhibits degeneracies associated with symmetries and transport effects. By combining a Lyapunov-Schmidt reduction, Nash-Moser scheme, and spectral analysis with sharp asymptotic expansions of the eigenvalues in order to overcome the degeneracy, we construct families of non-rigid, time-periodic vortex patch solutions for a large Cantor set of parameters. The analysis reveals that translating dipoles possess a surprisingly rich nearby dynamics, far beyond the classical rigid paradigm usually associated with vortex patch motion. More generally, the approach developed in this work is flexible and robust, and is expected to extend to a broader class of nonlocal PDEs from Fluid Mechanics with degenerate behaviours.

### [103] [Spontaneous patterning of cell size on curved surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07102)
*Yuan He,Shi-Lei Xue*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建适用于任意曲面的顶点模型（vertex model），揭示了椭球表面上细胞大小的自发空间模式：高曲率区域的细胞因黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）导致的机械竞争而变大，从而建立了一种基于自组织细胞尺寸变化的曲率感知（curvature sensing）物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织表面在胚胎发生（embryogenesis）和肿瘤发生（oncogenesis）过程中表现出复杂的曲率，已有证据表明细胞能主动感知曲率以调控行为和命运，但其背后的机制尚不明确。

Method: 开发了一个适用于任意曲面的顶点模型，用于模拟和分析曲面上的细胞行为。

Result: 在椭球表面上发现自发细胞大小模式：高曲率区域的细胞一致大于低曲率区域；该非均匀性源于黎曼几何编码的机械竞争——正高斯曲率（positive Gaussian curvature）降低多边形细胞的周长-面积比，从而松弛高曲率区域的细胞边缘张力，并通过面积扩张补偿以维持全局力平衡。该面积模式对模型参数变化具有鲁棒性，并与生物学观测一致。周长模式则受内在几何趋势与力平衡所需形变之间的竞争支配，并在临界形状指数（shape index）处发生反转。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了自组织的细胞大小空间变化作为曲率感知的一种潜在物理机制。

Abstract: Tissue surfaces exhibit complex curvature during embryogenesis and oncogenesis. Evidence shows that cells can actively sense curvature to regulate behavior and fate, yet the underlying mechanism remains unclear. Here, we develop a vertex model for arbitrary curved surfaces and uncover spontaneous cell size patterning on ellipsoidal surfaces: cells in high-curvature regions are consistently larger than those in low-curvature regions. This non-uniformity arises from a mechanical competition encoded in Riemannian geometry: positive Gaussian curvature reduces the perimeter-to-area ratio of polygonal cells, relaxing cell-edge tension in high-curvature regions, which is compensated by area expansion to maintain global force balance. This area pattern is robust against variations in model parameters and matches observations in biological systems. The perimeter pattern, in contrast, is governed by competition between the intrinsic geometric tendency and the deformation required by force balance, and undergoes reversal beyond a critical shape index. Together, these findings establish self-organized spatial variations in cell size as a potential physical mechanism for curvature sensing.

</details>


### [104] [DNA handles bias force-dependent looping times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07561)
*Wout Laeremans,Jef Hooyberghs,Wouter G. Ellenbroek*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过分子动力学模拟和解析理论框架，揭示了DNA环化（looping）过程中，侧翼DNA片段（flanking segments）通过间接力传导（indirect force transmission）显著增强了环化时间对机械张力（mechanical tension）的依赖性，该效应在侧翼长度超过持续长度（persistence length）时不再敏感，并在连接点柔性化时消失。基于粗粒化DNA模型的理论预测与实验数据定量一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA环化动力学是基因调控的关键机制，其对机械张力敏感。然而，在单分子实验和生物环境中，张力通常通过侧翼DNA片段间接传递，而非直接作用于环化位点。这种间接力传导如何影响环化时间尚未被系统研究。

Method: 采用蠕虫状链（wormlike chain）模型的分子动力学模拟，并结合解析理论框架，该框架通过力依赖的有效自由能景观（effective free energy landscape）偏移来解析间接力传导效应。在弱力极限下，该偏移简化为零力平衡平均值，从而解析得出整个力依赖的环化时间。此外，采用将单个碱基视为刚体（rigid bodies）的粗粒化DNA模型进行预测。

Result: 侧翼片段显著增强了环化时间对力的依赖性（陡峭化关系）；该效应在侧翼长度超过持续长度后不再敏感；当环化区域与侧翼的连接点变为柔性时，该效应消失。基于粗粒化DNA模型的理论预测与实验环化数据定量一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，力传导的几何结构对环化动力学具有显著且可预测的影响，这对解释单分子实验和基因调控背景下张力依赖性环化现象具有直接意义。

Abstract: DNA loop formation is a key mechanism in gene regulation, and looping kinetics are sensitive to mechanical tension acting on the DNA. In both single-molecule experiments and biological settings, this tension is typically transmitted through DNA segments flanking the looping region, rather than acting directly at the looping sites. How this indirect force transmission affects the looping time has not been systematically investigated. Using molecular dynamics simulations of a wormlike chain, we show that such flanking segments significantly steepen the force dependence of the looping time, an effect that is insensitive to their length once it exceeds the persistence length, and vanishes when the junction to the looping region is made flexible. We develop an analytical framework that accounts for this effect through a force-dependent shift in the effective free energy landscape of the looping segment. In the limit of small forces, this shift reduces to a zero-force equilibrium average, after which the entire force dependence of the looping time follows analytically. Applying this framework using a coarse-grained DNA model that treats individual bases as rigid bodies, we obtain predictions in quantitative agreement with experimental looping data. Our results demonstrate that the geometry of force transmission has a significant and predictable effect on looping kinetics, with direct implications for the interpretation of tension-dependent looping in both single-molecule experiments and gene regulatory contexts.

</details>

### [105] [BatteryMat: a hierarchical machine-learning and DFT framework for average-voltage screening of lithium-ion cathode materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06645)
*Jaehyung Lee,Charles Rhys Campbell,Kent Zhang,Kamal Choudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出BatteryMat三层框架，结合图神经网络（ALIGNN）快速筛选与自动选择泛函的DFT验证，在保持热力学一致性的前提下实现组合化学空间的高通量平均电压预测，最终从约449万结构筛选出213个候选正极材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（DFT）能够准确预测正极电压，但无法扩展到现代材料数据库的组合化学空间；纯机器学习代理速度快，却不能保证热力学一致性。为此，需要一种兼顾速度与热力学一致性的高通量筛选框架。

Method: 提出BatteryMat三层框架：第一层以Atomistic Line Graph Neural Network (ALIGNN)作为主要筛选信号，实现单次平均电压预测；第二层用ALIGNN-FF力场脱锂剖面验证幸存结构；第三层进行自动化PBE+U或optB88-vdW+U超胞DFT计算。交换-关联泛函根据空间群（spacegroup）自动选择，锂金属参考态在与正极相同的平面波基组下重新计算，消除约1V的系统偏差。

Result: ALIGNN预测器在7,610个ALIGNN-FF脱锂电压上训练，平均绝对误差为0.17 V，决定系数为0.94。对四种商用正极材料（LiFePO4、LiMnPO4、LiMn2O4、LiCoO2），DFT层将实验平均电压误差控制在0.3 V以内，理论体积容量误差在5%以内。管道从JARVIS-DFT池中筛选出71个候选结构，从约449万Alexandria结构中筛选出213个候选结构。

Conclusion: BatteryMat框架优先筛选而非生成现有结构，能够高效地从大规模数据库中识别候选正极材料，所输出的候选结构仍需DFT验证才能确认为正极材料。该框架开源可用，兼顾了机器学习的速度与DFT的热力学一致性。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) predicts cathode voltages accurately but does not scale to the combinatorial chemical spaces of modern materials databases, while pure machine-learning surrogates are fast but cannot guarantee thermodynamic consistency. We introduce BatteryMat, a three-tier framework that promotes single-pass average-voltage prediction with the Atomistic Line Graph Neural Network (ALIGNN) as the primary screening signal across JARVIS-DFT, then validates survivors with ALIGNN-FF force-field delithiation profiles and automated PBE+U or optB88-vdW+U supercell DFT. The exchange-correlation functional is selected automatically by spacegroup, and the lithium metal reference is recomputed in the same plane-wave basis as the cathode runs, removing a systematic offset of about 1 V present in tabulated values. Trained on 7,610 ALIGNN-FF delithiation voltages, the ALIGNN predictor reproduces the force-field labels with a mean absolute error of 0.17 V and a coefficient of determination of 0.94; this measures distillation fidelity to the force-field protocol, not agreement with DFT or experiment. On four commercial chemistries (LiFePO4, LiMnPO4, LiMn2O4, LiCoO2) the DFT tier reproduces the experimental average voltage to within 0.3 V and the theoretical volumetric capacity to within 5%; a fifth, non-stoichiometric layered entry is carried as an edge case. The pipeline prioritises, rather than generates, existing structures: it ranks the lithium-containing JARVIS-DFT pool into 71 candidates and a scan of about 4.49 million Alexandria structures into 213, all surrogate-level leads awaiting DFT validation rather than confirmed cathodes. BatteryMat is available at https://github.com/atomgptlab/batterymat with a demo at https://atomgpt.org/battery.

### [106] [Origin of the reaction temperature in solid-state materials synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06685)
*Shibo Tan,Gabrielle E. Kamm,Alex Stangel,Paul Chao,Alexander Mensah,Varun Srinivas Venkatesh,Eymana Maria,Nishkarsh Agarwal,Woohyeon Baek,John Ferrari,Katsuyo Thornton,Ashwin Shahani,Robert Hovden,Karena W. Chapman,Wenhao Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出瞬态液相（transient liquid phase）形成于亚稳共晶温度（metastable eutectic temperature）之上，该非平衡液相作为快速扩散介质混合前驱体并引发固态反应，从而解释了固态反应中最佳温度的存在机理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态材料合成对温度高度依赖，但目前缺乏能够解释或预测固态反应最佳温度的机制性理论（mechanistic theory）。

Method: 通过实验证据表明，在临界起始温度（critical onset temperature）以上，亚稳共晶温度处会形成瞬态液相，该非平衡液相充当快速扩散介质，使粉末前驱体得以混合并启动固态反应。

Result: 固态反应可在临界起始温度以上于数分钟内完成，而非传统认为的缓慢扩散限制过程；瞬态液相的存在是关键驱动因素。

Conclusion: 该热力学原理与反应物的结构或化学性质无关，可广泛应用于多种复杂材料的合成与制造。

Abstract: Temperature plays a crucial role in solid-state materials synthesis, but there is currently no mechanistic theory to explain or predict which temperature is best to conduct a solid-state reaction. Reactions between powder precursors are conventionally assumed to be slow diffusion-limited processes; however, recent in situ experiments show that solid-state reactions can complete in minutes above a critical onset temperature. Here, we present evidence that a transient liquid phase forms above the metastable eutectic temperature, and that this non-equilibrium liquid serves as a fast diffusion medium to intermix precursors and initiate a solid-state reaction. This thermodynamic principle is agnostic to the structure or chemistry of the reactants, and can be applied towards the synthesis and manufacturing of a wide range of complex materials.

### [107] [Fluctuation-Driven Enhancement of Spin-Orbit Torque near the Curie Temperature of Ultrathin Ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06703)
*Mateusz Szurek,Sergei Ivanov,Sergei Urazhdin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究受限条件下磁性超薄膜中磁涨落如何影响自旋轨道转矩，特别是理解居里温度（Curie temperature）附近反常的阻尼类与场类贡献行为。

Method: 通过实验测量超薄膜磁性异质结构在居里温度附近的阻尼类自旋轨道场和场类自旋轨道场的变化，并结合界面自旋电导的涨落驱动混合机制进行理论解释。

Result: 居里温度以上，阻尼类自旋轨道场显著增强，场类自旋轨道场被抑制，两者表现出相反的场依赖性。

Conclusion: 上述行为源于纵向与横向界面自旋电导的涨落驱动混合，增强了铁磁体对横向极化自旋流的吸收。该机制在居里温度以下可通过工程化微观磁态或利用自旋流产生的短波长磁振子（magnons）激活，为热辅助磁记录提供了自旋电子学模拟方案。

Abstract: We investigate how magnetic fluctuations influence spin-orbit torque in ultrathin-film magnetic heterostructures whose Curie temperature $T_C$ is suppressed by confinement. Above $T_C$, the damping-like contribution to spin-orbit field is significantly enhanced while the field-like contribution is suppressed, with the two contributions exhibiting opposite field dependencies. We show that these behaviors are consistent with fluctuation driven mixing between the longitudinal and transverse interfacial spin conductances, which enhances absorption of transversely polarized spin current by the ferromagnet. This mechanism can be activated below $T_C$ by engineering the microscopic magnetic state and by harnessing spin current-generated short-wavelength magnons, suggesting a spintronic analog of heat-assisted magnetic recording.

### [108] [Physical exact conditions as regularizers for exchange-correlation in solids and surface chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06729)
*Johannes Voss*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）在多相催化领域广泛用于表面反应机理研究，但其准确性强烈依赖于交换相关（exchange-correlation, XC）近似的选择。优化XC泛函以提升表面结合能描述时，可能对反应势垒的预测产生负面影响，这一矛盾有待澄清。

Method: 本文通过分析交换相关（XC）泛函的优化过程，检验了表面结合能与反应势垒之间的权衡关系，并考察了物理精确条件（exact conditions）对泛函性能的影响。

Result: 研究表明，若在优化交换相关（XC）泛函时未满足重要的物理精确条件，提升表面结合能描述会导致表面反应势垒的描述恶化。

Conclusion: 开发用于表面反应能量学的交换相关（XC）泛函时，必须在优化过程中遵守物理精确条件，以避免在改善结合能的同时牺牲反应势垒的准确性。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) often is the method of choice for simulating the electronic properties of extended solids and surfaces from first principles due to a favorable compromise between accuracy and computational cost. In the field of heterogeneous catalysis, DFT is indispensable for deriving mechanistic insights and understanding trends in surface reactivity. The accuracy of DFT for surface reaction energetics depends strongly on the exchange-correlation (XC) approximation. We show here that optimization of such XC functionals for surface binding energies can lead to a worse description of surface reaction barriers, unless important physical exact conditions are fulfilled.

### [109] [Spin-orbit magnetism in altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06730)
*Ruojia Wang,Yuntian Liu,Renzheng Xiong,Xiaobing Chen,Qihang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过定向自旋群理论和自旋-轨道耦合张量展开，系统揭示了反铁磁体（包括交变磁体）在净磁化强度极小时仍能产生显著反常霍尔效应的机制，并首次发现了一种同轴霍尔效应，即轨道和自旋磁化强度平行于奈尔矢量（Néel vector）排列。第一性原理计算在交变磁体KV₂Se₂O中验证了这一效应，为实现弱场下奈尔序（Néel order）确定性翻转提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体（antiferromagnet）包括交变磁体（altermagnet）在净磁化强度极小时仍能表现出显著的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect），该机制的长期未能得到解释。本文旨在揭示这一现象的微观机理，并寻找兼具大反常霍尔效应与最小净磁化的交变磁体候选材料。

Method: 采用定向自旋群理论（oriented spin group theory）和自旋-轨道耦合张量展开（spin-orbit-coupling tensor expansion），系统分析了轨道磁化强度（orbital magnetization）和自旋磁化强度（spin magnetization）关于自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的微扰行为。再利用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）在交变磁体KV₂Se₂O中进行验证。

Result: 发现只有当相反自旋的子晶格（sublattice）通过四重旋转（fourfold rotation）连接时，轨道磁化强度和自旋磁化强度才表现出不同的微扰阶数。在此类交变磁体中，进一步发现了一种同轴霍尔效应（coaxial Hall effect），即诱导的自旋和轨道磁化强度平行于奈尔矢量排列，并在KV₂Se₂O中通过第一性原理计算得到验证。

Conclusion: 该效应有望在弱外场下实现奈尔序的确定性翻转（deterministic switching）。本文提供了一种系统的对称性方法，用于识别潜在的交变磁体候选材料，从而在极小净磁化条件下实现大反常霍尔效应，为高性能、无杂散场（stray-field-free）的自旋电子学（spintronics）应用奠定基础。

Abstract: The mechanism enabling antiferromagnets, including altermagnets, to exhibit a prominent anomalous Hall effect despite a vanishingly small net magnetization has long remained elusive. Here, by employing oriented spin group theory and spin-orbit-coupling tensor expansion, we systematically disentangle the perturbative behaviors of orbital and spin magnetizations with respect to spin-orbit coupling. Remarkably, we find that only if the opposite-spin sublattices are connected through a fourfold rotation, the orbital and spin magnetizations exhibit distinct perturbative orders. In these altermagnets, we further discover a coaxial Hall effect characterized by the induced spin and orbital magnetizations aligning parallel to the Néel vector, which we further demonstrate by first-principles calculations in the altermagnet KV$_{2}$Se$_{2}$O. This effect holds great promise for achieving deterministic switching of the Néel order under weak external fields. Our work provides a systematic symmetry approach to identify potential altermagnetic candidates combining a large anomalous Hall effect with minimal net magnetization, paving the way for high-performance, stray-field-free spintronic applications.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于电子密度泛函理论（density functional theory）的总能量计算，结合统计力学（statistical mechanics）方法，构建了成分连续的自由能模型。研究聚焦于富V固溶体（V-rich solid solution）和一种复杂金属间化合物（complex intermetallic phase）。

Result: 在富V区域识别出三个基态（ground state），这些基态在升高温度时转变为固溶体。此外，发现AlV₃相以Al15结构作为中温相存在，该相由非简谐振动自由能（anharmonic vibrational free energy）所稳定。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了Al-V合金体系中有限温度下的相稳定性和相变行为，特别是非简谐振动自由能对AlV₃中温相的稳定化作用，为理解该体系中复杂相的热力学行为提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The Al-V alloy system contains a number of phases including several with complex structures and at least two exhibiting sites of partial occupation. Through electronic density functional theory-based total energy calculations combined with methods of statistical mechanics, we examine the relative stability of phases at finite temperatures. We construct composition-continuous free energy models for the V-rich solid solution and for one of the complex intermetallic phases. In the V-rich region, we identify three ground states that transform to the solid solution at elevated temperatures. We also suggest that \phase{Al}{V_3} takes the Al15 structure as an intermediate-temperature phase stabilized by anharmonic vibrational free energy.

### [111] [Topological charge, helicity and vorticity conservation and the reverse spin-current model in the II-nd type multifferoics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06756)
*Pavel A. Andreev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文追溯了拓扑荷（topological charge）与流体动力学螺旋度（hydrodynamic helicity）这两个运动积分之间的关系，并展示了自旋-电流模型（spin-current model）和自旋-场模型（spin-field model）在螺旋度守恒与电极化（electric polarization）形成中的作用，同时提出逆自旋-电流模型（reverse spin-current model）以解释电极化对自旋演化的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立拓扑荷与流体动力学螺旋度这两个运动积分之间的内在联系，并阐明不同电极化模型（自旋-电流模型与自旋-场模型）在螺旋度守恒和自旋结构形成中的作用机制。

Method: 通过理论推导追溯了两类运动积分（拓扑荷与流体动力学螺旋度）之间的关系；分析了自旋-电流模型和自旋-场模型在电极化形成中的不同起源（前者基于形变，后者基于非定常机制）；并提出了逆自旋-电流模型来展示极化对自旋演化方程的反向贡献。

Result: 自旋-电流模型和自旋-场模型均来源于相同原理，但具有不同的时间特性（前者为定常、后者为非定常）；逆自旋-电流模型揭示了电极化可以反作用于自旋结构的形成，并且该机制同时是螺旋度和拓扑荷守恒的必要条件。

Conclusion: 拓扑荷与流体动力学螺旋度之间存在密切关联；电极化的形成不仅受自旋分布调控，其逆过程（极化驱动的自旋结构形成）同样重要，且两者均以保持螺旋度与拓扑荷守恒为约束条件。

Abstract: The topological charge and its density are related to the spin vorticity, while the spin vorticity is a part of full vorticity of the medium. The full vorticity is related to an integral of motion called the hydrodynamic helicity. Relation between two integrals of motion (the topological charge and the hydrodynamic helicity) is traced. The role of the spin-current model of the electric polarization formation due to the specific spin distribution in the helicity conservation is demonstrated. The reverse spin-current model is suggested to demonstrate the contribution of the polarization in the spin evolution equation, its importance for the helicity conservation is shown as well. Spin-field model of the electric polarization is the second model for the electric polarization (the deformation, firstly) formation due to the specific spin distribution, which appears from the same principles, but it has nonstationary origin. Moreover, the reverse spin-current model gives a mechanism for the spin structure formation due to the electric polarization in the system. It also appears as the requirement for the conservation of the helicity and the topological charge.

### [112] [Symmetry-Enforced Chiral Phonons in Altermagnets via Magnon-Phonon Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06792)
*Philipp Rieger,Markus Weißenhofer,Sergiy Mankovsky,Peter M. Oppeneer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，在PT对称性破缺的交错磁体（altermagnet）CrSb中，展示了由相对论性磁振子-声子耦合产生的零场手性声子（chiral phonon），并揭示了交错磁g波对称性向声子角动量的转移以及有限贝里曲率（Berry curvature）导致的异常能斯特响应（Nernst response）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性声子（chiral phonons）在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有重要应用前景，但传统反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）中零场下手性声子的生成受到联合宇称与时间反演对称性（combined parity and time-reversal, $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry）的禁止。因此，亟需寻找无需外场即可产生手性声子的材料体系。

Method: 本文以原型交错磁体（altermagnet）CrSb为研究对象，采用第一性原理方法（first-principles methods）计算了全布里渊区（complete Brillouin zone）内杂化的磁振子-极化激元（hybridized magnon-polarons）。

Result: 研究发现，相对论性磁振子-声子耦合（relativistic magnon-phonon coupling）将交错磁体的g波对称性（$g$-wave symmetry）直接印刻到声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）上。此外，有限贝里曲率（Berry curvatures）导致了反常的自旋和声子角动量能斯特响应（anomalous spin and phonon angular momentum Nernst responses）。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明，手性格点动力学（chiral lattice dynamics）可以在无需外场的补偿磁基态（compensated magnetic ground states）中产生，将块体交错磁体（bulk altermagnets）定位为零场自旋热电子学（zero-field spin caloritronics）和手性声子学（chiral phononics）的候选材料。

Abstract: Chiral phonons are attractive for spintronics applications, however, their zero-field generation in conventional antiferromagnets is forbidden by combined parity and time-reversal ($\mathcal{PT}$) symmetry. Here we demonstrate the emergence of chiral phonons in $\mathcal{PT}$-breaking altermagnetic systems at zero field arising from relativistic magnon-phonon coupling. Focusing on the prototypical altermagnet CrSb, we utilize first-principles methods to calculate the hybridized magnon-polarons across the complete Brillouin zone. We show that this coupling imprints an altermagnetic $g$-wave symmetry directly onto the phonon angular momentum. Furthermore, we demonstrate anomalous spin and phonon angular momentum Nernst responses arising from finite Berry curvatures. These findings establish that chiral lattice dynamics can arise in compensated magnetic ground states without requiring external fields, positioning bulk altermagnets as material candidates for zero-field spin caloritronics and chiral phononics.

</details>


### [113] [Large-scale pseudopotential density functional theory calculations using orthogonalized enriched finite element basis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06848)
*Avirup Sircar,Bikash Kanungo,Sambit Das,Vikram Gavini*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于富集有限元（EFE）基组的赝势Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论计算框架，通过将经典有限元（CFE）基组与紧凑原子中心函数（富集函数）相结合，并在正交化处理后结合残差型Chebyshev子空间迭代方法，实现了高效、可扩展的DFT计算。相较于CFE基组，EFE基组在自由度、计算成本和内存需求上分别降低了5-7倍、5-9倍和4-5倍，并展现出良好的并行可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典有限元（classical finite element, CFE）基组在Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论计算中虽然系统性收敛，但自由度（degrees of freedom）数量大，导致计算成本高、内存需求大，限制了计算规模和资源利用效率。为此，需要一种兼具系统性收敛性和原子中心基组高效性的新基组框架。

Method: 提出富集有限元（enriched finite element, EFE）基组，即在CFE基组基础上添加紧凑原子中心函数（enrichment functions）；通过将富集函数相对于底层CFE基组正交化，改善基组条件数（conditioning）并提升重叠矩阵（overlap matrix）求逆效率。采用基于残差的Chebyshev子空间迭代法（residual-based Chebyshev subspace iteration）求解Kohn-Sham特征值问题，该方法对重叠矩阵求逆的近似误差具有容忍性。

Result: 在最高包含39,083个电子的非周期基准算例中，EFE基组相比CFE基组：自由度减少5-7倍；计算成本降低5-9倍；内存需求减少4-5倍。同时，EFE基组展现出良好的并行可扩展性（parallel scalability），且精度与现有DFT软件包一致。

Conclusion: EFE基组为赝势DFT计算提供了一种系统性收敛、快速、可扩展且资源高效的基组方案，能够有效减少自由度数量、计算成本和内存需求，并支持并行计算，整体上优于传统CFE基组。

Abstract: We present an efficient and scalable computational framework for pseudopotential Kohn-Sham density functional theory (KS-DFT) calculations using an enriched finite element (EFE) basis. The EFE basis is formed by augmenting the classical finite element (CFE) basis with compact atom-centered functions, which we term enrichment functions. The key idea is to combine the completeness of a finite element basis with the efficiency of an atom-centered basis. We orthogonalize the enrichment functions with respect to the underlying CFE basis to simultaneously improve the conditioning of the EFE basis and the efficiency of evaluating the inverse of the overlap matrix. To efficiently solve the Kohn-Sham eigenvalue problem, we employ a residual-based Chebyshev subspace iteration approach that is tolerant to approximations in the evaluation of the inverse of the overlap matrix. We demonstrate the accuracy of the framework as compared to the widely available DFT packages. For benchmark non-periodic calculations, ranging up to 39,083 electrons, the EFE basis offers a $5-7\times$ reduction in degrees of freedom over the CFE basis. As a result of this, EFE achieves a $5-9\times$ reduction in computational cost over the CFE basis. The EFE basis also provides a $4-5\times$ reduction in the required memory compared to the CFE basis, thus allowing for optimal utilization of computational resources. Finally, we demonstrate that the EFE basis affords good parallel scalability. Overall, the EFE basis offers a systematically convergent, fast, scalable, resource-efficient basis for pseudopotential DFT calculations.

Abstract: We investigate the thermoelectric and magnetic properties of Si-substituted $n$-type and Ti-substituted $p$-type Heusler alloy Fe$_2$VAl using the bipolar random Anderson model, which has been introduced recently to study antisite-defect effects associated with the sign change of the Seebeck coefficient in thermally quenched Fe$_2$VAl. Based on the electronic states of both $n$-type and $p$-type compounds, with the rigid-band shift of the Fermi energy and a temperature-dependent scattering rate taken into account, we elucidate how antisite defects simultaneously influence thermoelectric transport and local magnetic moments. We find that the magnetic moments are enhanced in $n$-type Fe$_2$VAl, whereas they are suppressed in $p$-type Fe$_2$VAl compared with the undoped compound.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对MCN家族（M = Ag, Au, Cu）的晶体结构与力学响应进行模拟，通过计算弹性性质与各向异性来评估ZLC与NLC行为。
