Abstract: Negative linear compressibility (NLC) is the counterintuitive phenomenon in which a crystallographic axis expands under hydrostatic pressure. A related phenomenon, zero linear compressibility (ZLC), occurs when an axis shows no length change under pressure. Both responses are rare and arise in materials with highly anisotropic mechanical properties. Motivated by recent reports of anomalous behavior in metal cyanides - including negative thermal expansion and NLC - we use first-principles calculations to investigate the potential of the MCN family (M = Ag, Au, Cu) to exhibit ZLC or NLC. Our simulations reveal three main findings. First, we predict the existence of previously unreported phases: the P6mm phase for AgCN and CuCN, and the R3m phase for AuCN. Second, all six members of the MCN family studied exhibit extreme elastic anisotropy, which indeed leads to ZLC or NLC in each case. Third, we identify a mechanism for these responses distinct from previously reported ones. The mechanism arises from the unique "bamboo forest" geometry of the material: weakly interacting rigid rods whose sparse packing allows pressure to be accommodated through changes in packing density rather than rod compression. This mechanism enables the anomalous response to persist over a wide pressure range, contrasting favorably with other materials that exhibit similar behavior. Our findings expand the relatively small family of materials known to exhibit ZLC or NLC and provide deeper insight into the microscopic origin of these unusual mechanical responses.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: AI2Pot 可在单个 GPU 上实现包含数百万原子的快速推理；训练后的模型可部署到 ASE 和 LAMMPS 中进行 MD 模拟；同时提供命令行工具 AI2Pot-cli 和 Python API 以支持实用的 MLIP 工作流。

Here, we present AI2Pot, a scalable and unified MLIP framework that seamlessly integrates model training, evaluation, and large-scale MD simulations with PyTorch-compatible ecosystem. Instead of relying on generic automatic differentiation for expensive atomistic operators, AI2Pot re-engineers the core computations of Moment tensor potential (MTP) and Neuroevolution potential (NEP) for both training and inference using hand-crafted C++/CUDA code. These specialized operators constitute a unified computational backend shared by training and inference, improving training-inference consistency and reducing memory usage by avoiding large intermediate caches. As a result, AI2Pot enables fast inference for large-scale atomic systems containing millions of atoms on a single GPU, while retaining the flexibility of PyTorch for model construction, training, and evaluation. Trained models can be deployed in ASE and LAMMPS for MD simulations. Furthermore, AI2Pot provides a companion command-line toolkit (AI2Pot-cli) and Python APIs to facilitate practical MLIP workflows. By unifying high-performance atomistic computing with modern machine-learning ecosystems, AI2Pot offers an user-friendly end-to-end framework for the developing, training, and deploying MLIPs for large scale MD.

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，分析单层与双层 CDW 堆叠的电子结构，并计算从两层到八层厚度的表面态密度，与扫描隧道谱（STS）进行对比。

Here, using density functional theory calculations, we show that this insulating surface instead originates from a charge-density-wave (CDW) stacking reconstruction. Whereas the bulk stabilizes a single-layer CDW stacking that supports metallic transport, the surface energetically favors a bilayer stacking, in which interlayer hybridization of Ta $5d_{z^2}$ orbitals opens a $\sim$0.4 eV gap -- a band insulator requiring no on-site Coulomb repulsion. We have studied this phenomenon, known as size focusing, using a theoretical framework (which extends Zener's theory of diffusional growth to a core-shell precipitate) and multi-precipitate simulations based on a phase field model. Our results yield key theoretical insights as well as conclusions with practical significance. (a) On the theoretical front, we show clearly that size focusing is a growth phenomenon: it ends when shell growth ends, and coarsening begins. (b) On the practical front, our results offer guidelines for designing alloys with narrower size distributions: size focusing is promoted in alloys with greater shell volume fractions and greater inter-precipitate spacing.

### [119] [Minimizing propagated density errors of atomic core-electron for simultaneously accurate bandgaps and lattice constants in closed-shell Copper semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07037)

Abstract: Density functional theory struggles to accurately determine electron density of atoms, whose error is inevitably encoded into the pseudopotential and propagated into solid-state calculations. However, little is known about how this affects accuracy nor how to remedy it. In this work, through a systematic study of the effect of Cu atomic density on bandgap and lattice constants of over 50 Cu-containing simple closed-shell semiconductors, we find that core-electron density can drastically affect nuclear attraction to valence electrons and subsequent charge distribution and energy position of Cu 3$d$ electrons. The error can be eliminated at its source by employing modified Hartree-Fock pseudopotentials for Cu core while retaining (semi-)local functionals for valence electrons. This real-space partitioning approach leads to simultaneous high-accuracy in bandgap and lattice constants across the entire material class.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高折射率电介质（high refractive index dielectrics）是光子学应用的核心，但经验的Moss定则（Moss rule）指出了折射率与光学透明度之间存在根本性的权衡（trade-off）。现有定则无法有效描述那些吸收被抑制至远高于电子带隙（electronic gap）的材料体系，因此亟需一种改进的筛选指标来发现突破此权衡的新型材料。

Method: 首先提出一种修正的Moss定则，将锚定点从基本带隙更换为光学吸收边，从而纳入多种吸收抑制机制的材料。基于该指标对Materials Project数据库进行高通量筛选，识别出具有最佳折射率/透明度权衡的材料，并通过杂化密度泛函理论计算对候选材料进行电子结构和光学性质的精确验证。

Result: 筛选揭示了具有重复性化学组成和结构原型的材料家族，包括黄铜矿（chalcopyrites）、Zintl磷族化物（Zintl pnictides）以及早期过渡金属多元阴离子氮硫化物（chalconitrides）和氧硫化物（oxychalcogenides）。其中(Hf,Zr)₂(S,Se)N₂族化合物实现了超高折射率、低有效质量以及深紫外透明窗口的独特组合，性能超越了当前最先进的TiO₂和SiC。

Conclusion: (Hf,Zr)₂(S,Se)N₂族化合物被确认为一类此前尚未充分探索的独特材料体系，有望用于下一代光子学应用。修正的Moss定则为发现更多突破折射率-透明度权衡的新材料提供了理论指导。

Abstract: High refractive index dielectrics are central to photonic applications, yet the empirical Moss rule imposes a fundamental trade-off between refractive index and optical transparency. We introduce a modified Moss rule anchored to the optical absorption edge rather than the fundamental bandgap, capturing materials where various physical mechanisms suppress absorption well above the electronic gap. Screening the Materials Project database with this metric reveals recurring chemical compositions and structural prototypes in the materials with the most promising refractive index/transparency trade-offs. These materials include chalcopyrites, Zintl pnictides, and early transition metal multi-anion chalconitrides and oxychalcogenides compounds. Hybrid density functional theory calculations reveal that the chalconitride (Hf,Zr)2(S,Se)N2 family can achieve a combination of ultra-high refractive indices, low effective masses and transparency windows extending deep into the UV, surpassing state-of-the-art TiO2 and SiC. Our results establish (Hf,Zr)2(S,Se)N2 compounds as a unique and largely unexplored material family for next-generation photonic applications.

</details>


### [121] [Phonon scattering mechanisms in WTe$_2$ observed by ultrafast coherent phonon spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07087)
*Mizuki Akei,Yu Mizukoshi,Muneaki Hase*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过宽温区（4.6–300 K）时间分辨泵浦探测光谱研究Weyl半金属T$_d$-WTe$_2$中的相干声子，发现高频光学模的温变行为符合常规非谐声子-声子散射模型，而低频2.4 THz模式呈现反常行为，可归因于声子-电子散射的贡献。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间分辨泵浦探测光谱学（time-resolved pump-probe spectroscopy），在4.6到300 K的宽温区内测量Weyl半金属T$_d$-WTe$_2$中相干声子（coherent phonons）的频率和衰减率的温度依赖性。

Conclusion: 在Weyl半金属T$_d$-WTe$_2$中，不同频率的声子模式受不同的散射机制主导：高频模符合非谐声子-声子散射，低频模则体现出声子-电子散射的贡献。

Abstract: Revealing the mechanisms of phonon scattering is crucial for understanding material properties such as transport characteristics and optical responses. It can be discussed by measuring the temperature dependence of the phonon energy and lifetime. To gain insight into these mechanisms in Weyl semimetal T$_d$-WTe$_2$, we investigated coherent phonons using time-resolved pump-probe spectroscopy in a wide temperature range from 4.6 to 300 K. The temperature dependence of the frequency and decay rate of the two high-frequency optical modes was described by the conventional anharmonic phonon-phonon scattering model. In contrast, the low-frequency mode at 2.4 THz exhibited anomalous behavior, which can be interpreted as the contribution of phonon-electron scattering.

### [122] [Ethaline deep eutectic solvent under nanoconfinement: Unveiling structural and dynamical changes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07090)
*Kamar Mohammad Nadim,Mozhdehei Armin,Lefort Ronan,Moréac Alain,Ollivier Jacques,Appel Markus,Viviana Cristiglio,Denis Morineau*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用中子衍射和中子准弹性散射技术，探测了低共熔溶剂（deep eutectic solvents, DES）ethaline（氯化胆碱与乙二醇的混合物）在SBA-15（孔径约8.1 nm）和MCM-41（孔径约3.5 nm）二氧化硅介孔中的纳米限制效应。结果显示，受限态下ethaline保持结构均匀，分子动力学保留体相关键特征，平移扩散为跳跃扩散（jump-diffusion）机制，扩散系数接近体相值，但跳跃间的停留时间（residence time）和局域笼内运动（in-cage motion）的弛豫时间显著增加，孔径越小效应越显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将低共熔溶剂（DES）嵌入多孔载体或固液界面形成的杂化纳米材料在多种应用中展现出潜力，在此条件下，界面效应与空间限制可能影响DES的性能。因此，有必要系统性研究纳米限制（nanoconfinement）对DES结构与分子动力学的影响。

Method: 采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和准弹性中子散射（quasielastic neutron scattering, QENS）技术，分别表征了ethaline在SBA-15（孔径约8.1 nm）和MCM-41（孔径约3.5 nm）两种介孔二氧化硅中的结构与分子动力学行为。

Result: Ethaline在纳米限制下保持结构均匀，未观测到孔横截面内的核-壳分离（core-shell segregation）。分子动力学保留体相关键特征：平移扩散遵循跳跃扩散机制，扩散系数在SBA-15中接近体相值，在MCM-41中仅小幅降低；跳跃间停留时间（t0）在SBA-15中增加约3–8倍，在MCM-41中增加多达十倍；局域笼内运动弛豫时间（tL）在SBA-15中增加约20%，在MCM-41中增加约50%；分子轨迹大致保持，仅笼内运动振幅（intra-basin motional amplitudes）略有减小。

Conclusion: 纳米限制对ethaline的整体结构和主要动力学机制影响较小，但显著延长了分子跳跃间的停留时间与局域运动弛豫时间，且这一效应随孔径减小而增强。

Abstract: Hybrid nanomaterials incorporating deep eutectic solvents (DES) in porous hosts or at solid interfaces are gaining increasing attention for their potential interest across a wide range of applications. Under these conditions, the performances of DESs may be influenced by interfacial effects and spatial restrictions. In this study, we examined the effects of nanoconfinement on both the structure and molecular dynamics of the prototypical DES ethaline (a mixture of choline chloride and ethylene glycol) when confined within the cylindrical mesopores of SBA-15 (Dp $\approx$ 8.1 nm) and MCM-41 (Dp $\approx$ 3.5 nm) silicas, using neutron diffraction and quasielastic neutron scattering. It demonstrates that ethaline remains structurally homogeneous under confinement, showing no evidence of core-shell segregation within the pore cross-section. The molecular dynamics of the confined ethaline preserve the key characteristics observed in its bulk state. Translational diffusion follows a jump-diffusion mechanism, with diffusion coefficients that remain remarkably close to the bulk values, showing only a modest reduction in MCM-41. A more pronounced increase in the residence time t0 between translational molecular jumps is observed. It corresponds to roughly a factor of 3-8 under confinement in SBA-15, and reaches up to a tenfold enhancement in MCM-41 relative to bulk. Similarly, the characteristic relaxation time, tL, associated with the localized in-cage motion of ethaline, increases by approximately 20% in SBA-15 and up to 50% in MCM-41. However, the molecular trajectories, modeled from the elastic incoherent structure factor, remain largely preserved under confinement, showing only a marginal reduction in intra-basin motional amplitudes.

Conclusion: 氮化镓表面山丘结构的形貌主要由电子能量损失决定，而高温通过降低液态镓的粘度和表面张力进一步诱导穿透性纳米通道的形成，揭示了离子辐照下表面损伤的复杂多尺度动力学。

Abstract: This work systematically unveils the nanoscale surface damage dynamics in gallium nitride by investigating the atomistic mechanisms of hillock formation. The results identify two distinct hillock morphologies dependent on electronic energy loss (Se) values. Bell-shaped hillocks form under 18.2 keV/nm Kr irradiation, whereas crater-rim hillocks with central holes emerge under 40.2 keV/nm Ta irradiation. Microstructural analysis reveals that Ga-rich hillocks are accompanied by the generation of metastable zincblende nanodomains. These nanodomains preferentially aggregate around the periphery or sidewalls of the hillocks and exhibit a high spatial correlation with screw dislocations. Further temperature-dependent studies indicate that elevated temperatures significantly enlarge the overall dimensions of the hillock structures without altering their fundamental morphologies. Notably, under Ta irradiation above 1200 K, the high temperatures drastically reduce the viscosity and surface tension of liquid gallium. This enhanced fluidity of the transient molten phase promotes the formation of penetrating nanochannels.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Surface reconstructions induced by atomic adsorption can strongly reshape metallic surface states, providing a direct pathway to tune their electronic structure. Using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we investigate the electronic structure of Sb/Au(111) during the coverage-driven evolution from the clean Au(111) surface to the $(14\times14)$ and Rec$(3\times\sqrt{3})$ phases. In the Rec$(3\times\sqrt{3})$ phase, triangular Fermi pockets emerge at the Brillouin-zone boundary. Their momentum positions are consistent with a reciprocal-space folding construction, but their reduced size near the Fermi level indicates a modification of the Au-derived $sp$ dispersion. These results show that the electronic structure of Sb/Au(111) is governed by the interplay between reconstruction-induced Umklapp scattering and interfacial orbital hybridization, highlighting adsorbate-substrate hybridization as a key mechanism for tuning and engineering surface electronic structures.

### [125] [Terahertz Phase Inversion via Field-Free Spin-Orbit Torque Switching in an Antenna-Integrated Spintronic Heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07220)

Result: 在时域信号中直接观测到太赫兹相位反转；实现了微秒级电控太赫兹发射相位调制，速率可达兆赫兹（megahertz）量级；该无场操作显著降低了系统复杂度并大幅扩展了调制带宽。

Conclusion: 建立了电可编程的自旋电子太赫兹发射器，可作为紧凑、可扩展的平台用于集成片上太赫兹器件及超快应用，尤其适用于需要高速、精准控制太赫兹波形的相位敏感谱学（phase-sensitive spectroscopy）与近场成像（near-field imaging）。

Abstract: We demonstrate microsecond-timescale electrical control of the terahertz (THz) emission phase in broadband field-free spintronic THz emitters, enabling megahertz-rate phase inversion while overcoming the kilohertz limitations of conventional mechanical and field-driven approaches. Our device integrates an H-dipole antenna with a spintronic heterostructure exhibiting uniaxial magnetic anisotropy, enabling deterministic spin-orbit torque induced in-plane magnetization switching without external magnetic fields. The corresponding THz phase inversion is directly observed in the time domain signal, by applying $1\,μ\mathrm{s}$ electrical pulses on the bias striplines of the H-dipole. This field-free operation reduces system complexity while significantly extending modulation bandwidth. Our results establish electrically programmable spintronic THz emitters that could be used to develop a compact and scalable platform for integrated on-chip THz devices and ultrafast applications, including phase-sensitive spectroscopy and near-field imaging, where high-speed and precise control of THz waveforms is essential.

### [127] [Improving feature resolution and pore back effect in focused ion beam tomography of porous GaN thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07273)
*Ben Thornley,Thom R. Harris-Lee,Menno J. Kappers,Simon M. Fairclough,Rachel A. Oliver*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的聚焦离子束（focused ion beam, FIB）断层扫描方法，通过旋转实验使孔隙垂直于样品表面成像，并引入基于体素强度（voxel intensity）的形式化指标来量化并减轻多孔氮化镓（porous GaN）薄膜中的孔隙背效应（pore back effect），无需延长总实验时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔GaN是一种介孔晶体薄膜材料，在电子学和光电子学领域应用迅速扩展，但由于缺乏对孔隙形成电化学机理的理解和结构控制而发展受限；FIB断层扫描是表征孔隙形态的重要工具，但受到孔隙背效应（电子从孔隙后壁散射导致图像中出现不必要对比度）的严重干扰，且此前缺乏对该效应的系统性量化和评估方法。

Method: 提出一种改进的FIB断层扫描实验方法：将样品旋转，使孔隙垂直于样品表面成像；同时引入基于体素强度的新形式化指标，用于在单个特征和全数据集层面上评估孔隙背效应的影响。该方法需要更复杂的前期实验设置。

Result: 新方法能够在无需增加总实验时长的情况下，显著减轻多种孔隙形态的多孔GaN薄膜中的孔隙背效应。

Conclusion: 该方法可有效量化和减轻多孔GaN及类似介孔薄膜在FIB断层扫描中的孔隙背效应，有助于提升孔隙形态表征质量。

Abstract: Porous gallium nitride (GaN) is a mesoporous crystalline material, typically in the form of a thin film on an unlike substrate, prepared by electrochemically etching conductive GaN. The use of porous GaN in electronics and optoelectronics is rapidly expanding, but is held back significantly by a lack of structural control and understanding of the principles of pore formation from underlying electrochemical mechanisms, where high-quality characterisation of pore morphology is essential to understanding these principles. Focused ion beam (FIB) tomography is an invaluable tool for such characterisation, but is hindered greatly by the pore back effect, where unwanted contrast appears in an image due to electrons scattering out from the back wall of a pore. No major attempts to formally quantify or assess the extent of the effect for different tomography experiments has been demonstrated. In this work, we demonstrate an advanced methodology for performing FIB tomography on porous GaN thin films, where the experiment is rotated to image pores perpendicular to the surface of the sample, and introduce new voxel intensity-based formalisms for assessing the impact of the pore back effect based on voxel intensities for individual features and the whole dataset. The new approach, which requires more complex preliminary setup, is found to significantly mitigate the pore back effect in porous GaN thin films with a range of pore morphologies without increasing the total experimental duration. The pore back effect can thus be quantified and mitigated in FIB tomography of porous GaN and similar mesoporous thin films.

</details>


### [128] [Bayesian Optimization of Genetic Algorithm Hyperparameters in a Multi-Fidelity Framework for Efficient Lattice Material Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07289)
*Sergei Zorkaltsev,Maciej Haranczyk,Christina Schenk*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一个多保真度（multi-fidelity）框架，用于系统优化遗传算法（genetic algorithm, GA）超参数。该框架整合了三个保真度层级：用于验证的高保真快速傅里叶变换（FFT）均质化、用于快速性能评估的中保真3D卷积神经网络代理模型，以及在贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）框架内引导超参数搜索的低保真高斯过程（Gaussian process, GP）代理模型。实验表明，优化后的超参数配置能使25代的GA运行达到与完整75代优化相当的弹性模量值，同时将计算成本降低24%（从225小时降至171小时）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的遗传算法超参数调优往往依赖经验或穷举搜索，计算成本高昂且效率低下。本研究旨在通过多保真度框架系统化地优化GA超参数，在保持机械性能的前提下显著降低计算开销。

Method: 框架包含三个保真度层级：高保真FFT均质化用于验证、中保真3D卷积神经网络代理模型用于快速性能评估、低保真高斯过程代理模型嵌入贝叶斯优化框架以引导超参数搜索。采用多种采集函数（acquisition function），其中logNEI因有效处理GA评估中的噪声而表现最佳。此外引入了带惩罚项的贝叶斯优化目标函数，以权衡性能与所需评估的晶格数量。

Result: 优化后的超参数使25代GA运行达到与完整75代优化相当的弹性模量。惩罚目标函数在仅小幅降低弹性模量的情况下显著减少了所需晶格数量。优化配置消除了晶格突变（lattice mutation）的需求，总计算成本降低24%（从225小时降至171小时），且机械性能得以保持。

Conclusion: 多保真度优化作为GA超参数调优的一种高效且实用的方法，不仅实现了快速收敛和计算成本节约，还为未来的实验晶格设计研究提供了方法论基础。

Abstract: This study presents a multi-fidelity framework for the systematic optimization of genetic algorithm (GA) hyperparameters. The framework integrates three fidelity levels: high-fidelity Fast Fourier Transform (FFT) homogenization for validation, a medium-fidelity 3D convolutional neural network surrogate for rapid property evaluation, and a low-fidelity Gaussian process (GP) surrogate within a Bayesian optimization (BO) framework to guide the hyperparameter search. Various acquisition functions are evaluated, with logNEI achieving the best performance by effectively accounting for the noise inherent in GA evaluations. The proposed framework identifies hyperparameter configurations that enable a 25-generation GA run to achieve elastic modulus values comparable to those obtained in a full 75-generation optimization. Furthermore, introducing a penalized BO objective significantly reduces the number of required lattices with only minor decreases in absolute achieved elastic modulus, revealing a practical trade-off between performance and the number of structures that must be evaluated. High-fidelity FFT validation verifies the effectiveness of the surrogate-driven optimization strategy. The optimized hyperparameters allow for rapid convergence, eliminate the need for lattice mutation, and reduce the overall computational cost by 24% (from 225 to 171 hours) while preserving mechanical performance. These results demonstrate the potential of multi-fidelity optimization as an efficient and practical approach for GA hyperparameter tuning and future experimental lattice design studies.

Abstract: A topotactic phase transition involves the transformation of one crystalline solid to another, which may include the loss or gain of material, where the orientation of the parent crystal determines the orientation of the daughter. We set out an experimental approach, based on polyepitaxial thin film deposition, where the precise transformation mechanism in important physico-chemical processes can be revealed in brilliant detail. Here, we find a reversible topotactic transition from (001) cubic UO2 to a (130) orthorhombic U3O8 structure; a >35% expansion/contraction. Conclusion: 这些发现显著拓展了交错磁异质结的功能范围，为高度可扩展的交错磁存储器（altermagnetic memory）技术奠定了基础。

Abstract: Altermagnets, which combine antiferromagnetic-like magnetic compensation with ferromagnetic-like broken time-reversal symmetry, hold great promise for high-density and ultrafast spintronic applications. However, the detection and switching of perpendicular altermagnetic order are fundamentally constrained by magnetic symmetry, restricting both fundamental studies and practical implementation. We realize robust electrical reading and deterministic switching of perpendicular altermagnetic order by designing a Dirac semimetal/altermagnet heterostructure of PtTe2/CrSb. This engineered interface enables anomalous Hall readout via altermagnetic proximity effect and delivers efficient spin-orbit torque for manipulating the epitaxial perpendicular Neel vector in CrSb. ### [131] [Machine Learning Materials Properties by Encoding Orbital-Projected Density of States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07339)
*Paulo Pires,Pierre-Paul De Breuck,Mauro Fava,Hai-Chen Wang,Miguel A. L. Marques*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出在晶体性质预测的图神经网络（GNN）中，用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算得到的位投影轨道态密度（pDOS）指纹来增强原子节点特征，替代传统的静态元素描述符，在超导临界温度和光学介电常数预测任务中将误差降低22.9%和27.9%，效果接近训练集翻倍，并引入可解释的谱注意力门控机制揭示模型所学物理规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图神经网络（graph neural network）在预测材料性质时，原子节点的初始化特征通常依赖静态元素描述符（elemental descriptor），无法反映原子在晶体环境中的量子力学电子环境信息，这一问题并未得到充分关注。

Method: 从密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算中提取每个原子位点的投影轨道态密度（projected density of states, pDOS）作为指纹特征，与Pettifor元素嵌入（embedding）在消息传递（message passing）前进行融合；同时引入可解释的谱注意力门控机制（spectral attention-gating mechanism）分析模型所关注的轨道通道和能量窗口。

Result: 对于超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature $T_c$）和光学介电常数（optical dielectric constant $ε_{\infty}$），pDOS增强将预测误差分别降低22.9%和27.9%，提升幅度与训练集翻倍相当。但在Heusler化合物的磁交换能（magnetic exchange energy）这一小数据集中，提升效果减弱，表明pDOS增强在训练数据量超过pDOS特征向量长度时最为有效。

Conclusion: pDOS增强的图节点（graph node）是一种广泛适用的策略，能够将第一性原理电子结构知识注入图网络（graph network），为数据稀缺场景下的高精度性质预测提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Graph neural networks have become the dominant machine-learning architecture for predicting materials properties from crystal structures. Yet the initialization of atomic node features has received comparatively little attention, and conventional approaches rely on static elemental descriptors that carry no information about the quantum-mechanical electronic environment of each atom in its crystalline host. Here we show that augmenting atomic node representations with site-projected orbital density of states (pDOS) fingerprints, computed directly from density functional theory calculations, yields systematic and substantial improvements in predictive performance.These representations are fused with Pettifor elemental embeddings at each atomic site before message passing. For the superconducting critical temperature $T_c$ and the optical dielectric constant $ε_{\infty}$,the pDOS augmentation reduces prediction errors by 22.9% and 27.9%, respectively, relative to the elemental-descriptor baseline. These improvements are comparable to those achieved by doubling the training-set size. The gains are, however, contingent on training-set size. For the magnetic exchange energies of Heusler compounds, a substantially smaller dataset, the improvement is reduced,indicating that pDOS augmentation is most effective when the training data exceeds the length of the pDOS feature vector. We introduce an interpretable spectral attention-gating mechanism that reveals that the model autonomously learns to prioritize the orbital channels and energy windows most physically relevant to each target property. These results establish pDOS-augmented graph nodes as a broadly applicable strategy for infusing first-principles electronic-structure knowledge into graph networks, opening a practical route to high-accuracy property prediction in data-scarce regimes.

### [132] [Optimizing high-temperature electron mobility in single-crystal Bi$_2$O$_2$Se based on its unconventional dependence on concentration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07384)
*Antonín Sojka,Petr Knotek,Jan Zich,Martin Míšek,Roman Tesař,Kyo-Hoon Ahn,Petr Levinský,Jiří Navrátil,Pavlína Ruleová,Jiří Hejtmánek,Karel Knížek,Václav Holý,Čestmír Drašar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了准二维Bi₂O₂Se半导体中缺陷（尤其是替代型Se(Bi)缺陷）通过改变载流子有效质量（effective mass）来调控迁移率（mobility）的机制：富硒（Se-rich）条件下的缺陷会破坏Bi₂O₂通道、增大有效质量并引入空穴，导致迁移率降低；而贫硒（Se-poor）条件下的晶体更完整，迁移率更高。此外，单晶样品存在不均匀性，富硒条件会引入更多位错（dislocation）和杂相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bi₂O₂Se作为一种准二维半导体，在低温和低载流子浓度下展现出超高迁移率，但在300 K下迁移率平庸，且存在载流子浓度增加时迁移率反直觉上升的异常现象。先前研究已将其高迁移率归因于高介电常数（permittivity），但缺陷对迁移率的影响机制尚不明确。本文旨在阐明缺陷（尤其是本征缺陷）如何调控载流子有效质量，从而解释迁移率随浓度变化的反常行为。

Method: 通过对比富硒和贫硒两种生长条件下的Bi₂O₂Se单晶，结合载流子浓度与迁移率的实验关联，分析替代型Se(Bi)缺陷对电荷传输性能的影响。基于缺陷对有效质量（effective mass）的调控机制，将半导体转变为半金属（semimetal）并引入空穴（hole）参与传输。

Result: 富硒条件下出现的替代型Se(Bi)缺陷会破坏Bi₂O₂通道，增大载流子有效质量，将半导体转变为半金属并引入空穴，从而劣化电荷传输。富硒条件还导致更高的位错密度和杂相；单晶样品整体上存在不均匀性。相比之下，贫硒条件下晶体更完整，迁移率更高。

Conclusion: Bi₂O₂Se中载流子迁移率的反直觉增长源于缺陷对有效质量的调控。Bi₂O₂通道的完整性是保持高迁移率的关键，尤其对室温（room temperature）性能至关重要。这一发现为通过缺陷工程（defect engineering）优化准二维半导体材料的电荷传输性能提供了指导。

Abstract: Quasi-2D Bi$_2$O$_2$Se is part of an intensive materials research effort aimed at finding new semiconductors that outperform silicon-based electronics in terms of speed and power consumption. This material exhibits exceptionally high carrier mobility at low temperatures but mediocre mobility at 300 K. Its high mobility is generally associated with its high permittivity ($\varepsilon_r$~500), which is also associated with metallicity persisting down to very low carrier concentrations. This material exhibits a counterintuitive increase in carrier mobility as the concentration increases. The connection between low both carrier concentration and mobility in Se-rich conditions, and both high carrier concentration and mobility in Se-poor conditions suggests that the increase is related to native defects. We demonstrate that these defects can alter the effective mass of charge carriers. Specifically, substitutional Se(Bi) defects, which appear under Se-rich conditions, destroy the Bi$_2$O$_2$ channel and compromise charge transport properties. These defects increase the effective mass of charge carriers transforming the original semiconductor into a semimetal and introducing holes into charge transport. Additionally, we show that single crystals are generally inhomogeneous, particularly those grown under Se-rich conditions. Unlike Se-poor conditions, Se-rich conditions induce a higher concentration of dislocations and extraneous phases. These findings suggest that the perfection of the Bi$_2$O$_2$ channel is crucial for mobility, particularly at room temperature.

Motivation: 理解无序磁性合金的热力学性质需要对构型（化学、自旋等）和结构自由度进行统一处理，但现有计算框架无法同时涵盖这些耦合的无序类型。

Method: 提出一个通用框架，将机器学习模型（如图神经网络和机器学习原子间势，machine learning interatomic potentials）与统计采样方法（如蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）和分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations））相结合，用于研究合金中耦合的化学、自旋和结构无序。

Result: 在体心立方Fe-Co合金中，框架预测有序-无序相变温度为1,000 K，熔化温度为1,690 K，与实验测量值1,006 K和约1,700 K高度吻合。此外，框架还预测了Fe-Co-C合金中随温度升高发生的四方-近立方结构转变。

Conclusion: 该框架被证明是研究多无序合金的可靠工具，可应用于高熵合金（high-entropy alloys）、多铁性材料（multiferroics）和自旋电子器件（spintronic devices）等复杂无序体系。

Abstract: Understanding the thermodynamic properties of disordered magnetic alloys requires a unified treatment of configurational (chemical, spin, etc.) and structural degrees of freedom, which has remained beyond the scope of existing computational frameworks. Here we present a general framework that integrates machine learning models (such as graph neural networks and machine learning interatomic potentials) and statistical sampling methods (such as Monte Carlo and molecular dynamics simulations) to study the coupled chemical, spin, and structural disorder in alloys. We demonstrate the framework on body-centered-cubic Fe-Co alloys with interstitial carbon dopants, where the Fe-Co host exhibits intrinsic chemical and spin disorder, and the interstitial carbon introduces additional structural disorder through local lattice distortions, making the system a prototypical multi-disorder magnetic alloy. The framework predicts the order-to-disorder phase transition temperature and the melting temperature of Fe-Co alloy to be 1,000 K and 1,690 K, in excellent agreement with the experimentally measured values of 1,006 K and approximately 1,700 K, respectively. It also predicts the tetragonal-to-nearly-cubic structural transitions in Fe-Co-C alloy as temperature increases. These results establish the framework as a reliable tool for studying multi-disorder alloys, with applications to complex disordered systems such as high-entropy alloys, multiferroics, and spintronic devices.

Method: 论文提出了在局域轨道基组（localised orbital basis）中计算应力的方法，分别处理了精确对角化（exact diagonalisation）和线性标度（linear scaling）两类情况。在线性标度方法中，研究了应力随密度矩阵（density matrix）范围的收敛性，并将其与能量和力的收敛行为进行了对比。测试涵盖了不同带隙（band gap）的材料。

Conclusion: 本文成功在局域轨道基组的DFT框架内实现了应力的可靠计算，验证了其在精确对角化和线性标度方法中的有效性，并证明该方法可支持大规模、稳定的等温等压分子动力学模拟。

Abstract: We present the approach needed to calculate stress within density functional theory (DFT) using a localised orbital basis, both for exact diagonalisation and linear scaling approaches, and demonstrate our implementation within the large scale DFT code Conquest. For the linear scaling approach, we test the rate of convergence of stress with density matrix range, and compare it to the convergence of energy and forces for different materials with a range of band gaps. We show that excellent convergence is found for modest cutoffs, and show that large-scale isothermal-isobaric molecular dynamics is stable and accurate.

Method: 将线性化Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert (LLG) 方程表述为2×2非厄米本征值问题（non-Hermitian eigenvalue problem），从而推导出复共振频率、异常点条件（exceptional-point condition）以及稳定性阈值条件（stability-threshold condition）。

Result: 最大吸收响应可通过从稳定侧接近稳定性阈值来实现；阈值附近的吸收谱呈现强增强与线宽窄化，并表现出显著的手性依赖性（helicity dependence），可通过反转自旋轨道扭矩进行切换；跨越阈值则导致增益（gain）和自激振荡（self-oscillation）。

Conclusion: 稳定性阈值是亚THz/THz波段实现吸收增强和偏振选择性控制的关键控制原理。

Abstract: We study non-Hermitian antiferromagnetic resonance in an antiferromagnetic insulator/nonmagnetic metal junction with sublattice-dependent damping and spin-orbit torque. By formulating the linearized Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert (LLG) equation as a 2x2 non-Hermitian eigenvalue problem, we derive the complex resonance frequencies, the exceptional-point condition, and the stability-threshold condition. We show that the largest absorption response is maximized by approaching the stability threshold from the stable side. Near the threshold on the stable side, the absorption spectrum exhibits strong enhancement and linewidth narrowing, together with pronounced helicity dependence in the sub-THz regime that can be switched by reversing the spin-orbit torque. We also confirm by solving the full LLG dynamics that crossing the threshold leads to gain and self-oscillation. These results identify the stability threshold as the key control principle for enhancing absorption and achieving polarization selectivity in the sub-THz/THz regime.

Here, we report a study of human and LLM generated recipes for the synthesis of known and new materials. ### [140] [Acoustic-phonon-driven spin-lattice relaxation of the hBN boron vacancy in the sub-THz regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07642)

A microscopic understanding of spin relaxation in the high magnetic field regime remains elusive, as the relevant Zeeman transitions lie far below the optical phonon energies typically invoked to describe the relaxation process. Here, we apply an \textit{ab initio} acoustic mode spin-phonon relaxation theory to this problem and quantitatively reproduce the experimental magnetic field and temperature dependence of $T_1$ without empirical fitting parameters. ### [141] [Are Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials Truly Practical? A Benchmark of 23 Mainstream Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07647)
*Hanwen Kang,Tenglong Lu,Sheng Meng,Miao Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在低成本NVIDIA DGX Spark（128 GB本地内存，限制为80 GB以模拟普通实验室硬件）上，使用统一的基于ASE（Atomic Simulation Environment）的管线（pipeline），对23个主流开源MLIP进行基准测试。评估维度包括预测精度（predictive accuracy）、分子动力学（MD）模拟吞吐量（throughput）和原子可扩展性（atomic scalability）。

Conclusion: 单一维度的基准测试会误导领域发展方向；未来MLIP开发应将效率与可扩展性置于与精度同等重要的位置。

Abstract: Most MLIP benchmarks reward static accuracy while ignoring inference efficiency and hardware scalability -- driving model bloat with unclear real-world value. We benchmark 23 mainstream open-source MLIPs on a low-cost NVIDIA DGX Spark (128 GB native memory, capped at 80 GB to mimic ordinary lab hardware), using a fixed 192-atom system under a unified ASE-based pipeline. We evaluate three dimensions: predictive accuracy, MD simulation throughput, and atomic scalability. Our results expose a sharp accuracy-efficiency trade-off: large SOTA models deliver only 3-5 meV/atom more accuracy than lightweight ones, but lose orders of magnitude in throughput -- in the worst case, becoming only marginally faster than DFT itself. Lightweight MLIPs, by contrast, sit on the Pareto frontier and run on modest hardware. The lesson is that single-dimensional benchmarks mislead the field, and that future MLIP development should value efficiency and scalability alongside accuracy.

*Michael P. Path,Jeffrey McCord,Michael Vogel*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过深度卷积神经网络与基于物理可解释特征描述的神经网络推理相结合的方法，从单张高分辨磁光偏振图像中解码出磁性材料所受的外加磁场、温度及磁历史等多参数条件，证明磁畴纹理可作为外部条件的忠实记录，用于单图像多参数传感，并为复杂磁态的数据驱动研究奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在磁有序材料中，磁场和温度变化会通过耦合到局域能量景观来改变磁纹理（magnetic texture），在磁畴图案中留下独特指纹。然而，由于随机成核（stochastic nucleation）和磁滞（hysteresis）效应，磁畴形态（magnetic domain morphology）与外部刺激之间存在非线性、多变量且歧义性强的关系，使得从图案中恢复外部条件十分困难。

Method: 设计了一个受控的磁光推断实验（magneto-optical inference experiment），从掺铋钇铁石榴石薄膜（bismuth-substituted yttrium iron garnet film）的精细、高对比度、像素分辨的光学偏振图中重建磁场、温度和磁历史。采用深度卷积神经网络（deep convolutional neural networks），并辅以基于手工设计的、物理可解释描述符的特征驱动神经网络推断，从而将解码信息与材料依赖特征联系起来并探索其贡献。

Result: 实验结果表明，磁纹理能够作为外部条件的高保真记录，实现精确的单图像多参数传感（single image multiparametric sensing）。同时，通过揭示编码这些记录的物理可解释特征，为磁畴形成物理机制提供了新的认识。

Conclusion: 磁畴图案可作为一种忠实记录外部条件的载体，实现从单张图像中同时解码多个物理参数；该方法为数据驱动探索复杂磁态铺平了道路，并有助于深入理解磁畴形成的物理机制。

Abstract: In magnetically ordered materials, magnetic field and temperature variations modify the magnetic texture through their coupling to the local energy landscape, imprinting distinct fingerprints in the resulting magnetic domain patterns. Retrieving these conditions from the pattern remains challenging, as stochastic nucleation and hysteresis produce a nonlinear, multivariate, and ambiguous relationship between magnetic domain morphology and external stimuli. To decode these fingerprints, we designed a controlled magneto-optical inference experiment that reconstructs magnetic field, temperature, and magnetic history from a single fine-scale, high-contrast, pixel-resolved optical polarization map of feature-rich magnetic domain textures in a bismuth-substituted yttrium iron garnet film. Deep convolutional neural networks are complemented by feature-based neural-network inference using hand-crafted, physically interpretable descriptors of measured magneto-optical image data, linking the decoded information to material-dependent features and exploring their contributions. Together, these results establish magnetic texture as a high-fidelity record of external conditions enabling accurate single image multiparametric sensing and paving the way for data-driven explorations of complex magnetic states. Uncovering the physically interpretable features that encode this record sheds new light on the physics of magnetic domain formation.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [143] [The Positivity Geometry of Photon--Dark-Photon Effective Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06658)
*Sayantan Chakraborty,Yash Dadhwal,Arun M. Thalapillil*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了光子和无质量暗光子构成的完整八维有效场论中的正定性约束，通过修正的前向极限色散关系，解析地获得了线性和非线性弹性正定性界，揭示了光谱面体几何结构，并分析了这些约束对非前向振幅的影响以及暗物质紫外完备化场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）框架下，确保理论满足幺正性、因果性和解析性等基本物理原理要求正定性约束。对于同时包含光子和无质量暗光子的混合规范扇区，八维（dimension-eight）算符的结构更为复杂，需要系统性地推导其正定性条件。

Method: 采用修正的前向极限色散关系（modified forward-limit dispersion relation），对包含十二个CP偶（CP-even）Wilson系数和扩展螺旋度振幅（helicity-amplitude）结构的混合规范扇区进行解析分析，获得线性和非线性弹性正定性约束，并定义了光谱面体几何（spectrahedral geometry）。

Result: 推导出非平凡（non-trivial）的线性和非线性弹性正定性约束，这些约束共同定义了光谱面体几何结构。进一步分析了这些正定性界对非前向振幅（non-forward amplitudes）的限制作用。

Conclusion: 通过正定性约束，可以刻画有效场论在参数空间中的允许区域；动学混合（kinetic-mixing）和暗轴子门户（dark-axion-portal）的紫外完备化（UV completions）在该光谱面体几何中占据特定位置，揭示了不同紫外物理与低能正定性约束之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We derive positivity bounds on the complete dimension-eight effective field theory of photons and a massless dark photon. The mixed gauge sector contains twelve CP-even Wilson coefficients and an enlarged helicity-amplitude structure. Using a modified forward-limit dispersion relation, we analytically obtain non-trivial linear and non-linear elastic positivity constraints that define a spectrahedral geometry. We analyze implications of these bounds on non-forward amplitudes and discuss where kinetic-mixing and dark-axion-portal UV completions populate this geometry.

</details>


### [144] [Collins effect in pion-in-jet production in polarized $pp$ and $ep$ collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06821)
*Carlo Flore,Umberto D'Alesio,Marco Zaccheddu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了极化质子-质子和轻子-质子碰撞中喷注内π介子的Collins方位角不对称性。采用混合横动量依赖（hybrid TMD）方法，利用从半单举深度非弹性散射和正负电子湮没数据中提取的横向性（transversity）和Collins碎裂函数（Collins fragmentation function），在阶次和Weizsäcker-Williams近似下给出了电子-离子对撞机运动学下的预测。结果表明轻子-质子过程能更清晰地获取横向性分布，包括其海夸克成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Collins碎裂函数的普适性，并探索轻子-质子碰撞作为获取横向性分布（包括海夸克成分）的清洁探针的可行性。

Method: 采用混合横动量依赖（hybrid TMD）方法，对初态设置共线构型；利用从半单举深度非弹性散射（semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering）和正负电子湮没（e⁺e⁻ annihilation）数据中提取的横向性（transversity）和Collins碎裂函数（Collins fragmentation function）；在阶次（leading order）和Weizsäcker-Williams近似下进行预测。

Result: 在质子-质子碰撞中对STAR数据给出了良好描述，支持Collins函数的普适性；准实光子交换贡献显著，但不破坏夸克引发道的主导地位；轻子-质子过程能更清晰地获取横向性分布，包括其海夸克成分。

Conclusion: 轻子-质子碰撞中的π-in-jet Collins不对称性可作为研究横向性分布（尤其是海夸克组分）的清洁探针，验证了Collins碎裂函数的普适性，并为电子-离子对撞机（EIC）提供了可检验的理论预测。

Abstract: We study Collins azimuthal asymmetries for pion-in-jet production in polarized proton-proton and lepton-proton collisions. We adopt a hybrid transverse momentum dependent approach, with a collinear configuration for the initial state, and employ the transversity and Collins fragmentation functions extracted from semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering and $e^+e^-$ annihilation data. After recalling the good description of the STAR data in $pp$ collisions, which supports the universality of the Collins function, we present predictions for Electron-Ion Collider kinematics, both at leading order and by including the quasireal photon exchange in the Weizsäcker-Williams approximation. This contribution is sizable but does not spoil the dominance of quark-initiated channels. This implies that $\ell p$ processes allow for a clearer access to the transversity distribution, including its sea-quark component.

</details>


### [145] [Inclusive Charmless Non-Leptonic B Decays at NLO within and beyond the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07198)
*Stefan Meiser,Pol Morell,Angel Picazo,Javier Virto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory）框架下，计算了来自无粲（charmless）末态的全套超出标准模型（BSM）贡献对非轻子B介子寿命的影响，计算精度达到QCD的次领头阶（NLO）和重夸克展开（heavy-quark expansion）的领头幂次。通过计算切割图（cut diagrams）及对应的相空间积分，涵盖了双粒子、三粒子和四粒子切割的各种图。最后讨论了如何利用这些结果约束与半轻子和无粲非轻子衰变中观测到的反常相关的新的物理场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B介子衰变中的反常现象（anomalies）暗示可能存在超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理。现有对无粲非轻子衰变的研究缺乏系统的BSM贡献评估，因此有必要计算这些贡献并探讨其如何约束新物理场景。

Method: 在弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory）框架下，采用重夸克展开（heavy-quark expansion）到领头幂次，并计算至QCD次领头阶（next-to-leading order）。通过计算切割图（cut diagrams）及对应相空间积分（phase space integrals），处理了流-流（current-current）、企鹅-企鹅（penguin-penguin）、企鹅-偶极（penguin-dipole）和偶极-偶极（dipole-dipole）图，涉及双粒子、三粒子和四粒子切割。

Result: 获得了来自无粲末态的全套BSM贡献对包容性非轻子B介子寿命的修正结果，涵盖了各种类型的切割图，并描述了计算中遇到的技术难点。

Conclusion: 所得结果可用于约束与半轻子（semi-leptonic）和无粲非轻子（charmless non-leptonic）衰变中观测到的反常相关的新物理场景。

Abstract: We calculate the full set of BSM contributions to the inclusive non-leptonic $B$-meson lifetime from charmless final states within the framework of the Weak Effective Theory up to next-to-leading order in QCD and to leading power in the heavy-quark expansion. We do so by computing cut diagrams and the corresponding phase space integrals. This involves calculating current-current, penguin-penguin, penguin-dipole and dipole-dipole diagrams with two-, three- and four-particle cuts. We describe the technical difficulties of the computation. We then discuss how our results can be used to constrain new physics scenarios related to the anomalies observed in semi-leptonic and charmless non-leptonic decays.

</details>


### [146] [Double quarkonium production in hadronic collisions at fixed-target experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07312)
*Carlo Flore,Cristian Pisano*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对固定靶实验中（非）极化强子对撞的双夸克偶素（double quarkonium）产生，提出了新结果。研究结合了横动量依赖因子化（transverse momentum dependent factorization）与颜色单态模型（Color-Singlet Model），给出了夸克-反夸克（$q\bar q$）诱导道的截面角结构的新解析表达式，并为CERN和LHC的现有及未来固定靶实验提供了非极化截面和横向单自旋不对称性（transverse single-spin asymmetries）的预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双夸克偶素产生过程是检验量子色动力学（QCD）因子化框架和重夸克偶素产生机制的重要探针。固定靶实验提供了独特的运动学区域（如大$x$区域），能够对横动量依赖因子化等理论框架进行更严格的检验。

Method: 采用横动量依赖因子化（transverse momentum dependent factorization）框架，结合颜色单态模型（Color-Singlet Model），对$q\bar q$诱导的硬散射过程进行微扰计算，推导了截面角结构的解析表达式。

Result: 获得了$q\bar q$诱导道的双夸克偶素产生截面角结构的新解析表达式；给出了非极化截面和横向单自旋不对称性（transverse single-spin asymmetries）对于CERN与LHC的当前及未来固定靶实验的理论预言。

Conclusion: 该工作为固定靶实验中的双夸克偶素产生提供了新的理论预言，有助于利用未来实验数据对横动量依赖因子化框架和颜色单态模型进行直接检验。

Abstract: We present new results for double quarkonium production in (un)polarized hadronic collisions at fixed-target experiments. Our approach incorporates the transverse momentum dependent factorization in combination with the Color-Singlet Model. We present new analytical expressions for the angular structure of the cross section for the $q\bar q$-induced channel, and provide predictions for the unpolarized cross section and transverse single-spin asymmetries for present and future fixed-target experiments at CERN and the LHC.

</details>


### [147] [Single inclusive hadron and jet production in lepton-hadron scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07664)
*Jian-Wei Qiu,Kazuhiro Watanabe*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在联合QCD+QED因子化（joint QCD+QED factorization）框架下，首次计算了轻子-强子散射中大横动量单举强子与喷注产生过程。散射截面被因子化为红外安全的硬系数函数与轻子分布函数（LDFs）、部分子分布函数（PDFs）及碎裂函数（FFs）的卷积，并推导了相应的DGLAP演化方程。文章还给出了一组默认的LDFs，并讨论了从未来数据中提取普适非微扰LDFs的策略，最后展示了在杰斐逊实验室（Jefferson Lab）和未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）能量下的计算结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在轻子-强子散射的高横动量过程中，精确的唯象学描述需要同时考虑QCD与QED的联合效应，但此前尚无此类完整计算。本文旨在填补这一空白，为未来实验提供理论预言，并为提取普适的轻子分布函数（LDFs）奠定基础。

Method: 采用联合QCD+QED因子化方法，将散射截面分解为红外安全的硬系数函数与轻子分布函数（LDFs）、部分子分布函数（PDFs）及碎裂函数（FFs）的卷积。DGLAP型演化方程中的演化核同时包含QCD和QED贡献。此外，推导了一组默认的LDFs，并提出了从实验数据中提取普适非微扰LDFs的策略。

Result: 在杰斐逊实验室（Jefferson Lab）和未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的能量下，给出了单举强子和/或喷注产生的计算结果。

Conclusion: 联合QCD+QED因子化框架能够有效地描述轻子-强子散射中的大横动量强子与喷注产生过程，未来可通过实验数据提取普适的非微扰轻子分布函数（LDFs），从而进一步检验和约束理论模型。

Abstract: We present the first calculation of single inclusive hadron and jet production at large transverse momentum in lepton-hadron scattering in a joint QCD+QED factorization approach. The scattering cross section is factorized into a convolution of infrared-safe hard coefficient functions with universal lepton distribution functions (LDFs) and parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the colliding lepton and hadron, respectively, together with fragmentation functions (FFs) of the observed hadron (or jet). With joint QCD+QED factorization, the DGLAP-type evolution equations for LDFs, PDFs, and FFs necessarily have evolution kernels calculated in both QCD and QED. We derive a default set of LDFs for our calculations and discuss a strategy to extract universal, non-perturbative LDFs from future data. We present our calculations for single inclusive hadron and/or jet production at the energies of Jefferson Lab and the future Electron-Ion Collider.

</details>


### [148] [Higgs boson mass and thermal wino dark matter from Starobinsky supergravity with the MSSM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07193)
*Daniel Frolovsky,Alexander Belyaev,Sergei V. Ketov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个连接宇宙微波背景（CMB）可观测量与高能粒子现象学的理论框架，基于Starobinsky超引力（supergravity）与最小超对称标准模型（MSSM）的耦合。宇宙暴胀（cosmic inflation）和超对称（SUSY）破缺均发生在源自Starobinsky超引力的隐扇区中。暴胀标度确定了隐扇区的特征质量标度，进而通过引力中介（gravitational mediation）确定MSSM软破缺项（soft terms）。同一隐扇区还能动态产生高标度μ项。由此得到的MSSM能谱确定了希格斯四次耦合（Higgs quartic coupling）的高标度阈值修正和重整化群（RG）演化的边界条件。三圈RG演化给出的希格斯玻色子质量与测量值在理论和实验不确定度内一致，从而将原初标量扰动振幅与希格斯玻色子质量联系起来。在R字称（R-parity）守恒下，最轻超对称粒子（LSP）稳定，成为有说服力的暗物质候选者。观测到的遗迹丰度（relic abundance）选择了一个近乎纯热中微子（thermal wino），其物理质量约为3 TeV。其圈诱导的自旋无关中微子-核子散射截面低于LUX-ZEPLIN实验当前灵敏度，但在下一代多吨级液氙探测器的预期探测范围内。电弱辐射修正（electroweak radiative corrections）导致带电和中性中微子态之间产生小质量劈裂，产生长寿命带电中微子和特征性的消失径迹（disappearing-track）信号。未来的100 TeV质子对撞机可以探测到来自3 TeV中微子的消失径迹信号，或完全排除这一热中微子暗物质方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论框架未能将宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测与高能粒子物理现象充分联系起来，尤其是暴胀与超对称破缺的起源及其对暗物质和希格斯质量等可观测量的影响缺乏统一解释。本文旨在提出一个连接CMB可观测量与高能粒子现象学的统一框架。

Method: 将Starobinsky超引力与最小超对称标准模型（MSSM）耦合，暴胀和超对称破缺均源于同一隐扇区；暴胀标度固定隐扇区特征质量标度，通过引力中介确定MSSM软破缺项；同一隐扇区动态生成高标度μ项；利用三圈重整化群（RG）演化计算希格斯四次耦合，确定希格斯玻色子质量；通过遗迹丰度约束确定暗物质候选者（热中微子），并评估其探测前景。

Result: 三圈RG演化给出的希格斯玻色子质量与测量值在理论和实验不确定度内一致，建立了原初标量扰动振幅与希格斯玻色子质量之间的关联。在R字称守恒下，最轻超对称粒子（LSP）稳定，观测到的遗迹丰度选择了一个近乎纯热中微子，物理质量约3 TeV。其圈诱导的自旋无关中微子-核子散射截面低于LUX-ZEPLIN实验当前灵敏度，但在下一代多吨级液氙探测器的预期范围内。电弱辐射修正导致带电和中性中微子态之间的质量劈裂，产生长寿命带电中微子和消失径迹信号。未来100 TeV质子对撞机可探测该信号或排除热中微子暗物质方案。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功将CMB观测与高能粒子现象学联系起来，通过暴胀标度与MSSM参数之间的确定关系，同时解释希格斯质量、暗物质遗迹丰度和对撞机可观测信号。该热中微子暗物质方案可通过下一代液氙直接探测实验和未来100 TeV质子对撞机进行检验或排除。

Abstract: We propose a framework connecting cosmic microwave background (CMB) observables with high-energy particle phenomenology, based on Starobinsky supergravity coupled to the Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (MSSM). Cosmic inflation and supersymmetry (SUSY) breaking occur within the hidden sector emerging from Starobinsky supergravity. The inflationary scale fixes the characteristic mass scale of the hidden sector, which determines the MSSM soft terms through gravitational mediation of SUSY breaking. The same hidden sector can also dynamically generate a high-scale $μ$ term. The resulting MSSM spectrum fixes the high-scale threshold corrections and the boundary conditions for the renormalisation-group (RG) evolution of the Higgs quartic coupling. Three-loop RG evolution of the Higgs quartic coupling gives a Higgs boson mass consistent with the measured value within the theoretical and experimental uncertainties, thereby linking the amplitude of primordial scalar perturbations to the Higgs boson mass. With conserved R-parity, the lightest supersymmetric particle is stable, making it a compelling dark matter candidate. The observed relic abundance selects a nearly pure thermal wino with a physical mass of about 3 TeV. Its loop-induced spin-independent wino-nucleon scattering cross section lies below the current sensitivity of the LUX-ZEPLIN experiment, but within the projected reach of next-generation multi-ton liquid-xenon detectors. Electroweak radiative corrections generate a small mass splitting between the charged and neutral wino states, leading to a long-lived charged wino and the characteristic disappearing-track signature. A future 100 TeV proton collider can discover the disappearing-track signal from a 3 TeV wino or fully exclude this thermal wino dark matter scenario.

</details>


### [149] [Anomaly Realization in Charge-Flux Detector Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06667)
*João Barata,Ratmir Jumanov,Andrey V. Sadofyev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子反常（quantum anomalies）如何连接理论的高能（紫外, ultraviolet）与低能（红外, infrared）区域，具体通过轴向荷流（axial-charge-flow）观测量的角度分布和求和规则来展示非对易极限与反常控制的有限积分和规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示量子反常如何作为桥梁连接理论的高能属性与低能区，并通过轴向荷流观测量具体展示这一连接机制。

Method: 以轴向荷探测器探测反常三角图（anomalous triangle）的费米子割线（fermionic cut），分析质量为零的极限与角度积分之间的非对易性；进一步引入更高自旋螺旋度（higher-spin helicity, zilch）探测器，研究轴向反常控制的能量加权求和规则；并扩展到混合轴向-引力（mixed axial-gravitational）通道。

Result: 无质量极限与角度积分不交换：固定角度的贡献被抑制后，会坍缩到两个束流共线方向（beam-collinear directions），同时保留由轴向反常（axial anomaly）确定的有限积分求和规则。类似局域化机制与有限zilch流求和规则在混合轴向-引力通道中同样成立。

Conclusion: 量子反常通过非对易极限和奇异局域化机制在轴向荷流及其高自旋推广（zilch流）观测量的红外区保持有限求和规则，并可能推广到更一般态和多点关联函数（multipoint correlators）。

Abstract: Quantum anomalies provide a bridge between ultraviolet properties of a theory and its infrared sector. We study how this connection appears in axial-charge-flow observables. In the simplest example, an axial-charge detector probes the fermionic cut of the anomalous triangle and resolves its infrared content as an angular distribution. The massless limit does not commute with the angular integration: a contribution suppressed at fixed angle collapses onto the two beam-collinear directions while retaining the finite integrated sum rule fixed by the axial anomaly. We then replace the axial-charge detector by higher-spin helicity (zilch) detectors and study a family of axial-anomaly-controlled energy-weighted sum rules for the corresponding fluxes. We further show that the same singular localization mechanism and finite zilch-flux sum rules persist in the mixed axial-gravitational channel. We briefly comment on extensions to more general states and multipoint correlators.

</details>


### [150] [Particle Cosmology: 1980-2000](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06811)
*Edward W. Kolb*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了20世纪最后二十年（1980-2000年间）粒子宇宙学（Particle Cosmology）这一新领域的诞生与发展，重点围绕1984年在费米实验室举行的“内空间/外空间”会议和1994年举行的“下一个千年的粒子与核天体物理学”Snowmass夏季研究这两个标志性事件展开讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回顾粒子宇宙学作为基本粒子物理（elementary particle physics）与宇宙学（cosmology）交叉领域在1980-2000年间的发展历程，通过两个关键事件梳理该领域的形成脉络。

Method: 采用历史综述（historical review）方法，以1984年费米实验室“内空间/外空间”会议和1994年Snowmass夏季研究“下一个千年的粒子与核天体物理学”为主要线索，对这一时期粒子宇宙学的发展进行梳理和评述。

Result: 识别并阐述了粒子宇宙学领域在1980-2000年间通过两次关键学术活动得以确立和发展的历史过程。

Conclusion: 粒子宇宙学作为基本粒子物理与宇宙学交叉产生的新领域，在20世纪最后二十年经历了重要发展，而1984年和1994年的两次学术会议是这一发展历程中的标志性事件。

Abstract: A new field, \emph{Particle Cosmology}, emerged at the interface of elementary particle physics and cosmology in the last two decades of the 20th century. In this chapter of the \emph{Proceedings of the 4th International Symposium on the History of Particle Physics, the Standard Model and Beyond} I will review the development of Particle Cosmology in the period 1980-2000 centered on two events: a conference, \emph{Inner-Space/Outer-Space} held at Fermilab in May 1984 \cite{kolb1986innerspace} and the 1994 Snowmass Summer Study \emph{Particle and Nuclear Astrophysics in the Next Millennium} \cite{kolb1995particle}.

### [151] [First constraint on Born-rule violations at high-energy colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06938)
*Antony Valentini,Mira Varma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过PEP对撞机在质心能量29 GeV下的大角度Bhabha散射数据，对玻恩规则（Born rule）的可能违背给出了实验约束，在95%置信水平上设定高斯涂抹宽度参数ε的上限为0.042，该界限对应于角分辨实验中两倍bin宽度的涂抹范围，具有物理意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能对撞机中对玻恩规则（Born rule）的可能违背给出实验约束。玻恩规则是量子力学（quantum mechanics）中概率解释的核心，其实验检验对于量子力学基础具有重要意义。

Method: 将玻恩规则违背建模为微分散射截面（differential scattering cross section）$dσ/dΩ$在角度变量$x=\cosθ$上受到宽度为ε的窄高斯涂抹（angular smearing）；利用PEP对撞机在质心能量$\sqrt{s}=29\,\mathrm{GeV}$下的大角度Bhabha散射（$e^{+}e^{-} \rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}$）实验数据进行分析。

Result: 在95%置信水平上得到高斯涂抹宽度参数ε的上限为ε<0.042，该值对应于实验角分辨bin宽度两倍的角涂抹范围。

Conclusion: 所获得的界限为玻恩规则（Born rule）的偏离提供了具有物理意义的实验约束，并讨论了未来改进该极限的途径。

Abstract: We obtain an experimental constraint on possible Born-rule violations at high-energy colliders. We model Born-rule violations with differential scattering cross sections $dσ/dΩ$ subject to an angular smearing by a narrow Gaussian of width $\varepsilon$ (with respect to $x=\cosθ$ for scattering angle $θ$). For large-angle Bhabha ($e^{+}e^{-} \rightarrow e^{+}e^{-}$) scattering, at a centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s}=29\, \mathrm{GeV}$, data from the PEP collider at SLAC allow us to set an upper bound of $\varepsilon<0.042$ at $95\%$ confidence. This corresponds to a Gaussian smearing over an angular range of twice the experimental bin width, and hence provides a physically meaningful limit on deviations from the Born rule. Future prospects for improving this limit are discussed.

</details>


### [152] [Algebraic Structure of Three-Flavor Neutrino Oscillations in Constant-Density Matter: Cayley--Hamilton Evolution, DMP Resummation, and Closed-Form Uncertainty Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07213)
*Aaryan Chaulagain,Anju Dhakal,Daya Nidhi Chhatkuli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Cayley-Hamilton定理给出了常密度物质中三味中微子振荡演化算符的二次多项式闭式解，解释了DMP近似（精度优于10⁻⁴）的本质是重求和（resummation），并扩展至开放系统退相干与CP不对称性的解析处理，最终提供了NuFIT 6.0参数基下的闭式雅可比矩阵（Jacobians）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为三味中微子振荡在常密度物质中提供严格的解析闭式解，克服迭代求解器在参数连续性（parameter continuity）、透明极限（transparent limits）和闭式雅可比矩阵方面的不足。

Method: 利用Cayley-Hamilton定理将演化算符强制为哈密顿量（$\hat{H}$）的二次多项式，系数由Vandermonde系统从三个实本征值得出；本征值通过Cardano三角公式求解以恢复Zaglauer–Schwarzer表达式。采用密度矩阵（density-matrix）形式结合Lindblad项处理开放系统退相干（decoherence）与波包效应（wave-packet effects）。CP不对称性$\mathcal{A}_{\rm CP}(ν_μ\toν_e)$被拆分为真实贡献与物质诱导的赝贡献。

Result: DMP近似中1–3转动本质上是重求和，消除了在$\hat{A}\to 1$处使朴素展开失效的近简并性（near-degeneracy），将无界的$(1-\hat{A})^{-1}$替换为均匀有界的有效参数$ε_0\lesssim 0.015$，从而获得优于$10^{-4}$的分数精度。物质修饰的相干长度满足$L/L^{ij}_{\rm coh}\sim 10^{-3}$–$10^{-2}$（对地面基线）。闭式雅可比矩阵在Feldman–Cousins轮廓似然（profile-likelihood）映射检验中得到验证。

Conclusion: Denton–Parke NuFast-LBL算法仍是生产级拟合的首选工具，但本文提供的闭式解析表达式能够提供迭代求解器无法给出的参数连续性、透明极限和闭式雅可比矩阵。

Abstract: For three-flavor neutrino oscillations in constant-density matter, the Cayley--Hamilton theorem forces the evolution operator into a quadratic polynomial in $\hat{H}$, with coefficients determined by the three real eigenvalues through a Vandermonde system we write out explicitly. The eigenvalues follow from Cardano's trigonometric formula, recovering the Zaglauer--Schwarzer expressions. The Denton--Minakata--Parke (DMP) approximation achieves fractional accuracy better than $10^{-4}$ because its $1$--$3$ rotation is a resummation: it removes the near-degeneracy that makes the naive expansion diverge at $\hat{A}\to 1$, replacing the unbounded $(1-\hat{A})^{-1}$ with an effective parameter $ε_0\lesssim 0.015$ bounded uniformly in energy. A density-matrix treatment with a Lindblad term handles open-system decoherence and wave-packet effects in the same language; matter-dressed coherence lengths satisfy $L/L^{ij}_{\rm coh}\sim 10^{-3}$--$10^{-2}$ for terrestrial baselines. The CP asymmetry $\mathcal{A}_{\rm CP}(ν_μ\toν_e)$ is split into genuine and matter-induced fake contributions. Closed-form Jacobians in the NuFIT~6.0 parameter basis feed Monte Carlo and linearized uncertainty-propagation schemes, the latter validated against a Feldman--Cousins profile-likelihood mapping near physical boundaries. The Denton--Parke NuFast-LBL algorithm [Phys.\ Rev.\ D {\bf 110}, 073005 (2024)] remains the tool of choice for production fits; the analytic expressions here supply what iterative solvers cannot -- parameter continuity, transparent limits, and Jacobians in closed form.

</details>

### [153] [Majorana physics in a Luttinger liquid with attractive interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06751)
*Francesco Debortoli,Nitya Cuzzuol,Luca Barbiero,Fabian Grusdt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明在粒子数守恒、无能隙的Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquid）中，马约拉纳边缘物理（Majorana edge physics）的迹象仍然存在；通过两点关联函数（two-point correlator）可观察到边缘到边缘的回归（edge-to-edge revival），其符号依赖于费米子数宇称（fermion-number parity）。该回归在热力学极限下稳健，并存在于激发态和不同填充率中。此外，提出基于超冷偶极分子或原子的光晶格实现方案，为超越传统有能隙超导体的马约拉纳物理实验开辟了路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）通常出现在不守恒粒子数的有能隙平均场模型（如Kitaev链）中。本文旨在探索在粒子数守恒、无能隙的相互作用系统中是否仍能保留马约拉纳边缘物理的特征信号，从而拓展马约拉纳物理的适用范围。

Method: 考虑自旋less费米子（spinless fermions）的短程吸引相互作用Luttinger液体，通过分析两点关联函数诊断边缘到边缘回归现象，并引入粒子-空穴配对波函数（particle-hole ansatz）描述奇数费米子数基态。还提出了超冷偶极分子或原子光晶格实验方案，利用分束器干涉测量（beam-splitter interferometry）检测回归信号。

Result: 两点关联函数揭示出边缘到边缘的回归，其符号取决于费米子数宇称；该回归在热力学极限下稳健，并可在激发态和不同填充率下观测到。粒子-空穴ansatz在自由费米子极限和强相互作用马约拉纳区间均能有效描述系统。

Conclusion: 马约拉纳边缘物理可以在粒子数守恒、无能隙的Luttinger液体中稳健存在，突破了传统有能隙超导体范式的限制。提出的光晶格实验方案为在冷原子系统中实现和探测马约拉纳物理提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Majorana zero modes are the hallmark of topological superconductivity. In one-dimensional systems, these zero modes are usually introduced in the context of gapped, mean-field models that do not conserve particle number, such as the Kitaev chain. By non-locally encoding a conventional fermion across spatially separated Majorana zero modes, these systems become inherently immune to local decoherence. In this work, we show that signatures of Majorana edge physics persist in a number-conserving, gapless Luttinger liquid of spinless fermions with short-range attractive interactions. We identify the two-point correlator as a sharp diagnostic, revealing an edge-to-edge revival whose sign depends on the fermion-number parity. This revival is robust in the thermodynamic limit, and persists in the excited states of the system and at different fillings. A simple particle-hole ansatz for the ground state of the system with an odd number of fermions captures the physics of the system for a wide range of interaction strengths, interpolating between the free-fermion limit and the strongly interacting Majorana regime. Finally, we propose a concrete protocol to realize this model with ultracold dipolar molecules or atoms in an optical lattice, and to detect the revival via beam-splitter interferometry, opening an experimental route to Majorana physics beyond the conventional gapped-superconductor paradigm.

</details>


### [154] [A low-energy effective Hamiltonian for Landau quasiparticles: II Application to the contact Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07041)
*Pierre-Louis Taillat,Hadrien Kurkjian*

TL;DR: 本文基于先前发展的新重整化方案（renormalization scheme），将其应用于低温原子费米气体（atomic Fermi gas），通过恢复已知微扰结果（如Lee-Huang-Yang展开、Galitskii展开、Gor'kov-Melik Barkhudarov预指数修正）验证了重整化理论，进而发现零声速（zero sound）的预指数修正，并发展了一种高效数值方法求解输运方程以研究碰撞到流体动力学（hydrodynamic regime）的交叉行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用新重整化方案处理短程相互作用仅由s波散射长度（s-wave scattering length）a参数的低温原子费米气体；通过恢复已知微扰结果进行基准测试；在二阶a修正下研究输运动力学；开发精确数值方法求解输运方程。

Result: 成功恢复了费米气体的静态性质已知微扰结果，包括状态方程的Lee-Huang-Yang展开、动量分布的Galitskii展开以及临界温度的Gor'kov-Melik Barkhudarov预指数修正；发现了零声速中存在二阶a修正的预指数修正；开发了精确求解输运方程的数值方法并应用于密度和极化响应函数（polarisation response functions）从碰撞到流体动力学（collisionless to hydrodynamic regime）的交叉研究。

Conclusion: 新重整化方案在低温原子费米气体中得到了有效验证，不仅能恢复已知微扰结果，还发现了新的预指数修正，同时所发展的数值方法为研究输运交叉行为提供了高效工具。

Abstract: This article follows up on arxiv:2511.15938, in which we developed a new renormalization scheme to construct a quantized theory of Fermi liquids. Here, we apply this formalism to a low-temperature atomic Fermi gas where the short-range interactions are fully parametrized by the s-wave scattering length $a$. We benchmark our renormalized theory by recovering known perturbative results on the static properties of the Fermi gas, such as the Lee-Huang-Yang expansion of the equation of state, the Galitskii expansion of the momentum distribution, and the Gor'kov- Melik Barkhudarov preexponential correction to the critical temperature. We then turn to the transport dynamics and demonstrate the presence of a preexponential correction to the speed of zero sound when including corrections of second order in $a$. Finally, we develop an efficient numerical method to solve the transport equation exactly, and we apply to study the crossover from the collisionless to the hydrodynamic regime in the density and polarisation response functions.

### [155] [Wall tension of a Bose-Einstein condensate: Effects of quantum fluctuations and finite-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07203)
*Pham Duy Thanh,Nguyen Van Thu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过修正的Gross-Pitaevskii方程，研究了量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）和有限程相互作用对零温玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）基态与壁张力（wall tension）的影响，发现量子涨落使凝聚体硬化、密度分布变窄并提升壁张力，而有限程修正则降低壁张力，两种超越平均场效应在特定条件下可相互抵消。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子涨落和有限程原子间相互作用对BEC基态和壁张力的影响，以理解超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）的物理效应，并寻找通过壁张力精密测量实现实验探测的途径。

Method: 采用修正的Gross-Pitaevskii方程（modified Gross-Pitaevskii equations）对零温下的BEC系统进行理论研究，纳入量子涨落与有限程相互作用的修正。

Result: 量子涨落使凝聚体在硬壁附近硬化，密度分布变窄，壁张力在平均场值基础上增加一个正比于气体参数平方根（square-root of the gas parameter）的量；有限程修正总是相对于量子涨落修正值降低壁张力；在稀薄区域存在壁张力的排序关系 γ₀ < γ_II < γ_I，并找到了两种超越平均场贡献相互抵消的交叉条件（crossover condition）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过超冷玻色气体中壁张力的精密测量来探测超越LHY（beyond-LHY）物理提供了实验上可行的途径。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of quantum fluctuations (QFs) and finite-range interatomic interactions on the ground state and wall tension of a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) at zero temperature by means of modified Gross-Pitaevskii equations. The QFs are shown to stiffen the condensate near the hard wall, narrowing the density profile and raising the wall tension above its mean-field value by an amount proportional to square-root of the gas parameter. Finite-range corrections always reduces the wall tension relative to the QFs correction value regardless of the effective range. We find the ordering $γ_0 < γ_{\rm II} < γ_{\rm I}$ in the dilute regime and identify a crossover condition under which the two beyond-mean-field contributions mutually cancel. These results provide an experimentally accessible way for probing beyond-LHY physics through precision measurements of the wall tension in ultracold Bose gases.

### [156] [Evaporation-Driven Nanowire Self-Assembly in an Elongated Droplet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06794)
*Johannes Schöttner,Qingguang Xie,Jens Harting*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过介观尺度格子玻尔兹曼模拟，研究了含纳米线的细长液滴在浸润性图案化基底上的干燥过程，发现液滴几何形状、纳米线间吸引力及纳米线长度对沉积形态和电学连通性有重要影响，为印刷电子中的形貌与导电性协同优化提供了设计指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 印刷电子制造中，含纳米线的细长液滴干燥是常见工艺，其沉积图案直接影响器件性能。然而，目前对蒸发驱动沉积的物理理解多基于均匀基底上的球形液滴，难以预测和控制实际打印场景中的沉积形貌。本研究旨在弥合这一认知差距。

Method: 采用介观尺度的格子玻尔兹曼模拟（lattice Boltzmann simulation），研究含纳米线的细长液滴在浸润性图案化基底上的干燥过程，重点关注液滴几何形状、纳米线间相互作用及纳米线长度的影响。

Result: 细长液滴几何形状会内在引致最终沉积物的轴向和横向不均匀性。增大纳米线间有效吸引力（模拟表面化学或溶剂条件变化）可改善电学连通性，但会导致团簇化和局部有序化，降低结构均匀性。增大纳米线长度则可同时提升长程连通性和沉积均匀性。

Conclusion: 研究结果为在蒸发驱动的印刷电子中平衡电学输运与结构均匀性提供了设计指导。

Abstract: Drying of nanowire-laden elongated droplets is a ubiquitous process in printed electronics fabrication, where the resulting deposition pattern critically determines device performance by controlling nanowire alignment, connectivity, and percolating charge-transport pathways. However, the physical understanding of evaporation-driven deposition is still largely derived from studies of spherical droplets on homogeneous substrates. This gap limits the ability to predict and control deposit morphology in realistic printing scenarios. Here, we use mesoscale lattice Boltzmann simulations to investigate the drying of nanowire-laden elongated droplets on wettability-patterned substrates, focusing on the effects of droplet geometry, nanowire interactions, and nanowire length. The elongated droplet geometry is found to intrinsically induce distinct axial and transverse inhomogeneities in the final deposit. Increasing the effective attraction between nanowires, which mimics changes in surface chemistry or solvent conditions, can improve electrical connectivity but also promotes clustering and local ordering, reducing structural uniformity. In contrast, increasing nanowire length yields a dual benefit by improving long-range connectivity while simultaneously enhancing deposit homogeneity. Our findings provide design guidance for balancing electrical transport and structural uniformity in evaporation-driven printed electronics.

</details>


### [157] [Density-Induced Reentrant Coarsening in a Two-Temperature System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07113)
*Partha Sarathi Mondal,Anish Kumar,Nayana Venkatareddy,Prabal K. Maiti,Shradha Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过布朗动力学模拟和粗粒化场论模型，发现双温度系统中的相分离（phase separation）会展现出密度诱导的重入粗化行为（reentrant coarsening），其特征畴尺寸生长指数随密度增加呈现 t^{1/3} → t^{1/4} → t^{1/3} 的重入序列，中间密度区因输运瓶颈导致异常缓慢生长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡驱动（nonequilibrium driving）如何改变相分离动力学仍是一个基本挑战，作者旨在揭示双温度系统中密度如何调控粗化路径。

Method: 采用布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）和粗粒化场论模型（coarse-grained field-theoretic model）进行研究。

Result: 特征畴尺寸呈 $L(t)\sim t^{1/z}$ 生长，随密度增加呈现出重入序列 $(t^{1/3} \rightarrow t^{1/4}\rightarrow t^{1/3})$；低密度和高密度区受经典曲率驱动的体扩散（curvature-driven bulk diffusion）支配，中间密度区则表现出异常缓慢生长。

Conclusion: 中间密度区缓慢生长源于粒子扩散率、粒子可用性和附着动力学（attachment kinetics）之间相互作用导致的输运瓶颈（transport bottleneck），抑制了畴间有效质量流；在双温度驱动下，密度成为粗化路径的关键控制参数，这与平衡相分离（equilibrium phase separation）中密度主要影响形态和交叉尺度不同。

Abstract: Understanding how nonequilibrium driving modifies phase-separation kinetics remains a fundamental challenge. Here we show that phase separation in a two-temperature system exhibits a striking density-induced reentrant coarsening behavior. Using Brownian dynamics simulations and a coarse-grained field-theoretic model, we find that the characteristic domain size grows as $L(t)\sim t^{1/z}$, displaying a reentrant sequence $(t^{1/3} \rightarrow t^{1/4}\rightarrow t^{1/3})$ with increasing density. While the low- and high-density regimes are governed by classical curvature-driven bulk diffusion, the intermediate-density regime exhibits anomalously slow growth. We show that this slowdown originates from a transport bottleneck arising from the interplay of particle diffusivity, particle availability, and attachment kinetics, which suppresses the effective mass flux between domains. Unlike equilibrium phase separation, where density primarily affects morphology and crossover scales, the two-temperature drive renders density a key control parameter for coarsening pathways. Our results uncover a nonequilibrium mechanism for anomalous domain growth in two-temperature systems.

</details>


### [158] [Competing ferroelectric and smectic order: modulated structures through molecular design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07346)
*Grant J. Strachan,Ewa Górecka,Jadwiga Szydłowska,Damian Pociecha*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过分子工程系统性调控极性序与位置序之间的平衡，从而直接控制极性和调制液晶相的形成机制，为设计功能性铁电软材料提供通用策略。

Method: 通过系统改变分子结构（包括芳香核的自分离、末端链长度、氟化分子片段的空间分布以及纵向偶极相互作用强度），研究一系列同系液晶化合物的相行为与相稳定性。

Result: 强纵向偶极相互作用会通过惩罚层内分子偶极的平行排列而去稳定正交SmAF和SmAAF相；分子倾斜可有效缓解偶极挫拆，使倾斜铁电SmCF相在整个同系列中保持稳定；微相分离与静电相互作用可稳定具有非公度电子密度波的新型调制SmCM相；对于长链同系物，通过调控氟化片段分布和链长可形成破层型调制极性相（2D/3D）。

Conclusion: 极性序与位置序之间的平衡可通过分子工程系统性调控，为功能铁电软材料的设计提供了通用且灵活的策略。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the balance between polar and positional order can be systematically tuned through molecular engineering, providing direct control over the emergence of polar and modulated liquid-crystalline phases, allowing for versatile strategy for the design of functional ferroelectric soft materials. We show that polar orthogonal smectic phases (SmAF and SmAAF), promoted by the self-segregation of aromatic cores and sufficiently long terminal chains, are readily destabilized by strong longitudinal dipolar interactions that energetically penalize parallel alignment of molecular dipoles within a smectic layer. In contrast, the tilted ferroelectric SmCF phase is remarkably robust across the entire homologous series, indicating that molecular tilt efficiently relieves dipolar frustration within the smectic layers. We further demonstrate that the interplay between microsegregation and electrostatic interactions stabilizes the new modulated SmCM phase, characterized by incommensurate electron-density waves, particularly for compounds with short terminal chains. For longer homologs controlling the spatial distribution of fluorinated molecular fragments and terminal-chain length enabled the targeted formation of broken-layer-type modulated polar phases (2D or 3D).

### [159] [Hyperuniform systems are maximally irreversible](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07411)
*Mathias Casiulis,Satyam Anand,Stefano Martiniani*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了超均匀（hyperuniform）系统自组装的能量代价，发现超均匀态在所有被考察的噪声粒子系统中均表现为最大不可逆性，以熵产生率（entropy production rate）量化，并通过路径积分（path integral）公式从微观动力学推导出熵产生率，建立长程结构与时间不可逆性之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超均匀系统（hyperuniform systems）作为非平衡自组装（non-equilibrium self-assembly）的范式，其自组装机制已被广泛研究，但自组装过程中的能量学（energetics）尚未被探索。这引出一个基本问题：自组装一个超均匀系统的能量代价是什么？本文旨在回答这一问题。

Method: 研究跨越了软物质（soft matter）和机器学习（machine learning）中的多个噪声粒子系统（noisy particle systems），通过调节噪声相关性（noise correlations）诱导超均匀性。利用熵产生率（entropy production rate）量化不可逆性，并发展了一个从微观动力学出发的路径积分公式（path integral formulation）来推导熵产生率。

Result: 尽管不同系统具有截然不同的微观动力学，但所有系统中均发现一个普适行为：超均匀态（hyperuniform states）是最大不可逆的（maximally irreversible），这一性质由熵产生率量化。路径积分公式成功解释了观测结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立了涌现的长程结构（emergent long-range structure）与时间不可逆性（time irreversibility）之间的直接联系，为探测超均匀自组装（hyperuniform self-assembly）的能量代价开辟了新途径，该自组装过程在物理学、生物学和材料科学中普遍存在。

Abstract: Hyperuniform systems, defined by the anomalous suppression of large-scale density fluctuations, are a paradigm of non-equilibrium self-assembly. While mechanisms underlying the self-assembly of hyperuniform states have been widely studied, the energetics of this process remain unexplored. This raises a fundamental question: what is the energetic cost of self-assembling a hyperuniform system? Here, we address this question across several noisy particle systems drawn from soft matter and machine learning, in which hyperuniformity can be induced by tuning noise correlations. Despite their distinct microscopic dynamics, we uncover a universal behavior across all systems: hyperuniform states are maximally irreversible, as quantified by the entropy production rate. Further, we develop a path integral formulation of the entropy production rate directly from the microscopic dynamics, which explains our observations. Our work establishes a direct link between emergent long-range structure and time irreversibility and opens a new avenue of probing the energetic cost of hyperuniform self-assembly, ubiquitous across physics, biology, and materials science.

### [160] [Time-state superposition in non-equilibrium fluidized granular matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07645)
*Marlo Kunzner,W. Till Kranz,Matthias Sperl,Jan Philipp Gabriel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过空气流化颗粒床（air-fluidized granular bed）的小振幅振荡剪切实验，发现其线性粘弹性响应在不同流化状态下遵循时间-状态叠加原理（time-state superposition principle），证明驱动颗粒物质的流变学与分子玻璃形成液体之间存在直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒材料虽本质上是非热（athermal）且强驱动的系统，却能展现出类似玻璃的动力学行为；然而，其流变学是否适用于与分子玻璃相同的标度（scaling）概念仍是一个未解决的问题。

Method: 采用小振幅振荡剪切（small-amplitude oscillatory shear）方法，在广泛的流化状态范围内测量空气流化颗粒床的线性粘弹性响应，并将频率依赖的光谱通过状态依赖的弛豫时间（state-dependent relaxation time）进行平移缩放。

Result: 频率谱通过状态依赖的弛豫时间平移后坍缩为一条主曲线（master curve），建立了类似于分子玻璃中时间-温度叠加（time-temperature superposition）的时间-状态叠加原理；该主曲线跨越超过五个数量级的弛豫时间，并由Cole-Davidson弛豫谱定量描述；通过连续剪切测量对比，发现摩擦起电（tribocharging）是导致偏离普适标度的历史依赖性偏差的起源。

Conclusion: 流化作用主要重新标度单一的 structural relaxation time，同时保持弛豫谱不变，从而在驱动颗粒物质的流变学和分子玻璃形成液体之间建立了直接联系。

Abstract: Despite being intrinsically athermal and strongly driven, granular materials can exhibit remarkably glass-like dynamics. Whether their rheology can be described by the same scaling concepts remains an open question. Here, we investigate the linear viscoelastic response of an air-fluidized granular bed using small-amplitude oscillatory shear over a broad range of fluidization states. We show that the frequency-dependent spectra collapse onto a single master curve when shifted by a state-dependent relaxation time, establishing a time-state superposition principle analogous to time-temperature superposition in molecular glasses. The master curve spans more than five decades in relaxation time and is quantitatively described by a Cole-Davidson relaxation spectrum. By comparison with continuous shear measurements, we identify tribocharging as the origin of history-dependent deviations from universal scaling. Our results demonstrate that fluidization primarily rescales a single structural relaxation time while preserving the underlying relaxation spectrum, establishing a direct connection between the rheology of driven granular matter and molecular glass-forming liquids.

</details>


### [161] [Ordering and Defect Dynamics in Passive and Active Nematopolars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07656)
*Fabio Aprile,Massimiliano Semeraro,Giuseppe Gonnella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了一个干性向列-极性（nematopolar）系统的最小单场模型，揭示了极性与向列相互作用竞争导致的去极化弦（depolarization strings）、非单调弦介导相互作用、运动诱导的电荷对称性破缺（motility-induced charge symmetry breaking）以及粗化停滞（arrested coarsening）等丰富现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性与向列相互作用的共存广泛存在于生物和合成活性系统（active systems）中，产生丰富的非平衡集体行为现象，但其理论理解仍面临挑战。本文旨在通过引入一个最小单场模型，系统地研究这类系统中相序（phase ordering）与缺陷动力学（defect dynamics）的基本机制。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究一个面向干性向列-极性系统（dry nematopolar systems）的最小单场模型。该模型在自由能中引入竞争性的极性与向列贡献，并通过自平流项（self-advection contribution）实现活性。

Result: 在极性与向列对准的最佳平衡下，系统形成连接半整数缺陷的去极化弦和闭合的去极化环，缺陷对与环展现出非单调的弦介导相互作用和不同的环塌缩路径。从无序态出发，特征长度按∼(t/ln t)^(1/2)动态标度。强活性导致运动诱导的电荷对称性破缺，即正整数缺陷与负半整数缺陷共存，并引起特征长度饱和与粗化停滞。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解生物与合成向列-极性系统中的序与缺陷动力学提供了一个简单统一的框架。

Abstract: The coexistence of polar and nematic interactions, observed in a broad range of biological and synthetic active systems, gives rise to a rich phenomenology that continues to challenge our theoretical understanding of non-equilibrium collective behaviour. In this paper, we numerically investigate phase ordering and defect dynamics in a newly introduced minimal single-field model for dry nematopolar systems, where competing polar and nematic contributions enter the free energy, and activity is implemented through a self-advection contribution. At optimal balance between the two alignments, the system develops depolarization strings connecting half-integer defects and separating domains with opposite polarization, together with closed depolarization loops. We first characterize the elementary relaxation mechanisms of defect pairs and loops, showing that the interplay between polar and nematic alignment gives rise to non-monotonic string-mediated interactions, finite equilibrium separations and distinct loop-collapse pathways. Large-scale simulations from disordered states instead show dynamic scaling with a characteristic length growing as $\sim(t/\ln t)^{1/2}$, consistent with coarsening in systems with non-conserved order parameters and point-like defects. Upon introducing self-advection, sufficiently strong activity leads to the coexistence of positive integer and negative half-integer defects, which we term motility-induced charge symmetry breaking, and to saturation of the characteristic length scales, ultimately resulting in arrested coarsening. Overall, our results provide a simple unified framework for understanding the ordering and defect dynamics in biological and synthetic nematopolar systems.

</details>
