### [162] [Physically consistent formulation for the bound vortex sheet strength in the Wagner model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06884)
*George L. S. Torres,Ashok Gopalarathnam,Flávio D. Marques*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文针对非定常薄翼理论（unsteady thin-airfoil theory, UTAT）中涡面强度在尾缘不连续导致的数学不一致性问题，提出了一种基于瓦格纳问题（Wagner problem）的物理一致的有环涡面强度（bound vortex-sheet strength）公式。通过推导瓦格纳系数的递推关系，构建了均匀收敛的级数展开式，确保有环涡面与尾迹涡面之间的连续性并恢复尾缘零载荷条件，从而实现了非定常库塔条件（unsteady Kutta condition）的数学一致表达。基于该框架的离散涡方法（discrete-vortex method）消除了尾缘附近的伪振荡行为，显著改善了涡量和压力分布的正则性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非定常库塔条件（unsteady Kutta condition）通常与尾缘零载荷条件相关联，但其对涡面强度（vortex-sheet strength）连续性的影响尚未被充分研究。经典非定常薄翼理论中有环涡量（bound vorticity）的级数展开在尾缘处非均匀收敛，导致涡面和压力分布出现数学不一致性。

Method: 推导了瓦格纳系数（Wagner coefficients）的递推关系，构建了有环涡面强度（bound vortex-sheet strength）的均匀收敛级数展开式。基于改进框架开发了离散涡方法，并与经典公式进行了对比验证。

Result: 所提出公式同时保证了有环涡面与尾迹涡面之间的连续性以及尾缘零压力载荷条件。数值结果表明，该方法消除了尾缘附近的伪振荡行为，显著改善了涡量和压力分布的正则性。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架为非定常库塔条件（unsteady Kutta condition）提供了数学一致的表征，提升了非定常薄翼理论（unsteady thin-airfoil theory）在降阶气动建模（reduced-order aerodynamic modeling）中的物理一致性和数值稳定性。

Abstract: Unsteady thin-airfoil theory (UTAT) coupled with discrete-vortex methods has been widely employed in reduced-order aerodynamic modeling. Due to the non-uniqueness of potential-flow solutions, the Kutta condition is imposed to determine the circulation around the airfoil. Although the unsteady Kutta condition is commonly associated with the zero-loading condition at the trailing edge, its implications for the continuity of the vortex-sheet strength remain comparatively underexplored. In particular, the classical series expansion employed for the bound vorticity in unsteady thin-airfoil theory is not uniformly convergent at the trailing edge, leading to mathematical inconsistencies in the vortex-sheet and pressure distributions. In this context, the present work seeks to advance the mathematical framework of unsteady thin-airfoil theory through a physically consistent formulation of the bound vortex-sheet strength for the Wagner problem. A recurrence relation is derived for the Wagner coefficients, allowing the construction of a uniformly convergent series expansion for the bound vorticity. The proposed formulation ensures continuity between the bound and wake vortex sheets while simultaneously recovering zero pressure loading at the trailing edge, thereby providing a mathematically consistent representation of the unsteady Kutta condition. To investigate the implications of the modified framework, a discrete-vortex method based on UTAT is developed and compared with the classical formulation. The results demonstrate that the proposed approach eliminates spurious oscillatory behavior near the trailing edge and significantly improves the regularity of the computed vorticity and pressure distributions.

</details>


### [163] [Interaction of vortex rings generated by two unsynchronised drop impacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07214)
*Anna A. L. Huttunen,Guilherme Moreira Bessa,Matilda Backholm*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究了两滴不同时下落的水滴撞击水面后形成的涡环（vortex ring）的相互作用，发现根据时间差（Δt）的不同，存在四种截然不同的涡环演化类别，并指出这些差异可由首个水滴产生的毛细波（capillary wave）解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际场景中相邻两滴液滴极少完全同时撞击液面，但前人研究仅关注同步或单滴撞击形成的涡环，尚未探究非同步双滴撞击下两涡环的相互作用机制。

Method: 实验使用两滴水滴以不同时间差（Δt）撞击水面，并利用粒子图像测速法（particle image velocimetry, PIV）定量测量涡环随时间演化的速度场。

Result: 根据Δt大小识别出四类演化模式：Δt<0.5 ms时发生完全对称合并；0.5<Δt<7 ms时合并变为不对称且不完全；7≤Δt<80 ms时第二个涡环的生成受到抑制；Δt≥80 ms时两涡环互不影响。首个水滴产生的毛细波是导致这些不同演化 regimes 的关键因素。

Conclusion: 滴落时间差对相邻双滴涡环的形成与相互作用至关重要，该发现对高通量应用中实现均匀可控的混合具有重要意义。

Abstract: A liquid drop falling into a deep pool can create a vortex ring at the right impact conditions. Such drop-formed vortex rings are of importance in nature and technology and the dynamics of rings created by single and synchronised double drop impacts have been extensively studied. In practice, two neighbouring drops rarely impact a liquid surface exactly at the same time, yet the interaction of two unsynchronised vortex rings have not been studied. Here, we have performed experiments with two water drops impacting a water pool at varying time differences $Δt$. By using particle image velocimetry, we have quantified the time-evolution of the resulting vortex rings. We find four distinct categories of vortex ring evolution depending on $Δt$. At $Δt<0.5$ ms, fully symmetric merging of the vortex rings occur. An unsynchronisation larger than this drastically influences the collision and merging, which either becomes asymmetric and incomplete ($0.5 < Δt<7$ ms) or does not happen at all ($Δt \geq 7$ ms). At $7 \leq Δt<80$ ms, the creation of the second vortex ring is impaired, whereas at $Δt\geq 80$ ms, the first impact no longer affects the formation of the second ring and eventually the two rings evolve without influencing each other. We show that these different regimes can be explained by the capillary waves created by the first droplet. Our results demonstrate the importance of the time difference between drop impacts in the creation and subsequent interaction of two adjacent drop-formed vortex rings, which is important for achieving uniform and controlled mixing in high-throughput applications.

</details>

### [164] [Anomalous Hall and Nernst effects driven by static and fluctuating spin chiralities on Kagome lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06966)
*He-Lin Li,Zhen-Gang Zhu,Gang Su*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛模拟结合紧束缚模型，系统区分了二维Kagome晶格中静态手性（通过动量空间贝里曲率）与动态手性涨落（通过实空间自旋涨落）对反常霍尔效应和反常能斯特效应的不同贡献，揭示了从磁性有序相到临界涨落区的输运机制转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在阻挫磁性系统中，静态与动态标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）对反常输运现象的具体贡献尚未被清晰区分，本文旨在理论层面厘清二者在Kagome晶格中的作用机制。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations），并结合通过s-d交换相互（s-d exchange interaction）作用的紧束缚哈密顿量（tight binding Hamiltonian），显式计算了反常输运系数。

Result: 将宏观响应系统分解为两部分：由静态手性诱导的动量空间贝里曲率（Berry curvature）主导的内禀（intrinsic）贡献，以及由实空间动态自旋涨落驱动的外禀（extrinsic）散射贡献。在斯格明子晶体（skyrmion crystal）等磁有序相中，内禀贝里曲率主导输运；而在有序-无序临界区，热涨落抑制静态非共面自旋构型，使动态手性涨落成为主导机制。

Conclusion: 通过划定静态手性与涨落手性各自主导的相区间，阐明了阻挫磁性系统中反常输运的不同微观机制，为理解相关材料中的输运行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the anomalous Hall and Nernst effects (AHE and ANE) in a two dimensional Kagome lattice to uncover the distinct roles of static and fluctuating scalar spin chi ralities. Employing Monte Carlo simulations incorporating with a tight binding Hamiltonian via the s-d exchange interaction, we explicitly evaluate the anomalous transport coefficients. A key finding is the systematic disentanglement of the macroscopic responses into an intrinsic contribu tion, governed by momentum space Berry curvature induced by static chirality, and an extrinsic skew scattering contribution driven by real space dynamical spin fluctuations. We demonstrate a pronounced mechanistic crossover: deep in magnetically ordered phases like the skyrmion crystal, the intrinsic Berry curvature dictates the transport behavior. However, approaching the magnetic order-disorder critical regime, strong thermal fluctuations disrupt static noncoplanar spin configu rations, drastically suppressing intrinsic responses. Here, dynamical chiral fluctuations emerge as the dominant driving force. By delineating the phase regimes governed by static versus fluctuating chiralities, this work elucidates the distinct microscopic mechanisms dictating anomalous transport in frustrated magnetic systems.

### [165] [Ab initio thermodynamic statistical modeling of the miscibility gap and the metal-insulator phase transition in SrTi$_{1-x}$V$_x$O$_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07067)
*Luka Wibmer,Chiara Ostendorf,Dominik Spath,Christoph Heil,Pedro N. Ferreira,Markus Aichhorn*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 替代合金 SrTi₁₋ₓVₓO₃ 在带绝缘体 SrTiO₃ 与关联金属 SrVO₃ 之间插值，其成分驱动的金属-绝缘体转变兼具 Mott 物理（Mott physics）与局域化学无序的起源。先前的第一性原理研究只能使用单独超胞，无法处理热无序固溶体，因为相同成分的不同构型会表现出截然不同的电子性质。

Method: 采用广义准化学近似处理合金，这是一种热力学自洽的统计框架，其中每个性质都被表示为所有对称不等价团簇（symmetry-inequivalent clusters）的系综平均（ensemble average），权重由最小化吉布斯混合自由能（Gibbs mixing free energy）的发生概率决定。将团簇系综与动力学平均场理论结合，追踪费米能级处态密度；同时将团簇分类为金属性或绝缘体并在简单立方格点上进行位点逾渗（site percolation）分析。

Result: 从混合热力学得到临界温度为 1443 K 的不混溶间隙，与实验证据一致。动力学平均场理论下的关联谱函数重现了转变过程：在 x<0.3 左右为绝缘体，x=1 附近为金属，而密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）单独预测所有 x>0 均为金属。位点逾渗分析显示在 x≈0.4 附近出现系统范围导通的陡峭 onset。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个热力学自洽的构型平均框架，可推广到更广泛的关联材料（correlated materials）类别。

Abstract: The substitutional alloy SrTi$_{1-x}$V$_x$O$_3$ interpolates between the band insulator SrTiO$_3$ and the correlated metal SrVO$_3$, exhibiting a composition-driven metal--insulator transition whose origin combines Mott physics with local chemical disorder. Previous first-principles studies relied on individual supercells, which cannot capture the thermally disordered solid solution, since configurations of identical composition can display very different electronic properties. Here we treat the alloy within a generalized quasi-chemical approximation, a thermodynamically consistent statistical framework in which every property is obtained as an ensemble average over all symmetry-inequivalent clusters, weighted by occurrence probabilities that minimize the Gibbs mixing free energy. This provides a well-defined procedure to average over different supercells, and places the structural and electronic descriptions on an equal footing. From the mixing thermodynamics we obtain a miscibility gap with a critical temperature of 1443 K, consistent with experimental evidence. Combining the cluster ensemble with dynamical mean-field theory, we track the density of states at the Fermi level across the full composition range: whereas density-functional theory alone predicts a metal for all $x>0$, the correlated spectral function reproduces the transition, evolving from insulating below $x\approx0.3$ to metallic near $x=1$. Finally, classifying clusters as metallic or insulating and performing site percolation on a simple cubic lattice yields a sharp onset of system-spanning conduction near $x\approx0.4$. These results establish a thermodynamically consistent, configuration--averaged framework applicable to the broader class of correlated materials.

Method: 以代表性三维拓扑绝缘体Bi₂Se₃为研究对象，在圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）照射下应用Floquet理论（Floquet theory），通过数值计算分析单光子共振导致的能带杂化与拓扑结构变化。

Result: 在中等频率区间，由原始能带与单光子共振Floquet能带（one-photon-resonant Floquet bands）之间的杂化（hybridization）介导，产生了四对Floquet-Weyl点，且这些点保持晶体结构的三重旋转对称性（threefold rotational symmetry）。通过空穴掺杂（hole doping）调节化学势，可获得与这些Floquet-Weyl点直接关联的巨反常霍尔电导（large anomalous Hall conductivity）。

Abstract: Quantum materials exhibit exotic phases and electronic responses under irradiation by circularly polarized light, which breaks time-reversal symmetry and generates Floquet replica bands. Recently, Floquet topological states arising from direct resonances have attracted much attention, e.g., the emergence of Floquet-Weyl points at a one-photon resonance, rather than topological features within the modulated original bands via high-frequency expansion. In this study, we investigate the effects of a one-photon resonance in a representative three-dimensional topological insulator, Bi$_2$Se$_3$, applying Floquet theory under circularly polarized light. We find that four pairs of Floquet-Weyl points emerge in the intermediate-frequency regime, mediated by hybridization between the original and one-photon-resonant Floquet bands, preserving the threefold rotational symmetry of the crystalline structure. Our numerical calculations demonstrate that tuning the chemical potential via hole doping yields a large anomalous Hall conductivity, directly associated with these Floquet-Weyl points. This work provides a highly accessible route toward the experimental realization of one-photon-resonant Floquet-Weyl semimetals.

### [167] [Critical SO(5) scaling of entanglement entropy at honeycomb lattice deconfined criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07248)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 多数情况下系统的标度行为与临界系统一致，但六边形子系统的反常振荡表明DQCP在六角晶格上可能存在更复杂的纠缠结构，需要进一步理解振荡起源及其对临界性判定的影响。

Abstract: The deconfined quantum critical point (DQCP) in square lattice S=1/2 quantum antiferromagnets has been extensively studied with a large body of evidence pointing to a weakly first-order transition scenario. Recent studies, which focused on entanglement at this nearly continuous DQCP in square lattice J-Q models, have observed conflicting bipartite entanglement entropy (EE) scaling behavior. One bipartition choice gave scaling coefficients in remarkable agreement with predictions from the unitary CFT corresponding to the putative DQCP. While another equally natural choice gave scaling coefficients in complete violation of unitary CFT that may be attributed to lack of scale invariance at the known weakly first-order behavior of the model. This motivates the exploration of DQCP behavior via entanglement measures in lattice models with distinct crystalline symmetries. Here we study a S=1/2 honeycomb model that hosts a nearly continuous transition between Néel and valence-bond-solid ground states relevant to probing DQCP. Using large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we compute the Rényi EE for a variety of bipartitions and test the CFT based description of the DQCP on the honeycomb lattice. For smooth bipartitions, we find no evidence of logarithmic corrections, in accordance with CFT, thereby essentially ruling out contributions from Goldstone modes. For subsystems with corners, CFT predicts universal logarithmic contributions, which we extract for corners with 60 and 120 degree angles and find close agreement with an emergent SO(5) CFT. While we observe scaling consistent with a critical system in the majority of cases, we also demonstrate an intriguing counterexample of the hexagon subsystem that exhibits a subtle period three oscillation. This results in three separate finite-size series, where the sign of the logarithmic term apparently changes depending on the series.

However, BaFe2Se3 had a T^3/2 dependence in electrical resistivity and a negative magnetoresistance. This suggested that BaFe2Se3 had non-Fermi-liquid properties near the insulator-metal transition. Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments showing pressure-induced suppression of magnetic order and the emergence of a dynamical ground state in the anisotropic kagome antiferromagnet Y-kapellasite Y3Cu9(OH)19Cl8, we perform ab initio density functional theory (DFT)calculations to investigate the evolution of magnetic exchange interactions under hydrostatic pressure. Our results provide a microscopic explanation for the experimentally observed pressure-induced enhancement of frustration and highlight the key role of hydrogen geometry.

### [172] [Quantitative DFT+DMFT description of spectra and transport in the moderately correlated metal SrVO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07378)
*Gurshidali P.,N. S. Vidhyadhiraja*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于DFT+DMFT框架，采用实频多轨道迭代微扰论（MO-IPT）杂质求解器，对典型中等关联金属SrVO₃的光谱及输运性质（直流电阻率、光导率）进行定量计算，发现仅需单个准粒子权重即可在全部实验（ω, T）范围内获得与实验一致的结果，表明该体系中自能k依赖性较弱且顶角修正可能不主导输运行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联材料的光谱与输运性质的定量、物材特异性描述，是关联电子理论长期面临的核心挑战。尽管DFT+DMFT已成为同时处理电子关联效应与物材特异性的有力框架，但在实际材料中能否在不引入复杂修正的情况下统一描述光谱与输运性质仍待检验。

Method: 采用DFT+DMFT结合实频多轨道迭代微扰论（MO-IPT）杂质求解器，对SrVO₃的简并t₂g活性空间进行单粒子谱、直流电导率（dc conductivity）和光导率（optical conductivity）的计算，并考察准粒子权重（quasiparticle weight）作为单一控制参数时的预测能力。

Result: MO-IPT方案在完整的实验（ω, T）范围内，以统一的单参数（准粒子权重）描述，获得了与dc电阻率和光导率实验测量合理一致的结果；该一致性不依赖于具体相互作用参数，只要准粒子权重保持恒定。

Conclusion: 对于SrVO₃，自能（self-energy）的k依赖性可能较弱，且顶角修正（vertex corrections）在dc和光学输运中可能不起主导作用。这表明该体系的低能性质可由有效质量（effective-mass）描述充分刻画。

Abstract: A quantitative, material-specific account of spectral and transport properties remains a central challenge in the theory of strongly correlated materials. Combining density functional theory with dynamical mean-field theory (DFT+DMFT) has proven to be a powerful approach for treating electron correlation effects and material specificity on an equal footing. Here, we examine the single-particle spectra and the dc and optical conductivity of SrVO$_3$, a prototypical, moderately correlated metal, within this framework. The degenerate $t_{2g}$ active space of SrVO$_3$, together with its well-established Fermi-liquid behavior, admits an effective-mass description governed by a single quasiparticle weight, yielding a nearly universal picture of the low-frequency, low-temperature regime. Employing a computationally efficient, real-frequency multi-orbital iterative perturbation theory (MO-IPT) impurity solver, we find reasonable agreement with experimental measurements of dc resistivity and optical conductivity across the entire experimentally relevant $(ω, T)$ range within a single, unified scheme. The agreement is shown to not depend on specific interaction parameters provided the quasiparticle weight is kept constant. These results indicate that, in SrVO$_3$, the $\mathbf{k}$-dependence of the self-energy may be weak, and vertex corrections may not dominate the dc and optical transport in this material.

</details>


### [173] [Crossover and Changeover in Spin-1 Kitaev-$Γ$ Chain with Uniaxial Single-ion Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07501)
*Qiang Luo,Shijie Hu,Wang Yang,Yuhai Liu,Jinbin Li,Jize Zhao,Xiaoqun Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）和玻色化（bosonization）分析，研究了自旋-1 Kitaev-Γ链中单轴单离子各向异性（SIA）驱动的量子相变与交叉行为，发现负SIA下从一阶相变到SU(2)₂ Wess-Zumino-Witten连续相变的转变，中心荷c=3/2，属于缺乏连续对称性系统中的罕见实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 键方向自旋链（bond-directional spin chains）的最新进展揭示了大量涌现现象（emergent phenomena）和非常规临界性，但自旋-1 Kitaev-Γ链中单轴单离子各向异性（uniaxial single-ion anisotropy, SIA）对量子相变与交叉行为的影响尚不清楚，亟需系统性研究。

Method: 采用大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）数值计算结合玻色化分析（bosonization analysis），通过调节SIA强度系统研究自旋-1 Kitaev-Γ链的基态相变与热力学性质。

Result: 调节SIA强度可诱导从Kitaev相到large-D相的交叉（crossover），表现为激发能隙从二次型变为线性、自旋向列序参量（spin-nematic order parameter）与弦序参量（string order parameter）共存且平滑演化、以及双峰比热（double-peak specific heat）的抑制。负SIA下，二聚化相（dimerized phase）与Haldane相之间发生从一级相变（first-order transition）到连续相变（continuous transition）的转变（changeover），后者属于SU(2)₂ Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW）普适类，中心荷（central charge）c=3/2，这是缺乏连续对称性系统中的罕见实例。

Conclusion: Kitaev-Γ链可作为控制交叉（crossover）与转变（changeover）现象的最小平台，为研究非常规临界行为提供了新的模型体系。

Abstract: Recent advances in bond-directional spin chains have revealed extensive emergent phenomena and unconventional criticality. Here we investigate the spin-1 Kitaev-$Γ$ chain with uniaxial single-ion anisotropy (SIA) using large-scale density-matrix renormalization group calculations and bosonization analysis. Tuning the SIA strength reveals a crossover from the Kitaev phase to the large-$D$ phase, evidenced by the excitation gap changing from quadratic to linear, the coexistence and smooth evolution of spin-nematic and string order parameters, and the suppression of the double-peak specific heat. For negative SIA, we uncover a changeover from a first-order transition to a continuous one between the dimerized and Haldane phases. The continuous transition belongs to the \textrm{SU(2)$_2$} Wess-Zumino-Witten universality class with central charge $c=3/2$, a rare instance in a system without continuous symmetry. Our results establish the Kitaev-$Γ$ chain as a minimal platform for controlling crossover and changeover phenomena.

</details>


### [174] [Strain-tunable charge localization coupled to complex magnetic orders in EuAl$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07544)
*M. Baumgartner,Xunyang Hong,Tianren Wang,Fazhi Yang,Yuetong Wu,Junzhang Ma,Tian Shang,J. Oppliger,J. Küspert,M. Hücker,O. Ivashko,F. Igoa Saldaña,M. v. Zimmermann,S. Pyon,K. Kudo,M. Nohara,P. Sačer,A. Akrap,N. Barišić,M. Novak,Qisi Wang,J. Chang*

TL;DR: 该论文通过X射线衍射和外场调控实验，系统研究了EuAl₄中电荷局域化（charge localization）与反铁磁、斯格明子晶格（skyrmion lattice）等复杂自旋结构之间的直接耦合，发现应力方向和磁场可灵活调控这种耦合，为设计手性电荷序（chiral charge order）等对称性破缺态提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在施加外磁场和单轴压力（uniaxial pressure）的条件下，利用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）技术，对EuAl₄中电荷局域化与磁性相之间的耦合关系进行测量与分析。

Result: 在没有外场时，进入磁有序相后电荷局域化显著增强；该效应对应变高度敏感：沿电荷序传播方向施加单轴压力会进一步增强局域化，而垂直方向施加则会削弱它；外加磁场则显示出自旋与电荷序之间既存在竞争也可能存在协同作用。

Conclusion: 自旋与电荷序之间的灵活耦合为设计对称性破缺态（symmetry-breaking state）开辟了新途径。例如，手性电荷序可能从具有相同对称性的自旋结构中被图案化出来。

Abstract: Charge localization is particularly interesting when coupled to antiferromagnetic spin structures. Coupled spin-charge orders are well established in elemental chromium and correlated oxide superconductors, yet the interplay between charge order and more complex magnetic textures -- such as skyrmion lattices and chiral spin structures -- remains largely unexplored. Here we report a comprehensive study of how charge localization couples to the unusually rich sequence of magnetic phases in EuAl$_4$. Using x-ray diffraction under applied magnetic field and uniaxial pressure, we demonstrate a direct coupling between the charge and spin order parameters. In the absence of external stimuli, charge localization is markedly enhanced upon entering the magnetically ordered phases. Strikingly, this effect is highly susceptible to strain: uniaxial pressure applied along the charge-order propagation direction further enhances localization, whereas pressure applied perpendicular to it weakens it. Application of magnetic field reveals both competitive and possible collaborative interactions between spin and charge ordering.This flexible coupling between spin and charge ordering opens a new route to designing symmetry-breaking states. Chiral charge order may for example be patterned from spin structures with that symmetry.

### [175] [Raman spectroscopic signature of Kitaev magnetism and complex spin-lattice coupling in S = 1/2 antiferromagnet SrLaCoNbO$_6$ double perovskite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07630)
*Ajay Kumar,Clemens Ulrich,Rajendra S. Dhaka*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过温度依赖的拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和扩展X射线吸收精细结构（EXAFS）分析，在准自旋-1/2绝缘反铁磁体SrLaCoNbO₆中发现远高于奈尔温度（T_N≈15 K）的声子反常（~60 K及160–180 K），揭示了晶格-自旋耦合、局域结构畸变及可能的近邻Kitaev关联（Kitaev-like correlations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用温度依赖的拉曼光谱和Co K边扩展X射线吸收精细结构（EXAFS）对SrLaCoNbO₆单晶进行实验分析，重点监测声子频率（phonon frequency）、线宽（linewidth）、光谱权重（spectral weight）、Fano不对称参数（Fano asymmetry parameter）以及键长和德拜-沃勒因子（Debye-Waller factor）的温度演变。

Result: 在约60 K（远高于T_N≈15 K）观察到声子频率、线宽和光谱权重的显著反常，同时在160-180 K附近检测到高低能拉曼模式的线宽、强度变化以及Fano不对称参数的变化，并出现新的低能特征。EXAFS分析显示Co离子附近键长和德拜-沃勒因子在60 K和160 K附近存在关联变化，表明局域结构畸变和可能的磁致伸缩效应（magnetostrictive effects）.

Conclusion: 远高于T_N的异常晶格动力学与激发能无关的连续谱共同表明，体系中存在涨落的键取向相互作用和近邻Kitaev型关联，而非仅仅由长程反铁磁有序驱动。

Abstract: We report a detailed analysis of temperature-dependent Raman spectroscopy and Co $K$-edge extended x-ray absorption fine structure (EXAFS) for a pseudospin-$\tilde{S}=1/2$ insulating antiferromagnet SrLaCoNbO$_6$, a B-site--ordered double perovskite hosting Co$^{2+}$ ($3d^7$) ions on an {\it f.c.c.} sublattice. Notably, pronounced anomalies in the phonon frequency, linewidth and spectral weight are observed around 60~K, well above the long-range antiferromagnetic transition at $T_{\rm N} \approx 15$~K. These renormalizations indicate a significant coupling between lattice and spin degrees of freedom, although a purely structural contribution cannot be excluded. Additional modifications of both high- and low-energy Raman modes are detected near 160-180 K, including changes in linewidth and intensity, variations of the Fano asymmetry parameter, and the emergence of an additional low-energy feature. The asymmetric Fano line shape of selected low-energy modes, together with a broad low-energy continuum and quasielastic response, suggests coupling between discrete phonons and fluctuating magnetic excitations. Moreover, the EXAFS analysis reveals correlated changes in bond distances and Debye-Waller factors around the Co ions near 60~K and 160~K, evidencing subtle local structural distortions and possible magnetostrictive effects. The persistence of anomalous lattice dynamics far above $T_{\rm N}$, combined with the excitation-energy--independent continuum, is consistent with fluctuating bond-directional interactions and proximate Kitaev-like correlations.

### [176] [Wavelength-resolved small-angle neutron spectroscopy of spin waves in MnSi under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07660)
*E. V. Altynbaev,D. O. Skanchenko,Z. Xie,Y. Ke,Y. Bao,A. V. Tsvyashchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报告了在中国散裂中子源（CSNS）上首次实现波长分辨的自旋波小角中子散射（SWSANS），并将其拓展至MnSi的高压测量。通过提取截止角得到自旋波刚度（spin-wave stiffness）$A$，发现11 kbar下刚度显著降低，而结构场标度$H_{C2}$仍保持较高值，表明无法仅从静态结构参数推断$A$。这是首次在脉冲中子源上实现SWSANS，并首次在高压下测定自旋波刚度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自旋波刚度的测量方法在高压环境下存在局限性，且无法仅通过静态结构参数推断其变化。因此，需要发展一种能够在高压条件下直接测量自旋波刚度的实验技术，以更深入地理解磁有序与压力之间的相互作用。

Method: 利用中国散裂中子源（CSNS）BL01飞行时间小角中子散射（TOF-SANS）仪器，采用波长分辨的自旋波小角中子散射（SWSANS）方法。在固定磁场下，飞行时间测量提供中子波长谱。针对每个探测器分支$s=\pm1$，将强度分布相对于波长依赖的布拉格角（Bragg angle）$\theta_B(\lambda)$重新定心，并在局部分支坐标系中提取截止角（cutoff angle）$\theta_C(\lambda)$。自旋波刚度$A$通过对$\theta_C^2$与$\lambda^2$进行线性拟合获得。在常压以及名义5和11 kbar下进行结构SANS测量，以验证磁态并对压力测量提供内部压力状态检查。

Result: 常压下的测量结果复现了MnSi已知的自旋波刚度标度。在名义11 kbar下，基于当前截止模型得到的截止角导出的自旋波刚度显著降低，而结构场标度$H_{C2}$仍保持较高水平。这一对比表明在压力下无法仅从静态结构参数推断$A$的值。

Conclusion: 这是首次在脉冲中子源上实现SWSANS，并首次在高压下通过SWSANS测定自旋波刚度。该实验还表明，在脉冲源上进行可靠的高压SWSANS需要高源亮度、稳定的波长依赖归一化以及每个波长窗口内足够的统计量。

Abstract: We report wavelength-resolved spin-wave small-angle neutron scattering (SWSANS) on the time-of-flight SANS instrument BL01 at the China Spallation Neutron Source and extend the method to pressure-cell measurements of MnSi. MnSi is used as a benchmark B20 helimagnet because its helimagnetic order and spin-wave stiffness are well characterized at ambient pressure. In a fixed magnetic field, the time-of-flight measurement provides a spectrum of neutron wavelengths. For each detector branch $s=\pm1$, the intensity profile is recentered relative to the wavelength-dependent Bragg angle $θ_B (λ) = k_s λ/ 2π$, and the cutoff angle $θ_C (λ)$ is extracted in the local branch coordinate. The cutoff-derived spin-wave stiffness $A$ is obtained from a linear fit of $θ_C^2$ as a function of $λ^2$. Ambient-pressure measurements reproduce the known stiffness scale of MnSi. Structural SANS at ambient pressure and at nominal 5 and 11 kbar verifies the magnetic state and provides an internal pressure-state check for the pressure-cell measurements. At nominal 11 kbar, within the present cutoff model, the cutoff-derived stiffness is substantially reduced, whereas the structural field scale $H_{C2}$ remains high. This contrast shows that $A$ cannot be inferred from static structural parameters alone under pressure. To our knowledge, these measurements constitute the first SWSANS implementation on a pulsed neutron source and the first SWSANS determination of spin-wave stiffness under pressure. The experiment also shows that reliable high-pressure SWSANS on a pulsed source requires high source brilliance, stable wavelength-dependent normalization, and sufficient statistics in each wavelength window.

</details>


### [177] [Multistage development of short-range spin correlations and weak magnetic order in the two coupled trillium lattices of K2Fe2(MoO4)(PO4)2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07681)
*J. Khatua,Sritharan Krishnamoorthi,Changhyun Koo,Gyungbin Ban,Taeyun Kim,Yugo Oshima,Marc Uhlarz,John Wilkinson,Peter J. Baker,Kyeong Jun Lee,Mani Shankar,Seo Hyoung Chang,R. Sankar,Kwang-Yong Choi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过磁化率、比热、电子自旋共振（ESR）和μ子自旋弛豫（μSR）测量，系统研究了K₂Fe₂(MoO₄)(PO₄)₂单晶的磁性行为，发现其在trillium晶格上表现出强反铁磁相互作用与弱磁有序共存，并存在残余相互作用驱动的自旋重取向以及有序态中的动态自旋涨落，外加磁场可抑制奈尔温度（T_N），提示该材料是探索三维耦合trillium晶格中场致自旋液体行为的候选体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Trillium晶格（trillium lattice）是由磁性离子构成手性共角三角形网络的三维磁结构，理论上可承载易碎经典自旋液体态（fragile classical spin-liquid state），但实验上对这类三维耦合体系的研究仍有限。本文旨在通过综合实验手段表征K₂Fe₂(MoO₄)(PO₄)₂单晶的磁性，验证其是否具备场致自旋液体行为的潜力。

Method: 对K₂Fe₂(MoO₄)(PO₄)₂单晶进行了磁化强度（magnetization）、比热（specific heat）、电子自旋共振（ESR）和μ子自旋弛豫（muon spin relaxation, μSR）测量，系统分析了其热力学和微观自旋动力学响应。

Result: 磁化测量显示强反铁磁相互作用与T_N=5.2 K的弱磁有序共存，伴随磁化率λ型异常、μ子自旋弛豫率临界增强以及ESR信号消失。T_N以上在T_H=34 K和T_L=10 K处出现两段短程自旋关联发展，由磁比热异常、ESR线宽与g因子温度演化所支持。T_N以下在T^*=3.2 K处出现热力学观测量和μ子自旋弛豫率的异常，表明残余相互作用驱动自旋重取向。μSR实验发现有序态中仍存在动态自旋涨落。外加磁场（μ₀H≥2 T）可抑制T_N。

Conclusion: K₂Fe₂(MoO₄)(PO₄)₂在三维耦合trillium晶格中表现出反铁磁有序与自旋涨落共存的复杂磁性行为，且外加磁场能有效抑制磁有序，使其成为探索三维trillium晶格中场致自旋液体行为（field-induced spin-liquid behavior）的有前景候选材料。

Abstract: Trillium lattices, where magnetic ions form a chiral network of corner-sharing triangles, offer a three-dimensional magnetic framework that can host fragile classical spin-liquid states. Herein, we report on the magnetization, specific heat, electron spin resonance (ESR), and muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) of K$_{2}$Fe$_{2}$(MoO$_{4}$)(PO$_{4}$)$_{2}$ single crystals. Magnetization measurements reveal strong antiferromagnetic interactions coexisting with weak magnetic order at $T_{\rm N} = 5.2$~K, as evidenced by a $λ$-like anomaly observed in the magnetic susceptibility, a critical enhancement of the muon spin relaxation rate and the wipeout of the ESR signal as the temperature approaches $T_{\rm N}$. Above $T_{\rm N}$, two distinct developments of short-range spin correlations are identified at $T_{\rm H} = 34$~K and $T_{\rm L} = 10$~K, supported by magnetic specific heat anomalies and the temperature dependence of the ESR linewidth and $g$-factor. Upon cooling below $T_{\rm N}$, an anomaly appears at $T^{*} = 3.2$~K in thermodynamic observables and the muon spin relaxation rate, indicative of spin reorientation driven by residual interactions. Despite the presence of magnetic order, $μ$SR experiments reveal dynamically fluctuating spins persisting even in the ordered state. Moreover, the suppression of $T_{\rm N}$ under applied magnetic fields ($μ_{0}H \geq 2$~T) suggests that K$_{2}$Fe$_{2}$(MoO$_{4}$)(PO$_{4}$)$_{2}$ constitutes a promising candidate for exploring field-induced spin-liquid behavior in three-dimensionally coupled trillium lattices.

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [178] [Moiré Phonon Condensation in Magic-Angle Twisted Bilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06711)
*Zhanghao Zhouyin,Jyun-jie Jiang,Xianghua Kong,Hong Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）在魔角（magic angle）附近发生从弱呼吸褶皱（breathing corrugation）到大尺度共同弯曲（common bending）的结构重构，其机制为层对称 $A_1$ 莫尔弯曲声子的软模凝聚（soft-mode condensation），称为莫尔声子凝聚（Moiré Phonon Condensation, MPC）。仅两个 $A_1$ 声子模式即可捕捉莫尔超胞中 11164 个原子的位移（光谱权重 >99.5%）；一阶谐波连续场理论（first-harmonic continuum theory）识别出无量纲控制参数，揭示魔角附近莫尔尺度增长放大应力-弯曲竞争（stress-bending competition），导致弯曲刚度变号。MPC 被确立为一种扭曲控制的结构序参量（structural order parameter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲双层石墨烯在魔角附近存在从弱呼吸褶皱到共同弯曲的结构重构（reconstruction），但该集体交叉（collective crossover）的起源此前尚不明确，亟需揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用声子模式分析识别软模凝聚现象；构建一阶谐波连续场理论以提取无量纲控制参数；利用模式分辨的紧束缚计算（mode-resolved tight-binding calculations）研究凝聚声子坐标对电子性质的影响。

Result: 在 $θ=1.08^\circ$ 时，仅两个 $A_1$ 声子模式即可捕获莫尔超胞中全部 11164 个原子的位移（光谱权重 >99.5%，最大原子位移 2.30 Å）；连续场理论证明，魔角附近莫尔尺度增大导致应力-弯曲竞争放大，直至弯曲刚度变号；模式分辨紧束缚计算显示凝聚声子坐标具有电子活性（electronically active）。

Conclusion: 确立了莫尔声子凝聚（MPC）作为扭曲控制的结构序参量，解释了魔角附近扭曲双层石墨烯结构重构的集体起源。

Abstract: Twisted bilayer graphene reconstructs from weak breathing corrugation to large common bending near the magic angle, but the origin of this collective crossover has remained unclear. Here we show that the crossover is a soft-mode condensation of layer-symmetric $A_1$ moiré flexural phonons: these modes soften on the breathing branch, lose stiffness near the magic angle, and freeze into the bending morphology. We call this mechanism Moiré Phonon Condensation (MPC). At $θ=1.08^\circ$, it is extremely surprising that displacements of all 11164 atoms in the moiré supercell, with a maximum atomic position shift of 2.30 Angstrom, is captured by only two $A_1$ phonon modes at more than $99.5\%$ spectral weight. A first-harmonic continuum theory identifies a dimensionless control parameter of the phenomenon, showing that as the twist approaches the magic angle, the growing moiré length scale amplifies a smooth stress-bending competition until the flexural stiffness changes sign. Mode-resolved tight-binding calculations further show that the condensed phonon coordinates are electronically active. This work identifies MPC as a twist-controlled structural order parameter for moiré reconstruction.

</details>


### [179] [Mesoscopic routers and single-pole double-throw switches for electronic heat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06716)
*José Balduque,Rafael Sánchez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出基于三端结（three-terminal junctions）的热路由器（thermal routers）和热单刀双掷开关（thermal single-pole double-throw switches），通过单外部旋钮控制热量定向传输。讨论了基于共振隧穿能量滤波器（resonant tunneling energy filters）的两种模型：扫描尖端相位相干接触和栅压可调滤波器耦合，后者在理想滤波下热流被限制为开路电流的四分之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子纳米结构中的热量耗散不可避免，尤其是在低温操作时更为关键。需要找到能够在不对静电环境造成扰动的前提下控制和重新定向多余热量的器件。

Method: 提出两种基于共振隧穿能量滤波器的三端结模型：(i) 通过扫描尖端实现相位相干接触（phase-coherent contact），利用位置依赖的量子干涉（position-dependent quantum interference）调制两路输出电流的相对大小；(ii) 通过栅压可调谐滤波器（gate voltage tunable filter）耦合，在存在退相干（dephasing）的情况下选择性切换其中一路电流。

Result: 对于第二种模型（栅压可调滤波器耦合），在理想滤波条件下，热流被限制为开路电流的四分之一。

Conclusion: 所提出的三端结器件可作为热路由器或热单刀双掷开关工作，通过单一外部控制旋钮实现热量定向调控，为纳米尺度热管理提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The unavoidable dissipation of heat in electronic nanostructures is a crucial problem, specially when their operation requires low temperatures. It demands finding devices able to control and redirect the excess heat, ideally without perturbing the electrostatic environment. We propose three-terminal junctions working either as thermal routers or as thermal single-pole double-throw switches controlled by a single external knob. Two models are discussed based on resonant tunneling energy filters and different couplings to the heat source: (i) Phase-coherent contact via a scanning tip modulates the relative amount of the two output currents via position-dependent quantum interference; (ii) Coupling via a gate voltage tunable filter selectively switches one of the currents in the presence of dephasing. In the later case, we find that the heat flow using ideal filtering is bounded by fourth the open conductor current.

### [180] [Driven square lattice of quantum dots in a magnetic field coupled to a cylindrical FIR-photon cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06812)
*Vidar Gudmundsson,Vram Mughnetsyan,Hsi-Sheng Goan,Jeng-Da Chai,Nzar Rauf Abdullah,Chi-Shung Tang,Wen-Hsuan Kuan,Valeriu Moldoveanu,Andrei Manolescu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函理论（DFT）与多体组态相互作用（CI）相结合的数值方法，研究了方形量子点阵列在圆柱形远红外光子腔与外加磁场驱动下的电子-光子耦合动力学，揭示了谐振驱动下的两光子跃迁增强、光子泵浦及集体库仑呼吸模式激活等关键现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）处理电子-电子库仑相互作用，并在每次DFT迭代中利用多体组态相互作用（many-body configuration interaction）方法建模电子-光子耦合；外加磁场与圆柱形TE₀₁₁腔模的耦合用于实现选择性增强。

Result: 展示了通过圆柱形TE₀₁₁腔模可选择性地增强顺磁和抗磁两光子跃迁；发现谐波调制的有效性强烈依赖于驱动频率和每个量子点中的电子占据数；当驱动频率接近两倍腔光子频率时，系统出现谐振行为，表现为高效光子泵浦、高阶光子复制态的占据以及集体径向库仑呼吸模式（collective radial Coulomb breathing modes）的激活。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive computational study of driven quantum dot arrays in a square lattice configuration, subject to an external magnetic field and coupled to a cylindrical far-infrared photon cavity. The driving is introduced through a harmonic modulation of the full electron-photon interaction, therefore including both paramagnetic and diamagnetic contributions. The electron-electron Coulomb interactions are treated within density functional theory, while the electron-photon coupling is modeled using a many-body configuration interaction approach at each iteration of the density functional. By exploiting the unique properties of the cylindrical TE$_{011}$ cavity mode, we demonstrate selective enhancement of diamagnetic two-photon transitions. Our results reveal that the effectiveness of harmonic modulation of the electron-photon interaction is strongly dependent on both the driving frequency and the electron occupation number per dot. When the driving frequency approaches twice the cavity photon frequency, the system exhibits resonant behavior characterized by efficient photon pumping, occupation of higher-order photon replicas, and activation of collective radial Coulomb breathing modes. These findings establish a controllable mechanism for manipulating photon states in coupled quantum dot-cavity systems and provide insights into the interplay among harmonic modulation, photonic excitations, magnetic confinement, and many-body electron correlations in dimensionally reduced nanostructures.

### [181] [High-frequency nonlinear conductivity of a Wigner crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06846)
*A. J. Schleusner,M. T. Elewa,N. R. Beysengulov,C. A. Mikolas,J. Pollanen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了在微通道几何结构中，被困于超流氦表面的电子形成维格纳晶体（Wigner crystal）后，在高频驱动场下的强非线性输运响应。实验发现，该响应出现在比传统布拉格-切伦科夫效应（Bragg-Cherenkov effect）中涉及的纹波子（ripplon）频率高近一个数量级的频段，并归因于维格纳晶体与高阶布拉格矢量对应纹波子的耦合所导致的动态摩擦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统布拉格-切伦科夫效应在匀速运动条件下已被理解，但维格纳晶体在非平衡态（如高频驱动场下）的响应尚未被充分探索。本研究旨在通过微通道中的电子输运实验，揭示约束维格纳固体在高频驱动下的非线性行为及其物理机制。

Method: 采用超流氦表面电子在微通道几何结构中的输运测量方法，研究维格纳固体在高频驱动场下的非平衡响应，并与传统布拉格-切伦科夫效应中的纹波子频率进行比较分析。

Result: 实验观测到约束维格纳固体在高频驱动下出现强非线性输运响应，其特征频率比传统布拉格-切伦科夫效应中涉及的纹波子频率高近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该强非线性响应源于维格纳固体与高阶布拉格矢量对应的纹波子之间的耦合，这种耦合产生了动态摩擦（dynamical friction），从而为实验观测到的高频钉扎（high-frequency pinning）现象提供了解释机制。

Abstract: Electrons trapped above the surface of superfluid helium are a disorder-free platform for investigating the formation and dynamics of low-dimensional Wigner crystals. A characteristic nonlinear transport feature of this electronic solid suspended above the helium surface is the Bragg-Cherenkov effect, in which the mobility of the smoothly moving crystal is limited by the coherent emission of helium surface waves (ripplons). The effect has been understood in the conventional Cherenkov setting in which the crystal moves at a constant speed. Here we report on transport measurements of electrons on helium confined in a microchannel geometry to investigate the non-equilibrium response of the Wigner solid when it is subjected to a high-frequency driving field. Surprisingly, the experiments reveal a strongly nonlinear transport response of the confined Wigner solid at frequencies nearly an order of magnitude larger than the ripplon frequencies contributing to the conventional Bragg-Cherenkov effect. We relate this observation to the coupling of the Wigner solid to ripplons with higher-order Bragg vectors, which gives rise to a dynamical friction that provides a mechanism for the observed high-frequency pinning.

### [182] [Disorder signatures in coherent electronic waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06866)
*Alejandro Lopez-Bezanilla*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于电导平衡的学习框架（conductance-balanced learning framework），用于从相干量子输运谱中识别微观无序机制。通过在扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带中进行受控的紧束缚波导模拟，并去除平均电导这一主导捷径，研究比较了标量透射谱与本征值谱，利用监督分类、尺度归一化控制、平台分辨测试和主成分分析，揭示了多通道能窗中能区分不同无序类别的谱结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微观无序（microscopic disorder）在相干导体中编码于透射电流的幅度以及散射响应的能量分辨和通道分辨结构之中，然而平均电导常作为主导捷径掩盖不同无序类别的谱差异。本研究旨在开发一个去除此捷径的学习框架，以提取对无序机制真正有辨识力的谱特征。

Method: 采用电导平衡学习框架，以扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带（armchair graphene nanoribbon）作为受控的多通道紧束缚波导（multichannel tight-binding waveguide），生成不同无序类别但具有相同积分透射区间的系综。在此约束下，比较标量透射谱（scalar transmission spectrum）与透射本征值谱（transmission-eigenvalue spectrum）；应用监督分类（supervised classification）、尺度归一化控制、平台分辨测试（plateau-resolved test）和主成分分析（principal-component analysis, PCA）进行谱结构分析。

Result: 所学习的区分特征在电导包络归一化后仍然保持，且在发生模式混合与通道重新分布的多通道能窗中最为显著。主成分提供了可解释的输运坐标，其载荷（loadings）标定了对主要谱形变起决定性作用的能量和本征通道（eigenchannel）扇区。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种受控的 AI 辅助协议（AI-assisted protocol），能够从非线性量子散射数据中学习无序特征，为微观无序机制的识别提供了可解释、可推广的分析路径。

Abstract: Microscopic disorder in a coherent conductor is encoded in the magnitude of the transmitted current and in the energy- and channel-resolved structure of the scattering response. We develop a conductance-balanced learning framework for identifying microscopic disorder mechanisms from coherent quantum-transport spectra. Using armchair graphene nanoribbons as controlled multichannel tight-binding waveguides, we generate ensembles in which distinct disorder classes occupy the same intervals of integrated transmission, removing the dominant shortcut associated with average conductance. Within this constrained setting, we compare scalar transmission spectra with transmission-eigenvalue spectra, and use supervised classification, scale-normalizing controls, plateau-resolved tests, and principal-component analysis to identify the spectral structures that remain informative. The learned distinctions persist after normalization of the conductance envelope and are strongest in multichannel energy windows, where mode mixing and channel redistribution shape the scattering response. Principal components provide interpretable transport coordinates whose loadings identify the energy and eigenchannel sectors responsible for the dominant spectral deformations. The results establish a controlled AI-assisted protocol for learning disorder signatures from nonlinear quantum-scattering data.

Method: 采用格林函数形式化方法（Green's-function formalism），理论计算了耦合到二维d波交变磁衬底上的共振杂质的自旋分辨局域谱函数，模拟了扫描隧道显微镜/扫描隧道谱（STM/STS）的测量信号。

Abstract: Using a Green's-function formalism, we study the spin-resolved local spectral function of a resonant impurity coupled to a two-dimensional $d$-wave altermagnetic substrate. It is found that the interplay between the direct impurity-STM tip tunneling and altermagnet-mediated tunneling leads to dual Fano resonance in the absence of external magnetic field. Moreover, the anisotropic spin-dependent oscillation of the local density of states and/or Fano factor provide the information of the altermagnetic splitting strength from the local/global perspective. In addition, spin-selective tunneling can be achieved by tuning the Fermi energy and the tip position. In the presence of strong magnetic field with Landau level quantization, the dominant STS signature becomes a spin-dependent nodal structure of the real-space pattern: the nodal mismatch between opposite spin channels produces a large local spin contrast. We then identify open frontiers that we consider most promising for the next phase of the field: sensitivity analysis and robust design to bridge the gap between simulation and experiment; input shaping and transducer optimisation; the incorporation of nonlinear spin-wave effects as an explicit design resource; spatially structured amplification; self-adapting media and machine-learning-based design; and the long-term vision of a universal, reconfigurable magnonic platform. Method: 实验使用单晶CrSb薄片分别制备铁磁镍（nickel）接触和非磁性金（gold）接触两种样品，测量其一阶反常霍尔效应与二阶非线性霍尔效应，并改变霍尔棒（Hall-bar）接触配置方向以验证效应差异。

Result: 铁磁镍接触样品观察到显著的一阶反常霍尔效应和二阶非线性霍尔效应，而非磁性金接触的参考样品中两者均不存在。反常霍尔效应呈现蝴蝶结型（bow-tie）磁滞回线；同一样品中霍尔曲线斜率随霍尔棒接触配置方向改变而变号。非线性霍尔效应在磁场中呈现磁滞回线。

Conclusion: 观察到的符号反转与蝴蝶结磁滞回线归因于交变磁体CrSb中交替体自旋分裂（alternating bulk spin splitting）与自旋极化拓扑表面态（spin-polarized topological surface states）的联合效应。非线性霍尔效应的磁滞回线证实了自旋极化电子注入下有限贝里曲率偶极矩（Berry curvature dipole）的存在，即该交变磁候选材料具有拓扑特征。

Abstract: We experimentally investigate spin-polarized electron transport for the centrosymmetric altermagnet CrSb, which is known to reveal both altermagnetic and topological features. We demonstrate pronounced first-harmonic anomalous and second-harmonic non-linear Hall effects for a single-crystal CrSb flake with ferromagnetic nickel contacts, while both effects can not be seen for the reference samples with non-magnetic gold ones. For the anomalous Hall effect, we demonstrate bow-tie hysteresis loop in Hall voltage, which is usually ascribed to surface spin textures in magnetic materials. The slope of the Hall curve changes a sign for two orientations of the Hall-bar contact configuration for the same sample, i.e. for the same sign of the charge carriers. We interpret the observed sign inversion and bow-tie hysteresis as the joint effect of the alternating bulk spin splitting and spin-polarized topological surface states in CrSb. The pronounced non-linear Hall effect with hysteresis in magnetic field confirms finite Berry curvature dipole under injection of spin-polarized electrons, i.e. the topological features for the altermagnetic candidate CrSb.

</details>


### [187] [Force-Isosurface Simulations Probe the Limits of High-Resolution AFM on Three-Dimensional Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07363)
*Edward J Dunn,Robert J Young,Samuel P Jarvis*

Method: 采用探针-粒子模型模拟（probe-particle-model simulations），在具有递增结构复杂性的分子上方预测恒力等值线（constant-force contours）。通过从模拟的三维力场（three-dimensional force fields）中提取力等值面（force isosurfaces），系统比较恒高成像（constant-height imaging）与恒力成像（constant-force imaging）所保留的分子信息。

Result: 对于倾斜苯（tilted benzene）和吡咯（pyrrole），恒力成像能在一定吸附角度范围内保持分子骨架（molecular framework），并允许定量恢复分子取向（molecular orientation）。对于更大非平面和三维系统，模拟识别出与吸附几何（adsorption geometry）、低层分子结构（lower-lying molecular structure）和弯曲分子表面（curved molecular surfaces）相关的特征力等值面对比度（characteristic force-isosurface contrast）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为力等值面提供了目标对比度，可作为从三维力映射实验（three-dimensional force-mapping experiments）中提取力等值面的参考基准，评估了理想力等值面成像在逐步非平面体系中保留分子信息的能力。

Abstract: High-resolution atomic force microscopy has transformed molecular imaging by revealing intramolecular structure directly in real space. A major remaining challenge is to extend this capability from largely planar molecules to non-planar molecular systems, where the most important structural information may be distributed across different heights above the surface. Here we use probe-particle-model simulations to predict the constant-force contours expected above molecules with increasing structural complexity. By extracting force isosurfaces from simulated three-dimensional force fields, we compare the molecular information retained in constant-height and constant-force images. For tilted benzene and pyrrole, constant-force images preserve the molecular framework across a range of adsorption angles and allow the molecular orientation to be recovered quantitatively. For larger non-planar and three-dimensional systems, simulations identify characteristic force-isosurface contrast associated with adsorption geometry, lower-lying molecular structure and curved molecular surfaces. These results provide target contrasts for force isosurfaces that could be extracted from three-dimensional force-mapping experiments, evaluating the molecular information retained by ideal force-isosurface imaging across progressively non-planar systems.

In this paper, we study the nonlinear response of magnetic Hopfion to microwave fields. {We observe the emergence of higher-order harmonics of the driving microwave field as it interacts with the Hopfion}. By carefully selecting the {driving frequency, the corresponding harmonic can efficiently excite localized magnon state of a Hopfion. Our results demonstrate the promising potential of hopfions in nonlinear magnonics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在400 nm的源漏间距上维持了650 mK的温差，并通过调节隧穿率实现了对热电流极性和幅度的精确控制。

Abstract: Solid-state quantum technologies, including qubits and quantum metrology circuits, demand milli-Kelvin operation to preserve fragile quantum states from classical noise. While the negligible electron-phonon coupling is the major impediment, reaching 50 mK electron temperature is further suffered by the high electrical resistance and sub-micron-scale dimensions of typical devices, limiting conventional heat dissipation. Though the phonons are effectively frozen, thermoelectric techniques could offer a viable path for heat management.This work explores thermally driven electrical transport in a gated quantum dot (QD) on a GaAs-AlGaAs two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG), to control heat flow between the source and drain reservoirs.By exploiting the QD's discrete energy spectrum and tuneable tunnel rates, a precise control over the polarity and magnitude of the resulting thermoelectric current is demonstrated. The results presented here show that tuneable tunnel barriers can be used for local heat control, and could lead to advanced quantum refrigerators that work efficiently in mesoscopic circuits.

### [190] [Unveiling the Spin-Valley Structure of Dipolar Exciton Ladders in R-stacked WSe$_2$/WS$_2$ Moiré Heterobilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07590)
*Byeong Wook Cho,Tatyana V. Ivanova,Zhe Li,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Brian D. Gerardot,Mauro Brotons-Gisbert*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用螺旋分辨磁光致发光（helicity-resolved magneto-photoluminescence）揭示了R型堆叠WSe₂/WS₂莫尔异质双层（moiré heterobilayer）中偶极激子阶梯（dipolar exciton ladder）的自旋-谷微观起源，识别了电荷中性点和单电子填充下的多种激子和双激子态的自旋-谷构型及其相互作用能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔异质双层中的局域层间激子（localized interlayer excitons）可形成偶极激子阶梯，但其内部的精细自旋-谷结构（spin-valley structure）尚未被解析。

Method: 采用螺旋分辨磁光致发光（helicity-resolved magneto-photoluminescence）光谱技术，对R型堆叠WSe₂/WS₂异质双层在电荷中性点（charge neutrality）和莫尔晶格单电子填充（one-electron filling）条件下进行测量与分析。

Result: 在电荷中性点，前两个发射峰对应自旋三重态层间激子（spin-triplet interlayer exciton）和 triplet-triplet 双激子态，能隙38 meV源于在位偶极相互作用（on-site dipolar interaction）；第三个阶梯并非自旋守恒三激子态，而是 triplet-singlet 双激子构型，22 meV能差由WS₂导带自旋劈裂（conduction-band spin splitting）决定。在单电子填充下，关联电子背景产生带电单/双激子态及谷间/谷内双激子构型，同时减弱有效激子-激子相互作用。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了莫尔异质双层中偶极激子阶梯超越简单占据数物理的自旋-谷分辨图像（spin-valley-resolved picture），为理解该类系统中的多体激发态提供了微观基础。

Abstract: Localized interlayer excitons in moiré heterobilayers can form dipolar exciton ladders, yet their internal spin-valley structure remains unresolved. Here, we use helicity-resolved magneto-photoluminescence to identify the microscopic origin of the ladder in R-stacked WSe$_2$/WS$_2$ at charge neutrality and one-electron filling of the moiré lattice. At charge neutrality, the first two emission peaks correspond to a spin-triplet interlayer exciton and a triplet-triplet two-exciton state separated by 38 meV, reflecting the on-site dipolar interaction. The opposite Zeeman response of the apparent third rung of the ladder rules out its assignment as a spin-conserving three-exciton state and instead identifies it as a triplet-singlet two-exciton configuration with a 22 meV offset set by the WS$_2$ conduction-band spin splitting. At one-electron filling, the correlated electronic background gives rise to charged one- and two-exciton states and intervalley/intravalley two-exciton configurations, while reducing the effective exciton-exciton interaction. Our results establish a spin-valley-resolved picture of dipolar exciton ladders beyond simple occupation-number physics in moiré heterobilayers.

### [191] [Geometric Interpretation of Sum Photon Blockade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07591)
*Timur Khudaiberganov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了多模量子光学系统中总光子阻塞效应（sum photon blockade）的几何解释，将阻塞条件诠释为希尔伯特空间中振幅向量与目标模式向量的正交性，分析了退相干下的最大阻塞概率，并引入“暗态典型性”（dark-state typicality）概念，证明随模式数增加暗子空间渐近占据整个n玻色子希尔伯特空间的单位比例，从而将脆弱精细的阻塞机制转化为宏观鲁棒的非经典光产生方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有光子阻塞机制（photon blockade）通常依赖精细的参数调谐，在退相干（decoherence）下鲁棒性不足，难以扩展到多模大尺度量子光学架构。本文旨在为多模系统中的总光子阻塞提供统一的几何框架，并探索其在大规模系统中保持鲁棒性的条件与潜力。

Method: 采用几何方法，将阻塞条件 \(c^{(n)} \cdot v = 0\) 解释为 N 维希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中 n 光子振幅向量与目标模式向量的正交性，系统状态被限制在一个超平面（hyperplane）上。利用该几何图像分析退相干（尤其退相位，dephasing）下系统停留在阻塞子空间的最大概率，并引入“暗态典型性”概念，研究随模式数 M 增加时被集体模式算符湮灭的暗子空间在海森堡极限下的渐近行为。

Result: 推导了退相干过程下总光子阻塞的最大概率表达式，定量刻画了该效应的实际可行性与鲁棒性。发现随模式数 M 增大，暗子空间（dark subspace）占 n-玻色子希尔伯特空间的分数渐近趋于 1，即“暗态典型性”成立。该方法可推广至高阶关联函数 \(g^{(2)}_Σ\) 和交叉关联（cross-correlation），支持可扩展量子器件的设计。

Conclusion: 总光子阻塞效应可从精细调谐的机制过渡到宏观鲁棒的非经典光（non-classical light）产生方案，适用于大型多模玻色子架构。该几何框架为进一步探索关联零点（correlation zeros）、不变流形（invariant manifolds）以及阻塞-纠缠（blockade-entanglement）关系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We present a geometric interpretation of the sum photon blockade effect in multimode quantum optical systems, such as semiconductor microresonators. The blockade condition \(c^{(n)} \cdot v = 0\) reflects the orthogonality of the \(n\)-photon amplitude vector to a target mode vector in an \(N\)-dimensional Hilbert space, visualized as the confinement of the state to a hyperplane.
  A key result is the calculation of the maximum probability of the system remaining in the blockade subspace under the influence of decoherence processes (in particular, dephasing), which determines the practical feasibility and robustness of the effect. This approach extends to higher-order correlators \(g^{(2)}_Σ\) and cross-correlations, enabling the design of scalable quantum devices.
  We introduce the concept of "dark-state typicality": as the number of modes \(M\) increases, the dark subspace annihilated by the collective mode operator asymptotically occupies a unit fraction of the \(n\)-boson Hilbert space. This allows the transition from fragile, finely tuned mechanisms to macroscopically robust non-classical light in large multimode bosonic architectures.
  We consider continuum collective modes, hypotheses on correlation zeros and invariant manifolds, as well as the relationship between blockade and entanglement.

### [192] [Non-Hermitian Edge State Endocytosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07703)
*Si-Yu Yuan,Wen-Tan Xue,Ching Hua Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文发现非厄米（non-Hermitian）有限开链中的孤立边缘态（isolated edge state）在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit, TDL）下并非必然存活，而可能经历一种称为“边缘态内吞”（edge state endocytosis）的现象——边缘态在有限尺度下先作为连续谱中的瞬态束缚态（bound state in the continuum, BIC）存在，随后在更大系统尺寸中被吸收消失。该机制的数学根源在于开链特征行列式（characteristic determinant）的Widom展开中，来自次主导子集（subleading subsets）的隐藏投影格林函数（proj-GF）零点，具有平台无关性（platform-independent），并可通过投影格林函数定量预测内吞尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认知认为，有限开链中的孤立边缘态在热力学极限（TDL）下仍应存在，其定域化（localization）机制不同于非厄米趋肤累积（non-Hermitian skin accumulation）。本文旨在揭示一类尺度敏感（scale-sensitive）非厄米系统中边缘态的不同命运——边缘态可能在有限尺度下渐次消失，而非持久存在。

Method: 通过Widom展开（Widom expansion）将开链特征行列式分解为若干可容许非布洛赫模式子集（admissible non-Bloch mode subsets）的贡献；每个子集贡献进一步分解为边界投影格林函数（boundary-projected Green's function, proj-GF）行列式与子集分辨体传播因子（subset-resolved bulk propagation factor）的乘积，分别编码晶格截断（lattice truncation）和系统尺寸依赖。

Result: 发现了热力学极限边缘态（TDL edge states）与内吞态（endocytosed states）之间的根本性区别：前者是主导子集proj-GF行列式的零点，后者则是来自次主导子集（subleading subsets）的隐藏proj-GF零点，在有限尺寸下控制能谱。建立了边缘态内吞的定量预测框架，可预测内吞尺度（endocytosis scale）并揭示其竞争机制如何通过实验相关的格林函数（Green's functions）显现。

Conclusion: 边缘态内吞机制具有完全的平台无关性（platform-independent），无需精细调谐（fine-tuning）即可在非厄米耦合引入非局域性（non-locality）的条件下普遍发生。该框架深化了对有限尺寸非厄米体系中边缘态命运的理解，并为实验观测提供了可操作的定量预测工具。

Abstract: An isolated edge state observed in a finite open chain is usually expected to survive the thermodynamic limit (TDL), with a localization mechanism distinct from non-Hermitian skin accumulation, which localizes the \emph{entire} bulk continuum. We show that scale-sensitive non-Hermitian systems can generically admit a different fate: as we scale up the system size, a detached edge-localized eigenstate can remain sharply visible over a broad window until a critical scale is reached, where it forms an ephemeral bound state in the continuum (BIC) of the open-boundary bulk before being absorbed (entocytosed) at even larger system sizes. We call this phenomenon edge state endocytosis. Its mechanism is fundamentally traced to the Widom expansion of the open-chain characteristic determinant (energy dispersion equation) into contributions corresponding to admissible non-Bloch mode subsets. Each subset contribution factorizes into a boundary-projected Green's function (proj-GF) determinant, which encodes lattice truncation, and a subset-resolved bulk propagation factor, which encodes the system size dependence. We uncover the fundamental distinction: TDL edge states are zeros of the leading-subset proj-GF determinant, whereas endocytosed states are a hitherto-ignored class of hidden proj-GF zeros from subleading subsets that control the spectrum at finite sizes. Due to its fundamental mathematical origin, the endocytosis mechanism is completely platform-independent, occurring generically without fine-tuning when isolated edge states, topological or otherwise, are subject to non-Hermitian couplings that generate the requisite non-locality. Our new framework quantitatively predicts the endocytosis scale and sheds light on how its intricate competitive mechanism can be revealed through experimentally relevant Green's functions.

</details>

### [193] [On the Geometrical and Kinematical Foundations of the Symmetric Relativity Model: Lorentz Transformation and Time Dilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06800)
*Miodrag Mateljević*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过放宽爱因斯坦第二公设（单程光速不变），仅基于可直接观测的双程光速（two-way speed of light），结合时空均匀性、线性和互易性公理，重构了狭义相对论的动力学基础。研究发现，经典的洛伦兹变换可沿坐标轴精确恢复，朗之万光钟论证要求纵向尺度因子等于标准洛伦兹因子，横向长度严格不变。为解决多个共存波前中心的存有论悖论，引入了一个绝对宇宙学静止参考系$K$下的对称运动模型，允许各向异性单程光传播，推导出线性的速度叠加律、广义多普勒效应及平坦但倾斜的时空度规，并证明所有双程可观测量在同步规范变换下严格不变，所得非对角度规结构与萨尼亚克效应（Sagnac effect）完全自洽。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索狭义相对论的运动学基础是否可以脱离爱因斯坦第二公设（单程光速不变），仅基于可直接观测的双程光速以及时空对称性公理重新推导出来，并解决其中存在的多个共存波前中心之存有论悖论。

Method: 采用操作主义（operationalism）框架，基于时空均匀性、线性变换和互易性，仅以可直接测量的双程光速为观测基础；引入Reichenbach型参数（$\varepsilon$ 或 $\kappa$）描述各向异性单程光传播，并建立相对于绝对宇宙学静止参考系$K$的对称运动模型。

Result: (i) 在广义双程同步方案下，无需爱因斯坦第二公设即可沿坐标轴精确恢复经典洛伦兹变换；(ii) 朗之万光钟论证要求纵向尺度因子$b$等于标准洛伦兹因子$\gamma$；(iii) 横向长度严格不变（$b_z = 1$）；(iv) 在对称框架下推导出线性速度叠加律、广义多普勒效应和平坦但倾斜的时空度规；(v) 所有双程可观测量在同步规范变换下严格不变，非对角度规结构与萨尼亚克效应一致。

Conclusion: 狭义相对论的运动学框架可以在不依赖单程光速不变假定的前提下重建，双程光速与时空对称性公理构成的公理化基础更为简洁且自洽；引入绝对参考系$K$及Reichenbach参数能有效解决波前中心悖论，且所得理论在可观测量层面与标准相对论不可区分。

Abstract: We examine the kinematic foundations of relativity by considering two inertial frames, $S$ and $S'$, in a standard configuration, where $S'$ moves along the common spatial $x$-axis at a constant velocity $v$. By relaxing Einstein's second postulate regarding the universal invariance of the one-way speed of light, we adopt an operational framework grounded strictly on the directly observable two-way (round-trip) speed of light, evaluated alongside the principles of spacetime homogeneity, linearity, and reciprocity.
  Within this setting, we demonstrate that: (i) the classical Lorentz transformation is recovered exactly along the coordinate axes under a generalized two-way synchronization scheme without requiring Einstein's second postulate; (ii) Langevin's light-clock argument fundamentally implies that the longitudinal scale factor $b$ matches the standard Lorentz factor $γ$; and (iii) transverse lengths remain strictly invariant ($b_z = 1$).
  Crucially, to resolve the ontic paradox of multiple co-existing wavefront centers, we introduce a kinematically symmetric model relative to an absolute cosmological rest frame (or geometric anchor) $K$, wherein $S$ and $S'$ move with equal and opposite velocities ($u$ and $-u$, respectively). Within this generalized framework, allowing for anisotropic one-way light propagation via Reichenbach-type parameters ($\varepsilon$ or $κ$) yields a consistent, linear velocity-addition law, a generalized Doppler effect, and a flat but oblique spacetime metric. Finally, we prove that all round-trip observables remain strictly invariant under synchronization gauge transformations (reflecting the Tangherlini-Edwards perspective) and demonstrate that the resulting non-diagonal metric structure is fully consistent withthe Sagnac effect over closed spatial loops.

</details>


### [194] [Global time-analytic strong solutions for a class of 3-wave kinetic equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06836)
*Nguyen Gia Hien,Gigliola Staffilani,Minh-Binh Tran*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对波湍流理论（wave turbulence theory）中一类带有正则化核（regularized kernels）的三波动力学方程（3-wave kinetic equations），构造了一类全局时间强解（global-in-time strong solution），该解保持非负性且在时间上解析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波湍流理论中的动力学方程通常难以获得全局解析解，现有方法在处理共振相互作用面（resonant interaction surfaces）的奇异性时面临困难。本文旨在为正则化核情形下的三波动力学方程构造精确的全局强解。

Method: 方法结合了共振相互作用面的精细分析、时间幂级数构造（time power-series construction）以及基于能量矩守恒（conservation of the energy moment）的延拓论证（continuation argument）。

Result: 对于径向、非负的初始数据，构造了精确的全局时间强解，该解始终保持非负性，且在时间上是解析的。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，在正则化核的设定下，三波动力学方程具有良好的适定性，所构造的解析解为进一步研究波湍流系统的长期行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study a class of 3-wave kinetic equations arising in wave turbulence theory, with regularized kernels. For radial, nonnegative initial data, we construct an exact global-in-time strong solution which remains nonnegative and is analytic with respect to time. The proof combines a careful analysis of the resonant interaction surfaces with a time power-series construction and a continuation argument based on the conservation of the energy moment.

</details>


### [195] [Invariant Measures for Soliton Systems Generated by Mealy Automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06942)
*Takahiro Kanazawa,Yutaro Nakabayashi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由Mealy自动机描述的孤子系统的不变测度，给出了伯努利乘积测度与马尔可夫分布不变性的充分条件与判据，并将其应用于三类变体盒-球系统，分别证明了不变性并计算了孤子相互作用相移与孤立子速度，为广义流体动力学研究奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期关于2字母、3状态Mealy自动机孤子模型的启发，本文旨在系统性地研究由Mealy自动机在双无穷位形空间上诱导的时间演化下不变测度的存在性与条件，从而为这些系统的广义流体动力学（generalized hydrodynamics）与广义吉布斯系综（generalized Gibbs ensembles）的理论分析提供基础。

Method: 本文首先在双无穷位形空间（bi-infinite configuration space）上形式化定义了由Mealy自动机诱导的时间演化。随后，给出伯努利乘积测度（Bernoulli product measure）不变性的充分条件，并推导出双侧空间齐次马尔可夫分布（two-sided space-homogeneous Markov distribution）不变性的判据。最后，将上述一般性理论应用于三类可解释为盒-球系统（box-ball system, BBS）变体的孤子模型。

Result: 对于BBS-S(2)和BBS-V(2)两种模型，证明了伯努利乘积测度是不变测度；对于BBS-C(2)模型，进一步证明了双侧空间齐次马尔可夫分布的不变性，其中伯努利乘积测度作为其特例。此外，对所有三个模型计算了两个孤子相互作用时的相移（phase shift）以及孤立孤子的速度。

Conclusion: 这些结果构成了Mealy自动机孤子系统中不变测度、广义吉布斯系综与广义流体动力学行为研究的理论基础。尽管孤立子速度已有先前研究，但相移与速度共同构成了理解这些系统广义流体动力学的基本特征量。

Abstract: We study invariant measures for soliton systems described by Mealy automata. Motivated by recently introduced soliton models associated with 2-letter, 3-state Mealy automata, we formulate the time evolution induced by Mealy automata on bi-infinite configuration spaces. We provide sufficient conditions for the invariance of Bernoulli product measures and derive a criterion for the invariance of two-sided space-homogeneous Markov distributions. We then apply these general results to three soliton models, which can be interpreted as variants of the box-ball system (BBS). For two of these models, BBS-S(2) and BBS-V(2), we prove that Bernoulli product measures are invariant. For the remaining model, BBS-C(2), we establish a more general result: the invariance of two-sided space-homogeneous Markov distributions, which include Bernoulli product measures as a special case. Furthermore, for all three models, we compute the phase shift associated with the interaction of two solitons, as well as the velocity of an isolated soliton. Although the latter has already been studied previously, both quantities constitute fundamental characteristics for understanding the generalized hydrodynamics of these systems. These results provide a foundation for the study of invariant measures, generalized Gibbs ensembles, and generalized hydrodynamic behavior in Mealy-automaton soliton systems.

</details>


### [196] [Hamiltonian reduction from particular integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07057)
*R. Azuaje,A. M. Escobar-Ruiz,I. Gutierrez-Sagredo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种由特定积分（particular integrals）生成的几何约化机制：若一族函数的时间导数在该族上线性封闭，则定义了一个不变零级子流形；在哈密顿（Hamiltonian）情形下，若该族函数处于对合（involution）状态，受限动力学是预辛（presymplectic）的，其特征商空间承载约化哈密顿流，从而在特定积分、预辛约化和低维哈密顿动力学之间建立直接桥梁，并导出一种刘维尔型特定可积性（Liouville-type particular integrability）概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有约化方法多基于对称性（symmetry）或首次积分（first integrals），缺乏由特定积分直接生成几何约化的统一框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过特定积分构建一种新型几何约化机制，并将其与预辛约化（presymplectic reduction）和哈密顿动力学联系起来。

Method: 定义一族函数，其时间导数在该族上线性封闭，从而生成一个不变零级子流形（invariant zero-level submanifold）。在哈密顿情形下，要求该族函数处于对合关系，则受限动力学自然具有预辛结构，进一步通过特征商空间（characteristic quotient）得到约化哈密顿流。

Result: 建立了特定积分、预辛约化与低维哈密顿动力学之间的直接对应关系，并提出了刘维尔型特定可积性概念。通过力学示例及抬升构造（lift constructions）（包括艾森哈特抬升（Eisenhart lift）的变体）验证了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种从特定积分出发进行几何约化的新途径，扩展了哈密顿约化理论，并为特定可积系统（particular integrable systems）的分析提供了统一的几何语言。

Abstract: We develop a geometric reduction mechanism generated by particular integrals. A family of functions whose time derivatives close linearly on the same family defines an invariant zero-level submanifold. In the Hamiltonian case, if this family is in involution, the restricted dynamics is presymplectic, and its characteristic quotient carries a reduced Hamiltonian flow. This yields a direct bridge between particular integrals, presymplectic reduction, and lower-dimensional Hamiltonian dynamics, and leads to a Liouville-type notion of particular integrability. We illustrate the framework through mechanical examples and lift constructions, including variants of the Eisenhart lift.

</details>


### [197] [Error bounds for the truncated Baker--Campbell--Hausdorff and Zassenhaus formulas in unitary problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07692)
*A. Arnal,F. Casas,J. L. Ruiz-Benito*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该工作针对量子演化问题中涉及的斜埃尔米特（skew-adjoint）算子，提出了一套通用策略，为 Baker–Campbell–Hausdorff (BCH) 公式和 Zassenhaus 公式推导了严格的误差界（error bounds）与显式误差常数（explicit error constants）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BCH 公式与 Zassenhaus 公式在数学和物理的多个分支中有重要应用，但在实际计算中通常需要对无穷级数或无穷乘积进行截断（truncate），从而引入近似误差。因此，理解并量化这一截断误差，提供可靠的误差界，具有重要的理论与实际意义。

Method: 提出了一种通用策略（general strategy），用于在算子为斜埃尔米特（skew-adjoint）的条件下，系统性地推导 BCH 公式和 Zassenhaus 公式的严格误差界以及显式的误差常数。

Result: 给出了针对斜埃尔米特算子的 BCH 公式和 Zassenhaus 公式的严格误差界（rigorous error bounds）与显式误差常数（explicit error constants）。

Conclusion: 该策略适用于量子演化（quantum evolution）问题中涉及斜埃尔米特算子的情形，为截断后的 BCH 和 Zassenhaus 近似提供了可量化的误差保障。

Abstract: The Baker--Campbell--Hausdorff (BCH) formula plays a critical role in many branches of mathematics and physics. It expresses the logarithm of the product of exponentials of non-commuting operators as an infinite series of nested commutators of the operators involved. The Zassenhaus formula is the dual of the BCH formula: the exponential of a sum of operators is written as an infinite product of exponentials involving the operators and their commutators. In practical computations, however, one typically has to truncate the expansions, and so understanding the error committed by the resulting approximations and eventually providing suitable bounds for this error is of paramount interest. In this work we present a general strategy to derive rigorous error bounds and explicit error constants for the BCH and Zassenhaus formulas when the operators involved are skew-adjoint, as is the case for quantum evolution problems.

</details>

### [198] [When the Environment Speaks: Quantum Signatures in Non-Attractor Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07602)
*Mattia Cielo,Simone Scarlatella,Gianpiero Mangano,Ofelia Pisanti*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究暴胀（inflation）期间存在瞬态超慢滚（Ultra-Slow-Roll, USR）相时，绝热曲率扰动（adiabatic curvature perturbation）与质量熵标量环境（massive entropic scalar environment）之间的开放量子动力学。通过精确传输方程方法（Transport Equations Method）追踪系统协方差矩阵的非幺正、非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）演化，发现退相干效率对视界穿越时的背景运动学敏感，且环境相互作用会在原初标量功率谱和标量诱导引力波（Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves）上留下可观测印记，表明量子环境在暴胀中并非被动旁观者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暴胀宇宙学模型通常将量子涨落视为孤立系统，忽略环境噪声对其退相干和观测信号的影响。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究在包含瞬态USR相的场景下，熵标量环境如何通过开放量子动力学影响绝热曲率扰动的演化和可观测印记。

Method: 在高斯双场有效拉格朗日量（Gaussian two-field effective Lagrangian）框架下，采用精确传输方程方法（Transport Equations Method），模拟系统协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）在慢滚-超慢滚-慢滚（SR-USR-SR）相变过程中的完整非幺正、非马尔可夫演化。

Result: 退相干效率对背景运动学在视界穿越（horizon crossing）时的细节敏感。环境相互作用会部分或完全抹平USR驱动的增强峰之前的特征干涉谷（interference dip），改变增长斜率，并在峰值附近诱发振荡特征。这些畸变进一步传递到二阶标量诱导引力波上，打破单场暴胀预测，产生LISA可能探测到的独特谱特征。

Conclusion: 量子环境在暴胀期间并非被动旁观者（passive spectator），而是主动参与系统演化的活跃要素，其印记可能被下一代宇宙学观测所触及。

Abstract: We study the open quantum dynamics of the adiabatic curvature perturbation interacting with a massive entropic scalar environment during an inflationary scenario featuring a transient Ultra-Slow-Roll phase. Working within a Gaussian two-field effective Lagrangian, we employ the exact Transport Equations Method to track the full non-unitary, non-Markovian evolution of the system's covariance matrix across the SR-USR-SR transition. We find that the efficiency of decoherence is sensitive to the background kinematics at horizon crossing. Most importantly, the interaction with the environment leaves distinct observable imprints on the primordial scalar power spectrum: the characteristic interference dip preceding the USR-driven enhancement can be partially or completely erased, the growth slope modified, and oscillatory features induced near the peak. Propagated to second order, these distortions further imprint on the stochastic background of Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves, breaking single-field predictions and yielding unique spectral signatures potentially accessible to LISA. Our results demonstrate that the quantum environment is not a passive spectator during inflation, but an active agent whose imprint on the primordial universe may be within reach of the next generation of cosmological observations.

</details>

### [199] [Noncommutative vector field calculi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07243)
*Rita Fioresi,Emanuele Latini,Thomas Weber*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 该论文从向量场（vector field）视角出发，系统讨论非交换微分几何（noncommutative differential geometry），引入一阶向量场演算（FOVC）概念，建立其与一阶微分演算（differential calculi）的对偶关系，并拓展至协变情形、Hopf代数（Hopf algebras）及Hopf–Galois扩张（Hopf–Galois extensions），最终通过层论（sheaf-theoretic）方法丰富该框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非交换微分几何主要基于微分形式（differential form）视角，而向量场视角尚缺乏系统性的形式化表述。本文旨在以向量场为中心，建立一种与原微分形式途径对偶但不等价的完整理论框架。

Method: 以Borowiec先前提出的Cartan对（Cartan pair）为基础，形式化定义一阶向量场演算（FOVC），构造FOVC范畴与一阶微分演算范畴之间的伴随关系（adjunction），并将该对应扩展到协变情形。在Hopf代数上建立（双）协变FOVC与（双）协变量子切空间（quantum tangent spaces）的双射，在Hopf–Galois扩张中利用量子切空间定义纵向、底和水平向量场，并通过非交换Atiyah序列（noncommutative Atiyah sequence）关联它们。

Result: 证明了向量场视角与微分形式视角之间的对偶关系，建立了协变FOVC与协变微分演算之间的对应。在Hopf代数上给出了（双）协变FOVC与（双）协变量子切空间的双射。在Hopf–Galois扩张中构造了三种向量场及其联系，并通过非交换Atiyah序列加以刻画。提供了基于辫导子（braided derivations）、有限群（finite groups）和量子Hopf纤维化（quantum Hopf fibration）的多个示例。

Conclusion: 向量场视角为非交换微分几何提供了一种与微分形式途径对偶但不等价的系统框架，并通过层论处理将前述构造融入局部（仿射）图景（local, or affine, picture），从而丰富了非交换微分几何的理论工具。

Abstract: We discuss noncommutative differential geometry from a vector field centric point of view. This is based on the notion of first order vector field calculus (FOVC), which has been previously introduced by Borowiec under the name Cartan pair. We define the universal FOVC and construct an adjunction between the categories of FOVC and that of first order differential calculi, showing that the vector field approach is dual, though not equivalent, to the differential form one. This correspondence is then extended to covariant vector field and differential calculi. On Hopf algebras, (bi)covariant FOVC are in bijection with (bicovariant) quantum tangent spaces. For Hopf--Galois extensions, quantum tangent spaces give rise to vertical vector fields and in this setup we further describe base vector fields and horizontal vector fields and show that they are related via a noncommutative Atiyah sequence. Multiple examples, based on braided derivations, finite groups and the quantum Hopf fibration, are given. The vector field approach is further enriched by a sheaf-theoretic treatment, which recovers the former as a local, or affine, picture.

</details>

### [200] [On the generalised Lie derivative of (s)pinor fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07360)
*Frederik Ďalak,Fridrich Valach*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了Kosmann与Bourguignon-Gauduchon关于pinor场（或旋量场）的经典Lie导数构造，并将其推广至广义几何（generalised geometry）框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然微分同胚（diffeomorphism）在pinor场（或旋量场）上的作用在几何上是明确的，但自然Lie导数（Lie derivative）的定义更为微妙，需要理解某点处度规空间（space of metrics）的几何结构。本文旨在澄清这一构造并拓展其适用范围。

Method: 本文回顾了Kosmann与Bourguignon-Gauduchon的经典构造，并基于对度规在一点处的几何结构的分析，将相关理论发展至广义几何的框架中。

Result: 成功将pinor场上的自然Lie导数构造从经典黎曼几何推广到广义几何设定中。

Conclusion: 本文的工作为广义几何中pinor场的Lie导数提供了清晰的理论基础，拓展了经典构造的适用范围。

Abstract: Although the action of diffeomorphisms on pinor (or spinor) fields is geometrically unambiguous, the definition of a natural Lie derivative is more subtle and requires some understanding of the geometry of the space of metrics at a point. In this work we revisit the classical construction of Kosmann and Bourguignon-Gauduchon and develop the corresponding theory in generalised geometry.
